#Author:Keśava
#Text:Kauśikasūtrapaddhati
#Comments:Kauśikasūtra
#Data entry:Arlo Griffiths
#Notes:Markup complete.
#Todo:final formatting! “'” is used for marking quotations and avagraha.


1.1.1.[1]	athaśabda ānantaryārthaḥ /
1.1.1.[2]	saṃhitādhyayanānantaraṃ vidheradhikāraḥ /
1.1.1.[3]	saṃhitāvidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
1.1.1.[4]	śāntikapauṣṭikābhicārikādbhutādīni karmāṇi saṃhitāvidhāv uktāni /
1.1.1.[5]	trividhāni karmāṇi /
1.1.1.[6]	vidhikarmāṇy avidhikarmāṇy ucchrayakarmāṇi /
1.1.1.[7]	tripramāṇako vidhiḥ /
1.1.1.[8]	pratyakṣam anumānaṃ śabdaṃ ceti //
1.1.2.[1]	sa vidhir vedapratyayaḥ /
1.1.2.[2]	gopathabrāhmaṇapramāṇakaḥ //
1.1.3.[1]	āmnāyaśabdena kimu cyate /
1.1.3.[2]	tatrāha mantrabrāhmaṇam āmnāyaśabdenocyate //
1.1.4.[1]	yathā saṃhitāvidheḥ karmoktaṃ tathaivaṃliṅgā mantrā api bhavanti /
1.1.4.[2]	yathā vātājjāta iti śaṅkhaṃ badhnāti //
1.1.5.[1]	anyārthā api mantrā bhavanti /
1.1.5.[2]	yathā 'agniṃ brūmo utāmṛtāsuḥ śivāsta ityabhyākhyātāya prayacchati' //
1.1.6.[1]	'brahma ha vā idam agra āsīt' ityādi pūrvabrāhmaṇam /
1.1.6.[2]	evaṃrūpā api mantrā bhavanti /
1.1.6.[3]	yathā 'virāḍ vā idam agra āsīt' ityādyarthavādārthā api mantrā bhavanti //
1.1.7.[1]	saṃhitāvidhau yannāmnāyate tat sarvaṃ svaśākhānyāyena paramparayā sampradāyena kartavyam /
1.1.7.[2]	tathā coktaṃ bhaṭṭapādaiḥ - nyāyena sampradāyena yānti karmāṇi mīmāṃsakā iti /
1.1.7.[3]	tathā nadīvālukayā vedikaraṇaṃ śāntikakarmasu śāntavṛkṣakāṣṭhena vedimānaṃ ca /
1.1.7.[4]	tathā mīmāṃsāyāṃ smṛtipāde smṛtyācārāṇāṃ pramāṇam uktam //
1.1.8.[1]	ācārasampradāyaviṣaye vismṛtāni brāhmaṇāni /
1.1.8.[2]	śiṣyaiḥ sampradāyo rakṣitaḥ /
1.1.8.[3]	upavarṣācāryeṇoktaṃ mīmāṃsāyāṃ smṛtipāde kalpasūtrādhikaraṇe /
1.1.8.[4]	nakṣatrakalpo vaitānastṛtīyaḥ saṃhitāvidhiḥ /
1.1.8.[5]	caturtho'ṅgirasāṃ kalpaḥ śāntikalpastu pañcamaḥ //
1.1.8.[6]	iti /
1.1.8.[7]	'ete kalpā vedatulyā hi' iti bhagavatopavarṣācāryeṇa pratipāditam /
1.1.8.[8]	anye kalpāḥ smṛtitulyāḥ //
1.1.9-10.[1]	pākatantramājyatantraṃ ca yajñaśabdenocyate /
1.1.9-10.[2]	taṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ /
1.1.9-10.[3]	devānāṃ yajñaḥ śāntikapauṣṭikādi /
1.1.9-10.[4]	pitṝṇāṃ pitṛmedhapiṇḍapitṛyajñādi //
1.1.11.[1]	prāṅmukhaḥ sarvakarmāṇi karoti /
1.1.11.[2]	nityanaimittikakāmyāni karmāṇi /
1.1.11.[3]	upāṃśu ca /
1.1.11.[4]	ekapuruṣāntaraṃ dvitīyaḥ puruṣaḥ śṛṇoti śabdaṃ tadupāṃśvityucyate //
1.1.12-13.[1]	yajñopavītī bhūtvā nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ ca karma kuryāt /
1.1.12-13.[2]	apasavyaṃ kṛtvā pitṛkarma kuryāt piṇḍapitṛyajñādi //
1.1.14-15.[1]	prāṅmukho vodaṅmukho vā devakarmāṇi sarvāṇi kuryāt /
1.1.14-15.[2]	dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ pitṛkarmāṇi kuryāt /
1.1.14-15.[3]	kecit dakṣiṇapūrvamantardeśamabhimukhaḥ pitṛkarma kuryāt //
1.1.16-17.[1]	prāgudagvā karmasamāptirdaivakarmasu /
1.1.16-17.[2]	dakṣiṇā pratyagvā samāptiḥ pitṛkarmasu /
1.1.16-17.[3]	kecit-prāgudagantarāle samāptiḥ //
1.1.18-19.[1]	ācamanaprokṣaṇādiṣu pitṝṇāṃ sakṛt karma kuryāt /
1.1.18-19.[2]	devānāṃ caturvā trirvā sarvaṃ karma kuryāt /
1.1.18-19.[3]	nirvapaṇaparistaraṇājyagrahaṇādi karma //
1.1.20.[1]	yathāpaṭhitaṃ vā karma kuryāt /
1.1.20.[2]	yathā 'pari tvāgne puraṃ vayam iti triḥ paryagni karoti' //
1.1.21-22.[1]	pradakṣiṇaṃ devānāṃ karma kuryāt /
1.1.21-22.[2]	apradakṣiṇaṃ pitṛkarma //
1.1.23-24.[1]	devānāṃ havirdīyate svāhākāreṇa vaṣaṭkāreṇa vā /
1.1.23-24.[2]	'svāhāntābhiḥ pratyṛcaṃ homāḥ' sarvatra /
1.1.23-24.[3]	svadhākāreṇa namaskāreṇa pitṝṇāṃ dīyate //
1.1.25-26.[1]	samūlaṃ barhiḥ pitṝṇām /
1.1.25-26.[2]	lūnaṃ devānāṃ barhiḥ /
1.1.25-26.[3]	sakṛdācchinnaṃ pitṝṇāṃ barhiḥ /
1.1.25-26.[4]	upaharaṇam /
1.1.25-26.[5]	'uttarato'gnerupasādayatīdhmamuttaraṃ barhiḥ'
1.1.27.[1]	'pra yaccha parśum' ityādi 'ahiṃsantaḥ' ityantena //
1.1.28.[1]	'oṣadhīrdāntu parvan' ityādiśeṣeṇa barhir lūtvā tūṣṇīm āhṛtyottarato'gner upasādayati /
1.1.28.[2]	āvasathyāgneruttarato barhirupasādayati /
1.1.28.[3]	kecid vratopāyanāntaṃ kṛtvā barhirlavanaṃ kurvanti /
1.1.28.[4]	karmaṇāṃ dvyahakālatvāt //
1.1.29.[1]	agniṃ pṛṣṭhato na vaseta /
1.1.29.[2]	nāpradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt //
1.1.30.[1]	antarā madhye na gacchet /
1.1.30.[2]	agnau yajñapātreṣu brāhmaṇeṣu vyavāyaṃ na kuryāt //
1.1.31.[1]	homakarmakāle dakṣiṇaṃ jānu prapātya tato homaḥ kāryaḥ //
1.1.32-33.[1]	sāṅkhyāyanīye brāhmaṇe uktaṃ 'dve paurṇamāsyau dve amāvāsye' iti /
1.1.32-33.[2]	paurṇamāsī pratipaditi /
1.1.32-33.[3]	amāvāsyā pratipaditi /
1.1.32-33.[4]	pūrvopoṣyottarā yājyā /
1.1.32-33.[5]	kecit pūrvā caturdaśī manyante /
1.1.32-33.[6]	keciccaturdaśīmiśrā paurṇamāsyamāvāsyeti /
1.1.32-33.[7]	tithibhede caturdaśīmiśropoṣyā pratipanmiśrā yājyā //
1.1.34.[1]	tithibhede mukhyā paurṇamāsī /
1.1.34.[2]	bhede yā pūrvā sopoṣyā /
1.1.34.[3]	upavāsaṃ karoti /
1.1.34.[4]	upavāso vede bhaktamaśanam /
1.1.34.[5]	yena yāgaṃ karoti tannāśnāti yajamānaḥ //
1.1.35.[1]	etānyupavasathe nāśnīyāt /
1.1.35.[2]	etāni dravyāṇi prasiddhāni /
1.1.35.[3]	vratopāyanāntaṃ kṛtvā tato vratagrahaṇaṃ karoti /
1.1.35.[4]	brahmacaryādi karoti /
1.1.35.[5]	trividhāni karmāṇi /
1.1.35.[6]	vidhikarmāṇyavidhikarmāṇyucchrayakarmāṇi /
1.1.35.[7]	medhājananādi piṇḍapitṛyajñāntaṃ vidhikarmatvam /
1.1.35.[8]	anadhyāyakaṇḍikā ca /
1.1.35.[9]	madhuparkādīndramahāntam avidhikarmatvam /
1.1.35.[10]	yatra sūktaviniyogaṃ kṛtvā punarṛcāṃ viniyogastatrocchrayakarmatvaṃ yathā 'uduttamam' iti /
1.1.35.[11]	paribhāṣā prathame'dhyāye sarvārthā vidhikarmārthā'vidhikarmārthā ca /
1.1.35.[12]	pariśiṣṭānāṃ paribhāṣātvam /
1.1.35.[13]	pañcakalpānāṃ vidhikarmatvam /
1.1.35.[14]	adbhuteṣu dvitīyā paribhāṣā /
1.1.35.[15]	kulaṃ vā grāmo vā janapado vā tatra rājā bhūmipatir vidvāṃsaṃ bhūgvaṅgirasaṃ vṛṇīyāt ityādi tatroktam /
1.1.35.[16]	kauśikoktānāṃ karmaṇāṃ viduṣāṃ hitārthāyānuṣṭhānapaddhatiḥ kriyate //
1.1.35.[17]	'avyasaśca' barhirlavanavedyuttaravedyagnipratiṣṭhāpanāntaṃ kṛtvā
1.1.36-39.[1]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti samidha ādhāya 'vratena tvaṃ vratapate' ityṛcā bhaktaṃ juhoti /
1.1.36-39.[2]	etat kṛtvā tato dvitīye'hanīdaṃ karoti //
1.1.40-41.[1]	'karmaṇe vām' iti mantreṇa hastaprakṣālanam /
1.1.40-41.[2]	apareṇāgner darbhān āstīrya teṣūttaram ānaḍuhaṃ rohitaṃ carma stṛṇāti /
1.1.40-41.[3]	pavitre kurute darbhāv apracchinnaprāntau /
1.1.40-41.[4]	prakṣālyānulomam anumārṣṭi 'viṣṇor manasā pūte sthaḥ' iti mantreṇa //
1.2.1.[1]	sāyamprātarhomavaiśvadevapiṇḍapitṛyajñādi uddhṛte'gnau kāryāṇi /
1.2.1.[2]	'tvaṃ bhūmim' ity ṛcā carmaṇi pavitre nidhāya caturo muṣṭīn nirvapati 'devasya tvā' iti /
1.2.1.[3]	tūṣṇīṃ caturtham /
1.2.1.[4]	'agnaye juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' //
1.2.2.[1]	'agnīṣomābhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' iti vikāraḥ //
1.2.3-5.[1]	'agnaye tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi' iti /
1.2.3-5.[2]	agnīṣomābhyāṃ ca /
1.2.3-5.[3]	prokṣaṇaṃ dvayorapi //
1.2.6.[1]	'arātīyoḥ' ityṛcolūkhalamusalaṃ takṣati 'yat tvā śikvaḥ' ity ṛcā prakṣālayati 'yad yat kṛṣṇaḥ' ityṛcā mārjapati /
1.2.6.[2]	tataḥ ulūkhale vrīhīnopya 'haviṣkṛd ā dravehi' ity anenāvahanti triḥ /
1.2.6.[3]	tataḥ śūrpaniṣpavanam /
1.2.6.[4]	tatas triḥ prakṣālanaṃ taṇḍulānām //
1.2.7.[1]	agne carur ityṛcā carum adhidadhāti //
1.2.8.[1]	'śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ' ity ṛcodakamāsiñcati //
1.2.9.[1]	'brahmaṇā śuddhāḥ' ityṛcā taṇḍulānāvapati pavitre antardhānaṃ kṛtvā //
1.2.10.[1]	'pari tvāgne puraṃ vayam' ityṛcā triḥ paryagnikaraṇam //
1.2.11-14.[1]	agner uttarata idhmam upasādayati /
1.2.11-14.[2]	tato barhiḥ //
1.2.15.[1]	'agnaye tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi' itīdhmaprokṣaṇam //
1.2.16.[1]	'pṛthivyai tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi' iti barhiḥprokṣaṇam //
1.2.17.[1]	darbhamuṣṭimabhyukṣya paścādagneḥ stṛṇāti 'ūrṇamradam' iti mantreṇa //
1.2.18.[1]	'ṛṣīṇāṃ prastaro'si' iti dakṣiṇato'gnerbrahmāsanaṃ nidadhati /
1.2.18.[2]	'bhūpate' iti brahmavaraṇam /
1.2.18.[3]	tathā ca gobhilabrāhmaṇam /
1.2.18.[4]	pratyakṣaṃ vā darbhamayaṃ vāsanamudakakamaṇḍaluṃ vā brahmasthāne kuryāt /
1.2.18.[5]	tato brahmāsanasaṃskāraḥ //
1.2.19.[1]	tataḥ staraṇaṃ purastādagneriti /
1.2.19.[2]	kartā bravīti
1.2.20-21.[1]	tato 'devasya tvā' iti stṛṇāti //
1.2.22-23.[1]	paribhojanīyān stṛṇāti //
1.2.24-29.[1]	sarvatra eṣā paribhāṣā //
1.2.30.[1]	sruvam ājyadhānīṃ nidadhati //
1.2.31-35.[1]	'viṣṇor manasā pūtam asi' iti //
1.2.36.[1]	śṛtaṃ havirabhighārayati 'madhvā samañjan' iti //
1.2.37.[1]	'udvāsayāgneḥ' ityṛcodvāsayati //
1.2.38.[1]	tataḥ paścād ājyasya nidhāyālaṅkṛtyājyena carum abhighārya samānenotpunāti //
1.2.39-40.[1]	carum avekṣate //
1.3.1.[1]	'agnir bhūmyām oṣadhīṣu', 'agnirdiva ā tapati', 'agnivāsāḥ pṛthivyasitajñūḥ', 'asmai kṣatrāṇi dhārayantamagne', 'etamidhmam' iti vā, 'yunajmi tvā' ityebhiḥ pañcabhir idhmam upasamādadhāti //
1.3.1.[2]	dvitīyā kaṇḍikā //
1.3.2.[1]	dakṣiṇato 'gner jāṅmāyanamudapātraṃ kāṃsyapātram upasādyābhimantrayate 'tathodapātraṃ dhāraya' ity ṛcā //
1.3.3.[1]	'iheta devīḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ santatadhārayodapātramavasiñcati //
1.3.4.[1]	'ṛtaṃ tvā satyena' iti saha havirbhiḥ paryukṣya sarvatra sthaṇḍilakarmaṇi hoṣyan 'ṛtaṃ tvā satyena' hutvā 'satyaṃ tvartena' iti sampradāyagrantha uktam /
1.3.4.[2]	'jīvā stha' iti sūktena trirācāmati /
1.3.4.[3]	'satyaṃ bṛhat' iti navabhiḥ 'śāntivā' ityṛcā 'udāyuṣā' iti dvābhyāmuttiṣṭhati /
1.3.4.[4]	vedaprapadbhiḥ prapadyate 'oṃ prapadye bhūḥ' ityṛcā '...prapadye' iti //
1.3.5-8.[1]	āsane darbhān āstīrya 'ahe daidhiṣavyodatastiṣṭha' ity āsanasaṃskāraṃ karoti //
1.3.9.[1]	darbhaiḥ sruvaṃ nirmṛjya 'niṣṭaptaṃ rakṣaḥ' iti sruvaṃ pratapati //
1.3.10-14.[1]	sruveṇājyadhānyāṃ grahagrahaṇaṃ karoti 'oṃ bhūḥ śaṃ bhūtyai tvā' iti caturbhiḥ //
1.3.15-19.[1]	purastāddhomān paścād agner juhoti /
1.3.15-19.[2]	ājyabhāgau pārśvata uttarato dakṣiṇataś ca juhoti /
1.3.15-19.[3]	madhye anye sarve homāḥ /
1.3.15-19.[4]	udapātre sampātaḥ //
1.3.15-19.[5]	tṛtīyā kaṇḍikā //
1.4.1-2.[1]	'vṛṣṇe bṛhate' 'tvaṃ soma divyaḥ' ityājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā tata āgneyaṃ caruṃ juhoti 'ud enam uttaraṃ naya' iti tribhir ṛgbhiḥ 'prajāpate na tvat' iti ca catasra āhutīr juhoti //
1.4.3-10.[1]	ityādi pratyāhuti yojayitavyam //
1.4.11-18.[1]	sarvatra havir ājyaṃ ca caturgṛhītam /
1.4.11-18.[2]	uktaṃ ca 'sarvatra caturgṛhītena homaḥ' //
1.4.19.[1]	agnīṣomīyaṃ caruṃ juhoti 'asmai kṣatram' ityekā, 'agnīṣomā savedasā' iti tribhiḥ //
1.4.19.[2]	caturthī kaṇḍikā //
1.5.2-3.[1]	āmāvāsyāyāmaindrāgnau dvitīyo bhavati 'indrāgnī rocanā' iti catasraḥ //
1.5.4-5.[1]	'pūrṇā paścāt' iti paurṇamāsyāṃ pārvaṇahomaḥ //
1.5.6.[1]	'yat te devāḥ' ity amāvāsyāyāṃ pārvaṇahomaḥ //
1.5.7.[1]	'ākūtyai tvā' iti caturbhiḥ 'ṛcā stomam' iti ca samṛddhihomāñ juhoti /
1.5.7.[2]	udapātre sampātānānayati //
1.5.8.[1]	'pṛthivyām agnaye' ityaṣṭabhiḥ sannatihomāñjuhoti 'prajāpate na tvadetāni' iti ca //
1.5.9-11.[1]	'ā devānām' iti sviṣṭakṛtaṃ juhoti //
1.5.12.[1]	'svāheṣṭebhyaḥ' ityevamādibhirekādaśabhiḥ sarvaprāyaścittīyāñjuhoti /
1.5.12.[2]	'punarmaitvindriyam' iti ca //
1.5.12.[3]	pañcamī kaṇḍikā //
1.6.1-2.[1]	'yanme skannaṃ', 'yadasmṛti' iti ca dvābhyāṃ juhoti /
1.6.1-2.[2]	ājyahome sarvatra sruveṇa homaḥ //
1.6.3.[1]	'yad adya tvā prayati' iti saṃsthitahomāñ juhoti /
1.6.3.[2]	udapātre sampātān ānayati //
1.6.4.[1]	'manasaspate' ity ṛcā caturgṛhītena juhoti //
1.6.5-5.[1]	barhiḥ sthālyāmājyenānakti 'pṛthivyai tvā' iti mūlam 'antarikṣāya tvā' iti madhyaṃ 'dive tvā' ityagram //
1.6.5-5.[2]	trirmantrāvṛttiḥ //
1.6.7-9.[1]	'saṃsrāvabhāgāḥ' ityājyadhānyā ājyaṃ juhoti //
1.6.10.[1]	'sruvo'si ghṛtādaniṣitaḥ' ityṛcā sruvaṃ prāgdaṇḍaṃ nidadhāti //
1.6.11.[1]	'vi muñcāmi' ityṛcā samidhamādadhāti //
1.6.12-14.[1]	'viṣṇoḥ kramo'si' iti tisṛbhir viṣṇukramān kramate /
1.6.12-14.[2]	agner dakṣiṇataḥ /
1.6.12-14.[3]	agnibrahmaṇor madhye kramate //
1.6.15-16.[1]	'aganma svaḥ' iti paryāyadvayenādityamīkṣate //
1.6.17.[1]	'indrasya vacasā' ityṛcodapātramutthāpayati /
1.6.17.[2]	uttarato'gnerudapātreṇa 'āpo hi ṣṭhā' iti mārjayitvā barhiṣi sruvaṃ ca pavitre ca patnyā añjalau kṛtvodapātraṃ ninayati 'samudraṃ vaḥ pra hiṇomi' iti //
1.6.18-20.[1]	'satyaṃ tvartena' iti paryukṣya udañci havirucchiṣṭāny udvāsayati //
1.6.21.[1]	tato brahmakartṛvācanam /
1.6.21.[2]	'uttiṣṭha brahmaṇaspate' ityṛcā brahmāṇamutthāpayet //
1.6.22.[1]	tasmān nādakṣiṇam /
1.6.22.[2]	haviḥśabdenājyatantraṃ pākatantraṃ cocyate /
1.6.22.[3]	karmamātramabhimantraṇādyadakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt /
1.6.22.[4]	pākatantre pūrṇapātramānaṃ prasṛtiprasthadroṇāḍhakādi /
1.6.22.[5]	pūrṇapātraṃ yajamānaśaktyapekṣam /
1.6.22.[6]	'śaktyā vā dakṣiṇāṃ dadyānnātiśaktirvidhīyate' ityuktaṃ navame /
1.6.22.[7]	ājyatantre dhenuḥ sarvatra //

1.8.17.[1]	pramando gendukaḥ /

1.8.21.[1]	grahaṇaṃ pratīkagrahaṇam /

1.9.1.[1]	sarvāṇi sūktāni pratyetavyāni /
1.9.1.[2]	yatra śāntigaṇas tatrāyaṃ gaṇaḥ pratyetavyaḥ /
1.9.1.[3]	śambhumayobhū 'āpo hi ṣṭhā' 'śaṃ no devī' krameṇa prayogaḥ /
1.9.1.[4]	tathā vyākaraṇe 'alpāctaram' iti pūrvanipātaḥ kṛtaḥ samāse /
1.9.1.[5]	'hiraṇyavarṇāḥ' 'nissālām' iti ṣaḍarcam /
1.9.1.[6]	'ye agnayaḥ' iti saptaḥ /
1.9.1.[7]	'brahma jajñānam' ity ekā /
1.9.1.[8]	'uta devāḥ' iti saptarcaṃ sūktam /
1.9.1.[9]	'agner manvaḥ' iti sapta mṛgārasūktāni gṛhītavyāni /
1.9.1.[10]	prathame dve uttamaṃ ca varjayitvā /
1.9.1.[11]	'śaṃ ca no mayaś ca naḥ' ity ekā /
1.9.1.[12]	'punar maitv indriyam' ity ekā /
1.9.1.[13]	'śivā naḥ' ity ekā /
1.9.1.[14]	'śaṃ no vāto vātu' ity ekā /
1.9.1.[15]	śeṣāṇi sūktāni /
1.9.1.[16]	anena śāntigaṇena śāntyudakaṃ kuryāt /
1.9.1.[17]	yatra śāntis tatraitāni sarvāṇi pratyetavyāni //
1.9.2.[1]	yatra śāntyudakaṃ kriyate tatra 'pṛthivyai śrotrāya' iti tribhir ṛgbhiḥ śāntyudakaṃ śāntyudakamadhye prakṣipet /
1.9.2.[2]	anenaiva kārayitā prokṣaṇācamanādīni pratyṛcaṃ karoti //
1.9.3.[1]	athavā'nena gaṇena śāntyudakaṃ karoti /
1.9.3.[2]	bṛhadgaṇena vā caturgaṇena vā śāntyudakaṃ karoti /
1.9.3.[3]	śantātīyam 'utaḥ devāḥ' iti /
1.9.3.[4]	śeṣāṇi pratīkāni kathitāni /
1.9.3.[5]	eṣa śantātīyo gaṇaḥ /

1.9.3.[7]	yathā śantātīyena tilān juhoti //
1.9.4.[1]	yatra śāntyudakaṃ tatra sarvatra pratyāsekaḥ /
1.9.4.[2]	kārayitā prokṣaṇam āsecanam ācamanaṃ karoti //
1.9.5.[1]	iha śāntyudake sarveṣāṃ sūktānāṃ samuccayaḥ /
1.9.5.[2]	anyatra sarvatra yathoktena nyāyena vikalpaḥ /
1.9.5.[3]	iha punargaṇavikalpo na sūktavikalpaḥ //
1.9.6.[1]	ubhayataḥ śāntigaṇasya prārambhe samāptau ca /
1.9.6.[2]	śannodevī sāvitrī ca prayoktavyā /
1.9.6.[3]	samāptau sāvitrī paścāc channodevī karoti /
1.9.6.[4]	tathā ca bhāṣyaṃ sasāvitrīkasya gaṇasya ubhayataḥ śannodevī bhavati //
1.9.6.[5]	atha śāntyudakavidhānam ucyate
1.9.7.[1]	kartā ahatavasano bhūtvā kāṃsyapātre śāntyudakaṃ karoti //
1.9.8.[1]	'atisṛṣṭo apāṃ vṛṣabhaḥ' iti sūktenāpo'tisṛjyāvakaraṃ visarjayati /
1.9.8.[2]	'sarvā imā āpa oṣadhayaḥ' iti pṛṣṭvā /
1.9.8.[3]	kartā brahmāṇaṃ pṛcchati /
1.9.8.[4]	brahmā bravīti 'sarvāḥ' iti /
1.9.8.[5]	cityādibhiḥ sarvābhir auṣadhībhiḥ sarvābhir adbhir gaṅgādinadīsamudrādihradaprabhāsāditīrthebhya āhṛtābhir adbhi śāntyudakaṃ karoti /
1.9.8.[6]	kartā bravīti 'bṛhaspatiprasūtaḥ karavāṇi' iti /
1.9.8.[7]	tato brahmā bravīti 'savitṛprasūtaḥ kurutāṃ bhavān' /
1.9.8.[8]	anujñātaḥ śāntyudakaṃ karoti /
1.9.8.[9]	'śaṃ no devī' ity ṛcā sāvitryā cāmbayoyantigaṇena ca śāntyudakaṃ karoti /
1.9.8.[10]	laghugaṇena bṛhadgaṇena caturgaṇena vā /
1.9.8.[11]	tataḥ sāvitrīśannodevyau /
1.9.8.[12]	tataḥ 'pṛthivyai śrotrāya' iti triḥ pratyāsiñcati /
1.9.8.[13]	śāntyudake śāntyudakaṃ prakṣipati //
1.9.9.[1]	etac chāntyudakaṃ pūrvayā śāntigaṇena kurvīteti gārgyapārthaśravasabhāgalikāṅkāyanoparibabhravakauśikajāṭikāyanakaurupathayaḥ /
1.9.9.[2]	ete śāntyudakaṃ kurvanti //
1.9.10.[1]	ācāryo manyate /
1.9.10.[2]	sarve te kartāro 'vikalpaṃ manyante /
1.9.10.[3]	yatrodakena karma tatra sarvatra śāntyudakaṃ kuryāt /
1.9.10.[4]	ācamanaprokṣaṇāvasecanāplavanādīni sarvāṇi prayojanāni śāntyudakena kāryāṇi /
1.9.10.[5]	yatra paṭhitaṃ tatra kuryāt /
1.9.10.[6]	śāntyudakasya prayojanatritayaṃ kalpapañcake /
1.9.10.[7]	paṭhitaṃ sūtrakāraiś ca śrautasmārteṣu karmasu //
1.9.10.[8]	kārayituḥ prokṣaṇācamanadvitayaṃ sarvadaiva hi /
1.9.10.[9]	agnīnāṃ tu tathā kuryāt śraute smārte dvitīyakam //
1.9.10.[10]	prokṣaṇaṃ vāstuśālāyās tṛtīyaṃ parikīrtitam /
1.9.10.[11]	āplavanāvasecanāni sarvāṇi paṭhitāni ca //
1.9.10.[12]	śāntyudakena kurvīta prayojanair vinā sadā /
1.9.10.[13]	kalpasūtrair na dṛṣṭaṃ yat tadayuktaṃ kadācana //
1.9.10.[14]	yatra punaḥ paṭhitam udakena prayojanaṃ tatra sarvatra karmamadhye kevalaṃ vā kuryāt śāntyartham /
1.9.10.[15]	yatra śāntyudakaṃ tatra kārayitur nityamācamanaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ ca bhavati /
1.9.10.[16]	vāstuprokṣaṇaṃ ca /
1.9.10.[17]	samāptaṃ śāntyudakaṃ karma /

2.1.16.[1]	karmavikalpaḥ /

2.1.16.[3]	iti jātakarma /
2.1.16.[4]	śuklapuṣpaharitapuṣpe iti /
2.1.16.[5]	śaṅkhapuṣpikāndhapuṣpiketi prasiddhe /
2.1.16.[6]	'ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ' iti sūktena śaṅkhanābhiṃ pippalīṃ ca piṣṭvābhimantrya prāśayati jātarūpaśakalena prāk stanagrahaṇāt /
2.1.16.[7]	iti jātakarma //
2.1.17.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ' iti sūktena māṇavakaṃ māturutsaṅge kṛtvā tāluni sampātānānayati /
2.1.17.[2]	samyagvacanakāmo medhākāmaśca /
2.1.17.[3]	prathamapravadasya /
2.1.17.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.1.18.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ' iti sūktena dadhimadhunī ekatrāsādya sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.1.18.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.1.19.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ' iti sūktaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ vācayati /
2.1.19.[2]	daṇḍapradānaṃ kṛtvopanayane nityaṃ vācanam /
2.1.19.[3]	'ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ' iti śuklapuṣpetyādi pañca karmāṇyāyuṣkāmo'pi karoti /
2.1.19.[4]	'vārṣaśatikaṃ karma' iti vācanāt //
2.1.20.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvaṃ no medhe' iti pañcarcena sūktena kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.1.20.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.1.20.[3]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvaṃ no medhe' iti sūktena puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.1.20.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.1.20.[5]	pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'tvaṃ no medhe' iti sūktena rasān sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.1.20.[6]	'tve kratum' iti /
2.1.20.[7]	tata uttaratantram /
2.1.20.[8]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'dyauśca ma idaṃ pṛthivī ca' ityekayā kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.1.20.[9]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.1.20.[10]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'dyauśca me' ityṛcā puroḍāśa sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.1.20.[11]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.1.20.[12]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'dyauśca me' ityṛcā rasān sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.1.20.[13]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.1.21.[1]	'tvaṃ no medhe' iti sūktenādityamupatiṣṭhate /
2.1.21.[2]	'dyauśca me' ityṛcādityamupatiṣṭhate /
2.1.21.[3]	sarvatra medhākāmaḥ //
2.1.22.[1]	āgrahāyaṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadagne tapasā' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ raudanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayet /
2.1.22.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.1.22.[3]	mārgaśīrṣapaurṇamāsyāṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadagne tapasā' iti dvābhyāṃ puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayet /
2.1.22.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.1.22.[5]	mārgaśīrṣapaurṇamāsyāṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadagne tapasā' ityṛgbhyāṃ rasān sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.1.22.[6]	uttaratantram //
2.1.23.[1]	'yad agne tapasā' iti dvābhyām agnim upatiṣṭhate mārgaśīrṣapaurṇamāsyām eva //
2.1.24.[1]	'prātaragnim' iti sūktena nidrāṃ tyaktvā mukhaṃ prakṣālayati /
2.1.24.[2]	'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' iti sūktena suptotthāya mukhaṃ vimārṣṭi /
2.1.24.[3]	udakena prakṣālanam /
2.1.24.[4]	'divaspṛthivyāḥ' 'yathā somaḥ prātaḥsavane' iti sūktābhyāṃ suptotthāya mukhaṃ vimārṣṭi /
2.1.24.[5]	hastena prakṣālayati /
2.1.24.[6]	mukhaprakṣālanaṃ varcaskāmo'pi karoti /
2.1.24.[7]	udakābhimantraṇaṃ svayaṃ vā'nyo'pi vā karoti /
2.1.24.[8]	medhāvyekaṃ karma kuryād dve vā sarvāṇi vā /
2.1.24.[9]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.1.24.[10]	karmabāhulyāt phalabāhulyam /
2.1.24.[11]	abhyāse ca punaḥ karmasiddhiḥ /
2.1.24.[12]	medhākarmāṇi samāptāni //
2.1.24.[13]	prathamā kaṇḍikā //10 //
2.2.1.[1]	paurṇamāsyāṃ nirṛtikarma kṛtvā sakṛt śvo bhūte sāmpadaṃ kurute //
2.2.2.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenaudumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
2.2.2.[2]	hastahomatvāt tantravikalpaḥ /
2.2.2.[3]	ato brahmacārī sampatkāmo'nuvartate /
2.2.2.[4]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena palāśasamidha ādadhāti /
2.2.2.[5]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena bṛhadbadarīsamidha ādadhāti //
2.2.3.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena brahmacārī gṛhādupastaraṇāni tṛṇānyādadhāti //
2.2.4.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenāraṇyapipīlikācchidre medomāṃsamadhuśyāmākaśaratūlānyājyaṃ caitāni dravyāṇi juhoti /
2.2.4.[2]	pañcakṛtvaḥ sūktāvṛttiḥ //
2.2.5.[1]	pañca dravyāṇi chidre hutvā tataḥ saṅgṛhyājyasthālyāṃ kṛtvā grāma āgatyābhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena sthālyāḥ sakṛjjuhoti /
2.2.5.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.2.6.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenānnamabhimantrya brahmacāriṇo bhojayet /
2.2.6.[2]	bhukte sati 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena dhānāḥ tilamiśrā abhimantrya dadāti /
2.2.6.[3]	samāptāni brahmacārisāmpadāni /
2.2.6.[4]	brahmacārisāmpadāni śiṣyasampattirbhavatītyarthaḥ /
2.2.6.[5]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ //
2.2.6.[6]	atha grāmasāmpadakarmocyate
2.2.7.[1]	pūrvedyurnirṛtikarma kṛtvā grāmasāmpadānāmadhikāraḥ //
2.2.8.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenaudumbaratakṣaṇānyādadhāti /
2.2.8.[2]	grāmasampatkāmo'nuvartate /
2.2.8.[3]	ā sarvasampatkāmebhyo yāvat /
2.2.8.[4]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena pālāśatakṣaṇānyādadhāti /
2.2.8.[5]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena karkandhūtakṣaṇānyādadhāti /
2.2.8.[6]	sthūṇāmūlatakṣaṇāni /
2.2.8.[7]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena sabhānāmupastaraṇānyādadhāti //
2.2.9.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenānnamabhimantrya grāmīṇebhyo dadāti //
2.2.10.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena surāmabhimantrya surāpebhyo dadāti /
2.2.10.[2]	samāptāni grāmasāmpadāni /
2.2.10.[3]	karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.2.10.[4]	sarvatra grāmo nāsti /
2.2.10.[5]	sarvatra hastahome vā tantram /
2.2.10.[6]	grāmaśabdaḥ samūhavacanaḥ /
2.2.10.[7]	grāmo vā pattanaṃ vā nagaraṃ vā durgāṅgaṃ sarvaṃ grāmaśabdenocyate /
2.2.10.[8]	grāmakāmo yadā bhavati tadā grāmasāmpadaṃ kuruta ityarthaḥ //
2.2.10.[9]	atha sarvasāmpadānāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.2.11.[1]	paurṇamāsyāṃ rātrau nirṛtikarma kṛtvā śvo bhūte karmaprayogaḥ /
2.2.11.[2]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenaudumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
2.2.11.[3]	sarvasampatkāmo'nuvartate /
2.2.11.[4]	ā sāmmanasebhyaḥ karmabhyo yāvat /
2.2.11.[5]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena pālāśasamidha ādadhāti /
2.2.11.[6]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena bṛhadbadarīsamidha ādadhāti /
2.2.11.[7]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena vrīhināvapati /
2.2.11.[8]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena yavānāvapati /
2.2.11.[9]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena tilānāvapati /
2.2.11.[10]	sarvaphalakāmaḥ /
2.2.11.[11]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.2.11.[12]	tata uttaratantram /
2.2.11.[13]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.2.11.[14]	tata uttaratantram /
2.2.11.[15]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena rasān sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
2.2.11.[16]	'tve kratum iti rasaprāśanī' /
2.2.11.[17]	tata uttaratantram //
2.2.12.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena trirahani madhya agniṃ prajvālayati sarvakāmaḥ //
2.2.13.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenāgnimupatiṣṭhate trikālam //
2.2.14.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena savyāt pāṇimadhyād rudhiraṃ rasamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.2.14.[2]	tata uttaram //
2.2.15.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena pṛśnimanthaḥ //
2.2.16-18.[1]	maiśradhānye mantha opyaivaṃ pṛśnimanthaḥ /
2.2.16-18.[2]	pṛśnimanthaṃ maiśradhānyaṃ ca dadhimadhumiśraṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.2.16-18.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.2.16-18.[4]	samāptaḥ pṛśnimanthaḥ //
2.2.19.[1]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'asmin vasu' iti sūktena yugmakṛṣṇalaṃ hiraṇyamaṇiṃ kṛtvā trayodaśyādayastisro dadhimadhuni vāsayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.2.19.[2]	taddadhimadhu prāśayati /
2.2.19.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
2.2.19.[4]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadābadhnan' iti sūktena yugmakṛṣṇalaṃ suvarṇamaṇiṃ vāsitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya puṇyāhānte badhnāti /
2.2.19.[5]	dadhimadhuprāśanam /
2.2.19.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.2.19.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'nava prāṇān' iti sūktena yugmakṛṣṇalaṃ suvarṇamaṇiṃ vāsitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.2.19.[8]	prāśanam /
2.2.19.[9]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.2.20.[1]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā sārūpavatsa odane puruṣākṛtimālikhya dvādaśarātraṃ 'asmin vasu' iti sūktena pratyahaṃ sampātya dvādaśe'hanyabhimantryānabhimukhamaśnāti /
2.2.20.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.2.20.[3]	prathame'hani tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadā badhnan' iti sūktena sārūpavatsaṃ puruṣagātraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvābhimantryānabhimukhamaśnāti /
2.2.20.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.2.20.[5]	prathame divase tantraṃ kṛtvā 'nava prāṇān' iti sūktena sārūpavatsaṃ puruṣagātraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvābhimantryānabhimukhamaśnāti /
2.2.20.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.2.20.[7]	dvitīyā kaṇḍikā //11 //
2.3.1.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'kathaṃ mahe' iti sūktena mādānakakāṣṭhaśṛtaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.1.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
2.3.2.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'kathaṃ mahe' iti sūktena camase sarūpavatsāyā dugdhe vrīhiyavāvavadhāya mūrcchayitvā madhvāsicya sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.2.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
2.3.3.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'pṛthivyai śrotrāya' iti sūktenājyaṃ juhoti /
2.3.3.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.3.4.[1]	'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcaudumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.4.[2]	'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā pālāśasamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.4.[3]	'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā bṛhadbadarīsamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.4.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.4.[5]	'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā vrīhīnāvapati /
2.3.4.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā yavānāvapati /
2.3.4.[7]	'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā tilānāvapati /
2.3.4.[8]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.4.[9]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.4.[10]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.4.[11]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.4.[12]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā rasān sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.4.[13]	uttaratantram /
2.3.4.[14]	'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā trikālamahanyagniṃ prajvālayati /
2.3.4.[15]	'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā trikālamagnimupatiṣṭhate /
2.3.4.[16]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā savyāt pāṇihṛdayāllohitaṃ rasamiśritaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.4.[17]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.4.[18]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vatso virājaḥ' ityṛcā pṛśnimantho jihvāyā ādi maiśradhānye mantha opya dadhimadhumiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.4.[19]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.4.[20]	sarvasāmpadāni karmāṇi samāptāni /
2.3.4.[21]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.3.4.[22]	sarvakāma ityarthaḥ /
2.3.4.[23]	sarvasāmpadāni putrapaśudhanadhānyaprajāpatnījayavijayalābhalakṣmīaśvahastinarayānāarāmagrāmagṛhakpataḍāgavāpīvedapāṭhakalpapāṭhavedārthajñānamīmāṃsājñānavyākaraṇajñānasūtrajñāna āvasathyāgnitretāgnikāmajyotiṣṭhomakāmasatrakāma dharmārthakāmaviśeṣeṣu /
2.3.4.[24]	pareṣu śatruṣu uccāṭanavaśīkaraṇagṛhakalahotpattividveṣaṇastambhanādijaturasāyanadhātuvādādirasastrībhogādikāmamedhyavastuvṛṣabhābhicārasvastyayanāyuṣyacaturaṅgabalapuṣṭidevatājñānādisampada iti /
2.3.4.[25]	anekakāmasampada ucyante /
2.3.4.[26]	sampado'pūrvalābha iti /
2.3.4.[27]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ kramo nāsti /
2.3.4.[28]	sarvatra vikalpaḥ /
2.3.4.[29]	phalārthinaḥ abhyāsena punaḥpunaḥ kriyābhyāsena karmasiddhiḥ /
2.3.4.[30]	kāmānantyāt kāmānāṃ parigaṇanaṃ kṛtam /
2.3.4.[31]	sarvasāmpadānīti loka anekakāmasampadityucyate /
2.3.4.[32]	dhanaviśeṣakāmāḥ /
2.3.4.[33]	putraviśeṣakāmāḥ /
2.3.4.[34]	kapilavarṇagauravarṇaputrā evaṃvidhaṃ bhavatīti /
2.3.4.[35]	karmaṇāṃ kramo'pi nāsti tantreṇa karma paṭhitam /
2.3.4.[36]	sāmpadasya karmapaddhatiḥ samāptā //
2.3.4.[37]	sāmmanasyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.3.5-6.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sahṛdayaṃ sāmmanasyam' iti sūktenodakulijamudakumbhaṃ sampātya grāmapārśve bhrāmayitvā madhye ninayati /
2.3.5-6.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.5-6.[3]	sāmmanasyādhikāra ā varcasyebhyaḥ karmabhyo yāvat /
2.3.5-6.[4]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tadū ṣu te' ityṛcā kumbhaṃ sampātya grāmapārśve bhrāmayitvā madhye ninayati /
2.3.5-6.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.5-6.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ jānīdhvam' iti sūktena kumbhaṃ sampātya taṃ ghaṭaṃ gṛhītvā grāmapārśve bhrāmayitvā madhye ninayati /
2.3.5-6.[7]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.5-6.[8]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'eha yātu' 'saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantām' iti sūktābhyāmudakumbhaṃ sampātya grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.5-6.[9]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.5-6.[10]	anena sūktena jñātiputrasya sāmmanasyaṃ kriyate /
2.3.5-6.[11]	yāvajjīvaṃ sajātānāṃ sagotrāṇāṃ sāmmanasyaṃ bhavati /
2.3.5-6.[12]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo manāṃsi' iti tisṛbhirṛgbhirudakumbhaṃ sampātya grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.5-6.[13]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.5-6.[14]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sañjñānaṃ naḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāmudakulijaṃ sampātya grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.5-6.[15]	tata uttaratantram //
2.3.7.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sahṛdayam' iti sūktena surākulijaṃ sampātitaṃ kṛtvā grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.7.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.7.[3]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tadū ṣu te' ityṛcā surākulijaṃ sampātitaṃ kṛtvā grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.7.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.7.[5]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ jānīdhvam' iti sūktena surākulijaṃ sampātitaṃ kṛtvā grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.7.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.7.[7]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'eha yātu' 'saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantām' iti sūktābhyāṃ surākulijaṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvā grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.7.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.7.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo manāṃsi' iti tisṛbhir ṛgbhiḥ surākulijaṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvā grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.7.[10]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.7.[11]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sañjñānaṃ naḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ surākulijaṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvā grāmaṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
2.3.7.[12]	tata uttaratantram //
2.3.8.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sahṛdayam' iti sūktena trivarṣavatsikāyāḥ śuktāni piśitāni māṃsāni sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.8.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.8.[3]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tadū ṣu te' ityṛcāmlena rasena siktāni māṃsāni sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.8.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.8.[5]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ jānīdhvam' iti sūktena śuktāni māṃsāni sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.8.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.8.[7]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'eha yātu' 'saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantām' iti sūktābhyāṃ traihāyaṇyā vatsataryāḥ śuktāni māṃsāni sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.8.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.8.[9]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo manāṃsi' iti sūktena śuktāni māṃsāni sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.8.[10]	uttaratantram /
2.3.8.[11]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sañjñānaṃ naḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ traihāyaṇyā vatsataryā śuktāni māṃsāni sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.8.[12]	tata uttaratantram //
2.3.9.[1]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sahṛdayam' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.9.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[3]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tad ū ṣu te' ity ekayā bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.9.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[5]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ jānīdhvam' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.9.[6]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.9.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'eha yātu' 'saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantām' iti sūktābhyāṃ bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.9.[8]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.9.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo manāṃsi' iti tisṛbhirṛgbhibhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.9.[10]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[11]	vedyāditantraṃ kṛtvā 'sañjñānaṃ naḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.9.[12]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[13]	brāhmaṇatarpaṇam /
2.3.9.[14]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sahṛdayam' iti sūktena surāṃ sampātyābhimantrya prayacchati /
2.3.9.[15]	sāmmanasyebhyaḥ puruṣebhyastraivarṇikebhyaḥ /
2.3.9.[16]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.9.[17]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'tadū ṣu te' ityekayā surāṃ sampātyābhimantrya prayacchati /
2.3.9.[18]	tata uttaratantraṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ jānīdhvam' iti sūktena surāṃ sampātyābhimantrya prayacchati /
2.3.9.[19]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[20]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'eha yātu' 'saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantām' iti sūktābhyāṃ surāṃ sampātyābhimantrya prayacchati /
2.3.9.[21]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[22]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo manāṃsi' iti tṛcena sūktena surāṃ sampātyābhimantrya prayacchati /
2.3.9.[23]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[24]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sañjñānaṃ naḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ surāṃ sampātyābhimantrya prayacchati /
2.3.9.[25]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[26]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sahṛdayam' iti sūktena prapodakaṃ sampātyābhimantrya pāyayet /
2.3.9.[27]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[28]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'tadū ṣu te' ityekayā prapodakaṃ sampātyābhimantrya pāyayet /
2.3.9.[29]	tata uttaratantram ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ jānīdhvam' iti sūktena prapodakaṃ sampātyābhimantrya pāyayet /
2.3.9.[30]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[31]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'eha yātu' 'saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantām' iti sūktābhyāṃ prapodakaṃ sampātyābhimantrya pāyayet /
2.3.9.[32]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[33]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo manāṃsi' iti tṛcena prapodakaṃ sampātyābhimantrya pāyayet /
2.3.9.[34]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.9.[35]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'sañjñānaṃ naḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ prapodakaṃ sampātyābhimantrya pāyayet /
2.3.9.[36]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.9.[37]	sāmmanasyāni samāptāni /
2.3.9.[38]	yena saha sāmmanasyaṃ karoti tasya bhaktādīni dadāti /
2.3.9.[39]	karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.3.9.[40]	yena saha sāmmanasyaṃ kartumicchati tasya karma karoti /
2.3.9.[41]	surādi śūdrāya dadāti /
2.3.9.[42]	māṃsāni cāṇḍālebhyaḥ /
2.3.9.[43]	kiñca yena sahaikacittakaraṇaṃ sāmmanasyamityucyate /
2.3.9.[44]	vaśīkaraṇamityarthaḥ /
2.3.9.[45]	brāhmaṇastrīśūdracāṇḍālādīnāṃ nāsti jātiniyamaḥ /
2.3.9.[46]	nāpi saṅkhyāniyamaḥ /
2.3.9.[47]	bahūnāmapi bhavati /
2.3.9.[48]	vaśīkaraṇaṃ sāmmanasyamityucyate /
2.3.9.[49]	iti vaśīkaraṇamiti sāmmanasyam /
2.3.9.[50]	sāmmanasyakarmapaddhatiḥ samāptā //
2.3.9.[51]	atha varcasyavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.3.10-11.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenaudumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.10-11.[2]	sarvatra varcaskāmo'nuvartate ā rājakarmabhyo yāvat /
2.3.10-11.[3]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena pālāśasamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.10-11.[4]	tejaskāmaḥ /
2.3.10-11.[5]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena bṛhadbadarīsamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.10-11.[6]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena vrīhīn āvapati /
2.3.10-11.[7]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena yavānāvapati /
2.3.10-11.[8]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena tilānāvapati /
2.3.10-11.[9]	tejaskāmaḥ /
2.3.10-11.[10]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.10-11.[11]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.10-11.[12]	varcaskāmaḥ /
2.3.10-11.[13]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.10-11.[14]	abhyātānādyuttarataram /
2.3.10-11.[15]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena rasān sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.10-11.[16]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.10-11.[17]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktenaudumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.10-11.[18]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena pālāśasamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.10-11.[19]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena bṛhadbadarīsamidha ādadhāti /
2.3.10-11.[20]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena vrīhīnāvapati /
2.3.10-11.[21]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena yavānāvapati /
2.3.10-11.[22]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena tilānāvapati /
2.3.10-11.[23]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.10-11.[24]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.10-11.[25]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.10-11.[26]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.10-11.[27]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena rasān sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.3.10-11.[28]	uttaratantram //
2.3.10-11.[29]	atha kumārīvarcasyamucyate
2.3.12.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena kumāryā dakṣiṇamūrumabhimantrayate /
2.3.12.[2]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena kumāryā dakṣiṇamūrumabhimantrayate /
2.3.12.[3]	kumārī rūpavatī varcasvinī bhartṛgṛhe pradhānā bhavati /
2.3.12.[4]	tasyā idaṃ karma kriyate //
2.3.13.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena vapāṃ kṛttvānīya juhoti /
2.3.13.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.13.[3]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena vapāṃ kṛttvānīya juhoti /
2.3.13.[4]	uttaratantram //
2.3.14.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenāgnimupatiṣṭhate /
2.3.14.[2]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktenāgnimupatiṣṭhate /
2.3.14.[3]	varcaskāmaḥ //
2.3.15.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena dadhimadhunī sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.15.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.15.[3]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' iti sūktena dadhimadhunī ekatra kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.15.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.3.15.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' ityarthasūktena dadhimadhunī ekatra kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.15.[6]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.3.15.[7]	atha kṣatriyavarcasyamucyate
2.3.16.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena dadhimadhu bhaktamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśayati kṣatriyam /
2.3.16.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.16.[3]	tejaskāmaḥ /
2.3.16.[4]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' iti sūktena dadhimadhu bhaktamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśayati kṣatriyam /
2.3.16.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.16.[6]	tejaskāmaḥ /
2.3.16.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' ityarthasūktena dadhimadhu bhaktamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśayati kṣatriyam /
2.3.16.[8]	vacaskāmaḥ /
2.3.16.[9]	tata uttaratantram //
2.3.16.[10]	atha vaiśyaśūdrādivarcasyamucyate /
2.3.16.[11]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati vaiśyaśūdram /
2.3.16.[12]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.16.[13]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati vaiśyān śūdrān anulomajāṃśca /
2.3.16.[14]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.16.[15]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' ityarthasūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśayati /
2.3.16.[16]	vaiśyaśūdrādīn /
2.3.16.[17]	tata uttaratantram /
2.3.16.[18]	tejaskāmaḥ /
2.3.16.[19]	tṛtīyā kaṇḍikā //
2.4.1.[1]	'hastivarcasam' iti sūktena hastinaṃ dṛṣṭvā upatiṣṭhate /
2.4.1.[2]	tejaskāmaḥ //
2.4.2.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'hastivarcasam' iti sūktena hastidantamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.2.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaram /
2.4.2.[3]	sarvatra varcasyādhikāro'nuvartate //
2.4.3.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'hastivarcasam' iti sūktena hastilomāni jatunā lākṣārasena sandihya hiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.3.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
2.4.4.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ snātakanābhilomāni lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya puṇyāhānte badhnāti /
2.4.4.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.4.[3]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ siṃhanābhilomāni lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.4.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.4.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ vyāghranābhilomāni lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.4.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.4.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ ajanābhilomāni lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.4.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.4.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ kṛṣṇanābhilomāni gṛhītvā jatunā sandihya jātarūpeṇāpidhāpya sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.4.[10]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.4.[11]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ vṛṣabhanābhiromāṇi lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.4.[12]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.4.4.[13]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ rājñānnābhiromāṇi lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.4.[14]	tata uttaratantram //
2.4.5.[1]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ pālāśādidaśavṛkṣaśakalāni lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.5.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.5.[3]	kecit vṛkṣavikalpaṃ manyante //
2.4.6.[1]	etayoḥ sūktayoḥ sthāne sūktena vikalpaḥ /
2.4.6.[2]	'prātaragnim' 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' iti tribhiḥ pratīkaiḥ snātakādisaptamarmāṇi sthālīpāke dattvā tantre sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
2.4.6.[3]	uttaratantram /
2.4.6.[4]	sthālīpāke ca idaṃ karma kṣatriyādīnām /
2.4.6.[5]	na brāhmaṇasya /
2.4.6.[6]	sthālīpākaṃ kevalaṃ kuryāt //
2.4.7-8.[1]	varcaskāmaḥ /
2.4.7-8.[2]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena snātakanābhimaṇiṃ lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[3]	udañci havirucchiṣṭāntaṃ samānam /
2.4.7-8.[4]	tantre 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena siṃharomamaṇiṃ saṃskṛtya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[5]	barhirlavanādi tantraṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena vyāghranābhiromamaṇiṃ lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya puṇyāhānte badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[6]	uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[7]	pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktenājanābhiromamaṇiṃ lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[8]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[9]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena kṛṣṇanābhiromamaṇiṃ lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[10]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[11]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena vṛṣabhanābhiromamaṇiṃ lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[12]	uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[13]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prātaragnim' iti sūktena rājñāṃ nābhiromamaṇiṃ sampātya lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[14]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[15]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' iti sūktena snātakaromamaṇiṃ lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[16]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[17]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' iti sūktena siṃharomamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[18]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[19]	pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvara' iti vyāghraromamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[20]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[21]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvara' ityajaromamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[22]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[23]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvara' iti sūktena meṣaromamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[24]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[25]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvara' iti sūktena vṛṣabharomamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[26]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[27]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'girāvara' iti rājñāṃ romamaṇiṃ lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[28]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[29]	abhyātānānte 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' ityarthasūktena snātakaromamaṇiṃ sampātya lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitamabhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[30]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[31]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' iti siṃharomamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[32]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[33]	abhyānātāntaṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' iti vyāghraromamaṇiṃ sampātya lākṣāsuvarṇena veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[34]	uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[35]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' iti sūktenājaromamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[36]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[37]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' iti sūktena meṣaromamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[38]	uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[39]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' iti vṛṣabharomamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[40]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' iti sūktena rājñāṃ romamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.4.7-8.[41]	uttaratantram /
2.4.7-8.[42]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.4.7-8.[43]	karmabāhulyāt phalabāhulyam //
2.4.9.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' 'prātaragnim' 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' ityetaiḥ sarvaiḥ sūktairudakumbhaṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
2.4.9.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.4.9.[3]	varcaskāmaḥ /
2.4.9.[4]	etadeva nitye snāne naimittike kāmye vā vidhānaṃ bhavati /
2.4.9.[5]	yathā vasanta ṛtau snānaṃ kriyate //
2.4.10.[1]	'siṃhe vyāghre' 'yaśo haviḥ' 'prātaragnim' 'girāvaragarāṭeṣu' 'divaspṛthivyāḥ' ityetaiḥ sūktairudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati //
2.4.11.[1]	candanādigandhānāsādya tasmin madhya ākāśodakaṃ prakṣipya caturaṅgulena darbhatṛṇenāloḍya tat tṛṇaṃ gṛhītvā //
2.4.12.[1]	'śuni kilāsamaje' iti mantreṇa dakṣiṇā diśaṃ nirasyati /
2.4.12.[2]	candanādi 'yaste gandhaḥ' iti tribhirṛgbhirabhimantrya rājñāṃ samālabhate /
2.4.12.[3]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.4.12.[4]	karmabāhulyāt phalabāhulyam /
2.4.12.[5]	nārita jātiniyamaḥ sarvasyādhikāraḥ /

2.5.0.[1]	atha rājakarmāṇyucyante /
2.5.0.[2]	sāṅgrāmikāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ aśvatthasya badhakasya vāraṇyoragniṃ manthati /
2.5.0.[3]	'indro manthatu' iti ṛcā mathyamānamanumantrayate /
2.5.0.[4]	'pūtirajjuḥ' ityardharcenāgnipatanasthāne kāśarajjuṃ nidadhāti /
2.5.0.[5]	'dhūmamagniṃ parādṛśya' ityardharcena dhūmamanumantrayate /

2.5.0.[7]	eṣa senāgniḥ //
2.5.0.[8]	sāṅgrāmikatantramucyate /
2.5.0.[9]	'avyasaśca' barhirlavanādi samānam /
2.5.0.[10]	senāgnipraṇayanaṃ, grahagrahaṇaṃ, pañcagṛhītamājyaṃ abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā lohitāśvatthasya śākhāṃ ropayati /
2.5.0.[11]	nīlalohitābhyāṃ sūtrābhyāṃ paritatyottarataḥ /
2.5.0.[12]	tataḥ pradhānakarma kuryāt /
2.5.0.[13]	tata uttaratantre viśeṣaḥ /
2.5.0.[14]	sannatihomāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ime jayantu svāhebhyaḥ' ityanena mantreṇājyaṃ juhoti /
2.5.0.[15]	tato badhakakāṣṭhaprajvalite'gnau vāmena hasteneṅgiḍaṃ juhoti 'parāmī jayantāṃ durāhāmībhyaḥ' iti mantreṇa /
2.5.0.[16]	tataḥ śākhāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ prakṣipati 'nīlalohitenāmūn' iti mantreṇa /
2.5.0.[17]	sviṣṭakṛdādyuttaratantram /

2.5.0.[20]	tantramadhye ye pradhānamantrāsta uccairbhavanti //
2.5.0.[21]	śatruhastitrāsanānāṃ karmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.5.1-2.[1]	sāṅgrāmikaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena rathacakraṃ sampātavat kṛtvā hastyabhimukhaṃ rathaṃ pravartayati /
2.5.1-2.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.5.1-2.[3]	hastitrāsanakāmaḥ /
2.5.1-2.[4]	rājakarmāṇyanuvartante ā nirṛtikarmabhyo yāvat //
2.5.3.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena hastyādi yānaṃ sampātyābhimantrya hastyabhimukhaṃ prerayati /
2.5.3.[2]	aśvādayaḥ /
2.5.3.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.5.4.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena vāditrāṇi bherīmṛdaṅgetyādi abhimantrya hastino'bhi purato gacchanti //
2.5.5.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena carmakhalvāyāṃ śarkarāḥ prakṣipyābhimantrya hastyabhimukhāḥ puruṣāḥ yānti /

2.5.7-8.[1]	sāṅgrāmikaṃ tantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vidmā śarasya pitaraṃ parjanyaṃ bhūridhāyasam' iti sūktenājyaṃ juhoti /

2.5.7-8.[7]	uttaratantram /

2.5.7-8.[12]	jayakāmaḥ /

2.5.9.[2]	idhmasamādhānasthāne dhanuridhmamādadhāti /

2.5.9.[5]	sāṅgrāmikaṃ pūrvatantraṃ dhanuridhmaviśiṣṭaṃ kṛtvā 'mā no vidan' iti tribhiḥ sūktaiḥ dhanuḥsamidha ādadhāti /
