2.5.25.[7]	svasenāyā utsāhakaraṇamucyate
2.5.26-27.[1]	abhiyoga utsāhaḥ /
2.5.26-27.[2]	yuddhe utsāhavardhanaṃ bhavati /
2.5.26-27.[3]	'tvayā manyo', 'yaste manyo' iti sūktadvayam /
2.5.26-27.[4]	senayormadhye sthito japati nirīkṣamāṇaḥ //
2.5.28.[1]	sāṅgrāmikaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tvayā manyo', 'yaste manyo' iti sūktābhyāṃ bhāṅgamauñjān pāśāniṅgiḍālaṅkṛtān sampātyābhimantrya parasenāyāṃ prakṣipati /
2.5.28.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.5.28.[3]	tantraṃ kṛtvā mauñjapāśāniṅgiḍālaṅkṛtān sampātyābhimantrya ucchvasan anūktagrahaṇāt kruddhenābhimantraṇamityucyate /
2.5.28.[4]	parasenākrameṣu vapati /
2.5.28.[5]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.5.29.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvayā manyo' iti sūktābhyām āmapātrāṇi sampātyābhimantrya kruddhaḥ senākrameṣu vapati /
2.5.29.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.5.29.[3]	atha jayaparājayavijñānamucyate
2.5.30-31.[1]	'tvayā manyo' 'yaste manyo' iti sūktābhyāṃ śaratṛṇānīṅgiḍena prokṣitānyabhimantrya tata āṅgirasenāgninā dīpayati senayormadhye kṛtvā /
2.5.30-31.[2]	yatra dhūmo gacchati tatra na jayaḥ /
2.5.30-31.[3]	iti svasenāyā utsāhakaraṇaṃ samāptam /
2.5.30-31.[4]	āṅgiro'gniścāṇḍālāgniḥ sūtīkāgniḥ /
2.5.30-31.[5]	svaramālatṛṇāni //
2.5.30-31.[6]	pañcamī kaṇḍikā //
2.6.1.[1]	'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāmāśvatthyāṃ pātryāṃ trivṛti gomayaparicaye'gniṃ prajvālya hastipṛṣṭhe śatrūnabhimukho gacchan ājyaṃ juhoti /
2.6.1.[2]	na tantram /
2.6.1.[3]	puruṣaśirasi vāśvatthyāṃ pātryāṃ trivṛti gomayaparicaye'gniṃ prajvālya śatrūnabhimukho gacchan 'ṛdhaṅmantra', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāmājyaṃ juhoti /
2.6.1.[4]	tat pātramabhiprakramya bhūmyāṃ prakṣipati //
2.6.2.[1]	varāhavihitamṛttikāyā rājāno vediṃ kurvanti //
2.6.3.[1]	tataḥ kartābhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāmājyaṃ juhoti /
2.6.3.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.6.3.[3]	jayakāmaḥ /
2.6.3.[4]	varāhavihitādi pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ saktūñjuhoti /
2.6.3.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.3.[6]	pūrvoktena tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ dhanuridhme dhanuḥsamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.3.[7]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.3.[8]	varāhavihitādīṣvidhme 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' 'tadidāsa' itīṣusamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.3.[9]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.3.[10]	varāhavihitādyabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ dhanuḥ sampātyābhimantrya vimṛjya rājñe prayacchati /
2.6.3.[11]	tata uttaratantram //
2.6.4.[1]	yuddhe mṛtasya puruṣasyādahana idhmamupasamādhāyopari rathacakraṃ dhārayitvā dīrghadaṇḍena sruveṇa 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ cakracchidreṇājyamagnau juhoti /
2.6.4.[2]	na tantram //
2.6.5.[1]	'uttiṣṭha' 'sannahya' 'prahara' 'yudhyasva' 'yojayasva' vacanaṃ śrutvā yuddhaṃ yojayet svasenāyāḥ //
2.6.6.[1]	'yadi cinnu tvā' ityṛcaṃ japitvā dveṣyamanvāha /
2.6.6.[2]	'namo devavadhebhyaḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā dveṣyamanvāha /
2.6.6.[3]	jayakarmāṇi sāṅgrāmikāṇi samāptāni /
2.6.6.[4]	karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.6.6.[5]	etaiḥ kṛtairavaśyaṃ jayo bhavati //
2.6.6.[6]	vaiśyāya saṅgrāmavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.6.7.[1]	agnimanthanādi sāṅgrāmikaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadi cinnu tvā' ityekayājyaṃ juhoti /
2.6.7.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.6.7.[3]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yadi cinnu tvā dhanā' ityekayā saktūñjuhoti /
2.6.7.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadi cinnu tvā' ityṛcā dhanuridhme dhanuḥsamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.7.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadi cinnu tvā' ityṛcā śaredhme śarasamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.7.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[9]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadi cinnu tvā' ityekayarcā dhanuḥ sampātyābhimantrya vimṛjya vaiśyāya prayacchati /
2.6.7.[10]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[11]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'namo devavadhebhyaḥ' iti sūktenājyaṃ juhoti /
2.6.7.[12]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[13]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'namo devavadhebhyaḥ' iti sūktena saktūñjuhoti /
2.6.7.[14]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[15]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'namo devavadhebhyaḥ' iti sūktena dhanuridhme dhanuḥsamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.7.[16]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[17]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'namo devavadhebhyaḥ' iti sūkteneṣvidhma iṣusamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.7.[18]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[19]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'namo devavadhebhyaḥ' iti sūktena dhanuḥ sampātyābhimantrya vimṛjya vaiśyāya prayacchati /
2.6.7.[20]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.7.[21]	vijayakāmaḥ /
2.6.7.[22]	samāptāni vaiśyayuddhakarmāṇi //
2.6.7.[23]	āyudhine grāmaṇye saṅgrāmavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.6.8.[1]	sāṅgrāmikaṃ tantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvayā vayam' ityekayājyaṃ juhoti /
2.6.8.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.8.[3]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tvayā vayam' ityekayā saktūñjuhoti /
2.6.8.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.8.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tvayā vayam' ityṛcā dhanuridhme dhanuḥsamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.8.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.8.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tvayā vayam' ityṛceṣvidhma iṣusamidha ādadhāti /
2.6.8.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.8.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvayā vayam' ityṛcā dhanuḥ sampātyābhimantrya vimṛjya balādhikṛtāya prayacchati /
2.6.8.[10]	tata uttaratantram /
2.6.8.[11]	samāptānyāyudhigrāmaṇīkarmāṇi /
2.6.8.[12]	karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.6.8.[13]	jayo bhavatītyarthaḥ /
2.6.8.[14]	samāptaṃ senāpatijayakarma /
2.6.8.[15]	daṇḍanāyakajayakarma /
2.6.8.[16]	koṭapālajayakarma /
2.6.8.[17]	svasenājayaparājayakarma /
2.6.8.[18]	balādhikṛtajayakarma /
2.6.8.[19]	anyeṣāṃ variṣṭhādīnāṃ jayakarma /
2.6.8.[20]	samāptameṣāṃ vijayakarma //
2.6.8.[21]	svasenājayaparājayapuruṣavadhaśaṅkāyāṃ ca vijñānamucyate
2.6.9.[1]	ni taddadhiṣe ityṛcodapātramabhimantrya tato dvau dvau yoddhārāvavekṣayet //
2.6.10.[1]	rājā yaṃ na paśyet na yudhyeta na yodhayet /
2.6.10.[2]	purohito mantraṃ brūyāt /
2.6.10.[3]	punaḥpunarudapātra abhimantraṇam /
2.6.10.[4]	samāptaṃ svasenāyā yoddhṛpuruṣāṇāṃ ca vijñānam //
2.6.10.[5]	atha nave rathe ghaṭite saṃskāra ucyate jayakāmasya
2.6.11.[1]	'ni taddadhiṣe' ityṛcā rathamabhimantrya sasārathiṃ rājānamāsthāpayati /
2.6.11.[2]	'vanaspate vīḍvaṅgaḥ' iti tṛcena sūktena navarathamabhimantrya sasārathiṃ rājānamāsthāpayati /
2.6.11.[3]	'ayā viṣṭhā janayan' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ navaṃ rathamabhimantrya sasārathiṃ rājānamāsthāpayati /
2.6.11.[4]	'agna indraśca dāśuṣe' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ navaṃ rathamabhimantrya sasārathiṃ rājānamāsthāpayati /
2.6.11.[5]	'diśaścatasraḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ navaṃ rathamabhimantrya rājānaṃ sasārathimāsthāpayati /
2.6.11.[6]	jayakāmaḥ /
2.6.11.[7]	nave ratha ārohaṇavidhānaṃ samāptam //
2.6.11.[8]	athārogyavidhānamucyate
2.6.12-13.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' 'anāptāḥ' iti sūktena tisraḥ snāvarajjūrabhimantrya tato'ṅgāreṣu nidadhāti //
2.6.14.[1]	yadi tā utkṣaranti tata ārogyatā bhavati /
2.6.14.[2]	samāptamārogyavijñānam //
2.6.14.[3]	atha sāṅgrāmikavijñānamucyate
2.6.15.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' 'anāptā ye' 'sahasradhāre' iti sūktena tisraḥ snāvarajjūrabhimantrya tataḥ saṅkalpaḥ /
2.6.15.[2]	ekā rajjurātmasenā /
2.6.15.[3]	madhye dvitīyā mṛtyuḥ /
2.6.15.[4]	tṛtīyā rajjuḥ parasenā /
2.6.15.[5]	evaṃ saṅkalpaḥ /
2.6.15.[6]	tataḥ aṅgāreṣu nidhāyeṣyate //
2.6.16.[1]	yasyā upari mṛtyurgacchati tasyāḥ senāyā jayo na bhavati /
2.6.16.[2]	yā mṛtyorupari patati tasyā jayo bhavati /
2.6.16.[3]	parasenāsammukhā yā yāti tasyā api jayo bhavati //
2.6.17.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' iti dvitīyena sūktena snāvarajjumekāmabhimantrya tato'ṅgāreṣu nidadhāti /
2.6.17.[2]	tato nirīkṣate /
2.6.17.[3]	agreṣu agreḥ paścimadigbhāgeṣūtkucatsu mukhyā hanyante /
2.6.17.[4]	madhyeṣu madhyāḥ /
2.6.17.[5]	anteṣu pūrvadiśānteṣvavarapadātivināśaḥ //
2.6.18.[1]	evamiṣīkāḥ karoti /
2.6.18.[2]	baddhvā rajjūḥ kṛtāḥ 'brahma jajñānam' iti sūktenābhimantrya karoti /
2.6.18.[3]	ārogyavijñānakarma /
2.6.18.[4]	jayaparājayavijñānakarma /
2.6.18.[5]	snāvarajjumukhyamadhyamāvaravijñānakarma /
2.6.18.[6]	etāni trīṇi karmāṇi bhavanti /
2.6.18.[7]	abhimantrya kartavyāni /
2.6.18.[8]	iṣīkāḥ śaramayā vā vīriṇamayā vā kartavyāḥ /
2.6.18.[9]	samāptaṃ sāṅgrāmikaṃ vijñānam /
2.6.18.[10]	ṣaṣṭhī kaṇḍikā //
2.7.1.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'uccairghoṣaḥ' iti sūktena bheryādivāditrāṇi prakṣālya tagarośīreṇa lepayitvā sampātya tataḥ svayaṃ purodhā trirāhatya prayacchati /
2.7.1.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.1.[3]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā vāditrāṇi prakṣālya tagarośīreṇa sandhāvya 'upa śvāsaya' iti sūktena vāditrāṇi sampātavanti kṛtvā trirāhatya prayacchati /
2.7.1.[4]	tata uttaratantram //
2.7.2.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vihṛdayam' iti sūktena sarvavāditrāṇi prakṣālya tagarośīreṇa lepayitvoccaistarāṃ hutvā sampātavanti trirāhatya prayacchati /
2.7.2.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
2.7.3.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vihṛdayam' iti sūktena somāṅkuramaṇiṃ hariṇacarmaṇāveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
2.7.3.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.3.[3]	'vihṛdayam' iti sūktasya sarvatra uccaistareṇa svareṇa prayogaḥ /
2.7.3.[4]	sūcanaṃ paratra /
2.7.3.[5]	samāptaṃ dviṣo vidveṣaṇaṃ trāsanaṃ ca //
2.7.4.[1]	'pari vartmāni sarvataḥ' iti sūktena rājā triḥ senāṃ paribhrāmyati /
2.7.4.[2]	'indro jayāti' iti sūktena rājā triḥ kaṭakaṃ bhrāmyet /
2.7.4.[3]	jayakāmaḥ /
2.7.4.[4]	triḥ sūktāvṛttiḥ //
2.7.5.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'pari vartmāni' iti sūktena somamaṇiṃ carmaveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya rājñe badhnāti /
2.7.5.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.5.[3]	jayakāmaḥ //
2.7.6.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sandānaṃ vaḥ', 'ādānena' iti sūktābhyāṃ bhāṅgapāśān sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.6.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.6.[3]	jayakāma idaṃ karma kuryāt /
2.7.6.[4]	jayakarmāṇyanuvartante 'asmin vasu' iti rāṣṭrāvagamanaṃ yāvat /
2.7.6.[5]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sandānaṃ vaḥ' 'ādānena' iti sūktābhyāṃ mauñjān pāśāniṅgiḍālaṅkṛtān sampātavato'nūktān abhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.6.[6]	tata uttaratantram //
2.7.6.[7]	svasenāyā abhayakarma ucyate
2.7.7.[1]	'marmāṇi te' ityṛcā sannāhamabhimantrya rājānaṃ sannāhaṃ paridhāpayati /
2.7.7.[2]	abhayakāmaḥ //
2.7.8.[1]	'abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī' iti sūktena saptarṣīn yajate pratidiśaṃ senāyāḥ /
2.7.8.[2]	'abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī' iti sūktena pratidiśaṃ senāyā upatiṣṭhate vā /
2.7.8.[3]	'śyeno'si gāyatram' iti sūktena saptarṣīn yajata upatiṣṭhate vā senāyāḥ pratidiśam /
2.7.8.[4]	caturṣu dikṣu kuryāt /
2.7.8.[5]	saṅgrāme vartamāne /
2.7.8.[6]	'abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī śyeno'sīti pratidiśaṃ saptarṣīnabhayakāmaḥ' /
2.7.8.[7]	yajate /
2.7.8.[8]	upatiṣṭhate vā /
2.7.8.[9]	ekasmin sthāne karmaprayogaṃ vā kuryāt /
2.7.8.[10]	diśi diśyabhimukhāni tantrāṇi kṛtvā yajate /
2.7.8.[11]	sūktavikalpaḥ /
2.7.8.[12]	upatiṣṭhate /
2.7.8.[13]	svasthāne urdhvasthito diśyabhimukhaścaturṣu dikṣu kuryāt /
2.7.8.[14]	samāptaṃ senāyā abhayakarma //
2.7.9-13.[1]	uktamagnimanthanamādau 'indro manthatu' iti //
2.7.9-13.[2]	atha sapatnakṣayaṇīkarma ucyate
2.7.14.[1]	araṇye sapatnakṣayaṇīkarma kuryāt /
2.7.14.[2]	na grāmamadhye kuryāt /
2.7.14.[3]	tantravikalpaḥ hastahomatvāt /
2.7.14.[4]	'indro manthatu' iti sūktena aśvatthasamidha ādadhāti /
2.7.14.[5]	śatrukṣayo bhavati /
2.7.14.[6]	'indro manthatu' iti sūktena karimālakasamidha ādadhāti /
2.7.14.[7]	senāgnau sarvatra /
2.7.14.[8]	'indro manthatu' iti sūktena eraṇḍasamidha ādadhāti /
2.7.14.[9]	'indro manthatu' iti sūktena tirṇisamidha ādadhāti /
2.7.14.[10]	'indro manthatu' iti sūktena khadirasamidha ādadhāti /
2.7.14.[11]	'indro manthatu' iti sūktena śarasamidha ādadhāti senāgnau /
2.7.14.[12]	sapatnakṣayaṇī samāptā /
2.7.14.[13]	śatrukṣayo bhavati /
2.7.14.[14]	karmavikalpaḥ //
2.7.15.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'indro manthatu' iti sūktena bhāṅgapāśān sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.15.[2]	sarvatra kruddhenābhimantraṇaṃ pāśādiṣu /
2.7.15.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.15.[4]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'indro manthatu' iti sūktena mauñjān pāśān sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.15.[5]	tantraṃ ca //
2.7.16.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'indro manthatu' iti sūktena āśvatthāni kūṭāni sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati tantraṃ ca /
2.7.16.[2]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'indro manthatu' iti sūktena bhāṅgāni jālāni sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.16.[3]	tata uttaratantram //
2.7.17.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'indro manthatu' iti sūktena bādhakadaṇḍāni sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.17.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.17.[3]	samāptāni jayakarmāṇi //
2.7.18-20.[1]	'svāhaibhyaḥ' iti mitrebhya ityādi nīlalohitaśākhāntaṃ sarvakarmasu bhavati /
2.7.18-20.[2]	ādau uktam //
2.7.18-20.[3]	āvaśyāni jayakarmāṇyucyante
2.7.21.[1]	'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākaṃ yuddhakāle japati kartā //
2.7.22.[1]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena pṛṣadājyaṃ juhoti /
2.7.22.[2]	tata ājyenottaratantram //
2.7.23.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena saktūñjuhoti /
2.7.23.[2]	tataḥ sāṅgrāmikamuttaratantram /
2.7.23.[3]	sāṅgrāmikaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena dhanuridhme'gnau pṛṣadājyenāktā dhanuḥsamidha ādadhāti /
2.7.23.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.23.[5]	pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākeneṣvidhme'gnau pṛṣadājyenāktā iṣusamidha ādadhāti /
2.7.23.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.23.[7]	ājyena pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena pṛṣadājyena dhanuḥ sampātyābhimantrya vimṛjya yoddhre prayacchati /
2.7.23.[8]	tata ājyenottaratantram /
2.7.23.[9]	ājyena pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena bhāṅgapāśān pṛṣadājyena sampātya kruddho'bhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.23.[10]	tata ājyenottaratantram /
2.7.23.[11]	sarvatra pāśeṣu āśvattheṣu kūṭeṣu bhāṅgeṣu jāleṣu bādhakadaṇḍeṣu vajrarūpeṣu pātreṣu ca iṅgiḍālaṅkaraṇaṃ kruddhābhimantraṇaṃ kuryāt /
2.7.23.[12]	ājyena tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena mauñjapāśān pṛṣadājyena sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.23.[13]	ājyena uttaratantram /
2.7.23.[14]	ājyena tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena āmapātrāṇi pṛṣadājyena sampātyābhimantrya senāyuddhasthāne vapati /
2.7.23.[15]	ājyenottaratantram //
2.7.24.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena triṣandhīni lohamayāni sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.24.[2]	uttaratantram /
2.7.24.[3]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena vajrarūpāṇi sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.24.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.24.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena vajrarūpāṇi lohamayāni arbudirūpāṇi sampātyābhimantrya senākrameṣu vapati /
2.7.24.[6]	tata uttaratantram //
2.7.25.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena śitipadīm ajāṃ pṛṣadājyena sampātyābhimantrya rājñe darbharajjvā upāsaṅgadaṇḍe badhnāti /
2.7.25.[2]	ājyenottaratantram //
2.7.26.[1]	sāṅgrāmikaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ye bāhavaḥ' ityanuvākena dvitīyāṃ śitipadīṃ sampātyābhimantrya śatrusenāṃ prakṣipati /
2.7.26.[2]	ājyena uttaratantram /
2.7.26.[3]	tataḥ senāgnyutsargaḥ /
2.7.26.[4]	avabhṛthaśca /
2.7.26.[5]	śatruṃ jitvā karmasamāptiṃ karoti /
2.7.26.[6]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
2.7.26.[7]	samāptāni sāṅgrāmikāṇi karmāṇi /
2.7.26.[8]	śitipadyoḥ dvayorapyekaṃ karma /
2.7.26.[9]	anyatra vikalpaḥ /
2.7.26.[10]	anena karmaṇā avaśyaṃ jayo bhavati //
2.7.26.[11]	atha rāṣṭrapraveśābhigamanakarmavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.7.27.[1]	svarāṣṭre yo niṣkrāntaḥ śatruṇā punaḥ praveśamicchati tasyedaṃ karma //
2.7.28.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'asmin vasu' iti sūktenānuśūkānāṃ vrīhīṇāmāvraskajaiḥ kāmpīlaiḥ śṛtaṃ sārūpavatsamodanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya rājānamāśayati /
2.7.28.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.7.28.[3]	rāṣṭre ya udvāsitastasyedaṃ karma praveśārtham /
2.7.28.[4]	anena karmaṇā svarāṣṭrapraveśo bhavati /
2.7.28.[5]	sarvasyāṃ marditāyāṃ bhūmau yadā niṣkrānto rājā tadedaṃ karma karoti /
2.7.28.[6]	rāṣṭrapraveśanakāmaḥ /
2.7.28.[7]	ānuśūkālanā vrīhayaḥ punarutthitāḥ /
2.7.28.[8]	chinnāni yāni punarutthitānyāvraskāni //
2.7.29.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'abhīvartena' iti caturbhir ṛgbhī rathacakranemimaṇimayaḥsīsaloharajatatāmraveṣṭitaṃ hemanābhiṃ trirvāsitaṃ kṛtvā sūtrotaṃ barhiṣi kṛtvā pratyṛcaṃ sampātyābhimantrya 'udasau sūryaḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ badhnāti /
2.7.29.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
2.7.29.[3]	atikrānta ardhamardite rāṣṭra idaṃ karma /
2.7.29.[4]	anena karmaṇā rāṣṭravṛddhiśca bhavati //
2.7.30-31.[1]	'acikradad', 'ā tvā gan' iti sūktābhyāṃ śayanākāraṃ puroḍāśamabhimantrya darbheṣūdake ninayati /
2.7.30-31.[2]	tato loṣṭena pūrayet /
2.7.30-31.[3]	darbhasthāne mṛttikābhistaraṇam /
2.7.30-31.[4]	abhyātānāntaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'acikradad', 'ā tvā gan' iti sūktābhyāṃ kṣīraudanaṃ sthālīpākaṃ sampātyābhimantrya rājānamāśayati /
2.7.30-31.[5]	tata uttaratantram //
2.7.32.[1]	tasmāt sthānāt sambhārāharaṇaṃ yasmānniṣkrānto rājā //
2.7.33.[1]	tisṛṇāṃ prātaraśite puroḍāśe bhakṣite punaratra rāṣṭre rājā praveśaṃ labhate /
2.7.33.[2]	etasya puroḍāśakarma vijñānārtham /
2.7.33.[3]	samāptāni rāṣṭrapraveśakāni karmāṇi /
2.7.33.[4]	avaśyaṃ praveśo bhavati /
2.7.33.[5]	bhayaṃ vā mṛtyurvā vighnaṃ daivopaghāto vā śatrorbhavati /
2.7.33.[6]	avaśyaṃ praveśo bhavatītyarthaḥ /
2.7.33.[7]	rājakarmāṇyeva vartante /
2.7.33.[8]	samāptaṃ svarāṣṭrapraveśanakarma //
2.7.33.[9]	saptamī kaṇḍikā //
2.8.1.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā śāntyudakavidhānena śāntyudakaṃ karoti /
2.8.1.[2]	mahānadyā udakaṃ vanapuṣkariṇīnāmudakaṃ devavṛṣṭyudakaṃ divyamudakaṃ ca /
2.8.1.[3]	udakānāṃ vikalpaḥ samuccayo vā śāntyudakamādiṣṭānām //
2.8.2.[1]	tataścaruṃ śrapayati nadyodakena samudrodakena vā /
2.8.2.[2]	vedyā dakṣiṇataḥ darbhānāstīrya tatroparyūrdhvaṃ sthitaṃ rājānaṃ 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena śāntyudakakalaśamabhimantrya purodhā rājānamabhiṣiñcati //
2.8.3.[1]	abhiṣiktaḥ snātaḥ /
2.8.3.[2]	khaṭvāyāmārṣabhaṃ carmāstīrya tatra rājānamārohayati 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena //
2.8.4-5.[1]	udapātramubhāvapyāsiñcato dhārāyā udakena //
2.8.6-7.[1]	'sahaiva no' iti rājā brūte /
2.8.6-7.[2]	brahmā brūyāt 'yo duṣkṛtam' iti //
2.8.8.[1]	tataḥ sthālīpākaṃ 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena sampātyābhimantryāśayati //
2.8.9.[1]	tato'śvamārohayati 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena /
2.8.9.[2]	aparājitāṃ pratipādayati /
2.8.9.[3]	vāhenopaniṣkramya punargṛha āgatyābhyātānādyuttaratantram //
2.8.10.[1]	sahasraṃ gavāṃ dakṣiṇā grāmavaraśca /
2.8.10.[2]	abhiṣekaḥ samāptaḥ //
2.8.11.[1]	māṇḍalikasya sāmantasya yuvarājasya senāpateranyasya kasyacidabhiṣekaḥ anena vidhānena kāryaḥ /
2.8.11.[2]	tasyāpi purohitavaraṇe kṛte satyabhiṣekaḥ kāryaḥ /
2.8.11.[3]	abhiṣekādanantaraṃ ghṛtāvekṣaṇamārātrikaṃ rājakarmāṇi piṣṭarātryādīni pratyahaṃ kartavyāni /
2.8.11.[4]	vidhānena sarvāṇi dānāni dadāti /
2.8.11.[5]	puṣpābhiṣekamahānavamīndrotsavavṛṣotsargajanmadinādi prativarṣaṃ kāryāṇi //
2.8.11.[6]	sārvabhaumābhiṣeka ucyate /
2.8.11.[7]	mahābhiṣekavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
2.8.12.[1]	sārvabhaumasya bhavati /
2.8.12.[2]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ śāntyudakaṃ karoti /
2.8.12.[3]	caturṇāṃ sāgarāṇāṃ tu mahānadīnāṃ śatasya ca /
2.8.12.[4]	tenodakena śāntyudakaṃ karoti vadhānena /
2.8.12.[5]	mantroktena udakena caruṃ śrapayati /
2.8.12.[6]	tato dakṣiṇato vedeḥ khaṭvāṃ stṛṇāti /
2.8.12.[7]	mañcikā /
2.8.12.[8]	yathā loke abhiṣekaḥ /
2.8.12.[9]	tasyā upari darbhān stṛṇāti /
2.8.12.[10]	tatra rājani upaviṣṭe 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena tena śāntyudakena rājānam abhiṣiñcati //
2.8.13.[1]	tataḥ khaṭvāyāṃ varṣīyasyāṃ vaiyāghraṃ carma stṛṇāti mañcake /
2.8.13.[2]	tatra rājānamārohayati 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena /
2.8.13.[3]	udapātraṃ samāsiñcete /
2.8.13.[4]	rājā brūte 'sahaiva no' iti /
2.8.13.[5]	purohito brūyāt 'yo duṣkṛtam' iti /
2.8.13.[6]	tataḥ purohitaḥ sūktaṃ japati //
2.8.14.[1]	catvāro rājaputrāstālpāḥ pṛthakpādeṣu gṛhītvā sabhāmadhye nidadhati //
2.8.15.[1]	dāsaḥ pādau prakṣālayati rājakīyo mahāśūdraḥ prakṣālanaṃ dadāti /
2.8.15.[2]	purohito 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktaṃ japati //
2.8.17.[1]	rājā dyūtakrīḍāṃ karoti /
2.8.17.[2]	punaḥ purohitaḥ 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktaṃ japati /
2.8.17.[3]	eko dāyaścaturṇāṃ varṇānām /
2.8.17.[4]	trayaḥ dāyāḥ rājñaḥ /
2.8.17.[5]	sarvavarṇān sarvatra pālayate rājā //
2.8.18.[1]	vaiśyaḥ rājānamupatiṣṭhate 'utsṛjāyuṣman' iti mantreṇa //
2.8.19.[1]	tato rājā brūte 'brāhmaṇāya' /
2.8.19.[2]	anujñām āhaitair mantraiḥ //
2.8.20-21.[1]	tataḥ sthālīpākaṃ 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena sampātyābhimantrya rājānamāśayati //
2.8.22.[1]	'bhūto bhūteṣu' ityanenāśvamabhimantryārohyāparājitāṃ pādayati //
2.8.23.[1]	punaḥ sabhāṃ pragacchati //
2.8.24.[1]	tato madhumiśraṃ miṣṭamannaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayati //
2.8.25.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā tato 'bhūto bhūteṣu' iti sūktena rasān sampātyābhimantrya rājānamāśayati /
2.8.25.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
2.8.25.[3]	sahasraṃ gavāṃ grāmavaraśca dakṣiṇā //
2.8.26.[1]	tataḥ strīṇāṃ gṛhe yāti //
2.8.27.[1]	tatra madhuparko deyaḥ /
2.8.27.[2]	mahābhiṣekaḥ samāptaḥ /
2.8.27.[3]	ataḥprabhṛti rājakarmādhikāraḥ /
2.8.27.[4]	ghṛtāvekṣaṇaṃ purohitakarmārātrikaṃ nakṣatrapūjāgrahapūjādikaṃ kartavyam //
2.8.28-29.[1]	'imamindra' ityudapātraṃ samāsiñcete udakadhārayā /
2.8.28-29.[2]	tato rājā brūyāt 'sahaiva nau' iti /
2.8.28-29.[3]	tataḥ purohito brūyāt 'yo duṣkṛtam' iti /
2.8.28-29.[4]	tataḥ purohitaḥ sūktaṃ japati //
2.8.30.[1]	tataḥ 'savitā prasavānām' iti sūktena paurohitye vatsyan śūdreṇa āhṛtāḥ samidha ādadhāti /
2.8.30.[2]	'atharvāṅgirasaḥ purohito bhavati' iti gopathabrāhmaṇe uktam /
2.8.30.[3]	rājakarmasu pañcagṛhītam ājyaṃ sarvatra /
2.8.30.[4]	hastitrasanādīni abhiṣekāntāni rājakarmāṇi //
2.8.31.[1]	'indra kṣatram' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāmupanayanam /
2.8.31.[2]	tantra 'asmin vasu' iti gaṇasthāne kṣatriyamabhimantrayate /
2.8.31.[3]	kṣatriyarayopanayanaṃ kuryāt /
2.8.31.[4]	kṣatriyasyopanayane viśeṣaḥ /
2.8.31.[5]	samānamanyat //
2.8.32-34.[1]	atha vācayediti vikalpaṃ manyante ācāryāḥ /
2.8.32-34.[2]	samāptaṃ kṣatriyasyopanayanakarma /
2.8.32-34.[3]	tatra ślokaḥ /
2.8.32-34.[4]	medhāsāmpadakarmāṇi sāmmanasyaṃ ca varcasam /
2.8.32-34.[5]	kramācca rājakarmāṇi dvitīye'smin maharṣiṇā //
2.8.32-34.[6]	aṣṭamī kaṇḍikā //
3.1.0.[1]	nirṛtikarmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
3.1.0.[2]	ā puṣṭikarmabhyo yāvat
3.1.1.[1]	paurṇamāsyāṃ rātrau nirṛtikarma kuryāt /
3.1.1.[2]	kṛṣṇavasanaparihito'gniṃ gṛhītvodakānte gatvā nāvyopari caṭitvāgniṃ prajvālya 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.1.1.[3]	na tantram //
3.1.2.[1]	śāpeṭaṃ gartaṃ nikhanet //
3.1.3.[1]	tatroparyapāṃ sūktaiḥ snātvā //
3.1.4-5.[1]	ahatavasano bhūtvopamucyopānahau tato gṛha āgacchati //
3.1.6.[1]	tataḥ sāmpadaṃ vā pauṣṭikaṃ vā kurute /
3.1.6.[2]	kevalaṃ vā kurute //
3.1.7-11.[1]	kṛṣṇavastraparihito vimucya jaradupānahau vāmena hastena jaracchatraṃ gṛhītvā dakṣiṇena hastena śālātṛṇapūlake'gniṃ kṛtvā jīrṇe vīriṇe'gniṃ prajvālyāpradakṣiṇaṃ bhūtvā nirṛtidiśamabhimukho bhūtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktenājyaṃ sakṛjjuhoti //
3.1.12.[1]	agnau chatropānahau praharati /
3.1.12.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.1.12.[3]	udakānte nāvyāyā dakṣiṇāvata śāpeṭaṃ nikhanet /
3.1.12.[4]	apāṃ sūktairavasiñcati /
3.1.12.[5]	apsu kṛṣṇaṃ jahāti /
3.1.12.[6]	ahatavasana upamucyopānahau tato gṛha āgacchati //
3.1.13.[1]	pūrvasyāṃ paurṇamāsyāmastamite kṛṣṇacailaparihito'gniṃ gṛhītvā bahirgatvā vīriṇastambe'gniṃ prajvālya 'ayaṃ te yoniḥ' iti sūktena vrīhīñ charkarāmiśrān sakṛjjuhoti //
3.1.14.[1]	'ā no bhara mā pari ṣṭhā' iti sūktena dhānāḥ śarkarāmiśrāḥ sakṛjjuhoti //
3.1.15.[1]	'ayaṃ te yoniḥ', 'ā no bhara' iti dvābhyāṃ sūktābhyāṃ saha piṭakena tṛtīyāmāhutiṃ juhoti /
3.1.15.[2]	tata udakānte śāpeṭaṃ nikhanet /
3.1.15.[3]	apāṃ sūktairavasiñcati /
3.1.15.[4]	apsu kṛṣṇaṃ jahāti /
3.1.15.[5]	ahatavasana upamucyopānahau jīvaghātyāyā udāvrajati //
3.1.16.[1]	pūrvasyāṃ paurṇamāsyāmastamita udakānte kṛṣṇacailaparihito nirṛtikarmāṇi prayuṅkte /
3.1.16.[2]	kākajaṅghāyāṃ lohakaṇṭakaṃ baddhvā kaṇṭake puroḍāśaṃ kṛtvā nirṛtyabhimukho bhūtvā 'pra pateta' ityṛcā kākaṃ visarjayati /
3.1.16.[3]	nāvyāyā dakṣiṇāvarte śāpeṭaṃ nikhanet /
3.1.16.[4]	apāṃ sūktairavasiñcati /
3.1.16.[5]	apsu kṛṣṇaṃ jahāti /
3.1.16.[6]	ahatavasana upamucyopānahau tato gṛha āgacchati //
3.1.17.[1]	pūrvasyāṃ paurṇamāsyāmastamita udakānte kṛṣṇacailaparihito nirṛtikarmāṇi prayuṅkte /
3.1.17.[2]	kārayitā nīlaṃ vastramadhaḥ paridhatte /
3.1.17.[3]	raktaṃ vastramuparyācchādya śuklaṃ vastramuṣṇīṣaṃ kṛtvā 'yā mā lakṣmīḥ' ityṛcā lohakhaṇḍena sahoṣṇīṣamudake prakṣipati vāmena hastena //
3.1.18.[1]	'ekaśataṃ lakṣmyaḥ' ityṛcā raktaṃ vastraṃ lohakhaṇḍena sahāpsu kṣipati vāmena hastena /
3.1.18.[2]	'etā enā vyākaram' ityṛcā nīlaṃ vastraṃ lohakhaṇḍena sahāpsu kṣipati vāmena hastena /
3.1.18.[3]	śāpeṭaṃ nikhanet /
3.1.18.[4]	apāṃ sūktairavasiñcati /
3.1.18.[5]	apsu kṛṣṇaṃ jahāti /
3.1.18.[6]	ahatavasano bhūtvopānahau paridhāya gṛha āgacchati /
3.1.18.[7]	tataḥ karmāṇi kuryāt pauṣṭikāni sāmpadāni ca /
3.1.18.[8]	samāptāni nirṛtikarmāṇi /
3.1.18.[9]	pañca pradhānāni karmāṇi /
3.1.18.[10]	evaṃ nirṛtikarma kṛtvā tataḥ sāmpadeṣu pauṣṭikeṣu cādhikāraḥ /
3.1.18.[11]	pratikarma vā kevalaṃ vā nirṛtikarma pāpakṣayārthaṃ karoti /
3.1.18.[12]	nirṛtikarmaṇāṃ kramo'pi nāsti /
3.1.18.[13]	pañcānāṃ madhya ekaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ pauṣṭikānāṃ prayogaḥ sāmpadānāṃ ca /
3.1.18.[14]	pūrvasya brahmacārisāmpadādīni sāmpadāni /
3.1.18.[15]	pūrvasya citrākarmādīni pauṣṭikāni /
3.1.18.[16]	etānyucyante ā bhaiṣajyebhyaḥ karmabhyo yāvat //
3.1.18.[17]	puṣṭikarmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
3.1.19-20.[1]	ājyatantre haritadarbhāstaraṇaṃ karoti /
3.1.19-20.[2]	abhyātānāntaṃ samānam /
3.1.19-20.[3]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena kulāyaśṛtaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ sthālīpākaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti kārayitā /
3.1.19-20.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.1.19-20.[5]	etat karma caitryāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ kuryāt /
3.1.19-20.[6]	athavā citrānakṣatre kuryāt /
3.1.19-20.[7]	nityaṃ caitrīkarma //
3.1.21.[1]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena ghṛtenāktāḥ pālāśādisamidha ādadhāti /
3.1.21.[2]	etadapi citrākarma nityaṃ ca //
3.1.22.[1]	nāvyanadīsaṅgame gatvābhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantrya paścādagnerbhūmau prakṣipya paśuvanmukhenāśnāti na hastena /
3.1.22.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.1.23.[1]	trirātraṃ karma bhavati /
3.1.23.[2]	pratyahaṃ tantram //
3.1.24.[1]	tejaskāmaḥ puṣṭikāmaśca /
3.1.24.[2]	samāptaṃ tejovratam //
3.1.25.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'āpo hi ṣṭhā' 'śaṃ no devīḥ' 'brahma jajñānam', 'anāptā ye' , 'asya vāmasya' anuvākaḥ, 'yo rohitaḥ' iti dve, 'udasya ketavaḥ' ityanuvākaḥ, 'mūrdhāham' iti dve sūkte, 'viṣāsahim' ityanuvākaḥ, etaiḥ kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.1.25.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.1.25.[3]	sarvatra 'āpo hi ṣṭhā' ityādisalilagaṇo jñātavyaḥ //
3.1.26.[1]	salilaiḥ audumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
3.1.26.[2]	salilaiḥ pālāśasamidha ādadhāti /
3.1.26.[3]	salilaiḥ karkandhūsamidha ādadhāti /
3.1.26.[4]	salilaiḥ vrīhīn juhoti /
3.1.26.[5]	salilairyavān juhoti /
3.1.26.[6]	salilaistilān juhoti /
3.1.26.[7]	tantre salilaiḥ kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
3.1.26.[8]	tantre salilaiḥ puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
3.1.26.[9]	tantre salilaiḥ rasān sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
3.1.26.[10]	salilaiḥ trirahno'gniṃ prajvālayati /
3.1.26.[11]	salilaiḥ triragnimupatiṣṭhate /
3.1.26.[12]	abhyātānānte salilaiḥ savyāt pāṇihṛdayāllohitaṃ rasamiśramaśnāti /
3.1.26.[13]	tata uttaratantram /
3.1.26.[14]	iti manthāntāni karmāṇi //
3.1.26.[15]	adhvānaṃ gacchataḥ puṣṭikarmāṇyucyante
3.1.27.[1]	'brahma jajñānam', 'anāptā ye' sūktenājyaṃ juhoti /
3.1.27.[2]	tantre 'brahma jajñānam' iti caturdaśena pālāśādisamidha ādadhāti /
3.1.27.[3]	anena sūktena puroḍāśaṃ juhoti /
3.1.27.[4]	dvitīyena brahmajajñānena payaḥ, udaudanaḥ, pāyasaḥ, paśuḥ, vrīhiḥ, yavaḥ, tilāḥ, dhānāḥ, karambhaḥ, śaṣkulyaḥ eteṣāṃ vikalpena homaḥ /
3.1.27.[5]	hastahome tantravikalpaḥ /
3.1.27.[6]	iti prasthānakarma //
3.1.28.[1]	yadā āgacchati tadā etat karma //
3.1.29.[1]	yadā grāmaṃ gacchati tadā etat karma kuryāt //
3.1.30.[1]	yathārthaṃ yācate tadā dravyakāma etat karma kuryāt //
3.1.31.[1]	athavā niṣkāmo'pi karoti //
3.1.31.[2]	atha samudrakarmeti /
3.1.31.[3]	sarvaphalakarma vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.1.32-34.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā tataścatvāraḥ pūlakā pālāśamindhanaṃ catvāro darbhapūlakāḥ /
3.1.32-34.[2]	vyatiṣaṅgena juhoti /
3.1.32-34.[3]	ekaṃ samidbhārakaṃ dvitīyaṃ tasyopari darbhabhārakaṃ punarapi tathaiva ca /
3.1.32-34.[4]	aṣṭau uparyupari kṛtvā tato 'brahma jajñānam' iti caturdaśenājyaṃ juhoti //
3.1.35.[1]	tato dhūmaṃ bhakṣayati //
3.1.36.[1]	lepaṃ prāśnāti /
3.1.36.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.1.37-38.[1]	sāttrikasyāgneḥ praṇayanam /
3.1.37-38.[2]	athavā tatra sthāne etat karma karoti /
3.1.37-38.[3]	dhanadhānyaputralakṣmīyaśomedhādharmakāmaḥ /
3.1.37-38.[4]	svargakāmaḥ /
3.1.37-38.[5]	āyurbalaprajñāsampadgrāmakūpādi patnīprādhānyābhayasvastyayanavijayagṛhavarastrīhiraṇyaratnādi sampadyate /
3.1.37-38.[6]	'samudra ityācakṣate karma' iti vacanāt //
3.1.37-38.[7]	prathamā kaṇḍikā //
3.2.0.[1]	atha gavāṃ rogeṣu gavāṃ puṣṭiprajananeṣu ca śāntirucyate
3.2.1.[1]	'ambayo yanti', 'āpo hi ṣṭhā' , 'śanno devīḥ' ityetaiḥ sūktairlavaṇamabhimantrya gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.1.[2]	brahmajajñānena prathamena lavaṇamabhimantrya gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.1.[3]	'ā gāvaḥ' iti sūktena lavaṇamabhimantrya gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.1.[4]	'ekā ca me' iti sūktena lavaṇamabhimantrya gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.1.[5]	bahudugdhā gāvo bhavanti /
3.2.1.[6]	jvaragaṇḍamālādiroge etat karma //
3.2.2.[1]	garbhagrahaṇārthametat karma bhavati //
3.2.3.[1]	'ambayo yanti', 'āpo hi ṣṭhā', 'śanno devīḥ' iti tribhiḥ sūktaiḥ udakamabhimantrya gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.3.[2]	puṣṭyarthī /
3.2.3.[3]	'brahma jajñānam' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.3.[4]	'ā gāvaḥ' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.3.[5]	'ekā ca me' iti sūktena taḍāgamavarudhya tato gāḥ pāyayati /
3.2.3.[6]	samāptāni gavāṃ puṣṭikarmāṇi //
3.2.3.[7]	sarvārthāni puṣṭikarmāṇyucyante
3.2.4.[1]	dvābhyāṃ mahānadībhyām udakam āhṛtya sarvata upāsicya kūpataḍāgādyudakaṃ tatrava prakṣipati //
3.2.5.[1]	tenodakena maiśradhānyaṃ śrapayitvābhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ saṃ sravantu' iti maiśradhānyaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.5.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.5.[3]	puṣṭyarthī //
3.2.6.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā mahānadībhyāmudakena saktumanthaṃ kṛtvā dadhimadhu nikṣipya 'saṃ saṃ sravantu' iti sūktena sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.6.[2]	uttaratantram /
3.2.6.[3]	puṣṭyarthī //
3.2.6.[4]	atha lakṣmīkarma vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
3.2.7.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā yasya gṛhe lakṣmī asti tasya gṛhāt vrīhyājyapaya āhārya kṣīraudanaṃ śrapayitvā 'saṃ saṃ sravantu' iti sūktena sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.7.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.2.8.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā śrīmato gṛhāt gomayamāhārya tataḥ śoṣayitvā trivṛti gomayaparicaye śṛtaṃ sārūpavatsa odanaṃ 'saṃ saṃ sravantu' iti sūktena sampātyābhimantryāśnāti //
3.2.8.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.8.[3]	samāptaṃ lakṣmīprāptikarma /
3.2.8.[4]	lakṣmīkarmaṇi kṛte lakṣmīrbhavati //
3.2.8.[5]	atha samudra idaṃ karma kriyate puṣṭikarma /
3.2.8.[6]	alakṣmīvināśakarmāṇyucyante
3.2.9.[1]	śāpeṭam ālipyāpsu nibadhya tatrāgniṃ praṇīya 'śerabhaka' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.9.[2]	tantram /
3.2.9.[3]	puṣṭyarthī //
3.2.10-11.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'śerabhaka' iti sūktenākhaṇḍitayavānāṃ saktūn raktājāyā dadhyudakena sannīya sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.10-11.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
3.2.12.[1]	tṛṇānāṃ granthīn kṛtvā tān granthīnudgṛhṇannapakrāmati udāvrajati //
3.2.13.[1]	'śerabhaka' iti sūktena udapātre vicṛtati pratyṛcam /
3.2.13.[2]	tenodapātreṇa snānaṃ kṛtvā mukhaṃ prakṣālayati /
3.2.13.[3]	puṣṭyarthī //
3.2.13.[4]	goṣṭhakarmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
3.2.14-15.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'eha yantu paśavaḥ' iti sūktena gṛṣṭeḥ pīyūṣaṃ śleṣmamiśritaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.14-15.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.2.14-15.[3]	puṣṭikāmaḥ /
3.2.14-15.[4]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo goṣṭhena' iti sūktena gṛṣṭeḥ pīyūṣaṃ śleṣmamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.14-15.[5]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.2.14-15.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prajāvatīḥ' ityekā, 'padajñā stha' iti dvitīyā /
3.2.14-15.[7]	ābhyāṃ gṛṣṭeḥ pīyūṣaṃ śleṣmamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.14-15.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.14-15.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prajāpatiśca parameṣṭhī ca' iti sūktena prathamaprasūtāyā goḥ pīyūṣaṃ vatsalālāmiśritaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.14-15.[10]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.2.16.[1]	'eha yantu paśavaḥ' iti sūktena gāmabhimantrya dadāti /
3.2.16.[2]	sarvatra puṣṭikāmo'nuvartate /
3.2.16.[3]	'saṃ vo goṣṭhena' iti sūktena gāmabhimantrya dadāti /
3.2.16.[4]	prajāvatīḥ 'padajñā stha' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ gāmabhimantrya dadāti /
3.2.16.[5]	'prajāpatiśca' iti sūktena gāmabhimantrya dadāti //
3.2.17-18.[1]	'eha yantu' iti sūktenodapātramabhimantrya goṣṭhamadhye ninayati /
3.2.17-18.[2]	govāṭe pāṃśukūṭaṃ vāmena hastena kṛtvā dakṣiṇena hastena ardhaṃ vikṣipati /
3.2.17-18.[3]	puṣṭyarthī /
3.2.17-18.[4]	'saṃ vo goṣṭhena' iti sūktena udapātramabhimantrya govāṭe ninayati /
3.2.17-18.[5]	samuhya savyenādhiṣṭhāyārdhaṃ dakṣiṇena vikṣipati /
3.2.17-18.[6]	puṣṭyarthī /
3.2.17-18.[7]	'prajāvatīḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāmudapātramabhimantrya ninayati /
3.2.17-18.[8]	samuhya savyenādhiṣṭhāyārdhaṃ dakṣiṇena vikṣipati /
3.2.17-18.[9]	'prajāpatiśca parameṣṭhī ca' iti sūktena udapātramabhimantrya ninayati /
3.2.17-18.[10]	savyena govāṭe pāṃśukūṭaṃ kṛtvārdhaṃ dakṣiṇena vikṣipati //
3.2.19.[1]	sārūpavatsa odane śakṛtpiṇḍān guggululavaṇaṃ prakṣipya tataḥ paścād agner nikhanati //
3.2.20-21.[1]	trirātraṃ yāvat /
3.2.20-21.[2]	caturthe utkhātya abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'eha yantu' iti sūktena sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.20-21.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.20-21.[4]	pūrvavaccaturthe'hani abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ vo goṣṭhena' iti sūktena sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.20-21.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.20-21.[6]	pūrvavaccaturthe'hani abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prajāvatīḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.20-21.[7]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.2.20-21.[8]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prajāpatiśca' iti sūktena pūrvavat sārūpavatsaṃ caturthe'hani sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.2.20-21.[9]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.2.20-21.[10]	samāptāni goṣṭhakarmāṇi /
3.2.20-21.[11]	iti samāptā gośāntiḥ //
3.2.20-21.[12]	atha sarvakāmamaṇiśāntirucyate
3.2.22.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'āyamagan parṇamaṇiḥ' iti sūktena pālāśamaṇiṃ trirvāsitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
3.2.22.[2]	'trayodaśyādayastisro dadhi madhuni vāsayitvā badhnāti' iti paribhāṣāvacanāt /
3.2.22.[3]	pālāśādiṣu caturṣu maṇiṣu sambadhyate puṣṭikāmastejaskāmo balakāma āyuṣkāmo dhanakāmaśca /
3.2.22.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.22.[5]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ayaṃ pratisaro maṇiḥ' ityarthasūktena tilakamaṇiṃ vāsitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
3.2.22.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.22.[7]	abhicāradoṣe puṣṭidhanakāmārthī dharmavīrya āyuṣyakṛtyāpratiharaṇārthī yaśorthī ca sapatnanāśārthī roge ca jayārthī /
3.2.22.[8]	balakāmo maṅgalārthī ca /
3.2.22.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ayaṃ me varaṇo maṇiḥ' ityarthasūktena varaṇamaṇiṃ vāsitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
3.2.22.[10]	uttaratantram /
3.2.22.[11]	śatrukṣayakāmaḥ rakṣārthī cābhicāre jayakāmo yaśakāmaḥ puṣṭikāmaśca //
3.2.23-25.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā khadiraphālamaṇiṃ trirvāsitaṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyaveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā 'etamidhmam' ityṛcā idhmamupasamādhāya 'tamimaṃ devatāḥ' iti vāsitamullupyāsādya 'arātīyoḥ' ityarthasūktena sampātyābhimantrya 'brahmaṇā tejasā' iti badhnāti khadiraphālamaṇim /
3.2.23-25.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.2.23-25.[3]	sarvakāmārthasiddhyartho maṇiḥ sarvakāmaḥ //
3.2.26.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'uttamo asyoṣadhīnām' iti sūktena pālāśamaṇiṃ trirvāsitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya puṇyāhānte badhnāti /
3.2.26.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.2.26.[3]	puṣṭikāmo'yaṃ maṇiḥ //
3.2.27.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'akṣitāste' ityṛcā yavamaṇiṃ trirvāsitaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
3.2.27.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.2.27.[3]	puṣṭyarthī /
3.2.27.[4]	puṣṭikāmādhikāro'nuvartate ā tṛtīyādhyāyaparisamāptiṃ yāvat /
3.2.27.[5]	samāptā maṇiśāntiḥ //
3.2.27.[6]	aṣṭakākarma puṣṭikarmāṇy ucyante /
3.2.27.[7]	puṣṭikāmo vā nityaṃ vā aṣṭakākarma kuryāt
3.2.28-29.[1]	māghāṣṭakāyāṃ 'pūrvāhṇe yajñopavītī śālāniveśanaṃ samūhayatyupavatsyadbhaktamaśitvā snāto'hatavasanaḥ prayuṅkte' rātrau /
3.2.28-29.[2]	vaśāmantrāḥ /
3.2.28-29.[3]	pākayajñavidhānam /
3.2.28-29.[4]	dhānādīnāṃ śrapaṇaṃ kṛtvā tata ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ 'purastādagneḥ pratīcīṃ gāṃ dhārayati paścādagneḥ prāṅmukha upaviśyānvārabdhāya śāntyudakaṃ karoti' /
3.2.28-29.[5]	tataḥ 'prathamā ha vyuvāsa sā' iti sarveṇa sūktena ghṛtaṃ juhoti /
3.2.28-29.[6]	triḥ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
3.2.28-29.[7]	tataḥ māṃsahome 'prathamā ha vyuvāsa sā' iti sarveṇa sūktena tisraḥ paśvāhutīrjuhoti /
3.2.28-29.[8]	triḥ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
3.2.28-29.[9]	tataḥ 'prathamā ha vyuvāsa sā' iti sarveṇa sthālīpākaṃ juhoti /
3.2.28-29.[10]	triḥ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
3.2.28-29.[11]	tataḥ aṣṭakāyāmaṣṭakāhomān juhuyāt /
3.2.28-29.[12]	tasyāṃ havīṣiṃ dhānādīnyājyamiśrāṇyekatra kṛtvā viśatiṃ piṇḍikāḥ kṛtvā /
3.2.28-29.[13]	paśordakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ nirlomaṃ sacarmaṃ sakhuraṃ prakṣālyāsādya /
3.2.28-29.[14]	tata abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prathamā ha vyuvāsa sā' iti pañcabhiḥ 'āyamagan' iti catasṛbhirvijñāyate /
3.2.28-29.[15]	'ṛtubhyaṣṭvā' iti vigrāhamaṣṭhau /
3.2.28-29.[16]	'indraputra' ityaṣṭādaśīm /
3.2.28-29.[17]	'ahorātrābhyām' ityūnaviṃśīm /
3.2.28-29.[18]	'iḍāyāspadam' iti dvābhyāṃ viṃśīm /
3.2.28-29.[19]	dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ juhoti /
3.2.28-29.[20]	'pūrṇā darve' iti sadarvīmekaviṃśīm //
3.2.30.[1]	tato'bhyātānāni hutvā dhānāḥ karambha ityādīni havirucchiṣṭānyājyamiśrāṇi kṛtvā 'prathamā ha vyuvāsa sā' iti sarveṇa sūktena tisra āhutīrjuhoti /
3.2.30.[2]	triḥ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
3.2.30.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.2.30.[4]	tataḥ paścādagnervāgyataḥ saṃviśati /
3.2.30.[5]	svapiti /
3.2.30.[6]	prabhāta uttiṣṭhati //
3.2.31.[1]	pṛthivyāpastejo vāyurākāśamiti smarati /
3.2.31.[2]	tataḥ prabhāte śrāddhaṃ mātaraṃ nāndīmukhamityaṣṭakākarma /
3.2.31.[3]	puṣṭikāmo vā nityaṃ vā karoti //
3.2.31.[4]	dvitīyā kaṇḍikā //19 //
3.3.0.[1]	kṛṣikarma vakṣyāmaḥ
3.3.1.[1]	kṣetre gatvā 'sīrā yuñjanti' iti sūktena yugalāṅgalaṃ badhnāti //
3.3.2.[1]	'sīrā yuñjanti' iti sūktena yugasya dakṣiṇato vṛṣabhaṃ yunakti //
3.3.3.[1]	'ehi pūrṇaka' iti mantreṇa uttarato dvitīyaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ yunakti //
3.3.4.[1]	'śunaṃ kīnāśā anuyantu vāhān' iti pādena hāliko'nyān caturo vṛṣabhān yunakti /
3.3.4.[2]	'ṣaïgavaṃ halam' iti vacanāt //
3.3.5-7.[1]	'aśvinā phālam' ityṛcā lohaphālamabhimantrya hale pratikarṣati /
3.3.5-7.[2]	'irāvānasi' iti mantreṇa phālamabhimantrayate /
3.3.5-7.[3]	'apahatāḥ' iti mantreṇāpūpānabhimantrya hale phālamukhe dadāti /
3.3.5-7.[4]	tataḥ 'sīrā yuñjanti' iti sūktena kartā halena kṛṣati //
3.3.8.[1]	sūktaṃ samāpya tato halaṃ hālikāya prayacchati //
3.3.9.[1]	tisraḥ sītāḥ prācīḥ hālikaḥ kṛṣati /
3.3.9.[2]	kalyāṇīrvāco vadantaḥ puṇyāhādīni ca //
3.3.10.[1]	'sīte vandāmahe tvā' ityṛcā kartānumantrayate /
3.3.10.[2]	trirmantrāvṛttiḥ /
3.3.10.[3]	uttarasmin sītāyā ante kṛtvā /
3.3.10.[4]	tatrājyabhāgāntaṃ pākatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sīrā yuñjanti' iti sūktenendradaivatyaṃ puroḍāśaṃ juhoti /
3.3.10.[5]	indradevatāke puroḍāśe carudharmā aviruddhāḥ puroḍāśasya sarve bhavanti //
3.3.11.[1]	aśvinādevatākaṃ caruṃ 'sīrā yuñjanti' iti sūktena juhoti //
3.3.12.[1]	tataḥ abhyātānāni hutvā 'sīrā yuñjanti' iti sūktenottarasyāṃ sītāyāṃ sampātānānayati //
3.3.13-14.[1]	udapātra uttarasampātān ānayati /
3.3.13-14.[2]	tata udapātre havīṃṣi śaṣpaṃ vrīhīn virūḍhaṃ ca nidadhāti //
3.3.15.[1]	tenodakena sarvaṃ halam anakti //
3.3.16-19.[1]	yatra sītā sampātitā tasmāt sthānāt mṛttikāṃ patnī gṛhṇāti hastena /
3.3.16-19.[2]	tata anyo manuṣyaḥ pṛcchati 'kim āhārṣīḥ' /
3.3.16-19.[3]	tataḥ patnī brūte 'vittiṃ bhūtim' iti //
3.3.20.[1]	tato madhyamāyāṃ sītāyāṃ mṛttikāṃ nidadhāti patnī tūṣṇīm //
3.3.21.[1]	tato lohaphālaṃ ghṛtenābhyajya tatraiva kṣetre nidadhāti tato'bhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.3.22.[1]	tataḥ sītāśiraḥsu darbhānāstīrya darbhopari plakṣacamasānaudumbaracamasāṃs trīṃs trīn nidadhāti //
3.3.23.[1]	ekaikasyāḥ sītāyāḥ dakṣiṇeṣu camaseṣu rasān prakṣipya madhyameṣu virūḍhaṃ prakṣipyottareṣu puroḍāśaṃ nidadhāti //
3.3.24.[1]	camasopari darbhān nidadhāti /
3.3.24.[2]	tataścamasān pāṃsunā pracchādayati /
3.3.24.[3]	mṛttikāṃ dadhāti tatra /
3.3.24.[4]	tataḥ prabhāte avaśyaṃ tasmin kṣetre dvitīye'hani karṣayitavyam /
3.3.24.[5]	etat sarvamekaṃ karma /
3.3.24.[6]	kṛṣikarma samāptam //
3.3.24.[7]	atha vṛṣabhalābhakarmocyate
3.3.25-26.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sīrā yuñjanti' iti sūktena sārūpavatsa odane śakṛtpiṇḍān prakṣipya guggulu lavaṇaṃ ca prakṣipya tasminnodane sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.3.25-26.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.3.25-26.[3]	dhenurdakṣiṇā /
3.3.25-26.[4]	vṛṣabhalābhakarma samāptam /
3.3.25-26.[5]	anena karmaṇā kṛtena bahavo vṛṣabhāḥ sampadyante /
3.3.25-26.[6]	'anaḍutsāmpadam' iti vacanāt //
3.3.25-26.[7]	tṛtīyā kaṇḍikā //
3.4.0.[1]	atha sphātikaraṇakarmocyate
3.4.1-2.[1]	śāntaphalaṃ tasyāvasitamākṛtiloṣṭaṃ valmīkamṛttikā tasyāmantaṃ vapā ca /
3.4.1-2.[2]	trīṇi kūdyāḥ prāntānyagrāṇi madhyamapalāśe kṛtvā darbheṇa pariveṣṭya śāntipuṣṭivadvā 'payasvatīḥ' iti sūktenābhimantrya rāśipalyeṣu karotyadhastāt //
3.4.3-6.[1]	'payasvatīḥ' iti sūktena yadā yadā bhaktaṃ rādhyate tadā tadābhimantrayate yadā dīyate /
3.4.3-6.[2]	kaṇḍane peṣaṇe niṣpavane randhane pariveṣaṇe dāne ca sarvatrābhimantraṇam //
3.4.7.[1]	'ayaṃ no nabhasaspatiḥ' iti sūktenāśmānaṃ abhimantrya palye nidadhāti /
3.4.7.[2]	aśmanopari trīn anvṛcaṃ muṣṭiṃ dhānyaṃ nidadhāti /
3.4.7.[3]	sthiradhānyamakṣayaṃ bhavati /
3.4.7.[4]	samāptāni sphātikaraṇāni //
3.4.7.[5]	puṣṭikarmāṇyeva vartante
3.4.8.[1]	'ā gāvaḥ' iti sūktena sandhyākāle gā āyatīḥ pratyuttiṣṭhati //
3.4.9.[1]	yadā prathamaṃ homamicchati tadedaṃ karma karoti pākayajñavidhānena /
3.4.9.[2]	tasyā dugdhenendradevatākaṃ caruṃ śrapayitvā 'ā gāvaḥ' iti ṣaïbhirṛgbhirdvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ trayo homāḥ kartavyāḥ /
3.4.9.[3]	'indrāya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' iti /
3.4.9.[4]	prokṣaṇe barhiḥpraharaṇe ca viśeṣaḥ //
3.4.10.[1]	'prajāvatīḥ sūyavasā' ityṛcāraṇye gacchantīrgā anumantrayate //
3.4.11.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sūryasya raśmīnanu' iti tisṛbhirdvādaśadāmnyāṃ sampātitāyāṃ vatsāṃ badhnāti /
3.4.11.[2]	'iha vatsāṃ nibadhnīmaḥ' iti pādena vatsāṃ badhnāti /
3.4.11.[3]	'ayaṃ ghāsaḥ' iti pādena ghāsaṃ dadāti gobhyo vatsebhyaśca /
3.4.11.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.4.11.[5]	samāptā gośāntiḥ //
3.4.11.[6]	vastrasāmpadāni karmāṇyucyante
3.4.12-13.[1]	'yaste śokāya' ityṛcā tisraḥ kūdīmayīḥ ūmayakulāyasūtreṇāveṣṭya ghūtenāktā ādadhāti /
3.4.12-13.[2]	trirmantrāvṛttiḥ /
3.4.12-13.[3]	ūmaya ūrṇanābhiḥ /
3.4.12-13.[4]	anena karmaṇā kṛtena vastrāṇi sampadyante //
3.4.14.[1]	'yaste śokāya' ityṛcā muñjena saha iṣīkāstisro madhunā praliptā cikkaśeṣvādadhāti /
3.4.14.[2]	trirmantrāvṛttiḥ /
3.4.14.[3]	samāptāni vastrasāmpadāni //
3.4.14.[4]	jyeṣṭhena putreṇa saha bhāgavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
3.4.15.[1]	'uta putraḥ' ityṛcā gṛhakāṣṭheṣṭakādyā abhimantrya gṛhaṃ kārayet /
3.4.15.[2]	puṣṭikāmaḥ /
3.4.15.[3]	putro vā sāmpadaṃ karoti pitā vā //
3.4.16.[1]	'uta putraḥ' ityṛcā sarvasāmpadaṃ kurute /
3.4.16.[2]	'uta putraḥ' ityṛcā audumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
3.4.16.[3]	'uta putraḥ' ityṛcā pālāśasamidha ādadhāti /
3.4.16.[4]	'uta putraḥ' ityṛcā bṛhadbadarīsamidha ādadhāti /
3.4.16.[5]	āvapati vrīhiyavatilānityādi /
3.4.16.[6]	grāmapaśuputradhanadhānyakāmaḥ sarvasāmpadaṃ kurute /
3.4.16.[7]	putraḥ karoti sāmpadāni karmāṇi //
3.4.17-18.[1]	'ardhamardhena' ityṛcā ārdrapāṇirbhūtvā śāntaśākhayā ṛcaṃ japitvā pitā putrasya bhāgaṃ prayacchati prāgbhāgamapākṛtya /
3.4.17-18.[2]	putrasya gṛhe godhanaṃ badhnāti //
3.4.19.[1]	agnisammukhaṃ kurute /
3.4.19.[2]	putrabhāgaṃ kurute //
3.4.20.[1]	agre yā amāvāsyā bhaviṣyati tasyāmamāvāsyāyām 'ardhamardhena' ityṛcā śākhāṃ bhittvā tisraḥ samidha ādadhāti /
3.4.20.[2]	trirmantrāvṛttiḥ /
3.4.20.[3]	putrāśca bhrātaro'pyanena vidhānena bhāgaṃ kurvanti /
3.4.20.[4]	samāptaṃ vibhāgakarma putrasya /
3.4.20.[5]	puṣṭikāmaḥ //
3.4.21-22.[1]	'tve kratumapi' ityṛcā rasakarmāṇi kurute /
3.4.21-22.[2]	rasān sampātyābhimantrya prāśayati /
3.4.21-22.[3]	yāni medhājananādīni vihitāni sarvāṇi vikalpenānayā ṛcā bhavanti /
3.4.21-22.[4]	kāmaḥ puṣṭireva /

3.5.0.[1]	punar anekaphalapuṣṭikarmāṇy ucyante
3.5.1.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ,' 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ maiśradhānyaṃ bhṛṣṭapiṣṭaṃ saktumajālohitamiśraṃ rasamiśritaṃ ca sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.5.1.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
3.5.2-4.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāmaudumbaracamaseṣu triṣu maiśradhānyaṃ prakṣipya rasāṃśca sampātyābhimantryāśnāti mantreṇa trikālaṃ ca /
3.5.2-4.[2]	'pūrvāhṇasya tejasā' ityādayo mantrāḥ /
3.5.2-4.[3]	pratimantraṃ bhakṣaṇam /
3.5.2-4.[4]	plakṣacamaseṣu vā /
3.5.2-4.[5]	ekaṃ camasaṃ pūrvāhṇe /
3.5.2-4.[6]	ekaṃ madhyāhne /
3.5.2-4.[7]	ekamaparāhṇe /
3.5.2-4.[8]	trikālabhedāḥ /
3.5.2-4.[9]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.5.5.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāmṛtumatyāḥ striyā lohitaṃ rasamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāṅgulibhyāṃ pradeśanīmadhyamābhyāṃ prāśnāti /
3.5.5.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.5.5.[3]	puṣṭyarthī //
3.5.5.[4]	kṣetrakāmasya karmocyate
3.5.6.[1]	yat kṣetraṃ kāmayate tasmin kṣetra idaṃ karma kuryāt /
3.5.6.[2]	ājyatantraṃ barhirlavanādyabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ bhaktaṃ dadhimadhumiśraṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.5.6.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
3.5.6.[4]	samāptaṃ kṣetrakāmasya karma //
3.5.7.[1]	saṃvatsaraṃ brahmacaryaṃ kṛtvā tato maithunaṃ kṛtvā śuktyāṃ reta ānīya taṇḍulamiśraṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.5.7.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.5.7.[3]	puṣṭikāmaḥ /
3.5.7.[4]	idaṃ saptagrāmalābhakarma kathyate //
3.5.8-9.[1]	dvādaśīmamāvāsyeti kṣīrabhakṣo bhavati /
3.5.8-9.[2]	amāvāsyāyāṃ dadhimadhubhakṣaḥ /
3.5.8-9.[3]	pratipadyabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ tasya mūtra udakadadhimadhugomayaṃ ca etānyekīkṛtya sampātyābhimantryāśnāti 'kravyādaṃ nāḍī' ityṛcā /
3.5.8-9.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.5.8-9.[5]	saptagrāmalābhakarma samāptam //

3.5.10-13.[1]	tṛtīyamāgrayaṇaṃ kṛtvābhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ', 'tadidāsa' iti sūktābhyāṃ vrīhiyavānekatra kṛtvā trivṛti gomayaparicaye śrapayitvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.5.10-13.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.5.10-13.[3]	sarvakāmaḥ /
3.5.10-13.[4]	samṛddhiputrapaśudhanādi //
3.5.10-13.[5]	atha samudrakarmocyate
3.5.14.[1]	śatrudeśe gatvā gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnyāhavanīyeṣu karma kuryāt /
3.5.14.[2]	tato gārhapatye'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena sārūpavatsamodanaṃ gārhapatyaśṛtaṃ gārhapatye prathamaṃ sampātya /
3.5.14.[3]	tato dakṣiṇāgnau tantraṃ kṛtvā pūtīkaiḥ kāśaiḥ staraṇam /
3.5.14.[4]	tameva sārūpavatsaṃ sampātya /
3.5.14.[5]	tata āhavanīye tantraṃ kṛtvā bhāṅgāstaraṇam /
3.5.14.[6]	tatastameva sārūpavatsaṃ sampātya tenaiva sūktena tataḥ paścāt sakṛdabhimantraṇaṃ kṛtvā tata aśnāti /
3.5.14.[7]	aśanaṃ gārhapatyadeśe karoti /
3.5.14.[8]	gārhapatyaprabhṛtyuttaratantraṃ kuryāt //
3.5.15.[1]	vratagrahaṇādi karoti /
3.5.15.[2]	dakṣiṇāgnyāhavanīyagārhapatyeṣu yathākramaṃ vratagrahaṇādi abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā sārūpavatsasya dakṣiṇāgnau śrapaṇaṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena sārūpavatsaṃ sampātyādiṣu yathākrameṇa /
3.5.15.[3]	tato gārhapatyaṃ dakṣiṇāgniṃ caikatra kṛtvā tato'bhimantrya dakṣiṇāgnideśa aśnāti yathākrameṇa /
3.5.15.[4]	uttaratantram /
3.5.15.[5]	evamāhavanīyagārhapatyadakṣiṇāgniṣu vratopāyanādyabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā sārūpavatsasyāhavanīye śrapaṇaṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktenāhavanīyādi yathākrameṇa /
3.5.15.[6]	sārūpavatsaṃ sampātya gārhapatyāhavanīyamekatra kṛtvā tato'bhimantryāśnāti /
3.5.15.[7]	tata āhavanīyagārhapatyadakṣiṇāgniṣu yathākrameṇa /
3.5.15.[8]	uttaratantram /
3.5.15.[9]	gārhapatyasya darbhaiḥ staraṇam /
3.5.15.[10]	dakṣiṇāgneḥ pūtīkaiḥ staraṇam /
3.5.15.[11]	āhavanīyasya bhāṅgābhiḥ staraṇam /
3.5.15.[12]	staraṇe viśeṣaḥ //
3.5.16.[1]	gārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnyāhavanīyeṣu yathākrameṇa punareva tantraṃ kṛtvā 'mamāgneḥ varcaḥ' iti sūktena droṇakalaśe rasān kṛtvā tataḥ sampātya yathākrameṇa /
3.5.16.[2]	abhimantraṇaṃ ca sakṛt kuryāt /
3.5.16.[3]	tato rasān prāśnāti gārhapatyādikrameṇa /
3.5.16.[4]	uttaratantram /
3.5.16.[5]	darbhapūtīkabhāṅgābhiḥ paristaraṇam /
3.5.16.[6]	gārhapatyādiṣu yathākramam /
3.5.16.[7]	samāptaṃ samudrakarma //

3.6.0.[1]	atha niveśakarmocyate
3.6.1.[1]	agniśālāyāṃ vā gośālāyāṃ vā grāme vā pure vānyatrābhinave gṛhe vā /
3.6.1.[2]	puṣṭikāmo'nuvartate /
3.6.1.[3]	pāṣāṇamaye vā kāṣṭhamaye vā tṛṇamaye vā iṣṭakāmaye vā sarvatra nave vāsitaṃ idaṃ karma /
3.6.1.[4]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yajūṃṣi yajñe' iti sūktāntena sakṛd ghṛtaṃ madhumiśraṃ juhoti //
3.6.2.[1]	'doṣo gāya' iti sūktena dvitīyāmāhutiṃ juhoti //
3.6.3.[1]	'yajūṃṣi yajñe', 'doṣo gāya' iti sūktābhyāṃ tṛtīyāmāhutiṃ juhoti //
3.6.4.[1]	'anumatiḥ sarvam' ityṛcā caturthīmāhutiṃ juhoti //
3.6.5.[1]	tataḥ śālām aṅgulibhyāṃ samprokṣya tūṣṇīṃ gṛhapatnyāsāda upaviśya udapātraṃ ninayati tūṣṇīm //
3.6.6.[1]	ādau vāgyamanaṃ kṛtam /
3.6.6.[2]	'ihaiva sta' iti vāgvisargaḥ /
3.6.6.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
3.6.6.[4]	navaśālāyāṃ puṣṭikāmaḥ karoti /
3.6.6.[5]	gṛhapraveśe ca nityam //
3.6.7.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ūrdhvā asya' iti sūktenāgnau audumbaraṃ dattvājyaṃ juhoti /
3.6.7.[2]	dhūmaṃ niyacchati /
3.6.7.[3]	lepaṃ prāśnīyāt /
3.6.7.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
3.6.7.[5]	puṣṭikāmādhikāro'nuvartate //
3.6.8.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvāsaṅkhyātā āgamaśaṣkulīradhiśṛtya 'ūrdhvā asya' iti sūktena sapta śaṣkulīragnau dattvājyaṃ juhoti /
3.6.8.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.6.8.[3]	śeṣāḥ śaṣkulīḥ kartre dadāti /
3.6.8.[4]	puṣṭikāmaḥ //
3.6.8.[5]	dāyādeṣu vibhāgakarma vakṣyāmaḥ
3.6.9.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvaṣṭā me daivyaṃ vacaḥ' iti sūktena sārūpavatsaṃ śrapayitvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.6.9.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.6.10.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvaṣṭā me daivyam' iti sūktena dhanurjyāṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
3.6.10.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
3.6.10.[3]	samāptāni vibhāgaśāntikarmāṇi dāyādavibhāgānām //
3.6.11.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvaṣṭā me' iti sūktena daṇḍaṃ sampātyābhimantrya vimṛjya tato dhārayati /
3.6.11.[2]	dhvajadaṇḍaṃ citraṃ dhanurdaṇḍaṃ śailakuntadaṇḍaṃ rājadaṇḍaṃ veṇvādi /
3.6.11.[3]	puṣṭyarthī //
3.6.11.[4]	atha citrākarma citrānakṣatre ucyate
3.6.12.[1]	'pūrvāhṇe yajñopavītī śālāniveśanaṃ samūhayatyupavatsyadbhaktamaśitvā snāto'hatavasanaḥ prayuṅkte', /
3.6.12.[2]	rātrau abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'tvaṣṭā me' 'vāyurenāḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ sambhārān sampātayati /
3.6.12.[3]	vṛkṣaśākhā udakaṃ audumbaraśakalaṃ tāmrachurikā eteṣu pratidravyaṃ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
3.6.12.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.6.13.[1]	tataḥ prabhāte idaṃ karma kriyate /
3.6.13.[2]	'vāyurenāḥ' ityṛcā śākhayodakadhārayā gāḥ parikrāmati //
3.6.14.[1]	prathamajasyekṣukāśakāṇḍyāḥ śakalamavadhāyaudumbareṇāsinā 'lohitena' iti mantreṇa vatsakarṇaṃ chinnati //
3.6.15-16.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yathā cakruḥ' ityṛcā ikṣukāśakāṇḍyā karṇalohitaṃ rasamiśritaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti puṣṭikāmaḥ /
3.6.15-16.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //

3.7.0.[1]	bījavāpanakarma karoti
3.7.1-2.[1]	'ucchrayasva' iti sūktena yavavrīhyādibījamāsādyājyamiśramabhimantrya kṛṣṭe vā kṣetre nivapati trīn muṣṭīn bījasya /
3.7.1-2.[2]	tataḥ pāṃśubhirācchādayati /

3.7.3-4.[1]	uccasthāne gatvā tato'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'abhi tyam' iti caturṛcena sūktenodapātraṃ sampātya kṛṣṇājine somaṃ vicinoti //
3.7.5.[1]	tadudapātraṃ somarasamiśraṃ sārūpavatsam odanaṃ śrapayitvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /

3.7.7.[2]	ekavāraprasūtā gauḥ gṛṣṭiḥ /
3.7.7.[3]	godāmamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti puṣṭyarthī /
3.7.7.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
3.7.8.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'saṃ mā siñcantu' ityṛcā grāmasya sarvodake maiśradhānyaṃ prakṣipya sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
3.7.8.[2]	tato havirudvāsanāntaṃ tantram /
3.7.8.[3]	puṣṭyarthī //

3.7.11.[1]	maunaṃ kṛtvā samidha ādāya gṛhaṃ dṛṣṭvā 'ūrjaṃ bibhrat' iti ṣaḍarcaṃ sūktaṃ japati //
3.7.12.[1]	vāmena hastena samidhaḥ kṛtvā dakṣiṇena śālāvalīkaṃ saṃstabhya japati 'ūrjaṃ bibhrat' iti //

3.7.14.[1]	'yad vadāmi' ityṛcā vāgvisargaṃ karoti //
3.7.15.[1]	tūṣṇīm /

3.7.18.[2]	kecit candramasaṃ dṛṣṭvā japaṃ kurvanti /

3.7.18.[4]	atha vṛṣotsargavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
3.7.19-21.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'indrasya kukṣiḥ' ityṛcā ṛṣabhaṃ sampātya vivāhavat agnipariṇayanaṃ kṛtvā saha vatsatarībhirvisarjayati /
3.7.19-21.[2]	'retodhāyai' iti ṣaṭ /
3.7.19-21.[3]	'etaṃ vo yuvānam' ityṛcābhimantraṇam /
3.7.19-21.[4]	tataḥ prokṣaṇam /
3.7.19-21.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
3.7.19-21.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sāhasraḥ' ityarthasūktena vṛṣabhaṃ sampātya vivāhavat sarvaṃ kṛtvā visarjayati /
3.7.19-21.[7]	'retodhāyai' ityetaiḥ /

3.7.19-21.[9]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /

3.7.19-21.[11]	vṛṣotsargaḥ samāptaḥ /
3.7.19-21.[12]	vṛṣabhapucchaṃ gṛhītvā 'devapitṛṛṣibhyo'haṃ dade ṛṣabham' uccārayati //

3.7.44.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yaṃ tvā pṛṣatī rathaḥ' iti caturbhiḥ raktavarṇāyāḥ goḥ kṣīraudanaṃ śrapayitvā sarvahutaṃ juhoti /

3.7.47.[2]	'brahma jajñānam', 'ambayo yanti' gaṇaḥ /

3.7.47.[33]	ete mantrāḥ pauṣṭikāḥ /
3.7.47.[34]	pauṣṭikānāṃ sarveṣāṃ mantrāṇāṃ havirupadhānam upasthānaṃ vā karoti vikalpena puṣṭikarmaṇāmupadhānopasthānam iti vacanāt /
3.7.47.[35]	puṣṭikarmaṇām upadhānam upasthānaṃ vā karoti puṣṭikāmaḥ /
3.7.47.[36]	upadadhītetyanādeśe ājyaṃ samitpuroḍāśapayaodanapāyasapaśuvrīhiyavatilāḥ dhānāḥ karambhaśaṣkulyaḥ etāni havīṃṣi jānīyāt /
3.7.47.[37]	yatra yatra homaḥ kartavyastatra tatra sarvatropadhānaṃ pauṣṭikānāṃ mantrāṇāṃ kartavyam /
3.7.47.[38]	upasthānaṃ vā /
3.7.47.[39]	gṛhe bahirvā vṛkṣārthaṃ puruṣārthaṃ paśvarthaṃ hastyartham aśvārthaṃ goarthaṃ mahiṣyartham ajāvikādigṛhapaśudhanadhānyamṛgārtham /
3.7.47.[40]	grāme nagare kṣetre bahirvā /
3.7.47.[41]	yatra nityanaimittikakāmyahomastatra sarvatra pauṣṭikahomaḥ kāryaḥ /
3.7.47.[42]	nāsti saṅkhyājātiniyamaḥ puṣṭikarmaṇām /
3.7.47.[43]	yatrānyaprayojanārthaṃ homaḥ na tatra pauṣṭikahomaḥ kāryaḥ /
3.7.47.[44]	sarvatra puṣṭyarthaprayojanam /
3.7.47.[45]	yatrayatra ca saṅkīrṇamātmānaṃ manyate dvijaḥ /
3.7.47.[46]	tatratatra tilairhomo nairṛtirna vidhīyate //
3.7.47.[47]	na tatra nirṛtikarma kuryādityarthaḥ /
3.7.47.[48]	puṣṭikarmaṇāmupadhānopasthānamityarthaḥ /
3.7.47.[49]	salilaiḥ sarvakāmaḥ /
3.7.47.[50]	ājyādi juhoti salilagaṇena /
3.7.47.[51]	tantraṃ yathāsambhavaṃ yojyam /
3.7.47.[52]	sarvaphalakāma ityarthaḥ /
3.7.47.[53]	salilagaṇenopadhānaṃ vā kuryāt /
3.7.47.[54]	upasthānaṃ vā kuryāt sarvakāmaḥ /
3.7.47.[55]	puṣṭiśabdena dravyādilābho dravyādivṛddhiśca puṣṭiśabdenocyate /
3.7.47.[56]	śarīrapuṣṭiśca dhanādipuṣṭiśca bhavati āyuḥpuṣṭiśca /
3.7.47.[57]	atha salilagaṇa ucyate - 'āpo hi ṣṭhāḥ', 'śanno devīḥ', 'brahma jajñānam' 'anāptā ye', 'sahasradhāra eva' , 'asya vāmasya', 'yo rohito vṛṣabha' dvyarcaṃ, 'udasya ketavaḥ', 'mūrdhāham', 'viṣāsahim' iti salilagaṇaḥ /
3.7.47.[58]	asya gaṇasya vā upadhānaṃ ājyādi vā karoti athavā upasthānam /
3.7.47.[59]	putrapaśudhanadhānyaratnagṛhapadātiaśvahastigomahiṣyavivastrajātadravyādihiraṇyabhojanārāmadevapūjādyuccāṭanavaśīkaraṇastambhanajambhanādi sarvaṃ salilagaṇena sidhyati /
3.7.47.[60]	upadhānopasthānaṃ karoti sarvaphalakāmaḥ putrapaśudhānyādisarvakāmaḥ /
3.7.47.[61]	samāptāni pauṣṭikāni /
3.7.47.[62]	tatra ślokaḥ /
3.7.47.[63]	pūrvaṃ nirṛtikarmāṇi sarvapāpāpanuttaye /
3.7.47.[64]	pauṣṭikāni tataḥ paścāt tṛtīye saṃhitāvidhau //

4.1.6.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.6.[3]	jvarabhaiṣajyaṃ atisāre ca atimūtre ca /
4.1.6.[4]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'ado yadavadhāvati' iti sūktena muñjaśiro rajjvā baddhvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.1.6.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.6.[6]	atisāre atimūtre ca bhaiṣajyam //
4.1.7.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti prathamasūktena kṣetramṛttikāmabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.1.7.[2]	atisāre atimūtre ca bhaiṣajyam /
4.1.7.[3]	'ado yad' iti sūktena ākṛtiloṣṭamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.1.7.[4]	atisāre atimūtre ca /
4.1.7.[5]	'vidmā śarasya' iti prathamena valmīkamṛttikāmabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.1.7.[6]	atisāre atimūtre ca /
4.1.7.[7]	'ado yad' iti sūktena valmīkamṛttikāmabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.1.7.[8]	atisāre atimūtre ca //
4.1.8.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti prathamena ghṛtamantryāpānaṃ mrakṣati /
4.1.8.[2]	atisāre bhaiṣajyam /
4.1.8.[3]	'ado yad' iti sūktena ghṛtamabhimantryāpānaṃ vā pralimpati /
4.1.8.[4]	atisāre ca //
4.1.9.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti carmakhalvāmukhamabhimantrya vraṇamukhaṃ dhamati /
4.1.9.[2]	atisāre bhaiṣajyam /
4.1.9.[3]	'ado yad' iti sūktena mukhena khalvā vābhimantryāpānaṃ śiśnaṃ vā nāḍīṃ vā vraṇamukhaṃ dhamati /
4.1.9.[4]	samāptāni jvarātisāra atimūtra aṅganāḍīpravāhe ca bhaiṣajyāni //
4.1.9.[5]	atiduḥkhamūtre duḥkhapurīṣakaraṇe śamanabhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.1.10.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena harītakīṃ karpuraṃ vā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.1.10.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.10.[3]	mūtranirodhe purīṣasya ca //
4.1.11.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena mūṣakamṛttikāmabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.1.11.[2]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena tallagnaṃ laṇḍikātṛṇamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.1.11.[3]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena dadhimathitaṃ pāyayati /
4.1.11.[4]	mūtrapurīṣapratibandhe bhaiṣajyam /
4.1.11.[5]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena jaradindukamabhimantrya piṣṭvā pāyayati /
4.1.11.[6]	mūtrādinirodhe /
4.1.11.[7]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena sūktena kāṣṭhatakṣaṇānyudake kṛtvābhimantrya pāyayati /
4.1.11.[8]	mūtrapurīṣapratibandhe //
4.1.12.[1]	'viṣitaṃ te vastibilam' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ mūṣakamṛttikoparyupaveśyābhimantrayate mūtrapratibandhe /
4.1.12.[2]	'viṣitaṃ te vastibilam' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ pūtīkatṛṇoparyupaveśyābhimantrayate /
4.1.12.[3]	mūtrapratibandhe /
4.1.12.[4]	'viṣitaṃ te vastibilam' iti dvābhyāṃ dadhimathitoparyupaveśya tato'bhimantrayate /
4.1.12.[5]	'viṣitaṃ te vastibilam' iti dvābhyāṃ jaratpramandasyoparyupaveśyābhimantrayate mūtrapratibandhe.'viṣitaṃ te vastibilam' ityṛgbhyāṃ dārutakṣaśakalānāmuparyupaveśya vyādhitamabhimantrayate mūtrapratibandhe /
4.1.12.[6]	'mūtraṃ mucyatām' iti liṅgāt //
4.1.13.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena hastyādiyānaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tato vyādhitamārohayati /
4.1.13.[2]	tato dhāvati vegena mūtramocanakāmaḥ //
4.1.14.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena dhanuḥśaramabhimantrya tato vyādhitaṃ prati śaraṃ kṣipati śīghraḥ //
4.1.15.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena śiśnamabhimantrya carma niḥsphoṭati /
4.1.15.[2]	śiśnaṃ carmaṇo niḥsārayatītyarthaḥ //
4.1.16.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena lohaśalākāmabhimantrya śiśnaṃ praveśayati /
4.1.16.[2]	mūtrapravāhaṃ vidārayati //
4.1.17.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena drughnīṃ jyādhanuṣaṃ jaghane śiśnadeśa ūrdhvaṃ kṛtvā godohanyāmudakaṃ kṛtvā yavānekaviṃśatiṃ prakṣipya tenodakena dhanuṣa upari phalaṃ siñcati /
4.1.17.[2]	yathodakaṃ śiśne patati tathā kāryam //
4.1.18-19.[1]	'vidmā śarasya' iti dvitīyena yavagodhūmavallī padmamūlaṃ pāṭhikā etāni kvāthayitvābhimantrya vyādhitaṃ pāyayati /
4.1.18-19.[2]	samāptāni mūtrapratibandhe duḥkhamūtrakaraṇe duḥkhapurīṣakaraṇa udāvartana udarapūrṇanirodhakaraṇe caitāni bhaiṣajyāni kāryāṇi /
4.1.18-19.[3]	ārogyakāmaḥ //
4.1.18-19.[4]	atha sarvarogabhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.1.20.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ambayo yanti' iti sūktenājyaṃ juhoti /
4.1.20.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.20.[3]	'ambayo yanti' sūktena pālāśaudumbarādyāḥ samidha ādadhāti /
4.1.20.[4]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.1.20.[5]	tantravikalpaḥ hastahomatvāt /
4.1.20.[6]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'vāyoḥ pūtaḥ' iti sūktena tṛcenājyaṃ juhoti /
4.1.20.[7]	uttaratantram /
4.1.20.[8]	sarvabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.1.20.[9]	atha somabhakṣaṇe bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.1.21.[1]	'vāyoḥ pūtaḥ' iti tṛcena pālāśādyāḥ samidhaḥ somarasenāktā ādadhāti /
4.1.21.[2]	somavamane somapāne somābhiṣave ca vyādhyutpanne bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.1.21.[3]	atha bhūtatantrakarmāṇyucyante /
4.1.21.[4]	bhūtapiśācaśaṅkāyāṃ śāntirucyate
4.1.22.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ kukusāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.22.[3]	piśācabhaiṣajyam /
4.1.22.[4]	'abhyādheyānāṃ dhūmaṃ niyacchati' /
4.1.22.[5]	piśācagṛhītaṃ puruṣaṃ dhūmaṃ pāyayati /
4.1.22.[6]	gṛhe grāme vā pattane kṣetre vā devagṛhe vā yatra kvacit piśācaśaṅkāsti tatra homaṃ kṛtvā dhūmaṃ niyataṃ kuryādityarthaḥ /
4.1.22.[7]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena kukusāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[8]	tantravikalpaḥ /
4.1.22.[9]	dhūmabhakṣaṇaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ /
4.1.22.[10]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ kukusāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[11]	dhūmabhakṣaṇaṃ ca /
4.1.22.[12]	'śanno devī pṛśniparṇī' iti sūktena kukusāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[13]	dhūmapānaṃ ca /
4.1.22.[14]	'ā paśyati' iti sūktena kukusāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[15]	dhūmaniyamanam /
4.1.22.[16]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti kukusāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[17]	vikalpena tantre dhūmaṃ karoti /
4.1.22.[18]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktena kukusāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[19]	piśācagṛhītasya dhūmapānaṃ kāryam /
4.1.22.[20]	piśācadoṣānmucyate /
4.1.22.[21]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena kukusāñjuhoti tantre /
4.1.22.[22]	dhūmabhakṣakaraṇaṃ ca /
4.1.22.[23]	piśācadoṣānmucyate /
4.1.22.[24]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ tuṣāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[25]	tantre vā /
4.1.22.[26]	dhūpanaṃ ca /
4.1.22.[27]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena tuṣāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[28]	piśācoccāṭanakāmaḥ /
4.1.22.[29]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ tuṣāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[30]	'śanno devī pṛśniparṇī' iti sūktena tuṣāñ juhoti /
4.1.22.[31]	tantravikalpaḥ /
4.1.22.[32]	dhūpanaṃ puruṣasya /
4.1.22.[33]	piśācoccāṭanakāmaḥ /
4.1.22.[34]	'ā paśyati' sūktena tuṣāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[35]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ tuṣāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[36]	tantravikalpaḥ /
4.1.22.[37]	sarvatra piśācoccāṭanakāmaḥ /
4.1.22.[38]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktena tuṣāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[39]	piśācoccāṭanakāmaḥ /
4.1.22.[40]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena tuṣāñjuhoti /
4.1.22.[41]	piśācoccāṭanakāmaḥ /
4.1.22.[42]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[43]	tantraṃ vā /
4.1.22.[44]	dhūmena puruṣaṃ dhūpayati /
4.1.22.[45]	yasmin sthāne piśācastasmin sthāne homaṃ karoti /
4.1.22.[46]	yathā dhūmo bhavati tathā kuryāt sthāne ca /
4.1.22.[47]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[48]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[49]	'śanno devī pṛśniparṇī' iti sūktena busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[50]	'ā paśyati' iti sūktena busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[51]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[52]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[53]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena busaṃ juhoti /
4.1.22.[54]	'abhyādheyānāṃ dhūmaṃ niyacchati' sarvatra /
4.1.22.[55]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ kāṣṭhaśakalāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[56]	tantravikalpaḥ /
4.1.22.[57]	sarvatra piśācoccāṭanaṃ sarvatra dhūpanaṃ ca /
4.1.22.[58]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktenāvatakṣaṇāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[59]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ śakalāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[60]	'śanno devī pṛśniparṇī' iti śakalāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[61]	'ā paśyati' iti sūktena śakalāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[62]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ śakalāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[63]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti śakalāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[64]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena kāṣṭhaśakalāni juhoti /
4.1.22.[65]	sarvatra tantravikalpaḥ hastahomatvāt /
4.1.22.[66]	dhūmaṃ ca karoti sarvatra /
4.1.22.[67]	puruṣasya sthāne nagare grāme gṛhe vā yatra śaṅkā vidyate tatra dhūmakaraṇaṃ homena /
4.1.22.[68]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ piśācagṛhītaṃ puruṣamanvāha /
4.1.22.[69]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena puruṣamanvāha /
4.1.22.[70]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ puruṣamanvāha /
4.1.22.[71]	'śanno devī' iti sūktena piśācagṛhītamākrośayet /
4.1.22.[72]	'ā paśyati' iti sūktena piśācagṛhītaṃ puruṣamākrośayet /
4.1.22.[73]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ' 'tvayā pūrvaṃ' sūktābhyāṃ piśācamanvāha /
4.1.22.[74]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvānvāha /
4.1.22.[75]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena piśācagṛhītaṃ puruṣamanvāha /
4.1.22.[76]	yadi grāme nagare vā rathyāyāṃ vā kṣetre vā tadā japaṃ kṛtvā piśācanāmagrahaṇaṃ kuryāditi /
4.1.22.[77]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ //
4.1.23.[1]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ karkaṭikāsamidha ādadhāti /
4.1.23.[2]	tantravikalpaḥ /
4.1.23.[3]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena karkaṭikāsamidha ādadhāti /
4.1.23.[4]	tantraṃ vā /
4.1.23.[5]	piśācagṛhītaṃ vā dhūpayati /
4.1.23.[6]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ trapusasamidha ādadhāti /
4.1.23.[7]	piśācoccāṭanakāmaḥ /

4.1.23.[12]	sarvatra sūktādigrahaṇe sūktaṃ pratīyāt /
4.1.23.[13]	ṛgādigrahaṇe ṛcaṃ pratīyāt /
