4.1.23.[61]	anyābhyāṃ śūdrādīnāmuccāṭanaṃ bhavati //
4.1.24.[1]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ khadiraśaṅkūn sapta nava vābhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.24.[2]	bhūmiṃ /
4.1.24.[3]	samām /
4.1.24.[4]	'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti ṛcā /
4.1.24.[5]	nikhananamantraḥ /
4.1.24.[6]	piśācopadrave /
4.1.24.[7]	'niḥsālam' iti sūktena sapta khadiraśaṅkūnabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' ityṛcā /
4.1.24.[8]	piśācabhaye /
4.1.24.[9]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ sapta khadirakīlakānabhimantrya 'akṣyau nividhya' ityṛcā paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.24.[10]	piśācarakṣārtham /
4.1.24.[11]	'śanno devīḥ' iti sūktena ayugmān khādirāñchaṅkūnabhimantrya 'akṣyau ni vidhya' ityṛcā paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.24.[12]	'ā paśyati' iti sūktena sapta kīlakānabhimantrya paścādagneḥ 'akṣyau ni vidhya' ityṛcā nikhanati /
4.1.24.[13]	sarvatra bhūmiṃ samāṃ karoti /
4.1.24.[14]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ sapta kīlakānabhimantrya 'akṣyau ni vidhya' ityṛcā nikhanati agneḥ paścāt /
4.1.24.[15]	piśācabhaye /
4.1.24.[16]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena khādiramayān sapta kīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti ṛcā /
4.1.24.[17]	piśācabhaye //
4.1.25.[1]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ lohakīlakān pañca sapta vābhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' ityṛcā /
4.1.25.[2]	sarvatra kīlakānāṃ nikhananam /
4.1.25.[3]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena lohakīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti /
4.1.25.[4]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ lohakīlakānabhimantrya nikhanati /
4.1.25.[5]	'śanno devīḥ' iti sūktena lohamayakīlakānabhimantrya nikhanati /
4.1.25.[6]	paścādagneḥ sarvatra nikhananam /
4.1.25.[7]	'ā paśyati' iti sūktena lohamayakīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.25.[8]	sarvatra 'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti /
4.1.25.[9]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ pañca sapta vā lohamayakīlakānabhimantrya nikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti /
4.1.25.[10]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktena lohamayakīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' ityṛcā /
4.1.25.[11]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena lohamayakīlakān pañca sapta vābhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' ityṛcā /
4.1.25.[12]	sarvatra nikhananam /
4.1.25.[13]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ tāmramayakīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati 'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti /
4.1.25.[14]	sarvatra piśācāya /
4.1.25.[15]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena tāmramayān kīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.25.[16]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhistāmramayān kīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.25.[17]	'śanno devī pṛśniparṇī' iti sūktena tāmramayān kīlakānabhimantrya nikhanati /
4.1.25.[18]	'ā paśyati' iti tāmramayān kīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.25.[19]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ' iti sūktena tāmrakīlakānabhimantrya 'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.25.[20]	'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktena tāmramayakīlakānabhimantrya 'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti nikhanati /
4.1.25.[21]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti tāmramayakīlakānabhimantrya nikhanati /
4.1.25.[22]	sarvatra piśācabhaye /
4.1.25.[23]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena tāmramayakīlakānabhimantrya paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.25.[24]	'akṣyau ni vidhya' iti sarvatra nikhananam /
4.1.25.[25]	sarvatra paścādagnernikhanati /
4.1.25.[26]	sarvatra piśācabhaye bhaiṣajyāni //
4.1.26.[1]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ taptaśarkarā abhimantrya śayanaṃ vāntarāṇi vā gṛhaṃ vā grāmaṃ vā eṣu sthāneṣu parikiret rakṣobhaye /
4.1.26.[2]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena taptaśarkarā abhimantrya gṛhādiṣu parikirati piśācabhaye /
4.1.26.[3]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ taptaśarkarā abhimantrya śayanarāśipalyāni parikirati /
4.1.26.[4]	yatra piśācabhayaṃ tatra parikirati /
4.1.26.[5]	'śanno devī' iti sūktena taptaśarkarā abhimantrya śayanarāśipalyāni parikirati /
4.1.26.[6]	'ā paśyati' iti taptaśarkarā parikirati /
4.1.26.[7]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ taptaśarkarā abhimantrya śayanarāśipalyāni parikirati piśācabhaye /
4.1.26.[8]	'purastādyukto vaha' iti sūktena taptaśarkarā abhimantrya śayanarāśipalyāni parikirati piśācabhaye /
4.1.26.[9]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena taptaśarkarā abhimantrya śayanarāśipalyāni parikirati piśācabhaye //
4.1.27-29.[1]	amāvāsyāyāmabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā śaramayaṃ barhiḥ stṛṇāti /
4.1.27-29.[2]	sarṣapedhmānāmupasamādhānam /
4.1.27-29.[3]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ sakṛdgṛhītayavasaktūñjuhoti pratyṛcam /
4.1.27-29.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[5]	etasmin tantre yavarāśimadhyānmuṣṭimekāṃ gṛhātvolūkhalena khaṇḍyata apradakṣiṇaṃ piṣyate /
4.1.27-29.[6]	tato vyādhitaṃ sampātya śaṇasūtreṇa jihvāmārjanaṃ karoti tato grahaṇamuktaḥ /
4.1.27-29.[7]	yadi na karoti śaṇena jihvāmārjanaṃ tadā na gato graha iti vijānīyāt /
4.1.27-29.[8]	amāvāsyāyāmājyatantraṃ śarastṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmamupasamāhitamabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'niḥsālām' iti sūktena sakṛdgṛhītān yavānanapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhoti /
4.1.27-29.[9]	mucyate /
4.1.27-29.[10]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[11]	yadi śaṇasūtreṇa jihvāmārjanaṃ karoti tadā gato grahaḥ /
4.1.27-29.[12]	amāvāsyāyāṃ śaramayaṃ barhiḥstṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmaviśiṣṭaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ sakṛdgṛhītān yavānanapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhoti /
4.1.27-29.[13]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[14]	yadi śaṇasūtreṇa jihvāmārjanaṃ karoti tato gato grahaḥ /
4.1.27-29.[15]	amāvāsyāyāṃ śaramayaṃ barhiḥstṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmaviśiṣṭaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ yavānapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhoti /
4.1.27-29.[16]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[17]	yadi śaṇasūtreṇa jihvāmārjanaṃ karoti tato gato grahaḥ /
4.1.27-29.[18]	amāvāsyāyāṃ prātarabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā śaramayaṃ barhiḥstṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmaviśiṣṭaṃ 'śanno devī pṛśniparṇī' iti sūktena yavānanapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhoti /
4.1.27-29.[19]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[20]	śaṇena jihvāmārjanam /
4.1.27-29.[21]	amāvāsyāyāṃ prātaḥ śaramayaṃ barhiḥstṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmaviśiṣṭaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ā paśyati' iti sūktena yavānanapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhoti /
4.1.27-29.[22]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[23]	śaṇena jihvāmārjanam.amāvāsyāyāṃ śaramayaṃ barhiḥstṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmaviśiṣṭaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ sakṛdgṛhītān yavānanapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhotiṭata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[24]	śaṇena jihvāmārjanam /
4.1.27-29.[25]	amāvāsyāyāṃ prātaḥ śaramayaṃ barhiḥstṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmaviśiṣṭamabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktena sakṛdgṛhītān yavānanapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhoti /
4.1.27-29.[26]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[27]	śaṇena jihvāmārjanam /
4.1.27-29.[28]	amāvāsyāyāṃ prātaḥ śaramayaṃ barhiḥstṛtaṃ sarṣapedhmaviśiṣṭamabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena sakṛdgṛhītān yavānanapahatānapratīhāraṃ piṣṭān saktūñjuhoti /
4.1.27-29.[29]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.27-29.[30]	śaṇasūtreṇa jihvāmārjanaṃ karoti /
4.1.27-29.[31]	yadi na karoti tadā na gato grahaḥ /
4.1.27-29.[32]	asādhyo grahaḥ /
4.1.27-29.[33]	asādhyo graha ityarthaḥ //
4.1.27-29.[34]	atha grahābhicāra ucyate /
4.1.27-29.[35]	idaṃ karma avaśyasya grahasya vaśīkaraṇamucyate /
4.1.27-29.[36]	ayamabhicāro'vaśyagrahasya vaśīkaraṇārthaḥ
4.1.30.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ vīriṇatūlamiśramiṅgiḍaṃ pūrṇapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.30.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.1.30.[3]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena vīriṇapuṣpamiśritamiṅgiḍamājyaṃ juhoti pālāśapuṭenājyatantre /
4.1.30.[4]	uttaratantram /
4.1.30.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiḥ vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ palāśapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.30.[6]	uttaratantram /
4.1.30.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'śanno devī pṛśniparṇī' iti sūktena vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.30.[8]	uttaratantram /
4.1.30.[9]	grahasyābhicāro'yam /
4.1.30.[10]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ā paśyati' iti sūktena vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.30.[11]	uttaratantram /
4.1.30.[12]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ vīriṇatūlamiśramiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.30.[13]	uttaratantram /
4.1.30.[14]	piśācasyābhicārakarma /
4.1.30.[15]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktena vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ parṇapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.30.[16]	uttaratantram /
4.1.30.[17]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākena vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhotyājyatantre /
4.1.30.[18]	grahābhicāraḥ samāptaḥ //
4.1.30.[19]	athāsmin gṛhe piśāco'sti vā na veti saṃśaye idaṃ karma ucyate
4.1.31-33.[1]	'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ sarṣapedhmaṃ śaramayaṃ barhirabhimantrya śālāyā upari nidadhāti /
4.1.31-33.[2]	śālāyā upari karoti /
4.1.31-33.[3]	tataḥ prabhāte nirīkṣaṇam /
4.1.31-33.[4]	vikṛte piśācaśaṅkā /
4.1.31-33.[5]	tadā ukto homaḥ /
4.1.31-33.[6]	vīriṇatūlamityādi /
4.1.31-33.[7]	'niḥsālām' iti sūktena tārṣṭāghedhmaṃ śaramayaṃ barhiścābhimantrya śālāyā upari nidadhāti /
4.1.31-33.[8]	yadi tadvikṛtaṃ tadā tadgṛhaṃ piśācagṛhītam /
4.1.31-33.[9]	tadā ukto homaḥ /
4.1.31-33.[10]	vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.31-33.[11]	tantre /
4.1.31-33.[12]	'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhiridhmābarhirabhimantrya śālāyā upari nidadhāti /
4.1.31-33.[13]	dvitīye'hani nirīkṣayet /
4.1.31-33.[14]	barhiṣi vikṛte piśācabhayam /
4.1.31-33.[15]	tatra vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.31-33.[16]	'śanno devī' itīdhmābarhirabhimantrya śālāyāmāsajati /
4.1.31-33.[17]	aparedyurvikṛte piśācato rugiti /
4.1.31-33.[18]	tato vīriṇatūlamiśritamiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.31-33.[19]	tantre /
4.1.31-33.[20]	'ā paśyati' iti sūktenedhmābarhiḥ śālāyāmāsajati /
4.1.31-33.[21]	aparedyurvikṛte piśācato rugiti /
4.1.31-33.[22]	tata idhmābarhiḥ śālāyā gṛhītvā tena tantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā vīriṇatūlamiśramiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.31-33.[23]	'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ idhmābarhirabhimantrya śālāyāmāsajati /
4.1.31-33.[24]	aparedyurvikṛte piśācato rugiti /
4.1.31-33.[25]	vīriṇatūlamiśramiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti tenaiva sūktena /
4.1.31-33.[26]	'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktenedhmābarhirabhimantrya śālāyāmāsajati /
4.1.31-33.[27]	aparedyurvikṛte piśācato rugiti /
4.1.31-33.[28]	tatra vīriṇatūlamiśramiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.31-33.[29]	'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākenedhmābarhiḥ śālāyāmāsajati /
4.1.31-33.[30]	aparedyurvikṛte piśācato rugiti /
4.1.31-33.[31]	tantraṃ kṛtvā tenānuvākena vīriṇatūlamiśramiṅgiḍaṃ prapuṭena juhoti /
4.1.31-33.[32]	piśācagrahābhicāraḥ //
4.1.34.[1]	vaiśravaṇāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudakamabhimantrya tamācāmayati samprokṣati ca /
4.1.34.[2]	vaiśravaṇāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'niḥsālām' iti sūktenodakamabhimantryācāmayati samprokṣati ca vyādhitam /
4.1.34.[3]	piśācagraharakṣākāmaḥ /
4.1.34.[4]	vaiśravaṇāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'arāyakṣayaṇam' iti tisṛbhirudakamabhimantryācāmayati samprokṣati ca piśācagṛhītaṃ puruṣam /
4.1.34.[5]	vaiśravaṇāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'śanno devī' iti sūktenodakamabhimantryācāmayati samprokṣati ca /
4.1.34.[6]	piśācarakṣārtham /
4.1.34.[7]	vaiśravaṇāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'ā paśyati' iti sūktenodakamabhimantryācāmayati samprokṣati ca vyādhitaṃ mānuṣam /
4.1.34.[8]	vaiśravaṇāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'tāntsatyaujāḥ', 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāmudakamabhimantrya vyādhitamācāmayati samprokṣati ca /
4.1.34.[9]	piśācabhaye /
4.1.34.[10]	vaiśravaṇāyāñjaliṃ kṛtvā 'purastādyuktaḥ' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya vyādhitamācāmayati samprokṣati ca /
4.1.34.[11]	piśācabhaye rakṣākāmaḥ /
4.1.34.[12]	vaiśravaṇāyāñjaliṃ kṛtvā 'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākenodakamabhimantryācāmayati samprokṣati ca vyādhitam /
4.1.34.[13]	piśācabhaye rakṣākāmaḥ /
4.1.34.[14]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
4.1.34.[15]	piśācagṛhītaṃ manuṣyam anvārabdhe sarvatra homaḥ kāryaḥ /
4.1.34.[16]	bhaiṣajyakarma ca /
4.1.34.[17]	gṛhe prayogaḥ //
4.1.34.[18]	rātrikarmāṇy ucyante
4.1.35-36.[1]	rātrau 'stuvānam', 'idaṃ haviḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ ulmuke dve abhimantrya parasparaṃ ghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[2]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena dakṣiṇena prakrāmati padāni dadāti /
4.1.35-36.[3]	piśācabhaye /
4.1.35-36.[4]	rātrau 'niḥsālām' iti sūktena ulmuke abhimantrya parasparaṃ ghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[5]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena dakṣiṇena prakrāmati /
4.1.35-36.[6]	piśācabhaye /
4.1.35-36.[7]	rātrau 'arāyakṣayaṇam' ityulmuke abhimantrya parasparaṃ ghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[8]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena padāni prakrāmati /
4.1.35-36.[9]	rātrau 'śanno devī' ityulmuke abhimantrya parasparaṃ ghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[10]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti padāni dadāti /
4.1.35-36.[11]	rātrau 'ā paśyati' ityulmukadvayaṃ parasparaṃ sarvatrābhimantraṇānte saṅghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[12]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā padāni prakrāmati /
4.1.35-36.[13]	rātrau 'tāntsatyaujāḥ' 'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktābhyāmulmuke abhimantrya saṅghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[14]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena padāni dadāti /
4.1.35-36.[15]	piśācarakṣārtham /
4.1.35-36.[16]	rātrau 'purastādyuktaḥ' iti ulmuke abhimantrya saṅghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[17]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā padāni prakrāmati /
4.1.35-36.[18]	sarvabhūtagrahavināśanaḥ /
4.1.35-36.[19]	gatena gaṇavikalpena homaḥ /
4.1.35-36.[20]	brahmarākṣasasyāpi śāntiḥ /
4.1.35-36.[21]	rātrauḥ 'rakṣohaṇam' ityanuvākenolmuke abhimantrya parasparaṃ saṅghṛṣyati /
4.1.35-36.[22]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā padāni prakrāmati /
4.1.35-36.[23]	samāptāni rātrikarmāṇi /
4.1.35-36.[24]	piśācarākṣasabhūtāpsaraḥpretayakṣagandharvā grahāśca /
4.1.35-36.[25]	ye'nye'pi kṣudrabrāhmaṇajātikāḥ kṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrādayo grahāḥ sarve ebhiḥ karmabhistuṣyanti /
4.1.35-36.[26]	rākṣasagrahaprakaraṇaṃ bhūtatantraṃ samāptam //
4.1.35-36.[27]	atha jalodarabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.1.37.[1]	'ayaṃ devānām' iti sūktena ghaṭe darbhapiñjulīḥ prakṣipyaikaviṃśatigṛhatṛṇāni ca prakṣipya taṃ ghaṭam abhimantrya tato vyādhitaṃ siñcati /
4.1.37.[2]	tato mārjanaṃ ca /
4.1.37.[3]	darbhatrayam ekatra baddhaṃ piñjūlīty ucyate /
4.1.37.[4]	samāptaṃ jalodarabhaiṣajyam /
4.1.37.[5]	abhyāsena karmasiddhiḥ /
4.1.37.[6]	dinedine kuryāt jalodaranāśanārtham //
4.1.37.[7]	bhaiṣajye prathamā kaṇḍikā samāptā //25 //
4.2.0.[1]	atha vātapittaśleṣmaṇi bhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.2.1.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena māṃsabhedo'bhimantrya pāyayati vātavikāre /
4.2.1.[2]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena madhvabhimantrya pāyayati śleṣmavikāre /
4.2.1.[3]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena ghṛtamabhimantrya pāyayati vātapittasahavikāre /
4.2.1.[4]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena tailamabhimantrya pāyayati vātaśleṣmavikāre /
4.2.1.[5]	samāptaṃ vātapittaśleṣmabhaiṣajyam //
4.2.1.[6]	atikāse śīrṣaktau śirovedanāyāṃ ca karmāṇyucyante
4.2.2.[1]	vyādhitaśiro mauñjaveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā vāmena hastena pavanaṃ lājasahitaṃ gṛhītvā /
4.2.2.[2]	dakṣiṇena hastena tān lājān pragṛhya 'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena lājān prakiran vrajati vyādhideśaṃ yāvat /
4.2.2.[3]	tatraiva muñjapraśnalājāpavanānāṃ prakṣepaḥ //
4.2.3-4.[1]	vāmena hastena pavanaṃ mauñjendukaṃ ca gṛhītvā dakṣiṇena hastena jyāṃ drughnīṃ gṛhītvā vyādhitamagre kṛtvā //
4.2.5.[1]	yatra vyādhirutpannastatra sthāne gatvā 'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā mauñjapraśnaṃ pavanaṃ ca prakṣipati vyādhitaḥ //
4.2.6-7.[1]	tatra sthāne tūṣṇīṃ jyāṃ prakṣipati //
4.2.8.[1]	vātajvare kaṭibhaṅge śirīroge ca vātagulme vātavikāre ca sarvaroge dhanurvāte'ṅgakampane vāte śarīrabhaṅge sarvavātavikāre bhaiṣajyam /
4.2.8.[2]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena ghṛtamabhimantrya nāsikānastaṃ dadāti /
4.2.8.[3]	śiroroge vātabhaṅge //
4.2.9-10.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena pañcaparvaveṇudaṇḍaṃ lalāṭe saṃstabhya japati /
4.2.9-10.[2]	śiroroge kaṭibhaṅge vā vātagulme vā vātavikāre ca /
4.2.9-10.[3]	liṅgyupatāpaḥ samāptaḥ //
4.2.9-10.[4]	atha lohite vahati śarīramadhye bahiśca śastraghāte pāṣāṇalakuṭeṣṭakādyabhighāte karmāṇyucyante /
4.2.9-10.[5]	pañcaparvaveṇudaṇḍaṃ rudhiravahanasthāne dattvā 'amūryāḥ' iti sūktaṃ japati /
4.2.9-10.[6]	rudhirapravāhe bhaiṣajyam /
4.2.9-10.[7]	'amūryāḥ' iti sūktena rathyāyāḥ pāṃsūn gṛhītvābhimantrya rudhiravraṇe vikirati /
4.2.9-10.[8]	'amūryāḥ' iti sūktena sikatā abhimantrya vyādhideśe kirati //
4.2.11.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'amūryāḥ' iti sūktenārmakapālikāṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.2.11.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
4.2.12.[1]	'amūryāḥ' iti sūktenārmakapālikāmabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.2.12.[2]	armakapālikā śuṣkapaṅkamṛttikā /
4.2.12.[3]	strīrajaso'tipravartane bhaiṣajyaṃ rudhirapravāhe ca //
4.2.13.[1]	'amūryāḥ' iti sūktena catvāri dūrvāgrāṇi piṣṭvā taiḥ saha dadhipalalamāṃsādyāloḍya tato'bhimantrya pāyayati /
4.2.13.[2]	rudhirapravāhe śarīramadhye śastrādyabhighāte bahiśca śoṇitavahane gudavahane mukhavahane nāsikārudhiravahane śiro'ṅgulyādirudhirapravāhe ca /
4.2.13.[3]	rudhirapravahane bhaiṣajyāni samāptāni //
4.2.13.[4]	atha hṛdroge kāmale ca bhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.2.14.[1]	'anu sūryam' iti raktavṛṣabharomamiśramudakamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.2.14.[2]	kāmale hṛdroge ca bhaiṣajyam //
4.2.15.[1]	'anu sūryam' iti sūktena raktavṛṣabhapṛṣṭha udakamānīya tato'bhimantryācāmayati //
4.2.16.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'anu sūryam' iti sūktena go raktacarmachidramaṇiṃ godugdhe dattvā taṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti //
4.2.17.[1]	dugdhaṃ ca pāyayati /
4.2.17.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.17.[3]	kāmale hṛdroge ca liṅgyupatāpaḥ //
4.2.18.[1]	haridraudanaṃ vyādhitasya bhojanaṃ dattvā tasyocchiṣṭaṃ cānucchiṣṭaṃ caikatra kṛtvā tena codvartanaṃ kṛtvā śiraḥprabhṛtyārabhya yāvatpādau /
4.2.18.[2]	tato vyādhitaṃ ca khaṭvāyāmupaveśya khaṭvāyā adhastāt /
4.2.18.[3]	śukaḥ kāṣṭhaśuko gopītilakā caite trayaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ /
4.2.18.[4]	savyajaṅghāyāṃ haritasūtreṇa baddhvā khaṭvāyā adhastād badhnāti /
4.2.18.[5]	tato 'anu sūryam' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya vyādhitaṃ snāpayati /
4.2.18.[6]	kāmale hṛdroge ca //
4.2.19.[1]	'anu sūryam' iti sūktena manthamabhimantrya prapādya prayacchati /
4.2.19.[2]	sarvatra gṛhadvāre'gre vyādhitaṃ kṛtvā tamagre praveśya svayaṃ praviśya tato bhaktamabhimantrya tato vyādhitāya prayacchati /
4.2.19.[3]	sarvatra yatra yatra 'prayacchati' śabdastatra tatraivaṃ boddhavyam //
4.2.20.[1]	'anu sūryam' iti sūktena śukaṃ vadantamabhimantrayet /
4.2.20.[2]	'anu sūryam' iti sūktena kāṣṭhaśukaṃ vadantamabhimantrayet /
4.2.20.[3]	'anu sūryam' iti sūktena gopītilakāṃ pakṣiṇīṃ yatra kutracid dṛṣṭvā vadantīṃ tatrābhimantrayed vyādhitaḥ /
4.2.20.[4]	kāmale ca vyādhau //
4.2.21.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'anu sūryam' iti sūktena vṛṣabhahṛdayalomabhirlākṣāraktaiḥ suvarṇaveṣṭitaṃ maṇiṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya vyādhitāya badhnāti /
4.2.21.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.21.[3]	sarvatra yatra bahūni karmāṇi vihitāni tatraikaṃ kuryād dve vā kuryāt sarvāṇi vā kuryāt /
4.2.21.[4]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
4.2.21.[5]	apasmāravismayahṛdrogakāmalakarohiṇakāni bhaiṣajyāni samāptāni //
4.2.21.[6]	atha śvetakuṣṭhabhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.2.22.[1]	śvetakuṣṭhaṃ gomayena praghṛṣya yāvallohitaṃ dṛṣṭvā 'naktañjātā', 'suparṇo jātaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ bhṛṅgarājaharindrendravāruṇī nīlikāpuṣpā etāḥ pañca piṣṭvābhimantrya kuṣṭhaṃ pralimpati /
4.2.22.[2]	tisṛṇāṃ vā catasṛṇāṃ vauṣadhīnāṃ grahaṇam //
4.2.23.[1]	palitanāśe tacca /
4.2.23.[2]	palitāni chittvā ghṛṣṭvālimpati //
4.2.23.[3]	atha mārutānyucyante
4.2.24.[1]	'naktañjātā', 'suparṇo jātaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ maruto yajate yathā varuṇaṃ pākayajñavidhānena /
4.2.24.[2]	śvetapalite śvetakuṣṭhe ca /
4.2.24.[3]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'naktañjātā', 'suparṇo jātaḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ sūktābhyāṃ kṛṣṇāyā gorājyaṃ juhoti /
4.2.24.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.24.[5]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'naktañjātā', 'suparṇo jātaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ kāsadividhuvakavetasā oṣadhīrekatra kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya tata udakamadhye praveśyādhomukhaṃ pātraṃ ninayati /
4.2.24.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.24.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'naktañjātā', 'suparṇo jātaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ kāsādyoṣadhīrudake kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
4.2.24.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.24.[9]	'naktañjātā', 'suparṇo jātaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ śvaśiro meṣaśiro mānuṣakeśarajjvā jaradupānahau ca vaṃśadvayāgre prabadhya yodhayati dhārayatītyarthaḥ /
4.2.24.[10]	palitanāśe śvetakuṣṭhe ca bhaiṣajyāni /
4.2.24.[11]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'naktañjātā', 'suparṇo jātaḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ sūktābhyāmudakaṃ sampātya tenāmapātraṃ prasicya tato'śmānaṃ nidadhāti /
4.2.24.[12]	tata āmapātramaśmānaṃ ca tripāde śikye nidadhāti /
4.2.24.[13]	tato'psu kṣipati /
4.2.24.[14]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.24.[15]	mārutāni karmāṇi samāptāni /
4.2.24.[16]	māruteṣu karmasu sarvatra mārutakṣīraudanaṃ mārutaśṛtaṃ mārutaiḥ paristīrya mārutena sruveṇa mārutenājyeneti bhavati /
4.2.24.[17]	samāptāni kuṣṭhabhaiṣajyāni /
4.2.24.[18]	śvetapalitanāśanaṃ durbhaganāśanaṃ ca //
4.2.24.[19]	atha jvarabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.2.25.[1]	nityajvare velājvare satatajvare ekāntarajvare cāturthakajvare śītajvare caturjvare ca 'yadagniḥ' iti sūktena lohakuṭhāramabhimantryāgnau tāpayati /
4.2.25.[2]	tato 'yadagniḥ' iti japitvā taṃ kuṭhāramuṣṇodakamadhye kvāthayati /
4.2.25.[3]	tato 'yadagniḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā tenodakena vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.2.25.[4]	ācamanaṃ tūṣṇīṃ mārjanaṃ ca /
4.2.25.[5]	jvarabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.2.25.[6]	athodvegavināśabhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.2.26.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'upa prāgāt' iti sūktena śuklavīriṇeṣīkācatuṣṭayenobhayataḥ pratyuṣṭamekatra baddhvā maṇiṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti puṇyāhānte /
4.2.26.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.26.[3]	udvegabhaiṣajyam //
4.2.27.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'upa prāgāt' iti sūktena trividagdhaṃ śuklavīraṇakāṇḍamaṇiṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.2.27.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.27.[3]	udvegabhaiṣajyam //
4.2.28.[1]	'upa prāgāt' iti sūktenolmukadvayamabhimantrya gharṣayet /
4.2.28.[2]	rātrau uṣākāle vaitat karma /
4.2.28.[3]	tataḥ prabhāte 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena dakṣiṇena pādena prakrāmati iti svastyayanam /
4.2.28.[4]	vṛddhabālayuvastrīpuruṣāṇāmakasmādudvegaḥ pralāpo vā bhavettadaitat kuryāt /
4.2.28.[5]	samāptānyudvegabhaiṣajyāni //
4.2.28.[6]	gandharvarākṣasāpsarobhūtagrahādiṣu bhaiṣajyāny ucyante
4.2.29.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'divyo gandharvaḥ' iti sūktena ghṛtāktāḥ sarvauṣadhīrjuhoti /
4.2.29.[2]	homaśeṣeṇa vyādhitaṃ mrakṣayati /
4.2.29.[3]	uttaratantram /
4.2.29.[4]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'imaṃ me agne' iti caturṛcenājyamiśrāḥ sarvauṣadhīrjuhoti /
4.2.29.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.29.[6]	tantre homaśeṣeṇa vyādhitaṃ mrakṣayati /
4.2.29.[7]	gandharvagrahādibhaiṣajyam //
4.2.30.[1]	catuṣpathe vyādhitaṃ kṛtvā tasya śirasi darbheṇḍukaṃ kṛtvā tasyopari kapālamagnipūrṇaṃ prajvālitaṃ kṛtvā tatra prajvālite'gnau 'divyo gandharvaḥ' iti sūktena ghṛtāktāḥ sarvauṣadhīrjuhoti /
4.2.30.[2]	catuṣpathe ca śirasi darbheṇḍve'ṅgārakapāle prajvālite'gnau 'imaṃ me agne' iti catasṛbhirājyenāktāḥ sarvauṣadhīrjuhoti pratyṛcaṃ śirasi home na tantram //
4.2.31.[1]	vyādhitasya vallaṇikāṃ sarvauṣadhisahitāṃ haste kṛtvā nadyudakasammukhaṃ praveśya tato'vagāhayati /
4.2.31.[2]	'davyo gndharvaḥ' iti sūktena sarvauṣadhīrudakamadhye vapati kartā /
4.2.31.[3]	'divyo gandharvaḥ' iti sūktena paścāt sthito vyādhitaṃ siñcati //
4.2.32.[1]	tato mṛnmaya āmapātre homaśeṣaḥ sarvauṣadhīḥ kṛtvā pakṣiṇo yasmin vṛkṣe vasanti tatra tripāde śikye kṛtvā badhnāti /
4.2.32.[2]	gandharvayakṣarākṣasabhaiṣajyam /
4.2.32.[3]	'imaṃ me agne' iti sūktena nadīmadhye vallaṇikāyāṃ sarvauṣadhīrghṛtāktā juhoti pratyṛcam /
4.2.32.[4]	tataḥ kartā tamavasiñcati vyādhitam 'imaṃ me' iti catasṛbhiḥ /
4.2.32.[5]	paścādāmapātra opyāsicya mauñje tripāde vayoniveśane vṛkṣe badhnāti /
4.2.32.[6]	rakṣograhe yakṣagrahe gandharvagrahe'psarograhe rājase grahe tāmase grahe grahabhaiṣajyāni samāptāni //
4.2.32.[7]	atha laukike śāpe vaidike śāpe ca strīṇāmākrośe puruṣāṇāṃ ca bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.2.33-40.[1]	sarvasmin saṃhitāvidhikarmaṇi pradhānakarmamadhye uttarataḥ udakumbhamāsthāpya tenodakena 'hiraṇyavarṇāḥ' iti sūktenābhimantritena kārayitābhiṣecayet sarvatra medhājananādikarmasu /
4.2.33-40.[2]	tataḥ paścānmaṇibandhanādi karma kuryāt /
4.2.33-40.[3]	bhaiṣajyeṣvabhiṣekaṃ na kuryāt /
4.2.33-40.[4]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'aghadviṣṭā devajātā' iti sūktena yavamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya punaḥ sūktaṃ japitvā badhnāti /
4.2.33-40.[5]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.33-40.[6]	laukika ākrośe vaidike ca brāhmaṇasya śāpe krūracakṣurdṛṣṭinipāte ca piśācarākṣasādiṣu bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.2.33-40.[7]	atha rakṣograhe bhaiṣajyam ucyate /
4.2.33-40.[8]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'śaṃ no devī pṛśniparṇī' iti sūktena pṛśniparṇīṃ sampātyābhimantrya ghṛṣṭvā punaḥ sūktaṃ japitvā vyādhitaṃ pralimpati /
4.2.33-40.[9]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.33-40.[10]	pāpagṛhīte ca strīgarbhastrāve ca mṛtāpatyāyāṃ ca kravyādagṛhīte ca piśācagṛhīte ca rakṣomayabhaiṣajyam samāptam //
4.2.33-40.[11]	atha rājayakṣmādibhaiṣajyamucyate /
4.2.33-40.[12]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'varaṇo vārayātā' iti tṛcena varaṇavṛkṣakāṣṭhamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya punaḥ sūktaṃ japitvā badhnāti /
4.2.33-40.[13]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.33-40.[14]	rājayakṣmādiṣūgravyādhiṣu śvetodumbarakuṣṭhādyaṣṭādaśajātiṣu jvarādisarvarogeṣu bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.2.33-40.[15]	atha vātavikāre bhaiṣajyamucyate /
4.2.33-40.[16]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'pippalī kṣiptabheṣajī' iti sūktena pippaladravyaṃ sampātyābhimantrya punaḥ sūktaṃ japitvāśayati /
4.2.33-40.[17]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.33-40.[18]	sarvatra /
4.2.33-40.[19]	vātavikāre dhanurvāte vātagulme vātaśūle kṣiptavātapradoṣe karmakṛte vāta utpanne sarvavātavikāre bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.2.33-40.[20]	jalodarabhaiṣajyamucyate /
4.2.33-40.[21]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vidradhasya balāsasya' iti tṛcena sūktena vyādhitasya mūrdhni sampātānānayati /
4.2.33-40.[22]	abhimantraṇaṃ ca /
4.2.33-40.[23]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.33-40.[24]	jalodarabhaiṣajyam /
4.2.33-40.[25]	sarvavyādhivisarpaṇe hṛdayāmaye vā jalodare ca eteṣāṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.2.33-40.[26]	'vidradhasya' iti sūktena pālāśaśakalaṃ caturaṅgulamānaṃ piṣṭvābhimantrya punaḥ sūktaṃ japitvā vyādhitaṃ limpati /
4.2.33-40.[27]	sarvavyādhivisarpaṇe prakope ca balāse cāntrādivisarpaṇe cākṣivisarpaṇe ca karṇavyādhivisarpaṇe hṛdayāmaye cājñātarājayakṣmaṇi ca /
4.2.33-40.[28]	eteṣāṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.2.33-40.[29]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yā babhravaḥ' iti sūktena daśavṛkṣaśakalāni lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ maṇiṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya punaḥ sūktaṃ japitvā badhnāti /
4.2.33-40.[30]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam //
4.2.33-40.[31]	atha kṣetriyavyādhibhaiṣajyamucyate
4.2.41.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'udagātām' iti sūktena udakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya vyādhitaṃ gṛhād bahiḥ kṛtvāplāvayati /
4.2.41.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.41.[3]	kṣetriyo vyādhirliṅgī pitṛpāramparyāgataḥ kṣetriyo rogaḥ /
4.2.41.[4]	kuṣṭhakṣayarogo grahaṇīdoṣaḥ sarvaśarīre visphoṭakaraktadoṣādiḥ kṣetriyaḥ //
4.2.42.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'apeyaṃ rātrī' ityṛcā ghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya gṛhādbahirāplāvayati /
4.2.42.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.2.42.[3]	apararātra etat karma kuryāt kṣetriyavyādhau //
4.2.43.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'babhrorarjunakāṇḍasya' ityṛcārjunakāṣṭhaṃ yavabusaṃ tilapiñjikāṃ caikatra trīṇi baddhvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.2.43.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.43.[3]	kṣetriyavyādhau /
4.2.43.[4]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'babhrorarjuna' ityṛcākṛtiloṣṭaṃ jīvakoṣaṇyāṃ baddhvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.2.43.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.43.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'babhrorarjuna' ityṛcā valmīkamṛttikāṃ carmajīvakoṣaṇyāṃ baddhvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.2.43.[7]	tata uttaratantram /
4.2.43.[8]	ekasmin vyādhau sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
4.2.43.[9]	jīvataḥ paśoścarma jīvakoṣaṇītyucyate /
4.2.43.[10]	ajāyāścarmāvervāśvāyā vā carmagrahaṇam /
4.2.43.[11]	mātṛpitṛvargādāyātaḥ kaulaḥ kulabhavaḥ /
4.2.43.[12]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ //
4.2.43.[13]	bhaiṣajyeṣu dvitīyā kaṇḍikā //
4.3.1.[1]	'namaste lāṅgalebhyaḥ' ityṛcodakaghaṭamabhimantrya vṛṣabhayuktasya halasyādhastāt kṛtvā vyādhitaṃ tato'bhiṣiñcati /
4.3.1.[2]	kṣetriyasya bhaiṣajyam //
4.3.2-4.[1]	tasmin garte vyādhitamupaveśyācāmayati /
4.3.2-4.[2]	uttaratantram /
4.3.2-4.[3]	kṣetriyabhaiṣajyam /
4.3.2-4.[4]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'namaḥ sanisrasākṣebhyaḥ' ityṛcodakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantryottarasampātān jaradgartaḥ ānayati /
4.3.2-4.[5]	śālātṛṇasahite garte vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.3.2-4.[6]	ācamanaṃ ca /
4.3.2-4.[7]	yatra kvacit snānaṃ tatra sarvatrācamanam /
4.3.2-4.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
4.3.2-4.[9]	yatra yatra snānaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ ca tatra sarvatra bhaiṣajyeṣu śiraḥprabhati mārjanaṃ kuryāt yāvat pādau /
4.3.2-4.[10]	samāptaṃ kṣetriyasya bhaiṣajyam //
4.3.2-4.[11]	atha brahmagrahe bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.3.5.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'daśavṛkṣa' iti sūktena vṛkṣavikalpena palāśādidaśavṛkṣaśakalāni gṛhītvā lākṣāhiraṇyena veṣṭitaṃ maṇiṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.3.5.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.3.5.[3]	brahmagrahe bhaiṣajyam //
4.3.6.[1]	daśa brāhmaṇā atharvāṅgirasaḥ suhṛdo 'daśavṛkṣa' iti sūktaṃ japanto vyādhitaśarīramabhimṛśanti /
4.3.6.[2]	sarvagrahe brahmagrahe /
4.3.6.[3]	grahabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.3.7.[1]	catuṣpathe gatvābhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'kṣetriyāttvā' iti sūktenodakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya kāmpīlaśakalāni vyādhitaparvaṇi dattvā piñjūlīr ghaṭe prakṣipya tato'bhiṣiñcati /
4.3.7.[2]	tata ācamanam /
4.3.7.[3]	uttaratantram /
4.3.7.[4]	kṣetriyagrahe //
4.3.8.[1]	'kṣetriyāttvā' iti sūktenodakaghaṭaṃ saha piñjūlībhirabhimantrya catuṣpathe vyādhitaṃ kṛtvāvasiñcati /
4.3.8.[2]	kṣetriye grahe kāmpīlaśakalairbandhayitvā /
4.3.8.[3]	kṣetriyabhaiṣajyam /
4.3.8.[4]	samāptāni kṣetriyabhaiṣajyāni //
4.3.8.[5]	udakatṛṣākrāntabhaiṣajyam ucyate
4.3.9-11.[1]	udita āditye prabhāte pṛṣṭhasaṃhitāvupaveśya dvau puruṣau /
4.3.9-11.[2]	prāṅmukhaṃ vyādhitaṃ pratyaṅmukhamavyādhitaṃ vaitasaśākhāsūpaveśya vaitase camase saktūdakaṃ prakṣipya vaitasaśalākābhyāṃ manthaṃ nirmathya tṛṣṇāgṛhītasya śirasi manthamupamathya 'pārthivasya' iti sūktena camasamabhimantrya tṛṣitāya prayacchati yasya vyādhirbhavati //
4.3.12.[1]	'pārthivasya' iti sūktenāpsūdakamabhimantryoddhṛtya pāyayati /
4.3.12.[2]	tṛṣārte bhaiṣajyam //
4.3.13.[1]	'savāsinau' iti sūktena manthamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.3.13.[2]	vyādhitāvyādhitāvekavastraparihitau santau /
4.3.13.[3]	tṛṣārtabhaiṣajyāni samāptāni //
4.3.13.[4]	aruṣodaragaṇḍulabhaiṣajyāny ucyante
4.3.14.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'indrasya yā mahī' iti sūktena kṛṣṇacaṇakān ghṛtamiśrāñjuhoti /
4.3.14.[2]	tantravikalpaḥ //
4.3.15.[1]	'indrasya yā mahī' iti sūktena govālān /
4.3.15.[2]	citrite śare savyaṃ pariveṣṭya pāṣāṇena cūrṇayati //
4.3.16.[1]	tataḥ sūktaṃ japitvāgnau pratapati //
4.3.17.[1]	tataḥ sūktāntenāgnāvādadhāti //
4.3.18.[1]	'indrasya yā mahī' iti sūktena savye haste pāṃsūn kṛtvā dakṣiṇena vimṛjya dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ sthitaḥ sūktaṃ japitvā vyādhitasyopari kirati /
4.3.18.[2]	aruṣīgaṇḍulakānāṃ bhaiṣajyam //
4.3.19.[1]	'indrasya yā mahī' iti sūktena pāṃsūn mardayati hastābhyāṃ vyādhitaḥ //
4.3.20.[1]	'indrasya yā mahī' iti sūktena pālāśaudumbarādyāḥ samidha ādadhāti /
4.3.20.[2]	samāptā udarakṛmaya udaragaṇḍulakāśca dṛṣṭakṛmayaśca teṣāṃ bhaiṣajyam //
4.3.20.[3]	atha gokṛmibhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.3.21-23.[1]	prātaḥ 'udyannādityaḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā gonāmoccārayitvā yasya krimayaḥ /
4.3.21-23.[2]	'te hatāḥ' iti mantreṇa darbhairāhanti krimīṇāṃ mukham //
4.3.24.[1]	etanmadhyandine kuryāt //
4.3.25.[1]	ādityasammukho'parāhṇe etat /
4.3.25.[2]	trikāle karmasamāptiḥ /
4.3.25.[3]	gonāmagrahaṇam 'asau' iti sthāne //
4.3.26.[1]	'udyannādityaḥ' iti sūktena ghṛtamiśrān kṛṣṇacaṇakāñjuhoti /
4.3.26.[2]	kṛmibhaiṣajyam /
4.3.26.[3]	'udyannādityaḥ' iti sūktena kalmāṣaṃ śaraṃ govālaveṣṭitaṃ dhārayati /
4.3.26.[4]	tataḥ pāṣāṇena cūrṇayati /
4.3.26.[5]	tataḥ sūktena pratapati /
4.3.26.[6]	tataḥ sūktena japitvāgnāvādadhāti juhotītyarthaḥ /
4.3.26.[7]	kṛmibhaiṣajyam /
4.3.26.[8]	'udyannādityaḥ' iti sūktena pāṃsūnabhimantrya vāme haste kṛtvā dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ pāṃsunā kṛmivraṇaṃ mardayati /
4.3.26.[9]	'udyann ādityaḥ' iti sūktena palāśavṛkṣādisamidha ādadhāti /
4.3.26.[10]	samāptaṃ sarvakṛmibhaiṣajyam manuṣyagajahastyaśvādiyūkālikṣādiṣu kṛmibhaiṣajyam //
4.3.26.[11]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam ucyate
4.3.27-28.[1]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā vyādhitaṃ parvasu baddhvā 'akṣībhyāṃ te' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātya tataḥ punaḥ sūktaṃ japitvāvasicya vyādhitasya parvagranthīn vimuñcati /
4.3.27-28.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.3.27-28.[3]	samāptam akṣiroganāsikākarṇamūlaśirojihvāgrīvārājayakṣmādisarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.3.27-28.[4]	'akṣībhyāṃ te' iti sūktenābhimantrayate vyādhitam /
4.3.27-28.[5]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.3.27-28.[6]	atha kṣetriyavyādhibhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.3.29.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'hariṇasya' iti sūktena hariṇaśṛṅgamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.3.29.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.3.29.[3]	kṣetriyabhaiṣajyam /
4.3.29.[4]	'hariṇasya' iti sūktena hariṇaśṛṅgeṇa sahodakamabhimantrya pāyayatyācāmayati ca /
4.3.29.[5]	athoṣākāla etat karma /
4.3.29.[6]	hariṇavarma śaṅkudhānaṃ prajvālyodake prakṣipya tato 'hariṇasya' ityabhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.3.29.[7]	mārjanamācamanaṃ ca /
4.3.29.[8]	kṣetriyabhaiṣajyam //
4.3.30.[1]	'hariṇasya' iti sūktena yavāñjuhoti pratyṛcaṃ rāśeraparimitān madhyāt sakṛd grāhyā yavā ityarthaḥ /
4.3.30.[2]	kṣetriyabhaiṣajyam //
4.3.31.[1]	'hariṇasya' iti sūktena bhaktamabhimantrya bhojane prapādya prayacchati /
4.3.31.[2]	samāptaṃ kṣetriyabhaiṣajyam /
4.3.31.[3]	bālarogagṛhīte ca //
4.3.31.[4]	maithunadoṣavyādhibhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.3.32.[1]	'muñcāmi tvā' iti sūktena pūtigandhamatsyasahitamodanamabhimantrya vyādhitāya prayacchati bhakṣaṇārthaṃ bhojanakāle //
4.3.33.[1]	'muñcāmi tvā' iti sūktenāraṇyakatilaiḥ prajvālitamudakaṃ pātre prakṣipati /
4.3.33.[2]	tato'bhimantryoṣākāle'vasiñcati vyādhitam /
4.3.33.[3]	maithunarājayakṣmaṇi bhaiṣajyam /
4.3.33.[4]	uṣākāla idaṃ karma /
4.3.33.[5]	'muñcāmi tvā' iti sūktenāraṇyaśaṇenāvajvālitamudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.3.33.[6]	mārjanamācamanaṃ ca /
4.3.33.[7]	maithunavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.3.33.[8]	'muñcāmi tvā' iti sūktenāraṇyagomayenāvajvālitamudakamabhimantryāvasiñcatyuṣākāle /
4.3.33.[9]	mārjanamācamanaṃ ca /
4.3.33.[10]	maithunavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.3.33.[11]	uṣākāle 'muñcāmi tvā' iti sūktena cityādyābhiḥ prajvālitamudakamabhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.3.33.[12]	mārjanamācamanaṃ ca /
4.3.33.[13]	kecit tilaśaṇādicaturṣu karmasvaraṇye'vasekamicchanti /
4.3.33.[14]	kecidgṛhe'vasekamicchanti /
4.3.33.[15]	vikalpaḥ /
4.3.33.[16]	samāptaṃ maithunavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.3.33.[17]	'muñcāmi tvā' iti sūktena vyādhitamabhimantrayate /
4.3.33.[18]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam //
4.3.33.[19]	atha sarvabhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.3.34.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ā gāvaḥ' iti daśabhiḥ sūktairghaṭamudakapūrṇaṃ sampātyābhimantrya vyādhitamāplāvayati /
4.3.34.[2]	mārjanācamane smartavye /
4.3.34.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.3.34.[4]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.3.34.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'muñca śīrṣaktyāḥ' ityṛcodakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati vyādhitam /
4.3.34.[6]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.3.34.[7]	āplavane sarvatra mārjanācamane ca /
4.3.34.[8]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.3.34.[9]	tṛtīyā kaṇḍikā //27 //
4.4.0.[1]	skandaviṣabhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.4.1.[1]	takṣakadevatāyai namaskāraṃ kṛtvā tato 'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāmudakamabhimantryācāmayati viṣakaram /
4.4.1.[2]	takṣakāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāmudakamabhimantrya samprokṣati viṣaduṣṭam /
4.4.1.[3]	skandaviṣabhaiṣajya //
4.4.2.[1]	'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāṃ kṛmukavṛkṣaśakalaṃ sahodakamabhimantrya tata ācāmayati /
4.4.2.[2]	skandaviṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.4.2.[3]	'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāṃ kṛmukavṛkṣaśakalaṃ sahodakamabhimantryābhyukṣati /
4.4.2.[4]	tato mārjanamācamanaṃ ca sarvaṃ tūṣṇīm /
4.4.2.[5]	dūrśāvajvālitamudakamabhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.4.2.[6]	mārjanācamane ca /
4.4.2.[7]	sarvaṃ tūṣṇīm /
4.4.2.[8]	'brāhmaṇo jajñe' iti sūktābhyāṃ jīrṇahariṇacarmāvajvālitamudake prakṣipya tamabhimantrya tato'vasiñcati /
4.4.2.[9]	viṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.4.2.[10]	'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāṃ sammārjanikāvakaratṛṇairavajvālitamudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.4.2.[11]	skandaviṣabhaiṣajyam //
4.4.3.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāmudapātraṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati viṣaduṣṭam /
4.4.3.[2]	viṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.4.3.[3]	'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāṃ viṣaliptābhyāṃ phalābhyāṃ saktumanthamupamathya tato'bhimantrya pāyayati /
4.4.3.[4]	viṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.4.3.[5]	'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāṃ madanaphalāni pratyṛcamabhimantrya bhakṣayati /
4.4.3.[6]	yathā chardayati tathā ca kartavyam /
4.4.3.[7]	skandaviṣabhaiṣajyam //
4.4.4.[1]	'brāhmaṇo jajñe' 'vāridam' iti sūktābhyāṃ haridrāṃ sarpiṣā sahitāmabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.4.4.[2]	samāptaṃ skandaviṣabhaiṣajyam //
4.4.4.[3]	atha śastrādyabhighāte rudhirapravāhe bhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.4.5.[1]	'rohaṇyasi' iti sūktena lākṣodakaṃ kvāthitamabhimantrya vyādhideśamavasiñcati /
4.4.5.[2]	uṣākāle karma /
4.4.5.[3]	asthibhaṅge rudhirapravāhe daṃśaśastrābhighātādau bhaiṣajyam //
4.4.6.[1]	'rohaṇyasi' iti pṛṣātakaṃ ghṛtamiśraṃ dugdhamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.4.6.[2]	'rohaṇyasi' iti sūktena kṣīraṃ ghṛtamiśraṃ kṛtvā vyādhideśaṃ mrakṣati /
4.4.6.[3]	aṅgabhaṅge 'ṅgachede 'ṅgarudhirapravāhe 'ṅgābhighāte 'ṅgabhagne 'ṅgamūḍhābhighāte 'ṅgavṛkṣābhighāte muṣṭiloṣṭeṣṭikāpaśuśṛṅgāgnipāṣāṇalakuṭaśastrādyabhighāte rudhirapravāhe vā śarīrachedādau bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.4.6.[4]	atha rakṣobhaiṣajyamucyate
4.4.7.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ā paśyati' iti sūktena sadampuṣpāmaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.4.7.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.4.7.[3]	sadampuṣpā trisandhyā prasiddhā /
4.4.7.[4]	brahmagrahe kṣatriyagrahe vaiśyagrahe śūdragrahe vānyeṣāṃ vyantarāṇāṃ piśācānāṃ rakṣasāṃ ca bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.4.7.[5]	atha sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyamucyate
4.4.8.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bhavāśarvau manve vām' iti sūktena saptarcenaikaikayarcā kāmpīlasaptapuṭakānudakapūrṇān sampātyarcarcā tataḥ pratyṛcamabhimantrya tato vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.4.8.[2]	tataḥ puṭaṃ paścāt kṣipati /
4.4.8.[3]	evaṃ dvitīyamevaṃ tṛtīyam /
4.4.8.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
4.4.8.[5]	samāptaṃ sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam //
4.4.8.[6]	sarvabhūtagrahabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.4.9.[1]	'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktena śamīparṇacūrṇaṃ śamīphale kṛtvābhimantrya saktumadhye dadāti bhakṣārtham /
4.4.9.[2]	rakṣograhe bhaiṣajyam //
4.4.10.[1]	'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktena śamīparṇacūrṇaṃ śamīphale kṛtvābhimantryālaṅkāre dadāti vyādhitasya /
4.4.10.[2]	sarvagrahabhaiṣajyam //
4.4.11.[1]	'tvayā pūrvam' iti sūktena śamīcūrṇaṃ kṛtvābhimantrya śālāṃ cūrṇaiḥ parikirati /
4.4.11.[2]	vyādhitasya śālām /
4.4.11.[3]	rakṣograhāpsarograhagandharvagrahasarvagrahabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.4.11.[4]	athāmatigṛhīte bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.4.12.[1]	'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcā bhojanakāle bhaktamabhimantrya dadāti bhakṣaṇārtham prajñāpranaṣṭe'jñānagṛhīte'dharmagṛhīte trivarge ca vinaṣṭe dyūtakrīḍādyatipratte kubuddhibhaiṣajyam //
4.4.12.[2]	rājayakṣmaṇi śiroroge kuṣṭhāmaye sarvagātravedanāyāṃ bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.4.13.[1]	'yo giriṣvajāyathāḥ' iti sūktena 'triḥ śāmbubhyo aṅgirebhyaḥ' iti caturṛcena kuṣṭhapiṣṭaṃ navanītamiśraṃ kṛtvābhimantryāpratīhāraṃ vyādhitasya śarīraṃ pralimpati /
4.4.13.[2]	rājayakṣmaṇi śiroroge kuṣṭhāmaye sarvagātravedanāsu bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.4.13.[3]	atha śastrādyabhighāte bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.4.14.[1]	'rātrī mātā' iti sūktena dugdhe lākṣāṃ kvāthayitvābhimantrya pāyayati /
4.4.14.[2]	śastrādyabhighāte pāṣāṇapatanābhighāte'gnidāhe sarvaśarīrābhighāte bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.4.14.[3]	sūtikā strī ariṣṭakasya ca bhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.4.15.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' 'anāptā ye' 'sahasradhāra eva te' iti sūktena bhaktamabhimantrya dadāti bhakṣaṇārtham /
4.4.15.[2]	pūrvaṃ strī praveśya tūṣṇīṃ tataḥ paścāt kartā tūṣṇīṃ praviśya sūktena bhaktamabhimantrya dadyāt //
4.4.16.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' 'anāptā ye' 'sahasradhāra eva te' iti sūktena saktumanthamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.4.16.[2]	tenaiva sūktenopasthānamādityasya /
4.4.16.[3]	'brahma jajñānam' iti sūktenodakamabhimantryācāmayati /
4.4.16.[4]	samāptaṃ strīprasavadoṣe sūtikāroge ca bhaiṣajyam /
4.4.16.[5]	adbhutadarśane doṣanāśanabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.4.16.[6]	sarvādbhuteṣu bhaktakarma vācamanakarma vā kuryāt /
4.4.16.[7]	yāni carakādivaidyakeṣvadbhutāni paṭhyante'svasthaśārīraviṣaye teṣāṃ sarveṣāmiyaṃ śāntirbhaiṣajyaṃ bhavati /
4.4.16.[8]	yāni cādbhutāni śarīraroge jyotiṣe paṭhyante teṣāmapīdaṃ karma //
4.4.16.[9]	atha sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyamucyate
4.4.17.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'dive svāhā' iti sūktena catura udapātre sampātānānayati //
4.4.18-19.[1]	dvau sampātau bhūmau dattvā tataḥ sampātitāṃ bhūmimṛttikāṃ saṅgṛhya tata udapātre prakṣipya tato'bhimantraṇaṃ kṛtvā vyādhitamāplāvayati /
4.4.18-19.[2]	'dive svāhā' iti tribhiḥ svāhākārairekaḥ sampātaḥ /
4.4.18-19.[3]	tribhiḥ svāhākāraistrayaḥ sampātāḥ /
4.4.18-19.[4]	dvau dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ sampātau /
4.4.18-19.[5]	evaṃ ṣaḍ bhavanti /
4.4.18-19.[6]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.4.18-19.[7]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'imaṃ yavam' iti sūktenārdharcenārdharcena homaḥ /
4.4.18-19.[8]	udapātre sampātānānīya dvau bhūmau sampātau /
4.4.18-19.[9]	tau gṛhītvodapātre prakṣipya tato'bhimantraṇam /
4.4.18-19.[10]	tata āplāvayati vyādhitam /
4.4.18-19.[11]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.4.18-19.[12]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam //
4.4.20.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'dive svāhā' iti sūktena ṣaṭ sampātān karoti yavasahita udapātre caturaḥ sampātānānayati /
4.4.20.[2]	dvau sampātau bhūmau dattvā mṛttikāmudapātre prakṣipya tato'bhimantraṇamāplāvanaṃ ca /
4.4.20.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.4.20.[4]	'dive svāhā' iti tribhiḥ svāhākārairekaḥ sampātaḥ /
4.4.20.[5]	anyat sarvaṃ yathārthaṃ kuryāt /
4.4.20.[6]	evaṃ ṣaṭ sarvatra kuryāt /
4.4.20.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'imaṃ yavam' iti sūktenārdharcena ṣaḍ homān kṛtvā catura udapātre sampātānānayati /
4.4.20.[8]	dvau pṛthivyām /
4.4.20.[9]	tāvudapātre prakṣipya tataḥ sūktenābhimantraṇam /
4.4.20.[10]	yavasahita udapātre sampātāḥ /
4.4.20.[11]	tato'bhiṣecanaṃ mārjanamācamanaṃ ca /
4.4.20.[12]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.4.20.[13]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam /
4.4.20.[14]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'imaṃ yavam' iti sūktena yavamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.4.20.[15]	tata uttaratantram /
4.4.20.[16]	śītajvarakṣudrajvarakāmajvaraśleṣmajvaragrīṣmajvara- varṣājvaradānadravyatyāgapratigrahayājanādhyayanādhyāpanayājyayājanabuddhidhvānte akṣipaṭalodvege strīṣu puruṣeṣu pāpalakṣaṇāpakāmahṛdaya- tāpaharṣaviṣādāpasmāreṣu /
4.4.20.[17]	sarvaśabdena kathyante /
4.4.20.[18]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyaṃ yatra ekasmin vyādhau bahūni karmāṇi vihitāni sarvasmin śāstre tatra sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
4.4.20.[19]	yatrābhiṣeko'vasecanaṃ tatrācamanaṃ mārjanaṃ ca sarvatra //
4.4.20.[20]	caturthī kaṇḍikā //28 //
4.5.0.[1]	sarpaviṣabhaiṣajyam ucyate
4.5.1.[1]	takṣakāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'dadirhi' ityṛcodakamabhimantryācāmayati sarpādiviṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.1.[2]	takṣakāya namaskāraṃ kṛtvā 'dadirhi' ityṛcodakamabhimantryāvasiñcati viṣadaṣṭam /
4.5.1.[3]	viṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.1.[4]	'dadirhi' ityṛcā kṛmukavṛkṣaśakalaṃ saṅghṛṣya tata udakaṃ ca prakṣipya tato'bhimantryāvasiñcati viṣadhāritam /
4.5.1.[5]	'dadirhi' ityṛcodakaṃ carmāgniprajvālitamabhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.5.1.[6]	'dadirhi' ity ṛcā hariṇajīrṇacarmāvajvālitam udakam abhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.5.1.[7]	'dadirhi' ity ṛcā mārjanikāvakaratṛṇāvajvālitodakam abhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.5.1.[8]	jaṅgamaviṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.1.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'dadirhi' ityṛcodapātraṃ sampātya tataḥ pāyayati /
4.5.1.[10]	'dadirhi' ityṛcā saktumanthamūrdhvaphalābhyāṃ viṣaliptābhyāṃ mathitvābhimantrya pāyayati sarpadaṣṭam /
4.5.1.[11]	jaṅgamaviṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.1.[12]	'dadirhi' ityṛcā madanaphalamabhimantrya bhakṣayati chardanārtham /
4.5.1.[13]	jaṅgamaviṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.1.[14]	'dadirhi' ityṛcā haridrāṃ ghṛtaṃ ca sahābhimantrya pāyayati /
4.5.1.[15]	jaṅgamaviṣabhaiṣajyam //
4.5.2-3.[1]	'yatte apodakam' ityṛcāpradakṣiṇaṃ vyādhitaṃ parikrāmati /
4.5.2-3.[2]	viṣastambhanabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.2-3.[3]	viṣaṃ stambhitaṃ nānyenottārayituṃ śakyate vana vedamantreṇa //
4.5.4.[1]	'yatte apodakam' ityṛcaṃ japitvā śikhāṃ badhnāti /
4.5.4.[2]	viṣastambhanabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.4.[3]	'yatte apodakam' ityṛcaṃ japitvā śvetavastreṇa granthiṃ badhnāti /
4.5.4.[4]	viṣastambhanabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.4.[5]	'yatte apodakam' ityekāṃ japitvā śaṇastambe granthiṃ badhnāti /
4.5.4.[6]	viṣaṃ na visarpati /
4.5.4.[7]	deśasthitaṃ bhavati /
4.5.4.[8]	śarīre na sarpati /
4.5.4.[9]	viṣastambhanaṃ bhavati //
4.5.5.[1]	'vṛṣā me ravaḥ' ityṛcā yasmin sthāne daṣṭaṃ taṃ sthānaṃ pīḍayati ṛcaṃ japitvā /
4.5.5.[2]	deśādviṣamanyatra gacchati /
4.5.5.[3]	viṣanāśane bhaiṣajyam //
4.5.6.[1]	'cakṣuṣā te cakṣuḥ' ityṛcācāryastataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parikrāmati /
4.5.6.[2]	'apehyarirasi' ityṛcaṃ japitvā tṛṇāni prajvālya tato'herabhimukhaṃ kṣipati //
4.5.7.[1]	'apehyarirasi' ityṛcaṃ japitvā yato daṣṭastato jvalitatṛṇāni kṣipati daśane //
4.5.8.[1]	'kairāta pṛśne' ityṛcodakaṃ gṛhatṛṇāvajvālitamabhimantrya vyādhitaṃ pāyayati prokṣati ca //
4.5.9.[1]	'asitasya' ityṛcārtnījyāpāśaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnātyājyatantre /
4.5.9.[2]	viṣabhaiṣajyam //
4.5.10.[1]	'āligī ca viligī ca' 'urugalāyāḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ madhumakṣikāṃ madhuvṛkṣamṛttikāṃ cābhimantrya pāyayati //
4.5.11.[1]	'karṇā śvāvittadabravīt' ityṛcā śukasārikṛśānāṃ purīṣaṃ śvāvitpurīṣamityucyate /
4.5.11.[2]	purīṣamabhimantrya pāyayati viṣadaṣṭam //
4.5.12.[1]	'karṇā śvāvittadabravīt' ityṛcā śalalīmāṃsamabhimantrya prāśayati /
4.5.12.[2]	viṣanāśanabhaiṣajyam //
4.5.13.[1]	'tābuvaṃ na tābuvam' ityṛcālābumadhya udakaṃ prakṣipya tato'bhimantryācāmayati /
4.5.13.[2]	sarpaviṣabhaiṣajyam //
4.5.14.[1]	'tastuvaṃ na tastuvam' ityṛcālābuvṛntaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnātyājyatantre /
4.5.14.[2]	sarpaviṣadaṣṭam /
4.5.14.[3]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ prayogo vikalpena na samuccayaḥ /
4.5.14.[4]	ekaṃ kuryād dve vā trīṇi vā sarvāṇi vā /
4.5.14.[5]	samāptaṃ sarpaviṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.14.[6]	ekavyādhau yatra bahūni karmāṇi vihitāni tatraikaṃ vā kuryāt karmabāhulyād dve vā sarvāṇi vā /
4.5.14.[7]	'sarvatra hastahome na tantram' iti vacanāt //
4.5.14.[8]	atha duṣṭavaktṝṇāṃ mukhabandhanamucyate
4.5.15.[1]	'ekā ca me' 'yadyekavṛṣo'si' iti sūktābhyāṃ kulapallavān madhūdakaṃ caitat tritayamekatra kṛtvābhimantrya tato vyādhita pāyayati /
4.5.15.[2]	duṣṭavaktṛmukhabandhanabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.15.[3]	duṣṭapuruṣāḥ parokṣe na vadanti //
4.5.16.[1]	'yadyekavṛṣaḥ' iti sūktena bhojanamabhimantrya bhakṣayati /
4.5.16.[2]	śāpabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.16.[3]	akṛtavatkṛtapāpabhaiṣajyam //
4.5.17.[1]	'yadyekavṛṣaḥ' iti sūktena gṛhadvāraṃ dadātyapidadhātītyarthaḥ /
4.5.17.[2]	praviśatītyarthaḥ /
4.5.17.[3]	duṣṭavaktṛmukhabandhane brāhmaṇaśāpe ca bhaiṣajyam //
4.5.17.[4]	atha jvarabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.5.18.[1]	'agnistakmānam' iti sūktena lājān pāyayati /
4.5.18.[2]	sarvajvarabhaiṣajyam //
4.5.19.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'agnistakmānam' iti sūktena tāmrasruveṇa mūrdhni sampātānānayati /
4.5.19.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.5.19.[3]	etasmin tantre dāvāgnipraṇayanam /
4.5.19.[4]	samāptaṃ jvarabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.19.[5]	sarvajvare kuryāt //
4.5.19.[6]	atha kṛmibhaiṣajyam ucyate
4.5.20.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ote me' iti sūktena karīramūlaṃ sampātyabhimantrya badhnāti /
4.5.20.[2]	'ote me' iti sūktena govālaiḥ karīrakāṣṭhaṃ veṣṭayitvā /
4.5.20.[3]	sūktaṃ japitvā pāṣāṇena cūrṇayati /
4.5.20.[4]	tataḥ sūktenāgnau pratapati /
4.5.20.[5]	tataḥ sūktenādadhāti /
4.5.20.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
4.5.20.[7]	kṛmibhaiṣajyam //
4.5.21.[1]	'ote me' iti sūktena grāmapāṃsūn abhimantrya savyena hastena dakṣiṇābhimukho bhūtvā pāṃsūn parikirati /
4.5.21.[2]	sarvakṛmibhaiṣajyam /
4.5.21.[3]	'ote me' iti sūktena pāṃsūnabhimantrya mathitvā hastena kṛmerupari kṣipati /
4.5.21.[4]	'ote me' iti sūktena śāntavṛkṣasamidha ādadhāti /
4.5.21.[5]	kṛmibhañjanam /
4.5.21.[6]	mukhakṛmikarṇakṛmisarvakṛmibhaiṣajyam //
4.5.22.[1]	'ote me' iti sūktena paścādagnermāturutsaṅge bālakaṃ kṛtvā navanītānvaktena musalabudhnena tāluni tāpayati /
4.5.22.[2]	triḥ sūktaprayogaḥ /
4.5.22.[3]	apānakṛmiṃ śirasi vā tasya /
4.5.22.[4]	sarvakṛmibhaiṣajyam //
4.5.23.[1]	'ote me' iti sūktena śigrubījairnavanītamiśritairabhimantrya vyādhideśaṃ pralimpati kṣatadeśam /
4.5.23.[2]	kṛmibhaiṣajyam //
4.5.24.[1]	'ote me' iti sūktenaikaviṃśatyuśīramūlānyabhimantrya tataḥ pāṣāṇena kuṭṭayati /
4.5.24.[2]	tataḥ sūktaṃ japitvośīrāṇyagninā dahati //
4.5.25.[1]	'ote me' iti sūktenaikaviṃśatyuśīrāṇyabhimantrya vyādhitāya samarpayati /
4.5.25.[2]	kṛmibhaiṣajyam //
4.5.26.[1]	'ote me' iti sūktenodakaghaṭamekaviṃśatyuśīrapiñjūlīsahitaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tato vyādhitamāplāvayatyājyatantre /
4.5.26.[2]	kṛmijātānāmakṣikarṇamukhaśironāsikādantakṛmīṇāṃ kṛṣmaśvetapītadṛṣṭānāmadṛṣṭānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kṛmīṇāṃ bhaiṣajyam /
4.5.26.[3]	samāptaṃ kṛmibhaiṣajyam //
4.5.26.[4]	atha rākṣasabhaiṣajyamucyate /
4.5.26.[5]	tatrāha
4.5.27.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ā yaṃ viśanti' ityṛcā vayoniveśanakāṣṭhaśṛtaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
4.5.27.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.5.27.[3]	rākṣasabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.5.27.[4]	atha sarpaviṣabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.5.28.[1]	'pari dyāmiva' iti tṛcena sūktena madhuśībhamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.5.28.[2]	madhukroḍamityarthaḥ /
4.5.28.[3]	sarpaviṣaliṅgyupatāpaḥ //

4.5.29.[4]	viṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.5.29.[5]	'pari dyāmiva' iti sūktena dullakāvajvālitamudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati vyādhitam /
4.5.29.[6]	'pari dyāmiva' iti sūktenāvakaratṛṇānyavajvālitam udakam abhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.5.29.[7]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'pari dyāmiva' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātyābhimantrya pāyayati /

4.5.29.[9]	'pari dyāmiva' iti sūktenordhvaphalābhyāṃ viṣadigdhābhyāṃ manthamupamathya tato'bhimantrya pāyayati /

4.5.30.[2]	apsviṭaṃ kṛtvā tatrāgniṃ prajvālya 'asthisraṃsam' iti sūktena kāṣṭhaśakalaṃ sampātya tena śakalena vyādhitamavasiñcati /

4.6.0.[1]	athākṣirogabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.6.1.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ābayo anābayo' iti sūktena caturṛcena sarṣapakāṇḍamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.6.1.[2]	sarṣapatailena sampātavantaṃ karoti /
4.6.1.[3]	tantrakṛtenaiva /
4.6.1.[4]	tato'bhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.6.1.[5]	akṣiroge bhaiṣajyam //
4.6.2.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ābayo anābayoḥ' iti sūktena sarṣapakāṇḍamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.6.2.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.6.2.[3]	ājyena pradhānamaṅgāni ca /
4.6.2.[4]	sarṣapatailenābhyajya maṇiṃ tato badhnāti /
4.6.2.[5]	akṣiroge bhaiṣajyam //
4.6.3.[1]	'ābayo' iti sūktena sarṣapaśākaṃ sarṣapatailenābhyaktamabhimantrya vyādhitāya prayacchati /
4.6.3.[2]	akṣiroge //
4.6.4.[1]	'ābayo' iti sūktena catvāri śākavṛkṣaphalānyabhimantrya prayacchati vyādhitāya /
4.6.4.[2]	akṣiroge //
4.6.5.[1]	'ābayo' iti sūktena mūlakṣīraṃ mukhena prāśya tato'bhimantryākṣiṇī āṅkte vyādhitasya /
4.6.5.[2]	mūlakṣīraṃ pāṭikālagnaṃ taducyate //
4.6.6.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ābayo' iti sūktena mūlakṣīraṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
4.6.6.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.6.6.[3]	samāptamakṣiroge bhaiṣajyam //
4.6.6.[4]	pittajvarabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.6.7.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'agnerivāsya dahata eti śuṣmiṇaḥ' iti tṛcena tāmrasruveṇa mūrdhni sampātānānayati /
4.6.7.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.6.7.[3]	asmin tantre dāvāgnipraṇayanaṃ kuryāt /
4.6.7.[4]	samāptaṃ pittajvarabhaiṣajyam //
4.6.7.[5]	atha keśavṛddhikaraṇe keśapatane ca bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.6.8.[1]	'imā yāstisraḥ' iti tṛcena sūktena vṛkṣabhūmijātauṣadhibhir avajvālitam udakam abhimantryoṣākāle'vasiñcati /
4.6.8.[2]	keśavṛddhau keśapatane ca bhaiṣajyam /
4.6.8.[3]	uṣākāla idaṃ karma //
4.6.9.[1]	'imā yāstisraḥ' iti sūktena madhusikthakaṃ kvāthayitvābhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.6.9.[2]	uṣākāle 'imā yāstisraḥ' iti sūktena bibhītakāni kvāthayitvābhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.6.9.[3]	keśabhaiṣajyam //
4.6.10.[1]	uṣākāle 'imā yāstisraḥ' iti dāruharidrāharidre ca dvābhyāṃ kvāthayitvābhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.6.10.[2]	samāptaṃ keśavardhanārthaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ keśapatane ca kṣaye ca //
4.6.10.[3]	atha udaratuṇḍabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.6.11.[1]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ cittyādyauṣadhyā sahitamudakamabhimantrya tato vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.6.11.[2]	udaratuṇḍabhaiṣajyam //
4.6.12.[1]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ maruto yajate pākayajñavidhānena yathā varuṇam /
4.6.12.[2]	'mārutaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ mārutaśṛtaṃ mārutaiḥ paristīya mārutena sruveṇa mārutenājyena varuṇāya trijuhoti' /
4.6.12.[3]	maruto yathā varuṇam /
4.6.12.[4]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāmājyaṃ juhoti /
4.6.12.[5]	ājyatantre /
4.6.12.[6]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāmoṣadhīḥ sampātya praveśyābhinyubjati /
4.6.12.[7]	ājyatantre /
4.6.12.[8]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ cittyādyoṣadhīḥ sampātya viplāvayetodakamadhye /
4.6.12.[9]	jalodare udare ca /
4.6.12.[10]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ śvaśiro'bhimantryodake viplāvayati /
4.6.12.[11]	eḍakaśiro vā viplāvayatyabhimantrodake /
4.6.12.[12]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ keśajaradupānahau vaṃśāgre baddhvābhimantrya yodhayati /
4.6.12.[13]	'kṛṣṇaṃ niyānam' 'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudapātreṇa sampātavatā /
4.6.12.[14]	samprokṣyāmapātraṃ tripāde'śmānamavadhāyāpsu nidadhāti /
4.6.12.[15]	jalodare nābhituṇḍe bṛhadudare bhaiṣajyāni samāptāni //
4.6.12.[16]	atha hṛdayadāghe jalodare kāmale ca bhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.6.13.[1]	'himavataḥ' iti sūktena nadyudakamanulomamāhārya tatra valīkatṛṇāni prakṣipya tato'bhimantrya tato vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.6.13.[2]	mārjanācamane ca /
4.6.13.[3]	hṛdayadoṣe jalodare kāmale ca bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.6.13.[4]	atha gaṇḍamālābhaiṣajyānyucyante
4.6.14.[1]	'pañca ca yāḥ' iti sūktena gopāṃśulikānāṃ pañcāśatpañcādhikā agnau prajvālyādhastādayaḥ samidha ādadhāti //
4.6.15.[1]	agnyupari kapāle parṇān dhṛtvā śrapayati /
4.6.15.[2]	tataḥ sūktaṃ japitvā tenaiva kāṣṭhena gaṇḍamālāṃ limpati //
4.6.16.[1]	'pañca ca yāḥ' iti sūktena śaṅkhaṃ ghṛṣṭvā tato'bhimantrya gaṇḍamālāṃ pralimpati /
4.6.16.[2]	'pañca ca yāḥ' iti sūktena śvānakuvakuralālāmabhimantrya pralimpati /
4.6.16.[3]	'pañca ca yāḥ' iti sūktena jalaukāmabhimantrya gaṇḍamālāyāṃ saṃsarjayati /
4.6.16.[4]	rudhirapravāhaṇārtham /
4.6.16.[5]	'pañca ca yāḥ' iti sūktena gṛhagodhikādi matsyādi abhimantrya gaṇḍamālāyāṃ saṃsarjayati //
4.7.1-4.[1]	'prāgnaye vācam' iti sūktena puroḍāśaṃ juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[2]	'prāgnaye vācam' iti sūktena payo juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[3]	'prāgnaye vācam' iti sūktenodaudanaṃ juhoti 'prāgnaye' iti sūktena pāyasaṃ juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[4]	'prāgnaye vācam' iti sūktena paśuṃ juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[5]	vapāmavadānāni caruṃ ca vaśāvidhānena /
4.7.1-4.[6]	'prāgnaye' iti sūktena vrīhīnāvapati /
4.7.1-4.[7]	rakṣograhabhaiṣajyam /
4.7.1-4.[8]	anuvartate vikāraḥ /
4.7.1-4.[9]	'prāgnaye vācam' iti sūktena yavāñjuhoti /
4.7.1-4.[10]	'prāgnaye' iti tilāñjuhoti /
4.7.1-4.[11]	'prāgnaye' iti dhānā juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[12]	'prāgnaye' iti dadhisaktūñjuhoti /
4.7.1-4.[13]	'prāgnaye' iti sūktena śaṣkulīrjuhoti /
4.7.1-4.[14]	pratyṛcaṃ homaḥ /
4.7.1-4.[15]	'prato yantu' ityacājyaṃ juhoti tantre /
4.7.1-4.[16]	rakṣograhabhaiṣajyam /
4.7.1-4.[17]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā śāntavṛkṣasamidha ādadhāti /
4.7.1-4.[18]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā puroḍāśaṃ juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[19]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā pāyasaṃ juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[20]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā paśuṃ juhoti /
4.7.1-4.[21]	vaśāvidhānena /
4.7.1-4.[22]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā vrīhīñjuhoti /
4.7.1-4.[23]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā yavāñjuhoti /
4.7.1-4.[24]	tantravikalpaḥ /
4.7.1-4.[25]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā dadhisaktūñjuhoti /
4.7.1-4.[26]	'preto yantu' ityṛcā śaṣkulīrjuhoti samāptaṃ rākṣasagrahabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.1-4.[27]	atha sarvabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.5.[1]	'vaiśvānaro na ūtaye' 'ṛtāvānaṃ vaiśvānaram' iti sūktābhyāmudapātramabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.7.5.[2]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.7.5.[3]	vaiśvānarīyābhyāṃ sūktābhyāṃ saktumanthamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.7.5.[4]	sarvabhaiṣajyam /
4.7.5.[5]	'vaiśvānaro na' 'ṛtāvānam' iti sūktābhyāṃ haridrāṃ sarpiṣyabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.7.5.[6]	'vaiśvānaro na' 'ṛtāvānam' iti sūktābhyāmuddhṛtamudakamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.7.5.[7]	ājya tantre'pi yat pīyate, tat saṃśṛtya pāyayati vaiśvānarīyābhyāṃ sūktābhyām /
4.7.5.[8]	samāptaṃ sarvabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.5.[9]	athāpavādabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.6.[1]	bahubhāṣaṇamadharme ca pravartate so'pavādaḥ /
4.7.6.[2]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'asthād dyauḥ' iti sūktena pūrveṇa svayampatitaṃ gośṛṅgaṃ sampātya tataḥ śṛṅga udakaṃ kṛtvābhimantryācāmayatyabhyukṣati ca /
4.7.6.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.7.6.[4]	apavādabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam /
4.7.6.[5]	apavādaścandragrahādiṣu bahubhāṣaṇādi //
4.7.6.[6]	athodare vā hṛdaye vāṅge vā sarvāṅge vā śūla utpanne bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.7.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yāṃ te rudraḥ' iti sūktena śūlamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.7.7.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.7.7.[3]	śūlo lohamaṇiḥ pāṣāṇo vā dārilabhadramatam /
4.7.7.[4]	'yāṃ te rudraḥ' iti sūktena vyādhitamabhimantrayate /
4.7.7.[5]	rudrabhāṣyamatam /
4.7.7.[6]	śūlabhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.7.7.[7]	rakṣograhabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.8.[1]	'ut sūryaḥ' iti sūktena cittyādyoṣadhibhiḥ sahodakaghaṭamabhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.7.8.[2]	'utsūryaḥ' iti sūktena śamīmudakena sahābhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.7.8.[3]	'utsūryaḥ' iti sūktena śamībimbamudakasahitamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.7.8.[4]	'utsūryaḥ' iti sūktena śīrṣaparṇīmudakena dattvābhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.7.8.[5]	samāptaṃ rakṣograhabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.8.[6]	duṣṭagaṇḍaviriṣṭabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.9.[1]	'dyauśca me idaṃ pṛthivī' iti tṛcena sūktena tailamabhimantrya gaṇḍamabhyajya hastena vyādhitamavamārṣṭi /
4.7.9.[2]	abhyukṣatītyarthaḥ /
4.7.9.[3]	duṣṭagaṇḍabhaiṣajyam /
4.7.9.[4]	'dyauśca me' iti sūktaṃ japan vyādhideśaṃ hastena mārṣṭi /
4.7.9.[5]	duṣṭagaṇḍe duṣṭavraṇe ca bhaiṣajyam //
4.7.10.[1]	'dyauśca me' iti sūktena sthūṇāyāṃ vraṇaṃ nikarṣati /
4.7.10.[2]	ghṛṣyatītyarthaḥ /
4.7.10.[3]	rudhirakṛte duṣṭavraṇe duṣṭagaṇḍe bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.7.10.[4]	akṣatavraṇabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.11.[1]	'idamidvā u bheṣajam' iti sūktena gomūtramabhimantrya /
4.7.11.[2]	tena vraṇaṃ mardayati //
4.7.12.[1]	'idamidvā u bheṣajam' iti sūktena mūtreṇa vraṇaṃ kṣipati //
4.7.13.[1]	tenaiva sūktena mūtreṇa vraṇaṃ prakṣālayati /
4.7.13.[2]	yasya vraṇasya mukhaṃ nāstyakṣatavraṇamucyate //
4.7.14.[1]	'idamidvā u bheṣajam' iti sūktena dantamalamabhimantrya pralimpati /
4.7.14.[2]	akṣatavraṇabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.15.[1]	'idamidvā u bheṣajam' iti sūktena tṛṇarajasya phenamabhimantrya vraṇa pralimpati /
4.7.15.[2]	yasya vraṇasya rudhiraṃ na vahati tasya /
4.7.15.[3]	samāptamakṣatavraṇabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.15.[4]	gaṇḍamālābhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.16.[1]	'apacitaḥ pra patata' iti sūktena śaṅkhaṃ ghṛṣṭvābhimantrya gaṇḍamālāṃ pralimpati /
4.7.16.[2]	'apacitaḥ' iti sūktena śvānalālāmabhimantrya gaṇḍamālāṃ pralimpati /
4.7.16.[3]	śvānaḥ kurkaraḥ /
4.7.16.[4]	gaṇḍamālābhaiṣajyam /
4.7.16.[5]	'apacitaḥ' iti sūktena jalaukāmabhimantrya gaṇḍamālāyāṃ saṃśleṣayati /
4.7.16.[6]	yathākathañcid rudhirapravāhaṇārtham /
4.7.16.[7]	'apacitaḥ' iti sūktena gṛhagodhikāmabhimantrya gaṇḍamālāyāmāsajati /
4.7.16.[8]	'ā susrasaḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ śaṅkhaṃ ghṛṣṭvābhimantrya tato gaṇḍamālāṃ pralimpati /
4.7.16.[9]	'ā susrasaḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ śvānalālāṃ kurkaralālāmabhimantrya gaṇḍamālāṃ pralimpati /
4.7.16.[10]	gaṇḍamālābhaiṣajyam /
4.7.16.[11]	'ā susrasaḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ jalaukāmabhimantrya gaṇḍamālāyāṃ saṃsarjayati rudhirapravāhaṇārtham /
4.7.16.[12]	'ā susrasaḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ gṛhagodhikāṃ maśakādīmabhimantrya gaṇḍamālāyāṃ saṃsarjayati rudhirapravāhaṇārtham //
4.7.17.[1]	'apacitaḥ' iti sūktena saindhavalavaṇaṃ cūrṇayitvābhimantrya gaṇḍamālāyāṃ upari prakirati /
4.7.17.[2]	tatastasyopari niṣṭhīvati /
4.7.17.[3]	mukhalālāṃ prakṣipati tūṣṇīm /
4.7.17.[4]	'ā susrasaḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ saindhavalavaṇaṃ cūrṇayitvābhimantrya vyādhyupari prakirati /
4.7.17.[5]	tatastūṣṇīmupari niṣṭhīvati /
4.7.17.[6]	samāptaṃ gaṇḍamālābhaiṣajyam //
4.7.17.[7]	atha pakṣiṇo'bhighāte bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.18.[1]	'antarikṣeṇa patati' iti sūktena śvānapadasthānamṛttikāmabhimantrya pakṣahataṃ deśaṃ pralimpati /
4.7.18.[2]	pakṣahatabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.19.[1]	'antarikṣeṇa patati' iti sūktena śuno makṣikāmabhimantryāgnau prakṣipya tato dhūpayati vyādhipradeśam /
4.7.19.[2]	kākagṛdhrakapotaśyenādīnāṃ pakṣiṇāmabhighāte bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.7.19.[3]	atha gaṇḍabhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.20.[1]	'glauritaḥ pra patiṣyati' ityardharcena gomūtramabhimantrya gaṇḍaṃ mardayati gaṇḍabhaiṣajyam /
4.7.20.[2]	'glauritaḥ pra patiṣyati' ityardharcena gomūtramabhimantrya gaṇḍaṃ prakṣālayati /
4.7.20.[3]	'glauritaḥ pra patiṣyati' ityardharcena dantamalamabhimantrya gaṇḍaṃ pralimpati /
4.7.20.[4]	'glauritaḥ pra patiṣyati' ityardharcena tṛṇarajaphenamabhimantrya gaṇḍaṃ pralimpati /
4.7.20.[5]	samāptaṃ gaṇḍabhaiṣajyam /
4.7.20.[6]	gaṇḍaḥ sphoṭaka ityarthaḥ //
4.7.20.[7]	gardabhaśvānādyurugaṇḍe bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.21.[1]	'vīhi svāmāhutiṃ juṣāṇaḥ' iti sūktena śāntyudakamabhimantrya tataḥ kṣataṃ prokṣati /
4.7.21.[2]	tata ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'vīhi svāmāhutim' iti sūktenājyaṃ juhoti /
4.7.21.[3]	tato manasā saṅkalpayati /
4.7.21.[4]	sampātān dadāti /
4.7.21.[5]	uttaratantram /
4.7.21.[6]	samāptaṃ gardabhadaśanakṣatagaṇḍabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.21.[7]	pāpagṛhīte jalodare ca bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.22.[1]	'yā oṣadhayaḥ somarājñīḥ' iti sūktena tṛcena somalatā agnau prakṣipya vyādhitaṃ dhūpayati //
4.7.23.[1]	'yā oṣadhayaḥ' iti tṛcena madhu takraṃ cābhimantrya pāyayati /
4.7.23.[2]	jalodare pāpe śāpe ca bhaiṣajyam //
4.7.24.[1]	'yā oṣadhayaḥ somarājñīḥ' iti tṛcena kṣīraṃ takreṇa miśrayitvābhimantrya pāyayati //
4.7.25.[1]	'yā oṣadhayaḥ' iti sūktena madhu takraṃ kṣīraṃ dadhyetaccatuṣṭayamekatra kṛtvābhimantrya pāyayati /
4.7.25.[2]	brāhmaṇākrośe pāpagṛhīte jalodare ca bhaiṣajyaṃ samāptam //
4.7.25.[3]	viṣa upaviṣe sthāvare jaṅgame ca bhaiṣajyamucyate /
4.7.25.[4]	makṣikāyāṃ ca bhaiṣajyam
4.7.26.[1]	'devā aduḥ' iti tṛcena valmīkapoṭṭalikāṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.7.26.[2]	ājyatantram /
4.7.26.[3]	'devā aduḥ' iti tṛcena valmīkamṛttikāmudakamadhye prakṣipya tato'bhimantrya pāyayati /
4.7.26.[4]	'devā aduḥ' iti tṛcena valmīkamṛdamudake prakṣipya tato'bhimantryācāmayati /
4.7.26.[5]	viṣabhaiṣajyam /
4.7.26.[6]	'devā aduḥ' iti tṛcena valmīkamṛttikāmuṣṇodake prakṣipya tato'bhimantrya pralimpati viṣadaṣṭavraṇam /
4.7.26.[7]	upaviṣe viṣe ca makṣikānāṃ bhaiṣajyam /
4.7.26.[8]	samāpta viṣabhaiṣajyam //
4.7.26.[9]	atha kāse śleṣmapatane ca bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.27.[1]	'yathā mano manasketaiḥ' iti sūktena bhojanamabhimantrya dadāti bhakṣaṇārthaṃ prathamaṃ prapādya /
4.7.27.[2]	'yathā manaḥ' iti saktumanthamabhimantrya bhakṣayati /
4.7.27.[3]	kāsapatane bhaiṣajyam /
4.7.27.[4]	upasthānamādityasya dviḥ sūktasya prayogaḥ /
4.7.27.[5]	'yathā mano manaḥ' iti sūktenodakamabhimantryācāmayati /
4.7.27.[6]	tata upasthānaṃ cādityasya /
4.7.27.[7]	dviḥ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
4.7.27.[8]	kāsapatane bhaiṣajyam /
4.7.27.[9]	'ava divastārayanti' ityṛcā prapādya gṛhe praveśya tato bhojanamabhimantrya dadāti bhakṣaṇārtham /
4.7.27.[10]	kāsapatane bhaiṣajyam /
4.7.27.[11]	'ava divastārayanti' ityṛcā saktumabhimantrya dadāti bhakṣaṇārthamupasthānaṃ ca /
4.7.27.[12]	'ava divastārayanti' ity ṛcodakam abhimantryācāmayaty upasthānam ādityasya /
4.7.27.[13]	sarvatra dviḥ sūktaprayogaḥ /
4.7.27.[14]	samāptaṃ kāsaśleṣmapatane bhaiṣajyam //
4.7.27.[15]	keśadṛḍhīkaraṇe keśavṛddhikaraṇe ca bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.7.28.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'devī devyām' 'yāṃ jamadagniḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ kācamācīphalamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.7.28.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.7.28.[3]	'devī devyām' 'yāṃ jamadagniḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ jīvantīphalamaṇiṃ badhnāti /
4.7.28.[4]	ājyatantram /
4.7.28.[5]	'devī devyām' 'yāṃ jamadagniḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ bhṛṅgarājaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnātyājyatantre /
4.7.28.[6]	keśadṛḍhīkaraṇe keśajanane hrasvakeśeṣu vṛddhikaraṇe bhaiṣajyam /
4.7.28.[7]	amāvāsyāyāmidaṃ karma kuryāt /
4.7.28.[8]	kṛṣṇavastraparihito bhūtvā māṣatilakṛṣṇamannaṃ bhaikṣayitvā kartā 'devī devyām' 'yāṃ jamadagniḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ kācamācīphalabhṛṅgarājābhyāṃ sahodakamabhimantrya rātrau brāhme muhūrte'vasiñcati /
4.7.28.[9]	tenodakena purā kākasampātādavanakṣatre'vasiñcati /
4.7.28.[10]	samāptaṃ keśavṛddhikaraṇaṃ keśajananaṃ khalatikeśajananaṃ keśadṛḍhīkaraṇaṃ palitanāśanaṃ bhaiṣajyam //
4.7.28.[11]	saptamī kaṇḍikā //31 //
4.8.0.[1]	jambhagṛhīte bhaiṣajyamucyate
4.8.1.[1]	'yaste stanaḥ' ityṛcā stanamabhimantrya bālakāya prayacchati pānārtham patiḥ karoti kartā vā karoti /
4.8.1.[2]	jambhagṛhīte bhaiṣajyam /
4.8.1.[3]	duḥkhanāśane bhaiṣajyam //
4.8.2.[1]	'yaste stanaḥ' ityṛcā priyaṅgutaṇḍulānabhyavadugdhānabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.8.2.[2]	bālakaṃ mātaraṃ vā pāyayati /
4.8.2.[3]	yatropari duhyate te'bhyavadugdhāḥ /
4.8.2.[4]	jambhagṛhīte duḥkhanāśe ca bhaiṣajyam //
4.8.2.[5]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyamucyate
4.8.3.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'agnāviṣṇū' iti dvābhyāṃ mauñjeḥ pāśairvyādhitaṃ baddhvā śarapiñjūlībhiḥ sahodakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
4.8.3.[2]	mārjanācamane ca /
4.8.3.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
4.8.3.[4]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.8.3.[5]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'somārudrā vi vṛhatam' iti dvābhyāmudakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tato mauñjeḥ parvasu vyādhita baddhvā darbhapiñjūlībhiḥ sahodakaghaṭenāplāvayati /
4.8.3.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
4.8.3.[7]	sarvabhaiṣajyam /
4.8.3.[8]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sinīvāli' iti navabhirṛgbhirudakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya mauñjeḥ parvasu baddhvā piñjūlībhirāplāvayati /
4.8.3.[9]	mārjanācamane ca smartavye sarvatra sarvabhaiṣajyam /
4.8.3.[10]	'vi te muñcāmi raśanām' iti dvābhyāmudakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya mauñjeḥ parvasu baddhvā piñjūlībhirāplāvayati /
4.8.3.[11]	ājyatantram /
4.8.3.[12]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'śumbhanī' 'muñcantu mā' iti dvābhyāmudakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya mauñjeḥ pāśaiḥ parvasu baddhvā piñjūlībhirāplāvayati /
4.8.3.[13]	tata uttaratantram //
4.8.4.[1]	'agnāviṣṇū' iti dvābhyāṃ piñjūlībhiḥ sahodakamabhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.8.4.[2]	'somārudrā' iti dvābhyāmudakamabhimantrya vyādhitamavasiñcati /
4.8.4.[3]	sarvabhaiṣajyam /
4.8.4.[4]	'sinīvāli' iti navabhirṛgbhirudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.8.4.[5]	'vi te muñcāmi' iti dvābhyāmudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.8.4.[6]	'śumbhanī' iti dvābhyāmudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
4.8.4.[7]	sarvatra mauñjaiḥ pāśairaṅgulītrayaṃ baddhvā tat āplāvanamavasevanaṃ ca sarvatra kuryāt /
4.8.4.[8]	asminnadhikāre āplāvane'vasecane ca mārjanamācamanaṃ ca sarvatra /
4.8.4.[9]	samāptāni sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyāni //
4.8.4.[10]	vṛścikabhaiṣajyamucyate

4.8.6.[1]	'tiraścirājeḥ' iti sūktena kṣetramṛttikāṃ jīvakoṣaṇyāṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.8.6.[2]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'tiraścirājeḥ' ityaṣṭarcena valmīkamṛttikāṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /

4.8.7.[2]	vṛścikabhaiṣajyam /

4.8.7.[5]	'tiraścirājeḥ' ityaṣṭarcena valmīkamṛttikāmabhimantrya pāyayati /

4.8.8.[1]	'apacitāṃ lohinīnām' iti dve /
4.8.8.[2]	'ā susrasaḥ' ityekā /
4.8.8.[3]	etābhistisṛbhirvaṃśadhanuṣā kṛṣṇorṇāmayīṃ jyāṃ kṛtvā citritena śareṇa gaṇḍamālāṃ vidhyati pratyṛcam /
4.8.8.[4]	trayaḥ śarā bhavanti //
4.8.9.[1]	'yā graivyā apacitaḥ' iti caturthyā ṛcā caturthena śareṇa gaṇḍamālāmabhinidhāya vidhyatyāhanti /
4.8.9.[2]	caturthaśareṇa gaṇḍamālāṃ praśleṣayati /
4.8.9.[3]	śarasya svaṃ bhallaṃ bahirvarjayitvā //
4.8.10.[1]	'apacitām' iti dve 'ā susrasaḥ' iti tṛtīyā 'yā graivyāḥ' iti caturthī etābhiścatasṛbhiḥ śarakṛṣṇorṇājyāvajvālitamudakamabhimantryoṣākāle rātriśeṣe tenodakenāvasiñcati vyādhitam /
4.8.10.[2]	dvividhā gaṇḍamālā /

4.8.26-27.[45]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /

4.8.26-27.[48]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvāṃholiṅgena gaṇenodapātraṃ sampātya tenodakena samprokṣati /

4.8.26-27.[51]	sarvabhaiṣajyam /
4.8.26-27.[52]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvāṃholiṅgena saptabhiḥ pratīkairudapātraṃ sampātyābhimantrya vyādhitamāplāvayati /
4.8.26-27.[53]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.8.26-27.[54]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
4.8.26-27.[55]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvāṃholiṅgena gaṇena sapta kāmpīlapuṭānudakena pūrayitvā sampātyābhimantrya pratyṛcaṃ vyādhitamavasiñcati paścādapavidhyati puṭān /
4.8.26-27.[56]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.8.26-27.[57]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvāṃholiṅgena gaṇena catura udapātre sampātānānayati dvau pṛthivyāmāvapati tau pratyāhṛtyāplāvayati /
4.8.26-27.[58]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.8.26-27.[59]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvāṃholiṅgena gaṇenodapātraṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /

4.8.26-27.[335]	evaṃ sarvavyādhiṣu /
4.8.26-27.[336]	tantraṃ kṛtvāṃholiṅgena gaṇena muñjaśiro rajjvā badhnāti /
4.8.26-27.[337]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.8.26-27.[338]	sarvabhaiṣajyam /
4.8.26-27.[339]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvāṃholiṅgena pramehaṇaṃ badhnāti /
4.8.26-27.[340]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.8.26-27.[341]	athavā taiḥ sūktaiḥ sarvāṇi kartavyāni /
4.8.26-27.[342]	athavāṃholiṅgena gaṇena kartavyāni sarvāṇi /
4.8.26-27.[343]	samidha ādadhāti /
4.8.26-27.[344]	ājyaṃ juhotītyevamādisarvabhaiṣajyam /
4.8.26-27.[345]	yānīha karmāṇi paṭhitāni tāni sarvāṇyaṃholiṅgena kartavyāni /
4.8.26-27.[346]	yāni vaidyakeṣvajīrṇaprabhavāni rogajātāni carakabāhaḍasuśruteṣu paṭhyante teṣu tatpaṭhitāni sarvāṇi vyādhiṣvauṣadhāni /
4.8.26-27.[347]	aṃholiṅgena gaṇena samāmnātam /
4.8.26-27.[348]	ajīrṇaprabhavā rogā iti sambhave kāryāṇi /
4.8.26-27.[349]	bandhanapāyanācamaneṣu badhnāti /
4.8.26-27.[350]	dhūpanasnānābhyañjanamardanapathyabhojana- vilepanavipulāñjanāvasecanaśayanādīni tānyaṃholiṅgena saṃskartavyāni /
4.8.26-27.[351]	abhimantrya kartavyānītyarthaḥ /
4.8.26-27.[352]	abhimantraṇaṃ saṃskāraḥ sarvatra kartavya ityarthaḥ /
4.8.26-27.[353]	'sarvāṇyabhimantryāṇi' iti vacanāt /
4.8.26-27.[354]	bandhane tantram /
4.8.26-27.[355]	yāni svaśāstrapaṭhitāni tānyaṃholiṅgena kartavyāni /
4.8.26-27.[356]	paraśāstrapaṭhitāni vaidyakapaṭhitāni ca tāni sarvāṇi kartavyāni /
4.8.26-27.[357]	sarvatra tantraṃ vā yathāsambhavaṃ yojyam /
4.8.26-27.[358]	tathā coktaṃ mūlakauśikagranthe /
4.8.26-27.[359]	oṣadhibandhanaṃ paṭhitaṃ tadaṃholiṅgena gaṇena kartavyam /
4.8.26-27.[360]	ājyatantramadhye sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.8.26-27.[361]	tatraivoktaṃ khananavidhānena bandhanaṃ ca sarvatra 'āśyabandhyāplavanayānabhakṣyāṇi sampātavanti' 'sarvāṇyabhimantryāṇi' iti vacanāt /
4.8.26-27.[362]	tathā coktam 'srajenauṣadhikhananaṃ vyākhyātam' /
4.8.26-27.[363]	oṣadhikhananaṃ vidhānenaiva /
4.8.26-27.[364]	bandhanamapi vidhānenaiva /
4.8.26-27.[365]	tathā gopatha uktam /
4.8.26-27.[366]	vaidyakajyotiṣapurāṇeṣu bandhanapāyanasnānādiṣvaṃholiṅgaḥ sarvatra prayoktavyaḥ /
4.8.26-27.[367]	adharmasamudbhavatvādroganāma /
4.8.26-27.[368]	hastivaidyakāśvavaidyakeṣūktametadeva bhaiṣajyam /
4.8.26-27.[369]	mantraviśeṣakṛto viśeṣaḥ /
4.8.26-27.[370]	anyathā kriyamāṇe dṛṣṭādṛṣṭeṣūpakāro nāsti /
4.8.26-27.[371]	śūdreṇaiva jyotiṣṭome na dṛṣṭaṃ nāpyadṛṣṭam /
4.8.26-27.[372]	dvividhā vyādhayaḥ āhāranimittā adharmanimittāśca /
4.8.26-27.[373]	āhāreṇa vyādhirutpadyate yastatra vaidyakam /
4.8.26-27.[374]	adharmeṇotpanne vyādhau vedoktena vidhānenādharmaśamanaṃ bhavati /
4.8.26-27.[375]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyāni samāptāni /
4.8.26-27.[376]	aṣṭottaraśatavyādhyapanodanāni vināśakāni //
4.8.26-27.[377]	atha bhaiṣajyāni iti yāni sūktāni bhaiṣajyāni kānicitpaṭhitāni tāni sarvāṇyupadhāne upasthāne ca viniyojyāni tatra tatra vyādhau rudrabhāṣyamate /
4.8.26-27.[378]	upadadhītetyanādeśa ājyasamitpuroḍāśapayaudaudanapāyasapaśuvrīhiyavatiladhānā- karambhaśaṣkulya etāni havīṃṣi jānīyāt /
4.8.26-27.[379]	hastahomatvāt tantravikalpaḥ /
4.8.26-27.[380]	upasthānaṃ cādityasya /
4.8.26-27.[381]	anvārabdhe yajamāne sarvatra homābhimantraṇam /
4.8.26-27.[382]	yathāsambhavaṃ tantrasambandhaḥ /
4.8.26-27.[383]	upadhānamupasthānaṃ ca kartavyam /
4.8.26-27.[384]	samāptāni bhaiṣajyāni //
4.8.26-27.[385]	atha strīkarmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
4.8.28.[1]	putrakāmāyai striyai mṛtāpatyāyai ca rajonāśe ca śāntirucyate /
4.8.28.[2]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti sūktena śāntauṣadhiṃ sahodakamabhimantrya strīmavasiñcati //

4.10.0.[1]	atha vandhyāprajananakaraṇamucyate
4.10.1.[1]	'idaṃ janāsaḥ' iti sūktena śiṃśapāśākhāsūpaviṣṭāyai śāntyauṣadhisahitamudakamabhimantrya vandhyāmavasiñcati //
4.10.2.[1]	tato gṛhe'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'idaṃ janāsaḥ' iti sūktena puroḍāśapramandālaṅkārān sampātavataḥ prayacchati /
4.10.2.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.10.2.[3]	samāptaṃ vandhyā kākavandhyā ca prajananakarma //
4.10.2.[4]	atha mṛtāpatyāyāḥ stryāstasyāḥ śāntirucyate
4.10.3.[1]	garbhāsrāve jātamātre mṛte vā stryāṃ vā puruṣe vā bāle vā yūni vā mṛte idaṃ karma /
4.10.3.[2]	trīṇi maṇḍapāni prāgdvārāṇi kṛtvaikasmin maṇḍape'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'niḥsālām' iti sūktena tataḥ strī kṛṣṇaṃ vāsaḥ paridhāya //
4.10.4.[1]	tata udapātre sampātyābhimantrya palāśapatre sīsaṃ kṛtvā sīseṣūttarasampātānānayati //
4.10.5.[1]	sīseṣūpari strīmadhiṣṭhāpya tenodapātreṇāplāvayati //
4.10.6.[1]	kṛṣṇavastraṃ tasmin maṇḍape nidhāya //
4.10.7.[1]	tata uttaratantram kṛtvā maṇḍapamagninā jvālayati //
4.10.8-9.[1]	tata dvitīyamaṇḍapa evaṃ kṛtvā śvetavastraṃ paridhānaṃ kṛtvā śiṃśapāśākhāsūpaveśya strīṃ 'niḥsālām' iti sūktena śāntauṣadhibhistadudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati snapanaṃ karoti /
4.10.8-9.[2]	tato gṛha āgatyājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'niḥsālām' iti sūktena puroḍāśapramandālaṅkārān sampātavataḥ prayacchati /
4.10.8-9.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
4.10.8-9.[4]	trimaṇḍapādyekaṃ karma //
4.10.10.[1]	ekaṃ maṇḍapaṃ kṛtvā prākpaścimadvāre iṣīkāṃ dvāryopari baddhvā tato 'niḥsālām' iti sūktenaudumbarīḥ samidho mṛtāpatyāyai ādadhāti /
4.10.10.[2]	tantravikalpaḥ /
4.10.10.[3]	mantraṃ kartā brūyāt //

4.10.11.[2]	tato gṛhe'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'niḥsālām' iti sūktena puroḍāśapramandālaṅkārān sampātavataḥ prayacchati /

4.11.0.[1]	puṃsavanānyucyante
4.11.1-2.[1]	nakṣatrakalpa uktāni punnakṣatrāṇi //

4.11.3.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yena vehat' iti sūktena śaramaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti puṇyāhānte /
4.11.3.[7]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
4.11.4.[1]	'yena vehat' iti sūktena phālacamase sārūpavatsāyā dugdhe vrīhiyavāvavadhāya mūrcchayitvādhyaṇḍe bṛhatīpalāśavidaryau vā ekatra piṣṭvābhimantrya dakṣiṇenāṅguṣṭhena dakṣiṇasyāṃ nāsikāyāṃ nastaṃ dadāti /

4.11.5-6.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'parvatāddivaḥ' iti sūktenāgamakṛśaraṃ carudvayaṃ śrapayitvaikaṃ caruṃ sampātyābhimantrya dvitīyaṃ caruṃ yugachidreṇa sampātyābhimantrya tataḥ prāśanam /
4.11.5-6.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
4.11.7.[1]	kelūnāṃśca palāśatsarūn nivṛtte nighṛṣya 'parvatāddivaḥ' iti sūktenābhimantrya śiśne ādhāya /
4.11.7.[2]	tato maithunaṃ karoti /
