4.11.7.[4]	punaḥpuṃsavanamucyate
4.11.8.[1]	'śamīmaśvatthaḥ' iti sūktenāgniṃ mathitvā tato'gniṃ sarpiṣi nikṣipya ghṛtamabhimantrya stryā dakṣiṇanāsikāyāṃ nastaṃ dadāti dakṣiṇenāṅguṣṭhena //
4.11.9.[1]	tato'gniṃ mathitvā tato madhumanthe'gniṃ nikṣipya 'śamīmaśvatthaḥ' iti sūktenābhimantrya pāyayati strīm //
4.11.10.[1]	'śamīmaśvatthaḥ' iti sūktena śamīgarbhāśvatthasyāgniṃ kṛṣṇorṇayā veṣṭayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.11.10.[2]	ājyatantre /
4.11.10.[3]	samāptaṃ punaḥpuṃsavanam //
4.11.10.[4]	atha garbhādhānamucyate
4.11.11.[1]	'yantāsi' iti sūktena hastāvartaṃ kaṅkaṇādikaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.11.11.[2]	ājyatantre /
4.11.11.[3]	samāptaṃ garbhādhānam //
4.11.11.[4]	atha garbhadṛṃhaṇāny ucyante
4.11.12-13.[1]	'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' ityekayā dhanurjyāṃ trirudgrathya sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.11.12-13.[2]	ājyatantram /
4.11.12-13.[3]	'yatheyaṃ pṛthivī' iti sūktam /
4.11.12-13.[4]	'acyutā dyauḥ' iti sūktam /
4.11.12-13.[5]	dvābhyāṃ dhanurjyāṃ trirudgrathya sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti striyāḥ /
4.11.12-13.[6]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
4.11.14.[1]	'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' ityekayā kṣetraloṣṭamṛttikāmabhimantrya prāśayati /
4.11.14.[2]	'yatheyaṃ pṛthivī' 'acyutā' iti sūktābhyāṃ kṣetraloṣṭamṛttikāmabhimantrya prāśayati garbhiṇīṃ pratyṛcam //
4.11.15.[1]	'ṛdhaṅmantraḥ' ityekayā kṛṣṇasikatā abhimantrya garbhiṇyāḥ śayanaṃ parikirati /
4.11.15.[2]	'yatheyaṃ pṛthivī' 'acyutā' iti sūktābhyāṃ śyāmasikatā abhimantrya pratyṛcaṃ garbhiṇyāḥ śayanaṃ parikirati /
4.11.15.[3]	jambhagṛhītāya prathamāvarjam /
4.11.15.[4]	samāptāni garbhadṛṃhaṇāni //
4.11.16.[1]	'dhātā dadhātu' iti catasṛbhirgarbhiṇyā udaramabhimantrayate /
4.11.16.[2]	brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāṇāṃ jātyādharmasvajātyādharmabalavīryādiyuktāḥ putrā bhavanti /
4.11.16.[3]	vīro jāyate /
4.11.16.[4]	vīrakarma samāptam //
4.11.16.[5]	atha prajananakarma
4.11.17.[1]	'prajāpatirjanayatu' iti sūktena prajākāmāyāḥ striya utsaṅge ājyaṃ juhoti /
4.11.17.[2]	prajananakarma //
4.11.18.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prajāpatirjanayatu' ityṛcā raktacchāgamāṃsaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
4.11.18.[2]	tata uttaratantram //
4.11.19.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prajāpatiḥ' ityṛcodakulijaṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvā garbhiṇīṃ parihṛtya madhye ninayati /
4.11.19.[2]	uttaratantram /
4.11.19.[3]	tantre surākulijaṃ sampātya strīṃ parihṛtyāgre ninayati /
4.11.19.[4]	bhaktaṃ surāṃ prapāṃ sampātyābhimantrya prajākāmāyai prayacchati tantre /
4.11.19.[5]	samāptaṃ prajākarma vandhyāyāḥ //
4.11.19.[6]	atha sīmantakarmocyate
4.11.20.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yau te mātā' ityarthasūktena śvetapītasarṣapān sampātyābhimantrya puṇyāhānte badhnāti /
4.11.20.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.11.20.[3]	samāptaṃ sīmantonnayanam /
4.11.20.[4]	samāptāni dṛṃhaṇāni //
4.11.20.[5]	atha strīvaśīkaraṇamucyate
4.11.21.[1]	vṛkṣatvak śarakhaṇḍaṃ tagaramañjanaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ jyeṣṭhīmadhu śleṣmavātasaṃśrayagatatṛṇametāni dravyāṇyājyamadhye peṣayitvā 'yathedaṃ bhūmyāḥ' iti sūktenābhimantrya striyā aṅgaṃ samālabhate /
4.11.21.[2]	rucyartham /
4.11.21.[3]	'yathā vṛkṣaṃ libujā' 'vāñcha me tanvam' iti sūktābhyāṃ vṛkṣatvak tagaramañjanaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ jyeṣṭhīmadhu vātasambhramatṛṇānyetāni dravyāṇyājyenāloḍyābhimantrya jāyāṃ pralimpati /
4.11.21.[4]	'yathāyaṃ vāhaḥ' ityetāni dravyāṇyāloḍya ghṛtena tato'bhimantrya jāyāṃ pralimpati /
4.11.21.[5]	vaśīkaraṇakāmaḥ //
4.11.22.[1]	'uttudastvā' iti sūktaṃ japitvā aṅgulyā nudati bhāryām udare pṛṣṭau rucyarthī //
4.11.23.[1]	'uttudastvā' iti sūktenaikaviṃśati badarīkaṇṭakānādadhāti /
4.11.23.[2]	ghṛtenābhyajya //
4.11.24.[1]	ekaviṃśatibadarīprāntāni sūtreṇa veṣṭayitvā 'uttudastvā' iti sūktena sakṛt juhoti /
4.11.24.[2]	rucyarthī //
4.11.25.[1]	'uttudastvā' iti sūktena kuṣṭhaṃ navanītenābhyajyāgnau prakṣipati prātarmadhyandine sāyaṃ ca /
4.11.25.[2]	ekarātrau vā //
4.11.26.[1]	'uttudastvā' iti sūktena khaṭvādhomukhapaṭṭikāṃ gṛhītvā saṃviśati svapiti /
4.11.26.[2]	trirātraṃ karma //
4.11.27.[1]	'uttudastvā' iti sūktenoṣṇodakaṃ tripāde śikye prabaddhāṅguṣṭhābhyāmardayañchete /
4.11.27.[2]	rucyarthī //
4.11.28.[1]	pratikṛtimāvalekhanīṃ dārbhyaṣeṇa bhāṅgajyena kaṇṭakaśalyayolūkapatrayāsitālakāṇḍayā 'uttudastvā' iti sūktena hṛdaye vidhyati /
4.11.28.[2]	samāptāni saṃvananāni vaśīkaraṇāni /
4.11.28.[3]	kāmaviṣaye striyā utsāho bhavati /
4.11.28.[4]	tathā ca yasya kāmo nāsti tasya kāmo'tiśayena kāmakaraṇamityarthaḥ /
4.11.28.[5]	anena karmaṇā kāmo bhavati //
4.11.28.[6]	ekādaśamī kaṇḍikā //35 //
4.12.0.[1]	svāpanavighnaśamanam /
4.12.0.[2]	strīsvāpanakarmocyate
4.12.1-2.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'sahasraśṛṅgaḥ' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātya śālāṃ samprokṣati /
4.12.1-2.[2]	śayanaśālāṃ sarvāṃ prokṣati /
4.12.1-2.[3]	abhyantaradvāre śeṣamudakaṃ nyubjati /
4.12.1-2.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.12.1-2.[5]	svāpanakarma //
4.12.3-4.[1]	'sahasraśṛṅgaḥ' iti sūktena nagno bhūtvolūkhalamabhimantrayate /
4.12.3-4.[2]	'sahasraśṛṅgaḥ' iti sūktena gṛhasyottaraṃ koṇamabhimantrayate /
4.12.3-4.[3]	'sahasraśṛṅgaḥ' iti sūktena striyāḥ khaṭavāyā dakṣiṇaṃ pādamabhimantrayate /
4.12.3-4.[4]	'sahasraśṛṅgaḥ' iti sūktena khaṭvāyā rajjumabhimantrayate /
4.12.3-4.[5]	karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
4.12.3-4.[6]	strīsvāpanam /
4.12.3-4.[7]	puruṣasya viṣaye kāma utpadyate /
4.12.3-4.[8]	kāmaviṣaye strīsvāpanaṃ samāptam /
4.12.3-4.[9]	lajjāpracchādanaṃ na bhavatītyarthaḥ /
4.12.3-4.[10]	svāpanaṃ sarveṣāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ nidrākāmānāṃ nidrā bhavati /
4.12.3-4.[11]	maithunamācarato vighnaṃ na bhavati /
4.12.3-4.[12]	antaḥsvāpanamityucyate /
4.12.3-4.[13]	maithunānnidrecchā bhavatītyarthaḥ //
4.12.3-4.[14]	atha palāyinyāḥ striyo bandhanakarma tantrakrameṇa kriyate /
4.12.3-4.[15]	rajjuḥ kalpate /
4.12.3-4.[16]	tadrajjuveṣṭanamucyate /
4.12.3-4.[17]	palāyamānāyā nirodhakaraṇaṃ karmocyate
4.12.5-6.[1]	'asthād dyauḥ' iti sūktena dvitīyena rajjuveṣṭanamabhimantrya vaṃśāgre baddhvā madhyamasthūṇe badhnāti //
4.12.7-9.[1]	'asthād dyauḥ' iti sūktena śayanapādamabhimantryotpale ca badhnāti /
4.12.7-9.[2]	'asthād dyauḥ' iti sūktenāṅkuśena tilāñjuhoti /
4.12.7-9.[3]	palāyinyāḥ striyā bandhanakarmāṇi samāptāni /
4.12.7-9.[4]	nirodhakaraṇāni //
4.12.7-9.[5]	jāyāpatyorakrodhakaraṇamucyate
4.12.10.[1]	'idaṃ yatpreṇyaḥ śiraḥ' iti sūktena strīśiraḥkarṇaṃ cānumantrayate /
4.12.10.[2]	puruṣasya ca //
4.12.11.[1]	'idaṃ yatpreṇyaḥ śiraḥ' iti sūktena keśān dhārayati /
4.12.11.[2]	samāptaṃ strīpuruṣayor akrodhakaraṇam //
4.12.11.[3]	saubhāgyakaraṇamucyate
4.12.12.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bhagena mā śāṃśapena' iti sūktena śaṅkhapuṣpīmūlamoṣadhivat khātvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.12.12.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.12.12.[3]	'bhagena mā' iti sūktena sauvacalapuṣpamabhimantrya yasya saubhāgyamicchati tasya śirasi baddhvā sa maithunaṃ karoti /
4.12.12.[4]	samāptaṃ saubhāgyakaraṇam //
4.12.12.[5]	saubhāgyasaṃvananamucyate /
4.12.12.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'nyastikā rurohitha' iti sūktena sauvarcalamūlaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti puṣpaṃ ca śirasi dadāti /
4.12.12.[7]	tata uttaratantram /
4.12.12.[8]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'idaṃ khanāmi' iti sūktena sauvarcalamūlaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
4.12.12.[9]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
4.12.12.[10]	sauvarcalaṃ sūryaveleti prasiddhā /
4.12.12.[11]	'idaṃ khanāmi' iti sūktena sauvarcalamūlamabhimantrya badhnāti /
4.12.12.[12]	tantre /
4.12.12.[13]	śirasi striyaḥ /
4.12.12.[14]	samāptaṃ patirucikaraṇam //
4.12.12.[15]	duṣṭāstrīvaśīkaraṇamucyate
4.12.13.[1]	'rathajitām' iti sūktaistribhirmāṣānabhimantrya striyā ākrameṣu vapati /
4.12.13.[2]	'rathajitām' iti tribhiḥ sūktaiścaṇakānabhimantrya striyā ākrameṣu vapati /
4.12.13.[3]	khaṭvāsthāne vā gṛhe śayanadeśe vā //
4.12.14.[1]	'rathajitām' iti tribhiḥ sūktaiḥ śarabhṛṣṭīrādīptā abhimantrya pratidiśamabhyasyati /
4.12.14.[2]	eṣu patiḥ pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvā 'rathajitām' iti tribhisūktaiḥ hṛdaye vidhyati dārbhyūṣeṇa bhāṅgajyena /
4.12.14.[3]	samāptāni duṣṭastrīvaśīkaraṇāni /
4.12.14.[4]	puruṣo vā strīṇāṃ dveṣaṃ karoti /
4.12.14.[5]	anena karmaṇā śāntirbhavati //
4.12.14.[6]	atha striyo vā puruṣasya vā daurbhāgyakaraṇamucyate
4.12.15.[1]	striyāḥ puṣpamālāniṣpramandadantadhāvanakeśāstānekīkṛtya /
4.12.15.[2]	jvarahatagocarmaṇāveṣṭya 'bhagamasyāḥ' iti sūktenābhimantryolūkhaladaraṇe triśile nikhanati /
4.12.15.[3]	tata ulūkhale dadāti /
4.12.15.[4]	daurbhāgyakāmaḥ /
4.12.15.[5]	mālāniṣpramandadantadhāvanakeśāstānekīkṛtya 'bhagamasyāḥ' iti sūktenābhimantrya /
4.12.15.[6]	dahanaghātitā gauranustaraṇītyucyate /
4.12.15.[7]	īśānahatā jvarahatetyucyate /
4.12.15.[8]	tasyāścarmaṇāveṣṭya tata ulūkhaladaraṇe triśile nikhanati /
4.12.15.[9]	tata ulūkhale dadāti upari /
4.12.15.[10]	yasya daurbhāgyaṃ kriyate tasyaitāni gṛhṇīyāt //
4.12.16.[1]	'bhagam asyā varcaḥ' iti sūktena strīpuṣpamālāṃ hastena mathitvā strīṃ dṛṣṭvānvāha /
4.12.16.[2]	japatītyarthaḥ /
4.12.16.[3]	daurbhāgyakāmaḥ //
4.12.17.[1]	'bhagamasyā varcaḥ' iti sūktena trīṇi keśamaṇḍalāni kṛṣṇasūtreṇa veṣṭayitvābhimantrya triśile'śmottarāṇi vyatyāsamaśmānaṃ śālāyā upari dadāti /
4.12.17.[2]	vyatyāsena nikhanati /
4.12.17.[3]	daurbhāgyakāmaḥ /
4.12.17.[4]	samāptaṃ daurbhāgyakaraṇam //
4.12.17.[5]	duṣṭastrī veśyākulaṭādi /
4.12.17.[6]	atha tasyāḥ saubhāgyakaraṇamucyate
4.12.18.[1]	'yaṃ te bhagaṃ nicakhnuḥ' ityṛcā śilā utkhanati /
4.12.18.[2]	utpāṭayati /
4.12.18.[3]	'bhagamasyāḥ' ityanena sūktena yatkṛtaṃ tadanayā vinaśyati /
4.12.18.[4]	samāptaṃ yasyā daurbhāgyaṃ kṛtaṃ tasyāḥ saubhāgyakaraṇam //
4.12.18.[5]	atha sapatnījayakarmāṇyucyante /
4.12.18.[6]	bhartrā saha vidveṣo bhavatītyarthaḥ
4.12.19.[1]	'imāṃ khanāmi' iti sūktena bāṇāparṇīṃ raktavarṇāyā ajāyā dadhyudakena sannīya tato'bhimantrya sapatnīśayane parikirati /
4.12.19.[2]	sapatnīvidveṣaṇaṃ bhartrā saha //
4.12.20.[1]	'abhi te'dhām' iti pādena bāṇāparṇīpatrāṇyabhimantrya śayanādhastāt prakṣipati /
4.12.20.[2]	sapatnīśayane jayakāmaḥ //
4.12.21.[1]	'upa te'dhām' iti pādena bāṇāparṇī-oṣadhipatrāṇyabhimantrya sapatnīśayana upari kṣipati /
4.12.21.[2]	bāṇāparṇī māsikā loke prasiddhā /
4.12.21.[3]	samāptāni sapatnījayakarmāṇi /
4.12.21.[4]	bhartrā saha vidveṣo bhavatītyarthaḥ //
4.12.21.[5]	atha strīviṣaye kāma utpanne kāmavināśakānyucyante
4.12.22.[1]	'apa naḥ śośucadagham' iti sūktenāsaṅkhyātāḥ śarkarā abhimantrya parikiran vrajati /
4.12.22.[2]	yasmin deśe kāma utpannaḥ tat sthānaṃ yāvat /
4.12.22.[3]	strī vā puruṣo vā //
4.12.23.[1]	'apa naḥ śośucat' iti sūktenāsaṅkhyātāḥ śarkarā haste gṛhītvā parikiran vrajati /
4.12.23.[2]	strīgṛhaṃ yāvat kāmotpattideśam //
4.12.24.[1]	'apa naḥ śośucat' iti sūktenāsaṅkhyātāḥ śarkarā haste gṛhītvā japati /
4.12.24.[2]	kāmo vinaśyati /
4.12.24.[3]	strīkāmaṃ yāvat /
4.12.24.[4]	strīṇāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ kāmavināśakāni samāptāni //
4.12.24.[5]	strīviṣaya īrṣyāvināśakānyucyante
4.12.25.[1]	'īrṣyāyā dhrājiṃ prathamām' iti sūktenerṣyāluṃ dṛṣṭvā japati /
4.12.25.[2]	īrṣyā vinaśyati /
4.12.25.[3]	'janādviśvajanīnāt' iti dvyṛcamīrṣyāluṃ dṛṣṭvā japati /
4.12.25.[4]	'tvāṣṭreṇāham' ityṛcerṣyāluṃ dṛṣṭvā japati /
4.12.25.[5]	īrṣyā vinaśyati /
4.12.25.[6]	'īrṣyāyā dhrājim' iti sūktena saktumanthamabhimantryerṣyālukāya dadāti /
4.12.25.[7]	īrṣyāvināśakāmaḥ /
4.12.25.[8]	'janādviśvajanīnāt' ityṛcā manthamabhimantryerṣyālukāya dadāti bhakṣaṇārtham /
4.12.25.[9]	'tvāṣṭreṇāham' ityṛcā manthamabhimantryerṣyālukāya dadāti /
4.12.25.[10]	'īrṣyāyā dhrājim' iti sūktamīrṣyāluṃ spṛṣṭvā japati /
4.12.25.[11]	'janādviśvajanīnāt' ityṛcerṣyāluṃ spṛṣṭvā japati /
4.12.25.[12]	'tvāṣṭreṇāham' ityṛcerṣyāluṃ spṛṣṭvā japati //
4.12.26.[1]	'īrṣyāyā dhrājim' iti sūktena kaṭipradeśe vakṣaṇe khalvāmabhimantrya dhamati /
4.12.26.[2]	īrṣyāvināśanam //
4.12.27.[1]	'agner iva' ity ṛcā paraśunā taptena kvāthitamudakamabhimantrya pāyayati /
4.12.27.[2]	samāptānīrṣyāvināśakāni /
4.12.27.[3]	strīviṣaye //
4.12.27.[4]	atha manyuvināśakānyucyante strīviṣaye puruṣasya
4.12.28.[1]	'ava jyām iva' iti sūktena manyumantaṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvāśmānam abhimantrya hastena gṛhṇāti /
4.12.28.[2]	sarvatra kartā karma karoti //
4.12.29.[1]	'sakhāyāviva sacāvahai' ityekāṃ japitvāśmānaṃ bhūmau nidadhāti //
4.12.30.[1]	'abhi tiṣṭhāmi te manyum' ityekāṃ japitvāśmanopari niṣṭhīvati //
4.12.31.[1]	'ava jyāmiva' iti sūktena manyumataḥ puruṣasya chāyāyāṃ dhanurabhimantrya sajyaṃ karoti /
4.12.31.[2]	caṭāpayatītyarthaḥ /
4.12.31.[3]	strīviṣaye puruṣasya manyur bhavati /
4.12.31.[4]	puruṣaviṣaye strīṇāṃ vā /
4.12.31.[5]	samāptāni strīviṣaye manyuvināśakāni //
4.12.31.[6]	atha sarvaviṣaye manyuvināśakānyucyante
4.12.32.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ayaṃ darbhaḥ' iti sūktena darbhamūlamoṣadhivat khātvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti manyuke /
4.12.32.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
4.12.32.[3]	manyuvināśam /
4.12.32.[4]	strīviṣaye manyuvināśo bhavati /
4.12.32.[5]	samāptāni strīmanyuvināśakāni //
4.12.32.[6]	avīrajananam ucyate /
4.12.32.[7]	aputrajananam ity arthaḥ
4.12.33-34.[1]	'agne jātān' ityacāśvatarīmūtreṇa pāṣāṇaṃ nighṛṣya tato'bhimantrya bhaktena saha dadāti vidveṣiṇya parastryai /
4.12.33-34.[2]	'agne jātān' ityṛcāśvatarīmūtramaśmamaṇḍalābhyāṃ saṅghṛṣyābhimantryālaṅkāraṃ samālabhate parastryai vidveṣiṇyai /
4.12.33-34.[3]	'agne jātān' ityṛcā sīmantamanvīkṣate parastryai /
4.12.33-34.[4]	duhitā vā puruṣo veti /
4.12.33-34.[5]	kṛṣṇo vā jāyate /
4.12.33-34.[6]	samāptānyavīrajananāni //
4.12.33-34.[7]	atha vandhyākaraṇamucyate /
4.12.33-34.[8]	'prānyāntsapatnān' iti tṛcenāśvatarīmūtramaśmamaṇḍalābhyāṃ saṅghṛṣyābhimantrya bhakte dadāti /
4.12.33-34.[9]	tadbhaktaṃ parastryai vidveṣiṇyai dadāti bhojanārtham /
4.12.33-34.[10]	'prānyāntsapatnān' iti tṛcenāśvatarīmūtramaśmamaṇḍalābhyāṃ saṅghṛṣyābhimantrya tasyālaṅkārām̐llepayati /
4.12.33-34.[11]	'prānyān' iti tṛcena sīmantamanvīkṣate vidveṣiṇyai /
4.12.33-34.[12]	samāptāni parastrīvandhyākaraṇāni //
4.12.33-34.[13]	jāroccāṭanamucyate
4.12.35.[1]	'api vṛśca' iti sūktaṃ tṛcaṃ jāraṃ dṛṣṭvā japati //
4.12.36.[1]	'api vṛśca' iti sūktena jārapadasthāne bādhakaṃ dhanurvṛścati //
4.12.37.[1]	'api vṛśca' iti tṛcena sūktena pāṣāṇamabhimantrya jāramaithunasthāne prakṣipatyuccāṭanārtham /
4.12.37.[2]	samāptaṃ jāroccāṭanam //
4.12.37.[3]	puruṣasya striyāḥ parasparavidveṣakaraṇānyucyante
4.12.38.[1]	'tṛṣṭikaḥ' iti dvyarcena sūktena bāṇāparṇīṃ lohitājāyā drapsena sannīyābhimantrya śayanamanu parikirati /
4.12.38.[2]	puruṣastrīśayane ca /
4.12.38.[3]	samāptaṃ vidveṣaṇakaraṇaṃ strīpuruṣasyobhayarucivināśakaraṇam //
4.12.38.[4]	atha daurbhāgyakaraṇamucyate
4.12.39-40.[1]	'ā te dade' ityekā /
4.12.39-40.[2]	hṛdayaṃ mukhaṃ vābhimantrayate parastryai /
4.12.39-40.[3]	'ā te dade' ityekāṃ japitvānvāha /
4.12.39-40.[4]	daurbhāgyakaraṇaṃ striyo vā puruṣasya vā /
4.12.39-40.[5]	samāptāni strīkarmakaraṇāni /
4.12.39-40.[6]	tatra bhadraślokaḥ /
4.12.39-40.[7]	bhaiṣajyakarmāṇi proktāni sarvavyādhyupaśāntaye /
4.12.39-40.[8]	strīkarmāṇi tataḥ paścāccaturthe saṃhitāvidhau //
5.1.0.[1]	atha vijñānakarmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
5.1.0.[2]	lābhālābhajayaparājayasukhaduḥkhotkarṣāpakarṣasubhikṣadurbhikṣakṣemākṣemabhayābhayarogārogatrāso'stīti na veti /
5.1.0.[3]	dhanādhanadharmādharmajīvājīvamaraṇāmaraṇadhānyaṃ bhaviṣyati na veti /
5.1.0.[4]	kṣetre bhaviṣyati na veti /
5.1.0.[5]	gṛhe vāso bhaviṣyati neti /
5.1.0.[6]	dhānyaputrapaśuhiraṇyaratnavastrāṇi ca /
5.1.0.[7]	vidyāśāstrādilābho bhaviṣyati na vā /
5.1.0.[8]	jīvitamaraṇe gamanāgamane balābale sadasadyogād /
5.1.0.[9]	vyādhitasya jīvitamaraṇābhyām /
5.1.0.[10]	prasave putrayogāt /
5.1.0.[11]	putre jāte dharmasaṃyogāt /
5.1.0.[12]	mitrāmitrasaṃyogāt /
5.1.0.[13]	grāmo'sti vā na veti /
5.1.0.[14]	puruṣasya vivāho'sti vā na veti /
5.1.0.[15]	saṃvatsare māse vā bhaviṣyati /
5.1.0.[16]	subhagā durbhagā vā /
5.1.0.[17]	gṛhaṃ grāmādi bhaviṣyati na vā /
5.1.0.[18]	adhyayanaṃ bhavati na veti /
5.1.0.[19]	ityādi manasā vācā vā sañcitya tatkarma kuryāt //
5.1.0.[20]	atha vidhānamucyate vijñānakarmaṇām
5.1.1.[1]	'ambayo yanti' iti sūktena rādhyamānaṃ kṣīraudanamabhimantrya tata āsiñcet /
5.1.1.[2]	manasā cintayedvātā cintayet /
5.1.1.[3]	odanaṃ śṛtaṃ bhavedaśṛtaṃ vā bhavet /
5.1.1.[4]	yadi yathācintitaṃ bhavati yadā tasya kāryasiddhirbhaviṣyati jānīyāt /
5.1.1.[5]	athāśaṃsitaṃ bhavati na kāryasiddhirbhaviṣyatīti vidyāt /
5.1.1.[6]	abhimantryāśaṃset /
5.1.1.[7]	yadi pākaścintitastadā pākenārthasiddhiḥ /
5.1.1.[8]	'ambayo yanti' iti sūktenedhmamupasamādhāyābhimantryāyācet /
5.1.1.[9]	utkucanenārthaḥ /
5.1.1.[10]	'ambayo yanti' iti sūktena darbhastambamabhimantryāyācet /
5.1.1.[11]	yatra samaviṣamabhāvenārthasiddhiḥ /
5.1.1.[12]	'ambayo yanti' iti sūktena pūrvedyuḥ pāṭhāmabhimantryāyācet /
5.1.1.[13]	patrāṇāṃ saṅkocenārthasiddhiḥ //
5.1.2.[1]	'ambayo yanti' iti sūktena saṅgrāme pūrvedyurvediṃ kṛtvābhimantryāyācet /
5.1.2.[2]	dvitīye'hani samaviṣamena bhāvena siddhiḥ /
5.1.2.[3]	'ambayo yanti' iti sūktena vyāsakaṣṭādayo'bhimantrya kartavyāni /
5.1.2.[4]	bhoge kevalyādi laukikānyupaśrutaye vyāsāṣṭakā vyāsaḥ kaṣṭādayaḥ /
5.1.2.[5]	anyāni jyotiḥśāstrapaṭhitāni sarvāṇi vijñānāni śāstrāṇyabhimantrya kartavyāni //
5.1.3.[1]	'venastat' iti sūktena pañcagranthiveṇudaṇḍamabhimantryāyācya same dhārayatyabhīṣṭadiśi patanenārthasiddhiḥ /
5.1.3.[2]	'venastat' iti sūkteneṣuṃ sandhāyābhimantryāyācet /
5.1.3.[3]	cintitaprakṣepaṇenārtham /
5.1.3.[4]	'venastat' iti sūktena kumbha udakapūrṇaṃ dugdhaṃ prakṣipyāyācet /
5.1.3.[5]	ūnādhikenārthasiddhiḥ /
5.1.3.[6]	yathācintitaṃ tathā siddhiḥ /

5.1.3.[24]	atha naṣṭadravye parīkṣaṇe kriyamāṇe ca idaṃ karma
5.1.4-5.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā kumbhamahatena pariveṣṭyādhāya śayane 'venastat' iti sūktena kumbhe sampātānānayati /
5.1.4-5.[2]	arajovitte kumāryau yena haretāṃ tato naṣṭam /
5.1.4-5.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
5.1.6.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'venastat' iti sūktenāhatena vastreṇa veṣṭitaṃ halaṃ sampātyābhimantrya yena haretāṃ tato naṣṭam /
5.1.6.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
5.1.6.[3]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'venastat' iti sūktenākṣān kumbhavat kṛtvā sampātya yena haretāṃ tato naṣṭam /
5.1.6.[4]	tata uttaratantram /

5.1.7-12.[1]	ākṛtiloṣṭavalmīkaloṣṭacatuṣpathaloṣṭaśmaśānamṛttikāḥ /

5.1.7-12.[4]	tāṃ mṛttikāsparśanam /

5.2.1.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena durdinamabhimukhamupatiṣṭhate /
5.2.1.[2]	sarvatra durdinavināśakāni //
5.2.2.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena pratyṛcamudakaṃ prakṣipati //
5.2.3.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena khaṅgaṃ gṛhītvopatiṣṭhate'bhimukham /
5.2.3.[2]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktenolmukaṃ gṛhītvopatiṣṭhate sūryasyābhimukhaḥ /

5.2.4.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena nagno lalāṭamunmṛjānaḥ arkamukho bhūtvopatiṣṭhate //
5.2.5.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktenābhyantare praviśyāṅgānyudvartya bahirniṣkramyāṅgārakapāle'gniṃ kṛtvā śigruṃ juhoti /
5.2.5.[2]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena kapāle'gniṃ kṛtvā śarkarāṃ juhoti //
5.2.6.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena paṭerakasamidha ādadhāti sthaṇḍile /
5.2.6.[2]	abhyantare praviśya tata udvartya tato homaḥ /

5.2.6.[4]	durdinamambhādi pāṃśuvṛṣṭyādi /

5.2.6.[6]	samāptāni durdinakarmāṇi /

5.2.6.[8]	vṛṣṭinivāraṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
5.2.7.[1]	'jarāyujaḥ' iti sūktena khadāṃ khātvā khadāṃ triṣparikramyārkaṃ nirlucitaṃ kṛtvā khadāyāṃ prakṣipati sūktāntena /
5.2.7.[2]	tataḥ pāṃśunā khadāṃ pūrayati /
5.2.7.[3]	nāgnim /
5.2.7.[4]	vṛṣṭinivāraṇaṃ samāptam //
5.2.7.[5]	aśaninivāraṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
5.2.8.[1]	'namaste astu vidyute' ityaśanyabhimukhamupatiṣṭhate /
5.2.8.[2]	'yaste pṛthu stanayitnuḥ' ityṛcāśanyabhimukhamupatiṣṭhate /
5.2.8.[3]	'namaste astu vidyute' iti sūktena khaṅgaṃ gṛhītvopatiṣṭhate /
5.2.8.[4]	'namaste astu' iti sūktena daṇḍaṃ gṛhītvopatiṣṭhate //
5.2.9.[1]	'namaste astu' iti sūktena somadarbhakeśānīkuṣṭhalākṣāmañjiṣṭhībadaraharidram etāni dravyāṇi bhūrje kṛtvā manthaśirasi kṛtvābhimantrya kṣetramadhye nikhanati /
5.2.9.[2]	etatkarma kṣetre /
5.2.9.[3]	aśaninivāraṇam //
5.2.9.[4]	ativṛṣṭiranāvṛṣṭiḥ śalabhā mūṣakāḥ śukāḥ /
5.2.9.[5]	svacakraṃ paracakraṃ ca saptaitā ītayaḥ smṛtāḥ //
5.2.9.[6]	samāptāny aśaninivāraṇāni //
5.2.10.[1]	avadīryamāṇe grāme vāvasāne vāgniśaraṇe vā samajyāyāṃ vā gṛhe vā prākāre vā yānyavātarakṣārthaṃ karma vakṣyāmaḥ
5.2.11-13.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'āśānāmāśāpālebhyaḥ' iti sūktena 'asrāmastvā' ityṛcaṃ varjayitvā catuḥpuroḍāśān sampātya gṛhakoṇeṣu nikhanati /

5.2.14.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'āśānāmāśāpālebhyaḥ' iti tṛtīyāvarjena sūktena puroḍāśānaśmanaścobhayān sampātavataḥ karoti /
5.2.14.[2]	sūktasyāṣṭāvāvṛttiḥ //

5.2.23.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' iti prathamena kāṇḍādinā sūktena vedaṃ vā anuvākaṃ vā sūktaṃ vā kalpaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā'dhyayanaṃ kartumicchati tadā tadā sūktaṃ japitvā tato'dhyayanaṃ kuryāt /

5.2.24.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' iti sūktaṃ japati vivāde jayārtham //

5.2.25.[4]	vibhāgakarmocyate
5.2.26.[1]	'mamāgne varco vihaveṣu' iti sūktena cākrikasya rajjumabhimantrya dhārayati hastena /

5.2.26.[3]	iti vivādakarturvadane kalaho na bhavati //

5.2.27.[1]	sabhāstambhanaṃ karma jayakarma /
5.2.27.[2]	tadā sabhāsadadharmādhikaraṇādi jīyate /
5.2.27.[3]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'sabhā ca mā samitiḥ' iti pañcarcena sūktena kṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
5.2.27.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
5.2.27.[5]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'sabhā ca mā' iti puroḍāśaṃ sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati /
5.2.27.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
5.2.27.[7]	'sabhā ca mā' iti pañcarcena rasān sampātyābhimantrya bhakṣayati ājyatantre //
5.2.28.[1]	'sabhā ca mā' iti pañcarcaṃ sūktaṃ japitvā sthūṇāṃ gṛhṇāti /
5.2.28.[2]	'sabhā ca mā' iti sabhāmupatiṣṭhate /
5.2.28.[3]	dharmādhikaraṇamapi jīyate /
5.2.28.[4]	sabhāstambhanam //
5.2.29.[1]	'yadvadāmi' ityṛcaṃ japitvā sabhāṃ vadet /
5.2.29.[2]	'yadvadāmi' ityṛcaṃ japitvā sabhāṃ nirīkṣate /

5.4.0.[1]	atha nadīpravāhavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
5.4.1.[1]	nadīpravāhaṃ khātvā 'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena prasiñcan vrajati /
5.4.1.[2]	udakaṃ prakṣipati vahanikāmadhyapravāhasthāne /
5.4.1.[3]	anyatraiva vahanaṃ kāryam /
5.4.1.[4]	vahanavirodho na bhavati /
5.4.1.[5]	iti nadīkarma /
5.4.1.[6]	nadīpravāhaṃ khātvā tasmin pravāha idaṃ karoti //
5.4.2.[1]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena kāśamabhimantrya tatra khāte ropayati /
5.4.2.[2]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena divi sevālaparṇīmabhimantrya ropayati nadīpravāhe /
5.4.2.[3]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena dhuvaka paṭerakamabhimantrya nadīpravāhe nikhanati /
5.4.2.[4]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena vetasaśākhāmabhimantrya ropayati /
5.4.2.[5]	iti nadīpravāhakarma //
5.4.3.[1]	'idaṃ va āpaḥ' iti pādena hiraṇyam abhimantrya nadīmārgakhāte nidadhāti //
5.4.4.[1]	'ayaṃ vatsaḥ' iti pādeneṣīkāñjimaṇḍūkaṃ nīlalohitābhyāṃ sūtrābhyāṃ baddhvābhimantrya nidadhāti khātapravāhe //
5.4.5.[1]	'ihetthameta' iti pādenāvakāmabhimantrya maṇḍūkopari nidadhāti //
5.4.6.[1]	'yatredam' iti pādenodakamabhimantrya maṇḍūkasyopari ninayati /
5.4.6.[2]	samāptaṃ vahanakarma /
5.4.6.[3]	vahane vighāto na bhavati /
5.4.6.[4]	pūrṇapravāho na bhavati //
5.4.6.[5]	atha navapravāha idaṃ kuryāt
5.4.7.[1]	varuṇadevatāpākayajñavidhānenājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena trirvibhajya juhoti /
5.4.7.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
5.4.7.[3]	kṛṣṇavrīhiḥ kṛṣṇāyā goḥ payaḥ ghṛtaṃ ca vetasakāṣṭhasruva indhanaṃ ca vetasapatraiḥ staraṇaṃ paṭerakena vā /
5.4.7.[4]	asmin tantre sarvaṃ mārutaṃ kartavyam /
5.4.7.[5]	udake pravāha udakapravāhabhaye nadībhaye grāme nagare vā yatrodakanadībhayaṃ bhavati tatra sarvatra vāruṇo homaḥ kartavyaḥ /
5.4.7.[6]	mukhyaṃ pravāhe karma //
5.4.8-9.[1]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena dadhisaktumanthaṃ baliharaṇaṃ kṛtvā vaitase camase vaitasābhyāmupamanthanībhyāmupamathya baliṃ haret /
5.4.8-9.[2]	tataḥ 'ati dhanvāni' iti dvābhyāṃ samprokṣaṇībhyāṃ mantrodakaṃ nadīpravāhe prasiñcan vrajati /
5.4.8-9.[3]	samāptaṃ nadīdūragamanakarma //
5.4.8-9.[4]	yadi na vahati nadī tadā vakṣyamāṇamidaṃ karma
5.4.10.[1]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena hastena nadīṃ vahanti /
5.4.10.[2]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena vetasaśākhāmabhimantrya nadīmavasiñcati /
5.4.10.[3]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā svayaṃ patati /
5.4.10.[4]	nivartamānāyāṃ nadīmadhye svapati niścayam /

5.4.14-15.[1]	kapikacchumūlaṃ oṣadhivat khātvā 'yāṃ tvā gandharvo akhanat' iti sūktena 'vṛṣaṇaste khanitā' iti mantreṇa dugdhe śrapayitvopaviṣṭaṃ dhanurutsaṅge kṛtvā dugdhe prakṣipya tato dugdhaṃ 'yāṃ tvā gandharvo akhanat' iti sūktena 'vṛṣaṇaste' ityabhimantrya pāyayati /
5.4.14-15.[2]	'yāṃ tvā gandharvo akhanat' 'vṛṣaṇaste' ityṛcā suravālakamoṣadhivat khātvā dugdhe śrapayati /

5.4.16.[2]	'yāṃ tvā gandharvo akhanat' iti sūktena 'vṛṣaṇaste khanitāraḥ' ityṛcaibhirmantraiḥ suravālakamoṣadhivat khātvā dugdhe kvāthayitvā muśala upaviśya dugdhamabhimantrya 'yāṃ tvā' iti mantraiḥ pibati /

5.5.6.[5]	'samutpatantu' iti sūktena mānuṣakeśajaradupānahau vaṃśāgre prabadhya yodhayati /
5.5.6.[6]	'pra nabhasva' iti sūktena keśajaradupānahau vaṃśāgre prabadhya yodhayati japan //
5.5.7.[1]	'samutpatantu' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātya tenodakena tuṣasahitamāmapātraṃ tripāde śikye'śmānamavadhāya sūktaṃ japtvā samprokṣyāpsu nidadhāti /
5.5.7.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.7.[3]	'pra nabhasva' iti sūktenodapātreṇa sampātavatā samprokṣyāmapātraṃ tripāde'śmānamavadhāyāpsu nidadhāti /
5.5.7.[4]	tantraṃ ca /
5.5.7.[5]	samāptāni vṛṣṭikarmāṇi /
5.5.7.[6]	ṣoḍaśa /
5.5.7.[7]	vṛṣṭi /
5.5.7.[8]	samānam /
5.5.7.[9]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
5.5.7.[10]	ekaṃ vā dve vā sarvān vā karoti /
5.5.7.[11]	kramo'pi nāsti //
5.5.7.[12]	arthotthāpane vighnaśamanavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
5.5.8.[1]	'ayaṃ te yoniḥ' iti sūktena haviṣāmupadadhītājyasamidādi /
5.5.8.[2]	tantravikalpo hastahome //
5.5.9.[1]	'ayaṃ te yoniḥ' iti sūktaṃ japati /
5.5.9.[2]	arthakāma udyamaṃ yadā karoti tadedaṃ karoti /
5.5.9.[3]	'ā no bhara' iti sūktenājyasamitpuroḍāśādi juhoti /
5.5.9.[4]	'ā no bhara' iti sūktaṃ japati /
5.5.9.[5]	dravyahastyaśvaratnadhanadhānyādyevaṅkāmo yadodyamaṃ vaṇijādi karoti tadedaṃ karma karoti /
5.5.9.[6]	yasminnārambho gṛhādi na sidhyati tadedaṃ karma /
5.5.9.[7]	'dhītī vā ye' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāmājyādyupadadhīta /
5.5.9.[8]	'dhītī vā' iti dvyarcaṃ sūktaṃ japati /
5.5.9.[9]	artha udyamaṃ kariṣyamāṇaḥ /
5.5.9.[10]	samāptam arthavighnaśamanaṃ dravyotthāpanam //
5.5.9.[11]	atha dyūtajayakarmocyate
5.5.10.[1]	pūrvāṣāḍhānakṣatre gartaṃ khanati tūṣṇīm //
5.5.11.[1]	uttarāṣāḍhānakṣatre sañcinoti pūrayati tūṣṇīm //
5.5.12-13.[1]	tatra dyūtasthānaṃ kṛtvā trayodaśyādayastisro dadhimadhuni vāsayitvā akṣayati tān pāśān vākṣān vā kapardikān vā /
5.5.12-13.[2]	'udbhindantīṃ sañjayantīm' iti sūktenābhimantrya dyūtakrīḍāṃ kuryāt /
5.5.12-13.[3]	pūrvāṣāḍhāsu gartaṃ khanatyuttarāsu samminoti pūrayati /
5.5.12-13.[4]	kapardakān dadhimadhuni vāsayitvā 'yathā vṛkṣamaśaniḥ' iti navarcena sūktenābhimantrya dyūtakrīḍāṃ karoti /
5.5.12-13.[5]	jayakāmaḥ /
5.5.12-13.[6]	dadhimadhuni akṣān vāsayitvā 'idamugrāya babhrave' iti saptarcena sūktenābhimantrya dyūtakrīḍāṃ karoti /
5.5.12-13.[7]	dyūte jayo bhavati /
5.5.12-13.[8]	samāptāni dyūtajayakarmāṇi /
5.5.12-13.[9]	dyūtakrīḍāṃ karoti tasyābhimantrya dadāti dyūtakārāya //
5.5.12-13.[10]	athārthotthāpanodyamakaravighnaśamanakarmocyate
5.5.14.[1]	'ambayo yanti', 'āpo hi ṣṭhā' 'śaṃ no devīḥ' iti tribhiḥ sūktairmaruto yajate pākayajñavidhānena yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[2]	'mārutaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ mārutaśṛtam' ityādi bhavati /
5.5.14.[3]	arthakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[4]	'hiraṇyavarṇāḥ' iti maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[5]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[6]	'punantu mā' iti sūktena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[7]	'sasruṣīḥ' iti sūktena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[8]	'himavataḥ' iti sūktena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[9]	'vāyoḥ pūtaḥ' iti tṛcena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[10]	'śaṃ ca no mayaśca naḥ' iti maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[11]	'anaḍudbhyastvaṃ prathamam' iti sūktena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[12]	'mahyamāpaḥ' iti sūktena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[13]	'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' iti sūktena maruto yajate yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[14]	evamādyā oṣadhīḥ sampātyābhinyubjanaṃ viplāvanaṃ śvaśira eḍakaśiraḥ keśajaradupānahayuddha udapātrakarma etānyabhivarṣaṇāni karmāṇi bhavanti /
5.5.14.[15]	ekaikasya sūktasya /
5.5.14.[16]	eke ācāryā marutayāgasthāne mantroktādevatāyāgaṃ kuryāt yathā varuṇam /
5.5.14.[17]	athauṣadhyādi samānam /
5.5.14.[18]	varṣakarmaṇāmarthotthāpanakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[19]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ambayo yanti' iti 'āpo hi ṣṭhāḥ', 'śaṃ no devīḥ' iti tribhiḥ sūktairudakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tata āplāvayati /
5.5.14.[20]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[21]	vighnopaśamanakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[22]	pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā 'hiraṇyavarṇāḥ' iti sūktenodakapūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tata āplāvayati /
5.5.14.[23]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[24]	arthotthāpanakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[25]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.5.14.[26]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[27]	vighnaśamanakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[28]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'punantu mā' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.5.14.[29]	uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[30]	arthamutthāpanakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[31]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'sasruṣīḥ', 'himavataḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.5.14.[32]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[33]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'vāyoḥ pūtaḥ' iti sūktenodakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.5.14.[34]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[35]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'śaṃ ca no mayaśca naḥ' ityṛcodapātraṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.5.14.[36]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[37]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'anaḍadbhyastvaṃ prathamam' iti sūktanodapātraṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.5.14.[38]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[39]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'mahyamāpaḥ' 'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudapātraṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.5.14.[40]	tata uttaratantram /
5.5.14.[41]	arthotthāpane vighnaśamanakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[42]	'ambayo yanti' 'āpo hi ṣṭhāḥ' 'śaṃ no devīḥ' iti tribhiḥ sūktairudakaghaṭamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
5.5.14.[43]	'hiraṇyavarṇāḥ' iti sūktenāvasiñcati /
5.5.14.[44]	'yadadaḥ samprayatīḥ' iti sūktenodakaghaṭamabhimantrya puruṣamavasiñcati /
5.5.14.[45]	vidyādhanaviṣaye vighnaṃ na bhavati /
5.5.14.[46]	'punantu mā' iti sūktenodakamabhimantryāvasiñcati puruṣam /
5.5.14.[47]	'sasruṣīḥ' 'himavataḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
5.5.14.[48]	'vāyoḥ pūtaḥ' ityudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
5.5.14.[49]	'śaṃ ca no mayaśca naḥ' ityṛcodakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
5.5.14.[50]	'anaḍudbhyastvaṃ prathamam' ityudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
5.5.14.[51]	'mahyamāpaḥ' 'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
5.5.14.[52]	vighnaśamanakāmaḥ /
5.5.14.[53]	samāptānyabhivarṣaṇāvasecanāni karmāṇi //
5.5.15.[1]	'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' sūktena 'udehi vājin' iti viṃśatibhirṛgbhiścodyantamupatiṣṭhate /
5.5.15.[2]	arthakāmaḥ //
5.5.16.[1]	'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' iti sūktena 'udehi vājin' iti viṃśatibhirṛgbhiśca snānaṃ kṛtvopatiṣṭhate /
5.5.16.[2]	arthamutthāpanakāmaḥ /
5.5.16.[3]	ahatavastraparidhānaṃ kṛtvā 'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' iti sūktena 'udehi vājin' iti viṃśatibhirṛgbhiścopatiṣṭhate /
5.5.16.[4]	arthasiddhikāmaḥ //
5.5.17.[1]	'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' 'udehi vājin' iti viṃśatibhirṛgbhiśca vastramabhimantrya paridhāpayati /
5.5.17.[2]	artho mama sidhyatām evaṅkāmaḥ /
5.5.17.[3]	'vaiśvānaro raśmibhiḥ' 'udehi vājin' iti viṃśatirṛgbhiśca vastramabhimantrya dadāti /
5.5.17.[4]	vidrāvanādiviṣaye śamanakāmaḥ /
5.5.17.[5]	samāptāni vighnaśamanakarmāṇi //
5.5.17.[6]	atha govatsadveṣavirodhe sāmmanasyamucyate
5.5.18-19.[1]	'yathā māṃsam' iti sūktena vatsaṃ snānaṃ kārayitvā gomūtreṇāvasicya tato vatsaṃ triḥ paribhrāmayitvā tato'bhimantrya tataḥ pānārthaṃ muñcati //
5.5.20.[1]	'yathā māṃsam' iti sūktena goḥ śiraḥ karṇaṃ cābhimantrayate /
5.5.20.[2]	gavāṃ vatsena saha virodhe /
5.5.20.[3]	vatsagovirodhe sāmmanasyaṃ karma /
5.5.20.[4]	samāptaṃ govatsasya virodhe sāmmanasyam /
5.5.20.[5]	akaraṇe gauḥ pūrvā vinaśyati //
5.5.20.[6]	aśvavināśe prakāra ucyate /
5.5.20.[7]	athāśvaśāntividhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
5.5.21.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā aśvān snāpayitvā agrekṛtya svāśvaṃ 'vātaraṃhā bhava' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātyābhimantrya //
5.5.22.[1]	tataḥ palāśapatre sarvauṣadhīḥ kṛtvottarasampātān auṣadhāv ānayati //
5.5.23-24.[1]	udapātreṇācāmayatyāplāvayati ca //
5.5.25-26.[1]	sarvauṣadhicūrṇairavakirati triḥ /
5.5.25-26.[2]	'ekayā ca daśabhiḥ' ityṛcā snātān mardhni parikirati /
5.5.25-26.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.5.25-26.[4]	aśvaśāntiḥ /
5.5.25-26.[5]	aśvāḥ śāntāstejasvino nirupadravā vegavanta ārogyavanto bhavanti /
5.5.25-26.[6]	aśvaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.5.25-26.[7]	pañcame'dhyāye pañcamī kaṇḍikā //
5.6.0.[1]	atha pravāsena dravyotthāpanamucyate
5.6.1.[1]	'bhadrādadhi' ityṛcājyaṃ juhoti /
5.6.1.[2]	ājyatantre /
5.6.1.[3]	'bhadrādadhi śreyaḥ' ityṛcā samidha ādadhāti śāntāḥ /
5.6.1.[4]	vighnaśamanakāmaḥ /
5.6.1.[5]	'bhadrādadhi śreyaḥ' ityṛcā puroḍāśaṃ juhoti /
5.6.1.[6]	tantravikalpaḥ /
5.6.1.[7]	'bhadrādadhi' ityṛcā payo juhoti /
5.6.1.[8]	tantre /
5.6.1.[9]	'bhadrādadhi śreyaḥ' ityṛcodaudanādi haviṣāmupadhānaṃ kuryāt /
5.6.1.[10]	sarvatra tantravikalpaḥ /
5.6.1.[11]	pravāse gatvā caurabhayamudakabhayaṃ gamane vighnaṃ na bhavati /
5.6.1.[12]	samāptaṃ pravāse gacchatāṃ vighnaśamanam //
5.6.2.[1]	'bhadrādadhi' ityṛcaṃ japati /
5.6.2.[2]	pathi gacchatāṃ vighnaṃ na bhavati /
5.6.2.[3]	iti vighnaśamanam //
5.6.3.[1]	'bhadrādadhi' ityṛcā yānaṃ sampātyābhimantryājyatantre grāme gatvā tata udakena samprokṣati vimocayati /
5.6.3.[2]	vighnaśamanakāmaḥ /
5.6.3.[3]	dravyotthāpanaṃ ca //
5.6.4.[1]	yadi yānena yāti tadā idaṃ karma /
5.6.4.[2]	ājyatantre sampātyābhimantryārohaṇaṃ kuryāt //
5.6.5.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bhadrādadhi' ityṛcā vaṇijadravyaṃ vastravalayāśvādi sarvadravyaṃ sampātyābhimantrya /
5.6.5.[2]	pratidravyaṃ mantrāvṛttiḥ /
5.6.5.[3]	aśvavastravalayādi /
5.6.5.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
5.6.5.[5]	vastrādidravyaṃ vikrayārthaṃ nayati /
5.6.5.[6]	yadā dravyaṃ gṛhṇāti tadedaṃ karma /
5.6.5.[7]	'bhadrādadhi' ityṛcābhimantrya gṛhṇāti /
5.6.5.[8]	samāptaṃ vaṇijalābhakarma /
5.6.5.[9]	pathi gṛhe'nyatra vā vaṇijavighāto na bhavati //
5.6.5.[10]	athābhyāgatapuruṣāṇāṃ sāmmanasyaṃ kriyate /
5.6.5.[11]	yadā viśiṣṭo gṛha āgacchati tadedaṃ maitrīkarma kriyate /
5.6.5.[12]	mitraṃ tveṣāṃ darśane āgatānāṃ yadā gṛha āgacchati tadedaṃ kuryāt //
5.6.6.[1]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'ubhā jigyathuḥ' ityṛcā hastyādi yānaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tata uttaratantram /
5.6.6.[2]	tasmin yāne yasya sāmmanasyaṃ kriyate /
5.6.6.[3]	sarve yānasyoparyupaviśanti /
5.6.6.[4]	sarve yānasyopari caṭanti //
5.6.7.[1]	tataḥ paścimadigbhāge gatvā punargṛha āgacchanti /
5.6.7.[2]	tata 'ubhā jigyathuḥ' ityṛcodanamabhimantrya prayacchati bhojanārtham /
5.6.7.[3]	manthaṃ vā /
5.6.7.[4]	sarvaiḥ saha bhuñjanti /
5.6.7.[5]	samāptaṃ sāmmanasyam /
5.6.7.[6]	ekasmin yuddhe kriyamāṇe sahāyagatasya karma /
5.6.7.[7]	anyasya ca sādhāraṇamityarthaḥ /
5.6.7.[8]	yo yuddhe sāhāyatvaṃ karoti tasyedaṃ karma /
5.6.7.[9]	prathamaṃ pādau prakṣālya tataḥ karma ceti /
5.6.7.[10]	kecit kṣatriyayoridaṃ karma manyante /
5.6.7.[11]	samāptaṃ sāmmanasyamarthotthāpanaṃ vighnaśamanaṃ yuddhādi //
5.6.7.[12]	atha gṛhe viruddhe sati sāmmanasyamucyate
5.6.8.[1]	kartāraṇye gatvā samidho gṛhītvā tūṣṇīṃ gṛha āgatya tataḥ 'ūrjaṃ bibhrat' iti sūktena tāḥ samidhaḥ sakṛtsarvāḥ sūktāntenādadhāti /
5.6.8.[2]	gṛhamānuṣāṇāṃ sāmmanasyaṃ bhavati /
5.6.8.[3]	kalahanivāraṇam /
5.6.8.[4]	kalaho na bhavatītyarthaḥ /
5.6.8.[5]	samāptaṃ gṛhasāmmanasyaṃ vighnaśamanaṃ ca //
5.6.8.[6]	mantrabrāhmaṇayordravyamicchati tasyedaṃ karma pratigrahādyucyate
5.6.9-11.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ṛcaṃ sāma' ityṛcājyaṃ juhoti /
5.6.9-11.[2]	'ṛcaṃ sāma yadaprākṣam' ityṛcājyaṃ juhoti /
5.6.9-11.[3]	'ṛcaṃ sāma' iti dvābhyāṃ tṛtīyāmāhutiṃ juhoti /
5.6.9-11.[4]	'anumataye svāhā' iti caturthīmāhutiṃ juhoti /
5.6.9-11.[5]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.6.9-11.[6]	vedapāṭhena śāstrapāṭhenārthotthāpanamicchannidaṃ karoti /
5.6.9-11.[7]	samāptaṃ vedena śāstreṇa arthotthāpane vighnaśamanam //
5.6.9-11.[8]	atha parimokṣasamāvartanavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
5.6.12-17.[1]	godānikaṃ tantramājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvābhimantrayate /
5.6.12-17.[2]	'apo divyāḥ' iti catasṛbhiḥ /
5.6.12-17.[3]	tato'bhyātānādi paridhāpanāntaṃ kṛtvā kecit paridānānte tato'bhyātānaṃ hutvā tata 'idāvatsarāya' iti kalpajaiścaturbhirṛgbhirājyaṃ juhuyāt /
5.6.12-17.[4]	punaḥ 'idāvatsarāya' iti catasraḥ samidha ādadhīta /
5.6.12-17.[5]	iti vratavisarjanam /
5.6.12-17.[6]	vrataśrāvaṇam /
5.6.12-17.[7]	vrataṃ visarjati /
5.6.12-17.[8]	tato'bhyātānāni juhoti /
5.6.12-17.[9]	tata 'ṛcaṃ sāma' iti prathamayarcājyāhutiṃ hutvā 'ṛcaṃ sāma yadaprākṣam' iti dvitīyām /
5.6.12-17.[10]	yuktābhyāṃ tṛtīyāmānumatīṃ caturthīm //
5.6.18.[1]	tato'bhyātānāni juhoti /
5.6.18.[2]	'doṣo gāya' iti sūktena bhaktaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
5.6.18.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.6.18.[4]	iti parimokṣaṃ samāptam /
5.6.18.[5]	vedavrataṃ kalpavrataṃ mṛgāravrataṃ viṣāsahivrataṃ yamavrataṃ śirovratam aṅgirovratam ityevamādiṣvabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'idāvatsarāya' iti vratavisarjanaṃ vrataśrāvaṇaṃ ca karoti /
5.6.18.[6]	tantravikalpo hastahomatvāt /
5.6.18.[7]	yatra kvacid vrataṃ vaidikaṃ laukikaṃ ca tatra sarvatra vratādānaṃ vratavisarjanaṃ ca bhavati vidhānena /
5.6.18.[8]	śirovratādīni nityāni /
5.6.18.[9]	kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni smṛtivihitāni /
5.6.18.[10]	kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni kāmyāni smṛtipurāṇaśāstravedavihitāni ca /
5.6.18.[11]	tasmāt sarvāṇi vrataśabdavācyāni /
5.6.18.[12]	tāni sarvāṇyeva vidhānena kartavyāni /
5.6.18.[13]	yatra vapanaṃ tatra sarvatra godānikaṃ kuryāt /
5.6.18.[14]	parimokṣādanantaraṃ trirātraṃ snātavrataṃ caret /
5.6.18.[15]	astamite 'apo divyāḥ' iti tisṛbhiḥ samidha ādadhāti /
5.6.18.[16]	tṛtīyāvarjam /
5.6.18.[17]	anye ekarātraṃ samidādhānaṃ kurvanti /
5.6.18.[18]	iti parimokṣaḥ samāptaḥ //
5.6.18.[19]	atha pāpalakṣaṇastrī tasyāḥ śāntirucyate
5.6.19.[1]	'nirlakṣmyam' iti sūktena sā strī mukhaṃ pratyṛcaṃ prakṣālayati /
5.6.19.[2]	tasyā mukhe hastayormaśakaśigruvārakāvasthānatilakaṃ hrasvakeśādipāpalakṣaṇaṃ sāmudrike strīlakṣaṇaṃ vyākhyātam /
5.6.19.[3]	'nirlakṣmyam' iti sūktenodakaghaṭamabhimantrya strīṃ pāpalakṣaṇāmabhiṣiñcati dakṣiṇāt keśādārabhya yāvaduttaraṃ pārśvam /
5.6.19.[4]	tataḥ pāpalakṣaṇaṃ vinaśyati //
5.6.20-21.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'nirlakṣmyam' iti sūktena pālāśaparṇena kukusāñjuhoti /
5.6.20-21.[2]	homaśeṣān kukusān savyāyāṃ pādapārṣṇyāṃ nidadhāti /
5.6.20-21.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
5.6.20-21.[4]	'nirlakṣmyam' iti sūktena phalīkaraṇāñjuhoti /
5.6.20-21.[5]	hastahomatvāt tantravikalpaḥ /
5.6.20-21.[6]	'nirlakṣmyam' iti sūktena vrīhituṣān juhoti /
5.6.20-21.[7]	homaśeṣān vrīhituṣān savyāyāṃ pādapārṣṇyāṃ nidadhāti /
5.6.20-21.[8]	'nirlakṣmyam' iti sūktena busaṃ juhoti /
5.6.20-21.[9]	savyāyāṃ pādapārṣṇyāṃ nidadhāti /
5.6.20-21.[10]	'nirlakṣmyam' iti sūktena kāṣṭhāvatakṣaṇāni juhoti /
5.6.20-21.[11]	savyāyāṃ pādapārṣṇyāṃ nidadhāti /
5.6.20-21.[12]	anena pāpalakṣaṇaṃ na bhavati /
5.6.20-21.[13]	iti pāpalakṣaṇadoṣaśamanaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.6.20-21.[14]	atha pāpadarśane śāntirucyate
5.6.22.[1]	'āre'sau' iti 'apa naḥ śośucadagham' iti sūktābhyāmanvīkṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā japet /
5.6.22.[2]	darśanadoṣo na bhavati /
5.6.22.[3]	eko vā yadi vā trīṇi pañca sapta navastathā /
5.6.22.[4]	puruṣasya bhāgyakāle hariṇā yānti pradakṣiṇāḥ //
5.6.22.[5]	apradakṣiṇeṣu hariṇeṣvayaṃ japaḥ /
5.6.22.[6]	pakṣiṣu ca /
5.6.22.[7]	grāme'pi bahirvāpaśakune dṛṣṭa idaṃ karoti /
5.6.22.[8]	śvānarudite kākarudite śivārudite cāyam /
5.6.22.[9]	kākamaithune puruṣasya maithune śyenamaithunadarśane nagnāstrīdarśane nagnapuruṣasya napuṃsakasya darśane puṃścalīcandramaṇḍalaśyāmasya ca /
5.6.22.[10]	kṛttikārohiṇī paṭhitā apaśakunāḥ /
5.6.22.[11]	yatra kvacidapaśakunāḥ paṭhitāstatra sarvatrāyaṃ japaḥ /
5.6.22.[12]	śrutau smṛtau vā paṭhitā adṛṣṭavyāsteṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ darśane'dbhutānāṃ darśaneṣvayaṃ japaḥ kartavyaḥ /
5.6.22.[13]	loke yadviruddham /
5.6.22.[14]	anvīkṣaṃ prasiddhamadṛṣṭavyāsteṣāmayaṃ japaḥ /
5.6.22.[15]	apaśakunajapaḥ samāptaḥ //
5.6.22.[16]	atha puruṣo strī vā kāryakaraṇe vighnaśamane ca karmocyate
5.6.23.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'dīrghāyutvāya' iti sūktena jaṅgiḍamaṇiṃ śaṇasūtreṇa baddhvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.6.23.[2]	tata uttaratantram /

5.7.0.[1]	punarvighnaśamanamucyate
5.7.1.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'karśaphasya' iti sūktena piśaṅgavarṇasūtre'ralumaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.7.1.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.7.1.[3]	viskandhavighnaśamano maṇiḥ /
5.7.1.[4]	spardhāvināśo bhavatītyarthaḥ /
5.7.1.[5]	spardhamānasya spardhā vinaśyatītyarthaḥ /
5.7.1.[6]	samāptā vighnaśamane maṇiśāntiḥ /
5.7.1.[7]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'karśaphasya' iti sūktena veṇudaṇḍādīn sampātya tataḥ sūktena vimṛjya dhārayati /
5.7.1.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
5.7.1.[9]	citradaṇḍe dhvajadaṇḍe cihnadaṇḍe vedayaṣṭau lakuṭādidaṇḍaṃ sarvaṃ sampātya yo dhārayati tasya sarpaśṛṅgidaṃṣṭrādi vighnaṃ na bhavati /
5.7.1.[10]	ajñāte jñāte tejavṛddhiśca bhavati /
5.7.1.[11]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'karśaphasya' iti sūktenāyudhaṃ sampātya vimṛjya dhārayati /
5.7.1.[12]	tata uttaratantram /
5.7.1.[13]	sarvaśastrasampātite māyādikaṃ māyājālayuddhe nivāraṇam /
5.7.1.[14]	saṅgrāma indrajālanivāraṇam /
5.7.1.[15]	yuddhe vighnaṃ na bhavati /
5.7.1.[16]	śatruhaṭhaṃ nivārayati /
5.7.1.[17]	śatravo gacchanti /
5.7.1.[18]	spardhamānaśatruṃ jayati /
5.7.1.[19]	haṭhaṃ vināśayati //
5.7.2.[1]	'karśaphasya' iti sūktena phalīkaraṇānagnau prakṣipya vighnagṛhītaṃ puruṣaṃ dhūpayati /
5.7.2.[2]	vighnaśamanaṃ bhavati /
5.7.2.[3]	yasyārambhā na sidhyanti tasyedaṃ karma bhavati /
5.7.2.[4]	iti vighnaśamanaṃ samāptam //
5.7.2.[5]	atha bhūmiśuddhiḥ /
5.7.2.[6]	gṛhaṃ kariṣyamāṇa idaṃ karoti
5.7.3.[1]	'ati dhanvāni' iti dvābhyāmudapātramabhimantrya tatra ninayati bhūmau yatra gṛhaṃ kariṣyati /
5.7.3.[2]	tatra vighnaśamanaṃ bhavati /
5.7.3.[3]	śyenadevatāyai pākayajñavidhānenājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ati dhanvāni' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ caruṃ juhoti /
5.7.3.[4]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
5.7.3.[5]	bhūmisthāne yatra gṛhaṃ kariṣyati tatra śyenayāgaṃ kṛtvā gṛhaṃ kuryāt /
5.7.3.[6]	athavā nave gṛhe śyenayāgaḥ kartavyaḥ /
5.7.3.[7]	vikalpa iti bhāṣyakāraḥ /
5.7.3.[8]	prathamato vā śyenayāgo nave gṛhe //
5.7.3.[9]	atha gṛhapraveśa ucyate /
5.7.3.[10]	vāstusaṃskāra ucyate
5.7.4-5.[1]	'ihaiva dhruvām' ityādi gaṇena bhūmiṃ halena karṣati /
5.7.4-5.[2]	tato dakṣiṇataḥ sambhāramāharatyagneḥ /
5.7.4-5.[3]	tataḥ śāntyudakaṃ karoti /

5.7.6.[1]	nikṣipati //

5.7.9.[1]	sthūṇāvaṃśaṃ ghṛtenābhyajya tūṣṇīm /

5.7.10.[1]	tataḥ puṇyāhavācanaṃ kṛtvā 'pūrṇaṃ nārī' ityṛcodakumbhasahitāṃ patnīmabhimantrya bāhyato gṛhaṃ praveśayanti /

5.7.13.[1]	tataḥ pākayajñavidhānena 'vāstoṣpataye juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' iti nirvāpaḥ /

5.7.13.[4]	vāstoṣpatidevatākaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ cājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vāstoṣpate prati jānīhi' iti dvābhyāṃ caruṃ juhoti /
5.7.13.[5]	tataḥ pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
5.7.13.[6]	kecidasmin tantre'bhyātānāntaṃ hutvā /
5.7.13.[7]	'yajūṃṣi yajñe' iti dvādaśarcena sūktena navaśālāyāṃ sarpirmadhumiśraṃ juhvati sakṛdekāmāhutim /
5.7.13.[8]	'doṣo gāyaḥ' iti dvitīyāmāhutiṃ juhoti /

5.7.13.[10]	ānumatīṃ caturthīm /
5.7.13.[11]	kalaśodakapānīyamācāryo gṛhītvā śālāmaṅgulibhyāṃ samprokṣya yajamānapatnīsahiteṣu gṛheṣu madhya āsāda upaviśya kalaśodakaṃ bhūmau ninayati tūṣṇīm /
5.7.13.[12]	ācāryādyā ādau vāṅmaunaṃ kurvanti /

5.8.28.[1]	śeṣam udakaṃ pārśvadeśe nikṣipya 'yatte krūraṃ yadāsthitaṃ tacchundhasva' iti mantreṇa tato patnī yathārthaṃ vrajati //
5.8.29.[1]	tato vapāśrapaṇyāvājyaṃ sruvaṃ svadhitiṃ darbhamādāya paśusthāne gacchati /

5.8.32-33.[2]	nikhanatītyarthaḥ //
5.8.34-36.[1]	'vapayā dyāvāpṛthivī' ityanena vapāśrapaṇyau vapayā pracchādya svadhitinā prakṛtyotkṛtya tataśchedanasthānaṃ ghṛtenābhighārya /
5.8.34-36.[2]	śāntavṛkṣamayāvekaikaśṛṅgā dvitīyā dviśṛṅgā //
5.8.37.[1]	'vāyave stokānām' iti darbhāgraṃ prāsyati kṣipati //
5.8.38.[1]	'pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ' ityanena mantreṇāgneḥ paścādbhāge nidadhāti //
5.8.39-40.[1]	'devastvā' iti mantreṇa śrapayati /
5.8.39-40.[2]	suśṛtāṃ karoti tataḥ //
5.8.39-40.[3]	pañcame'dhyāye'ṣṭamī kaṇḍikā //
5.9.1.[1]	yady aṣṭāpadī syād garbhañjalau sahiraṇyaṃ sayavaṃ vā 'ya ātmadā' iti sūktena khadāyāṃ tryaratnāv agnau sakṛjjuhoti //
5.9.2-5.[1]	avadānāni paśorekādaśa gṛhṇāti /
5.9.2-5.[2]	hṛdayam /
5.9.2-5.[3]	jihvā /
5.9.2-5.[4]	kroḍam /
5.9.2-5.[5]	vāmabāhuḥ /
5.9.2-5.[6]	pārśve dve /
5.9.2-5.[7]	yakṛt kāleyamityucyate /
5.9.2-5.[8]	pṛṣṭakau dvau /
5.9.2-5.[9]	gudaśca /
5.9.2-5.[10]	paścimadakṣiṇabāhuśca /
5.9.2-5.[11]	ekādaśa gṛhītvā /
5.9.2-5.[12]	tataḥ sviṣṭakṛdavadānāni gṛhṇāti /
5.9.2-5.[13]	tāni trīṇi /
5.9.2-5.[14]	dakṣiṇo bāhuḥ /
5.9.2-5.[15]	vāmajaṅghā ca /

5.9.2-5.[19]	'pari tvāgne' ityādi karoti //
5.9.6-7.[1]	tato yaddaivatyaḥ paśustaddaivatyaścaruḥ śrapayitavyaḥ //
5.9.8.[1]	tato vapāyāścatvāri khaṇḍāni karoti /
5.9.8.[2]	'samiddho adya' iti sūktenaikaṃ khaṇḍaṃ juhoti /
5.9.8.[3]	'ūrdhvā asya' iti sūktena dvitīyaṃ khaṇḍaṃ juhoti //
5.9.9.[1]	'samiddho adya' 'ūrdhvā asya' iti sūktābhyāṃ tṛtīyaṃ khaṇḍaṃ juhoti //
5.9.10.[1]	'anumataye svāhā' iti caturthaṃ khaṇḍaṃ juhoti //
5.9.11.[1]	tato 'jātavedo vapayā gaccha devān' iti mantreṇājyaṃ juhoti //
5.9.12-13.[1]	'ūrdhvaṃ nabhasaṃ mārutaṃ gacchatam' ityanena mantreṇa vapāśrapaṇyau dve saha juhoti /
5.9.12-13.[2]	prācīmekaśṛṅgāṃ pratīcīṃ dviśṛṅgāṃ kṛtvā //
5.9.14-15.[1]	tato'vadānāni juhoti 'ya ātmadā' iti sūktena /
5.9.14-15.[2]	pratyṛcaṃ juhoti /
5.9.14-15.[3]	punaḥ 'ya ātmadā' iti sūktena caruṃ juhoti //
5.9.16.[1]	'samrāḍasyadhi' iti mantreṇājyaṃ juhoti /
5.9.16.[2]	'sarvavīrāya svāhā sarvapuruṣāya svāhā sarvagaṇāya svāhā sarvakāmāya svāhā' catasra āhutīrjuhoti /
5.9.16.[3]	'anvadya no'numatiḥ /
5.9.16.[4]	pūṣā sarasvatī mahī yatkaromi tadṛdhyatāmanumataye svāhā' juhoti /
5.9.16.[5]	pārvaṇādi prajāpatiṃ ca hutvā tataḥ sakṛnmāṃsaṃ caruṃ cāvadya sviṣṭakṛtaṃ yajati /
5.9.16.[6]	'svāheṣṭebhyaḥ' ityādyuttaratantram /
5.9.16.[7]	samāptaṃ vaśāśamanavidhānam /
5.9.16.[8]	daivahataṃ tasya gṛhaṃ yasya gṛhe vaśā jāyate /
5.9.16.[9]	tasya dhanādināśo bhavati /
5.9.16.[10]	tasmācchāntiḥ kartavyeti /
5.9.16.[11]	vaśāyā dve pratipattī /
5.9.16.[12]	abhimantrya vā dadāti śamanaṃ vā vidhānena kuryāt /
5.9.16.[13]	etena vidhānena paśavo vyākhyātāḥ /
5.9.16.[14]	nitye naimittike kāmye paśavo vyākhyātāḥ /
5.9.16.[15]	'dvādaśarātre'gniṃ paśunā yajeta' iti nityam /
5.9.16.[16]	naimittikākāmyāśca dhūmaketuḥ pañca paśavastāyante /
5.9.16.[17]	dhātāraṃ ca paśunā ca purohitapariśiṣṭeṣu paṭhyate /
5.9.16.[18]	ityevamādayo naimittikāḥ /
5.9.16.[19]	paiṭhīnasinā kāmyāḥ paṭhitāḥ /
5.9.16.[20]	'chāgena svahutena trayodaśamāsān' ityādi puṣṭikarmaṇāmupadhānamadhye paśuḥ paṭhitaḥ /
5.9.16.[21]	tasmāt mantroktā devatāḥ /
5.9.16.[22]	kāmyāḥ paśavaḥ /
5.9.16.[23]	tathā vaitānasūtre aindrāgnaḥ paśurāyuḥprajāpaśukāmasyetyādayaḥ kāmyāḥ paśavaḥ /
5.9.16.[24]	teṣāṃ vidhirucyate /
5.9.16.[25]	pākayajñamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā śāntyudakābhivādanaparyantaṃ kṛtvā 'ya īśe paśupatiḥ paśūnām' ityādi bhavati /
5.9.16.[26]	samānaṃ nitye paśau /
5.9.16.[27]	'samiddho adya' iti 'ūrdhvā asya' iti vapāhomaḥ /
5.9.16.[28]	naimittike ca /
5.9.16.[29]	tathā dvayoḥ pradhānakarma homaḥ /
5.9.16.[30]	pradhānasūktenaiva kāmyeṣu tathaiva ca /
5.9.16.[31]	atha pitryeṣu kāmyeṣu viśeṣaḥ tatra 'vaha vapām' ityṛcā trirāvṛttiḥ /
5.9.16.[32]	vapāṃ trirjuhoti /
5.9.16.[33]	tathā avadānāni /
5.9.16.[34]	tathā caruṃ 'vaha vapām' iti trirjuhoti /
5.9.16.[35]	śeṣaṃ samānam //
5.9.16.[36]	atha duṣṭe pratigrahe saumye vā kṛte yājane vā dakṣiṇāpratigrahaṇe yena karmaṇā pāpaṃ vinaśyati taducyate
5.9.17-19.[1]	'ka idam' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ pratigrahamabhimantrya gṛhṇāti /
5.9.17-19.[2]	pratigrahadoṣo na bhavati /
5.9.17-19.[3]	'yadannam' iti tṛcena 'bhūmiṣṭvā' ityṛcā bhūmipratigrahe viśeṣaḥ /
5.9.17-19.[4]	'kāmastadagre' iti sūktena pratigrahamabhimantrya gṛhṇāti /
5.9.17-19.[5]	'yadannam' iti tṛcena sūktena pratigrahamabhimantrya gṛhṇāti /
5.9.17-19.[6]	'punarmaitvindriyam' ityṛcā pratigrahamabhimantrya gṛhṇāti /
5.9.17-19.[7]	samāptaṃ pratigrahadoṣanāśanakarma /
5.9.17-19.[8]	sarvāṇi karmāṇi kṛtvā 'punarmaitvindriyam' ityṛcā karma samāpya tata ātmānamanumantrayate /
5.9.17-19.[9]	sarvakarmasu bhavatītyātmaśāntiḥ /
5.9.17-19.[10]	sandhyāvandana ājyatantre pākatantre'smin karmaṇi nityanaimittikakāmyeṣu 'punarmaitvindriyam' ityṛcātmahṛdayamanumantrayate //
5.9.17-19.[11]	pañcame'dhyāye navamī kaṇḍikā //
5.10.0.[1]	atha akṛte pāpe loke pāpavacanam utpadyate tatra śāntir ucyate
5.10.1.[1]	'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcābhyākhyātamagre kṛtvā gṛhe praviśya tūṣṇīṃ tataḥ saktumanthamabhimantryābhyākhyātāya dadāti /
5.10.1.[2]	pāpaṃ vinaśyati /
5.10.1.[3]	prathamamagre kṛtvābhyākhyātaṃ gṛhe praveśya kartā paścāt praviśati /
5.10.1.[4]	'śivāste santvoṣadhayaḥ' ityṛcā saktumanthamabhimantrya tato'bhyākhātāya dadāti /
5.10.1.[5]	loke nindā bhavati /
5.10.1.[6]	'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcā bhaktamabhimantrya dadāti /
5.10.1.[7]	'śivāste santvoṣadhayaḥ' ityṛcā bhaktamabhimantrya dadāti /
5.10.1.[8]	loke nindā vinaśyati //
5.10.2.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcā drughaṇamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.2.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.2.[3]	abhiśasta idaṃ karma /
5.10.2.[4]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'śivāste santvoṣadhayaḥ' ityṛcā drughaṇamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.2.[5]	abhiśaste /
5.10.2.[6]	tata uttaratantram //
5.10.3.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcā pālāśamaṇiṃ drughaṇasadṛśaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.3.[2]	abhiśaste /
5.10.3.[3]	uttaratantram /
5.10.3.[4]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'śivāste' ityṛcā pālāśakāṣṭhamaṇiṃ drughaṇapratirūpaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.3.[5]	abhiśaste /
5.10.3.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.3.[7]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcā lohamaṇiṃ drughaṇasadṛśaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantryābhiśaste badhnāti /
5.10.3.[8]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.10.3.[9]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'śivāste' ityṛcā kṛṣṇalohamaṇiṃ drughaṇasadṛśaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.3.[10]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.3.[11]	pāpaśravaṇe pāpavināśo bhavati /
5.10.3.[12]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcā tāmramaṇiṃ drughaṇasadṛśaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.3.[13]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.3.[14]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'śivāste' ityṛcā tāmramayadrughaṇapratirūpaṃ maṇiṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.3.[15]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.3.[16]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'utāmṛtāsuḥ' ityṛcā hiraṇyamaṇiṃ drughaṇapratirūpaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.3.[17]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.3.[18]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'śivāste' ityṛcā hiraṇyamayamaṇiṃ kṛtvā drughaṇapratirūpaṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
5.10.3.[19]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.3.[20]	akṛte pāpe nindā yasya bhavati tasyedaṃ karma /
5.10.3.[21]	kṛte vā prāyaścittam /
5.10.3.[22]	yadi pāpaśravaṇaṃ bhavati tadedaṃ karma /
5.10.3.[23]	samāptaṃ loke nindāvighātakarma /
5.10.3.[24]	sarvatra kauśike karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
5.10.3.[25]	ekasmin viṣaye yatra bahūni karmāṇi paṭhitāni tatraikaṃ kuryād dve vā sarvāṇi vā //
5.10.3.[26]	atha yāge kriyamāṇe yena karmaṇā vighnaśamanaṃ bhavati taducyate
5.10.4.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yena soma' iti sūktena sārūpavatsaṃ pāyasaṃ sampātyābhimantrya ṛtvijo yajamānaṃ cāśayati /
5.10.4.[2]	avighnena yajñasiddhirbhavati /
5.10.4.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.4.[4]	yāge vighnaśamanaṃ samāptam //
5.10.4.[5]	yāgasamāptau vighnaśamanamucyate
5.10.5.[1]	somadevatyaṃ caruṃ pākayajñavidhānenājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yena soma' iti tṛcena caruṃ juhoti /
5.10.5.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
5.10.5.[3]	samāptaṃ somayāge yājanadoṣaśamanaṃ vighnaśamanaṃ ca /
5.10.5.[4]	anena karmaṇā ayājyayājanadoṣānmucyate //
5.10.5.[5]	atha dhanadhānyādipratigrahādiyācanamicchannidaṃ karma kṛtvā yācati /
5.10.5.[6]	vighāto na bhavati //
5.10.6.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yaṃ yācāmi' ityṛcā sārūpavatsaṃ pāyasaṃ śrapayitvā sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
5.10.6.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.6.[3]	yācitaṃ na pratiṣedhayati /
5.10.6.[4]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'yadāśasā' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ sārūpavatsaṃ pāyasaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
5.10.6.[5]	uttaratantram /
5.10.6.[6]	samāptaṃ yācane pratiṣedhaśāntiḥ //
5.10.6.[7]	atha kapota ulūke vā gṛhe praviṣṭe'nyatrābhīṣṭadeśe'pi tatra śāntirucyate
5.10.7.[1]	śāntyudakaṃ vidhānena kṛtvā tato mātalīṃ na karoti /
5.10.7.[2]	'devāḥ kapotaḥ' 'ṛcā kapotam' 'amūn hetiḥ' iti sūktatrayaṃ vāstoṣpatyaṃ cātanaṃ mātṛnāmā śāntigaṇaḥ ete catvāro gaṇāḥ /
5.10.7.[3]	śāntyudaka āvapati /
5.10.7.[4]	tato mātalīṃ kṛtvā śāntyudakaṃ samāpayet /
5.10.7.[5]	rātrau tena śāntyudakena tatsthānaṃ prokṣati 'yatāyai' ityetairmantraiḥ /
5.10.7.[6]	kapotolūkasthānaṃ yāvat /
5.10.7.[7]	kārayituḥ samprokṣaṇamācamanaṃ ca kartavyam /
5.10.7.[8]	gṛhādisthānaṃ prokṣati //
5.10.8.[1]	'parīme'gnim' ityṛcā gāmagniṃ gṛhītvā triḥ śālāṃ pariṇayati /
5.10.8.[2]	kapotasthānaṃ vā paribhrāmayet /
5.10.8.[3]	sakṛnmantraḥ /
5.10.8.[4]	kartā sarvaṃ kuryāt /
5.10.8.[5]	araṇyake pakṣiṇi praviṣṭa idaṃ karma kuryāt /
5.10.8.[6]	kapota ulūke vā praviṣṭe /
5.10.8.[7]	dvipadacatuṣpadavināśo vede śrūyate tasya doṣaśamanam /
5.10.8.[8]	kapotolūkaśāntiḥ /
5.10.8.[9]	samāptā mahāśāntiḥ /
5.10.8.[10]	ghṛtakambalādikaṃ karoti /
5.10.8.[11]	amṛtāṃ vā daśagaṇīṃ vā karoti //
5.10.8.[12]	atha svapnādhyāye paṭhita ugre svapnadarśane śāntirucyate /
5.10.8.[13]	svapnādhyāyapaṭhitaṃ duḥsvapnaṃ rudrabhāṣyakāramatena gṛhītavyam /
5.10.8.[14]	pakvamāṃse pretadamane pariṣvaṅgamarkaṭaśakaṭe dṛṣṭvā tailābhyaṅge nagnapuruṣadarśane nagnastrīdarśane ca kālasūtretyādi svapnādhyāyapaṭhitā anekaśaḥ /
5.10.8.[15]	iti duḥsvapnadarśane śāntirucyate
5.10.9-10.[1]	'paro'pehi' 'yo na jīvaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ svapnaṃ kutsitaṃ dṛṣṭvā mukhaṃ prakṣālayati /
5.10.9-10.[2]	'paro'pehi' 'yo na jīvaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ maiśradhānyaṃ puroḍāśaṃ śrapayitvāgnau juhoti /
5.10.9-10.[3]	tantravikalpaḥ /
5.10.9-10.[4]	'paro'pehi' 'yo na jīvaḥ' iti sūktābhyāṃ dvitīyaṃ puroḍāśaṃ śrapayitvā'bhimantrya śatrukṣetre nidadhāti /
5.10.9-10.[5]	samāptaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam //
5.10.11.[1]	'paryāvartaḥ' ityṛcaṃ japitvā paryāvartate //
5.10.12.[1]	'yatsvapne' ityṛcaṃ japati /
5.10.12.[2]	annaṃ svapne bhakṣayati tadedaṃ karoti //
5.10.12.[3]	atha punarghoraduḥsvapnanāśanakarmocyate
5.10.13.[1]	'vidma te svapna' iti ekena paryāyeṇa duḥsvapnaṃ dṛṣṭvā mukhaṃ vimārṣṭi /
5.10.13.[2]	'vidma te svapna' iti sūktena svapnaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārśveṇa dvitīyena bhayate /
5.10.13.[3]	'vidma te svapna' iti sūktenānnaṃ svapne dṛṣṭvā nirīkṣate /
5.10.13.[4]	'vidma te svapna' iti sūktena maiśradhānyaṃ puroḍāśaṃ juhoti /
5.10.13.[5]	tantravikalpaḥ /
5.10.13.[6]	samāptaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam //
5.10.13.[7]	atha ācārye mṛte brahmacārīdaṃ karma karoti śreyaskāmaḥ
5.10.14-16.[1]	ācāryasya dahane 'agnirbhūmyām' ityādi pañca sāmidhenīhutvā tato dahanaṃ triḥ paribhrāmya tato 'na hi te agne tanvaḥ' iti sūktāntena puroḍāśaṃ juhoti tasmin dahane /
5.10.14-16.[2]	trirātraṃ tasya dahanasamīpe śete'bhimukhasthitaḥ /
5.10.14-16.[3]	kauśikastatra śayanaṃ na manyate /
5.10.14-16.[4]	pretādibhayāt /
5.10.14-16.[5]	tadvighātaśamanam //
5.10.17-18.[1]	'apo divyāḥ' iti catasṛbhirṛgbhiḥ snānaṃ kṛtvā trirātraṃ gṛha āgatya tataḥ śayīteti kauśikamatam /
5.10.17-18.[2]	mṛtaṃ ācārya idaṃ karma /
5.10.17-18.[3]	prāyaścittaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ samāvartanaṃ kuryāt ityarthaḥ /
5.10.17-18.[4]	anyaṃ gurumupāsīta /
5.10.17-18.[5]	samāptaṃ brahmacāriprāyaścittam //
5.10.17-18.[6]	atha brahmacārī striyā maithunasaṃyoga idaṃ karoti so'vakīrṇītyucyate /
5.10.17-18.[7]	tasya prāyaścittamidaṃ karmocyate
5.10.19-21.[1]	brahmacāriṇaṃ darbharajjvā kaṇṭhe baddhvā 'yatte devī nirṛtiḥ' iti sūktena tilāñjuhoti /
5.10.19-21.[2]	brahmacāriṇaṃ darbharajjvā kaṇṭhe baddhvā tato 'yatte devī nirṛtiḥ' iti sūktena vrīhiñjuhoti /
5.10.19-21.[3]	avakīrṇinaṃ darbharajjvā kaṇṭhe baddhvā abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yatte devī' iti sūktenodapātraṃ sampātya tato darbharajjvā samprokṣya tato 'yatte devī' iti muñcati /
5.10.19-21.[4]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.19-21.[5]	darbharajjvāvakīrṇinaṃ kaṇṭhe baddhvā tataḥ śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā tato 'yatte devī' iti sūktena prokṣya tataḥ sūktenaiva darbharajjuṃ muñcati /
5.10.19-21.[6]	samāptamavakīrṇiprāyaścittam /
5.10.19-21.[7]	sarvatra karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
5.10.19-21.[8]	kramo'pi nāsti sarvatra //
5.10.19-21.[9]	atha svayamprajvalite'gnau prāyaścittamucyate
5.10.22.[1]	'saṃ samid' ityṛcā yavāñjuhoti /
5.10.22.[2]	'saṃ samid' ityṛcā tilāñjuhoti /
5.10.22.[3]	yadi jvalati svayamagnistadedaṃ karma /
5.10.22.[4]	svayamprajvalite śāntiḥ //
5.10.22.[5]	athāgniśabdakaraṇe śāntirucyate
5.10.23-24.[1]	atha sandeśe vismṛte 'yadasmṛti' ityṛcāgnimupatiṣṭhate /
5.10.23-24.[2]	yadi grāme vā gṛhe vā sandeśaṃ na kathayati tadā idaṃ prāyaścittam //
5.10.23-24.[3]	atha pāpanakṣatre jāte strī vā puruṣo vā yo jātastasya śāntirucyate
5.10.25.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā tasya muñjarajjvā kaṇṭhe ca pāde ca baddhvā tataḥ 'pratno hi' iti sūktenodakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya darbhapiñjūlī ghaṭe prakṣipya tato'bhiṣiñcati /
5.10.25.[2]	tato'bhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.10.25.[3]	grīvāṃ pāśaṃ nadīpheneṣu nidadhāti 'nadīnāṃ phenān' ityardharcena kaṭipāśamudakamadhye prakṣipati /
5.10.25.[4]	mātṛpitṛbhrātṛṣu doṣaḥ śrūyate tasmāt pāpanakṣatre śāntiḥ kartavyeti /
5.10.25.[5]	ārdrāśleṣā maghā citrā svāti viśākhā jyeṣṭhā mūlaṃ śatabhiṣak bharaṇī etāni pāpanakṣatrāṇi /
5.10.25.[6]	eteṣu yo jāyate tasyedaṃ karma gaṇḍena sandhau ca /
5.10.25.[7]	mūle nakṣatra idaṃ karma kriyate /
5.10.25.[8]	yo nakṣatrakalpoktaṃ karma kuryāttaducyate /
5.10.25.[9]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'pratno hi' iti sūktenāgamakṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /
5.10.25.[10]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.10.25.[11]	etasmin tantre samūlaṃ barhi stṛṇāti samūlamidhmamupasamādhāyaiṣa viśeṣaḥ /
5.10.25.[12]	nakṣatrakalpoktaṃ sarvaṃ ca /
5.10.25.[13]	kāle prayogaḥ /
5.10.25.[14]	etannakṣatrakalpa uktam /
5.10.25.[15]	etāni pāpanakṣatre jātasya samāptāni /
5.10.25.[16]	eṣā nakṣatrakalpoktā śāntiḥ /
5.10.25.[17]	āplāvanāvasecane ca kṣīraudanaprāśanaṃ caitāni trīṇi /
5.10.25.[18]	athavā 'pratno hi' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya pāpanakṣatrajātamavasiñcati śirasi /
5.10.25.[19]	etāni trīṇi karmāṇi bhavanti /
5.10.25.[20]	samāptā pāpanakṣatrajātaśāntiḥ //
5.10.25.[21]	atha jyeṣṭhe bhrātari jīvati vivāhamādhānaṃ dīkṣāṃ ca karoti tasya śāntirucyate
5.10.26-28.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'mā jyeṣṭham' 'trite devāḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudakaghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tato mauñjaiḥ pāśairbaddhvā tato darbhasahitena ghaṭenāplāvayati /
5.10.26-28.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
5.10.26-28.[3]	uttarapāśaṃ 'nadīnāṃ phenān' ityardharcena nadīphene nidadhāti /
5.10.26-28.[4]	adharapāśān gṛhītvā nadīmadhye praviśya tūṣṇīṃ prakṣipati //
5.10.29.[1]	'mā jyeṣṭham' 'trite devāḥ' iti sūktābhyāmudakamabhimantrya tato bandhanaṃ kṛtvā tato'vasiñcati /
5.10.29.[2]	pūrvavat pāśotsargaḥ /
5.10.29.[3]	abhyātānāntaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ambayo yanti' ityādibhiḥ sarvairapāṃ sūktairghaṭaṃ sampātyābhimantryāplāvayati /
5.10.29.[4]	uttaratantram /
5.10.29.[5]	parivittiparivettṛprāyaścittam /
5.10.29.[6]	'ambayo yanti' ityādibhiḥ sarvairapāṃ sūktairudakamabhimantryāvasiñcati /
5.10.29.[7]	samāptaṃ parivittiparivettṛprāyaścittam /
5.10.29.[8]	dvayoḥ pṛthak pṛthak bhavati //
5.10.29.[9]	atha mṛte ācārya idaṃ karma
5.10.30-32.[1]	devaheḍanenānuvākena sruveṇājyaṃ juhoti /
5.10.30-32.[2]	mṛta ācārya āhitāgnau idaṃ karma bhavati //
5.10.30-32.[3]	atha devapitṛvarjitakhadāśayahitasyānnasya yājñikena karmaṇā bhavati taducyate
5.10.33-35.[1]	'yaddevā devaheḍanam' ityanuvākena khadāyā annāduddhṛtya setikāmekāṃ juhoti /
5.10.33-35.[2]	tantravikalpaḥ /
5.10.33-35.[3]	pratyṛcaṃ yavahomaḥ /
5.10.33-35.[4]	vaivasvatadevatākaṃ pākayajñamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yaddevā devaheḍanam' ityanuvākena caruṃ juhoti /
5.10.33-35.[5]	khadāśayasya prāyaścittam /
5.10.33-35.[6]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
5.10.33-35.[7]	yaddevā devaheḍanamityanuvākena khadānnaṃ catuḥśarāvaparimitamabhimantrya tato brāhmaṇāya dadāti /
5.10.33-35.[8]	khadāśayānnasaṃskāraśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.33-35.[9]	atha mṛte dhanika ṛṇikasyarṇadānaśāntirucyate
5.10.36.[1]	'apamityamapratīttam' iti tribhiḥ sūktairdravyamabhimantrya putrāya dadāti /
5.10.36.[2]	anṛṇo bhavati //
5.10.37.[1]	'apamityamapratīttam' iti tribhiḥ sūktairdravyamabhimantrya gotriṇe dadāti /
5.10.37.[2]	anṛṇo bhavati //
5.10.38.[1]	'apamityamapratīttam' iti tribhiḥ sūktaiḥ dravyamabhimantrya dhanikasya śmaśāne nikṣipati /
5.10.38.[2]	anṛṇo bhavati //
5.10.39.[1]	'apamityamapratīttam' iti tribhiḥ sūktairdravyamabhimantrya grāmacatuṣpathe nikṣipet /
5.10.39.[2]	anṛṇo bhavati //
5.10.40.[1]	'apamityamapratīttam' iti tribhiḥ sūktairdravyamabhimantryāgnau prajvalite prakṣipya tato'nṛṇo bhavati /
5.10.40.[2]	ṛṇadānaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.40.[3]	ākāśodakena śarīrāplavane doṣo bhavati tasya śāntirucyate
5.10.41-42.[1]	'divo nu māṃ bṛhataḥ' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya śarīraṃ prakṣālayati /
5.10.41-42.[2]	ākāśabindupatanadoṣo na bhavati /
5.10.41-42.[3]	'divo nu māṃ bṛhataḥ' iti sūktenaikatra tailaṃ sarvauṣadhiḥ gandhaṃ hiraṇyaṃ vāsa etānyabhimantrya śarīramudvartayet /
5.10.41-42.[4]	tataḥ śāntirbhavati /
5.10.41-42.[5]	ākāśabindudoṣopaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.41-42.[6]	atha kumārasya kumāryā vā yasyottamadantau pūrvau jātau tatra mātāpitrormaraṇaśaṅkā bhavati tatra śāntirucyate
5.10.43.[1]	'yau vyāghrau' iti sūktena vrīhiñjuhoti /
5.10.43.[2]	'yau vyāghrau' iti sūktena yavāñjuhoti /
5.10.43.[3]	'yau vyāghrau' iti sūktena tilāñjuhoti /
5.10.43.[4]	tantravikalpaḥ /
5.10.43.[5]	sarvatra kramo nāsti //
5.10.44.[1]	'yau vyāghrau' iti sūktena vrīhiyavatilamāṣānekīkṛtvābhimantryottamajātadantābhyāṃ daṃśayati //
5.10.45-46.[1]	athājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā vrīhiyavatilamāṣānekīkṛtya tataḥ śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā tato'bhyātānāni hutvā 'yau vyāghrau' iti sūktena sthālīpākaṃ sampātyābhimantrya tata uttamajātadantamāśayati /
5.10.45-46.[2]	mātāpitarau vāśayataḥ /
5.10.45-46.[3]	śāntyudakena sthālīpākasya śrapaṇam /
5.10.45-46.[4]	ājyabhāgānte sarvatra śāntyudakakriyā kartavyā /
5.10.45-46.[5]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.10.45-46.[6]	uttamadantajātadoṣaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.45-46.[7]	atha śirasi aṅge vā kākopaviṣṭadoṣaḥ śrūyate tasya śāntirucyate
5.10.47.[1]	'idaṃ yatkṛṣṇaḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāmudakamabhimantrya śarīraṃ prakṣālayati /
5.10.47.[2]	kākopaviṣṭadoṣo na bhavati /
5.10.47.[3]	snānaṃ vā karoti //
5.10.48.[1]	'idaṃ yatkṛṣṇaḥ' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāmulmukamabhimantrya kākamukhenopamṛṣṭaṃ puruṣaṃ paryagni karoti /
5.10.48.[2]	upari bhrāmayitvā dūre nikṣipati /
5.10.48.[3]	kākopaviṣṭadoṣaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.48.[4]	atha saṃsargadoṣaśāntirucyate
5.10.49.[1]	barhirlavanādyājyatantra idhmasthāne'pāmārgedhmamupasamādhāya tato'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'pratīcīnaphalaḥ' iti tisṛbhirṛgbhirapāmārgasamidha ādadhāti /
5.10.49.[2]	sarvatra prādeśamātrīḥ samidho bhavati /
5.10.49.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
5.10.49.[4]	athavāpāmārgakāṣṭhaprajvalite'gnau 'pratīcīnaphalaḥ' iti tisṛbhirapāmārgasamidha ādadhāti /
5.10.49.[5]	hastahomatvāt tantravikalpaḥ /
5.10.49.[6]	sarveṣu rogeṣu śyāvadatā kunakhinā ṣaṇḍena jvareṇāpāmārgādi sarveṣu rogeṣu saṃsargeṣu sarvadoṣānmucyate /
5.10.49.[7]	saṃsarge doṣaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.50.[1]	'yadarvācīnam' ityṛcodakamabhimantryācāmayati /
5.10.50.[2]	anṛtamuktvācamanaṃ karoti //
5.10.50.[3]	vaṇijyanṛtaṃ kṛtvācamanaṃ karoti /
5.10.50.[4]	anṛtadoṣo na bhavati /
5.10.50.[5]	anṛtavacanadoṣaśamanaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.51.[1]	yatra kvacit khanati tatra sarvatra 'yatte bhūme' ityṛcā khanati gṛhanidhau vā sthūṇāgarte vā snānārthaṃ mṛttikāgrahaprakaraṇārthaṃ sarvatra mṛttikākhananaṃ vidhānena //
5.10.52.[1]	'yatta ūnam' ityṛcā gṛhādi pūrayati sarvatrānena vidhānena pūraṇam /
5.10.52.[2]	khanane khananadoṣo na bhavati /
5.10.52.[3]	pūraṇe pūraṇadoṣo na bhavati /
5.10.52.[4]	samāptā khananapūraṇaśāntiḥ //
5.10.52.[5]	atha śakunaśāntirucyate
5.10.53-54.[1]	'prehi pra hara vā dāvān' iti sūktena ṣaḍarcenāpaśabdaṃ śrutvā japati kapiñjalavāsitaṃ śrutvā grāme'raṇye pakṣivāsitaṃ śrutvā vā svayaṃ vā kruddhabhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvānyasyāsadvacanaṃ śrutvā sāgovāse vā ulūkavāsane kapotavāsane pūrvato vottarato vā loke ninditaḥ /
5.10.53-54.[2]	yatkiñcillokaviruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā vā sarvatra japane svastyayanaṃ bhavati /
5.10.53-54.[3]	'prehi pra hara' iti sūktaṃ nityaṃ japati /
5.10.53-54.[4]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
5.10.53-54.[5]	samāptaṃ nityajapasvastyayanam /
5.10.53-54.[6]	apaśakunajapastyayanaśāntiḥ samāptā //
5.10.55.[1]	ākāśe yaddhi svapiti araṇye vā gṛhe vā śūnye gṛhe vā parvate vā tadā 'yo abhyu babhruṇā' ityṛcaṃ japitvā svapiti /
5.10.55.[2]	rājasenā ākāśe svapiti araṇye tadedaṃ karma kuryāt /
5.10.55.[3]	naimittikānyavaśyaṃ kartavyāni /
5.10.55.[4]	akaraṇe dhanadhānyapaśvādivināśaḥ /
5.10.55.[5]	tasmānnityanaimittikāni kāryāṇi /
5.10.55.[6]	'jarāyuja iti durdinamāyan' ityādīni /
5.10.55.[7]	athādbhutāni varṣe yakṣaṣvādīni naimittikāni tānyavaśyaṃ kāryāṇi /
5.10.55.[8]	akaraṇe gṛhe grāme vā nagare vā janapade vā doṣa utpadyate /
5.10.55.[9]	medhājananagrāmasampadāsarvasampadāsāmmanasyavarcasyavijayarājakarmapauṣṭikastrīkarmasvastyayanāyuṣyakāmyādīni ijyāyāḥ pravṛttiḥ /
5.10.55.[10]	yadi kāmyecchā tadā tadā pravṛttiḥ /
5.10.55.[11]	athavā necchā tadā na prayuñjyāt /
5.10.55.[12]	nityāni jātakarmādīni /
5.10.55.[13]	nityānāṃ naimittikānāmakaraṇe pratyavāyo bhavati /
5.10.55.[14]	tathā coktam /
5.10.55.[15]	nityanaimittike kuryāt pratyavāyajighāṃsayā /
5.10.55.[16]	mantrakrameṇa naimittikānyuktāni saṃhitāvidhau //
5.10.55.[17]	mantravidhānaṃ kauśike /
5.10.55.[18]	brāhmaṇapāṭhatvāt samāptāni naimittikāni /
5.10.55.[19]	sarvajñānaprabodhārthaṃ vijñānaṃ proktavānṛṣiḥ /
5.10.55.[20]	duṣṭadoṣavināśāya naimittikāni pañcame //
5.10.55.[21]	daśamī kaṇḍikā //
6.1.0.[1]	atha kramaprāpto'tharvavedavihito'bhicāra ucyate /
6.1.0.[2]	mīmāṃsāyāmabhicāro niṣiddhaḥ /
6.1.0.[3]	'codanālakṣaṇo'rtho dharmaḥ' iti /
6.1.0.[4]	hiṃsācāraḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ /
6.1.0.[5]	punarupapāde'bhicāraḥ samarthitaḥ /
6.1.0.[6]	manusmṛtau ca vihito'bhicāro 'na brāhmaṇo vedayitā kadācit' ityādinā /
6.1.0.[7]	tasmāt śrutiratharvāṅgirasī kuryādabhicārakam iti /
6.1.0.[8]	doṣaśca śrūyate /
6.1.0.[9]	'ṣaṭsvabhicaran patati' iti manuḥ /
6.1.0.[10]	'pramāṇaṃ smṛtiḥ' ityuktaṃ mīmāṃsāyām /
6.1.0.[11]	tasmādvihito'bhicāraḥ kartavyaḥ //
6.1.1-2.[1]	āṅgirasakalpoktāḥ sambhārāḥ pratyetavyāḥ /
6.1.1-2.[2]	dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi maṇḍapaṃ kuryāt /
6.1.1-2.[3]	kṛttikānakṣatre prayogaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe vā rātrau nirodhi vā /
6.1.1-2.[4]	maṇḍapaṃ kārayettatra yathoktavidhinā guruḥ /
6.1.1-2.[5]	patākātoraṇairyuktaṃ dvāraṃ vā dakṣiṇaṃ smṛtam //
6.1.3.[1]	viṣamiśramiṅgiḍamājyam //
6.1.4-11.[1]	'tathā tadagne' ityādi smartavyaṃ sarvatra /
6.1.4-11.[2]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'dūṣyā dūṣirasi' iti sūktena tilakamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
6.1.4-11.[3]	kārayitā kartā sadasyāśca sarveṣāṃ bandhanamātmarakṣārtham //
6.1.4-11.[4]	adhunā dīkṣocyate
6.1.12.[1]	śuklapakṣe trayodaśyāṃ pūrvāhṇe'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'dyāvāpṛthivī urvantarikṣam' iti sūktam /
6.1.12.[2]	'kanakarajata' iti sūktam /
6.1.12.[3]	dvābhyāṃ veṇudaṇḍaṃ vṛścati chinatti kartā //
6.1.13.[1]	'mṛtyoraham' ityṛcā bādhakīrādadhāti samidhaḥ //
6.1.14-15.[1]	'ya imāṃ devo mekhalām' iti pañcarcena sūktena mekhalāṃ sampātya /
6.1.14-15.[2]	'ayaṃ vajraḥ' iti tṛcena sūktena daṇḍaṃ sampātya 'ya imām' iti tṛcena mekhalāṃ badhnāti //
6.1.16.[1]	'vajro'si sapatnahā' iti tṛcena sūktena daṇḍaṃ gṛhṇāti /
6.1.16.[2]	'namo namaskṛdbhyaḥ' iti saptarṣibhya upasthānaṃ karoti śālāyā bahiḥ /
6.1.16.[3]	tataḥ śālāyāṃ praviśya tato vratādānīyāḥ samidha ādadhāti śāntāḥ /
6.1.16.[4]	vrataśrāvaṇaṃ tasmin karoti /
6.1.16.[5]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
6.1.16.[6]	dīkṣitastrirātramanaśanam /
6.1.16.[7]	trirātre nivṛtte kṛṣṇapakṣe pratipadi karma bhaviṣyati /
6.1.16.[8]	'namo namaskṛdbhyaḥ sumati prayuñje na me prasūta taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇā nayāmenyā' ityupasthānamantraḥ /
6.1.16.[9]	'agne vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmi tacchakeyaṃ tatsamāpeyaṃ tasmin me ṛddhiḥ /
6.1.16.[10]	tasmai namastasmai svāhā' iti /
6.1.16.[11]	indra /
6.1.16.[12]	soma /
6.1.16.[13]	sūrya /
6.1.16.[14]	candra /
6.1.16.[15]	devā vratapatayaḥ /
6.1.16.[16]	āpo vratapatnyaḥ /
6.1.16.[17]	vratānāṃ vratapatayaḥ /
6.1.16.[18]	vratādānīyāḥ samidhamantrāḥ //
6.1.16.[19]	'kanakarajatakaredvasopā mārayiṣyāmi taṃ janam /
6.1.16.[20]	prajāṃ tasya paśūṃśca ete agne āvṛścāmyahan nyudito jane /
6.1.16.[21]	gṛhāṃśca tasya vināśanakāme kāmavānahaṃ' ca /
6.1.16.[22]	anvā vṛścāmi devebhya anvā vṛścāmyagnaye anvā pṛthivyai vṛścāmi anvā vṛścāmi mṛtyave //
6.1.16.[23]	āvṛkte asi devebhyo dṛṣṭvā oṣadhīṣu ca āvṛkta iti dve /
6.1.16.[24]	viṣṇo saṃ tvā vṛścāmi sarvataḥ //
6.1.16.[25]	'anvā vṛścāmi devamanuṣyebhyo bhūtaye /
6.1.16.[26]	anvā nirṛtyāḥ pāśebhyo vṛścāmi yathā mṛtyo na mocchiṣat' /
6.1.16.[27]	āṅgirasadaṇḍavṛścanasūktam //

6.3.4.[1]	'jiṣṇave yogāya' ityuttarārdharcaiḥ ṣaḍudakasamīpe ghaṭaṃ nidadhāti //
6.3.14.[1]	'idamahaṃ yo mā prācyā diśaḥ' ityaṣṭarcena kalpajena sūktenodakamadhye ghaṭaṃ nidadhāti /
6.3.14.[2]	'idamaham' iti ghaṭamudake'dhomukhaṃ karoti /
6.3.14.[3]	'idamaham' iti sūktena ghaṭamudakapūrṇaṃ kṛtvāpakrāmati /
6.3.14.[4]	'idamahaṃ yo mā prācyā diśaḥ' sūktenodakapūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ maṇḍape sthāpayati /
6.3.14.[5]	etadabhicāra udakāharaṇam /
6.3.14.[6]	yena vidhānena vajrapraharaṇaṃ kriyate taducyate /
6.3.14.[7]	'indrasyaujaḥ' ityādi sarvaṃ kṛtvā 'idamaham' iti sthāpanāntaṃ kṛtvā 'agnerbhāgaḥ stha' ityaṣṭābhirṛgbhirdvidhākaraṇam /
6.3.14.[8]	ardhaṃ ghaṭe kṛtvārdhaṃ bhājane karoti /
6.3.14.[9]	bhājanamagnau tāpayati /
6.3.14.[10]	ghaṭamanyasmai puruṣāya pradāpayati /
6.3.14.[11]	'agnerbhāgaḥ' ityaṣṭau tāpane mantrāḥ /
6.3.14.[12]	barhirāsane dakṣiṇāmukha upaviśya bhājanamagnau kṛtvā 'vātasya raṃhitasyāmṛtasya yoniḥ' iti mantreṇodakaṃ gṛhītvā 'śamagnaye' iti sūktena kalpajena sarvebhyo bhūtebhyo'bhayaṃ vadet /
6.3.14.[13]	'yo va āpo'pāṃ bhāgo'psvantaḥ' ityṛcodavajraprakṣepaḥ /
6.3.14.[14]	punarapi 'vātasya raṃhitasya' ityudakaṃ saṅgṛhya 'śamagnaye' ityabhayaṃ dattvā 'yo va āpo'pāmūrmirapsvantaḥ' ityṛcā vajraprakṣepaḥ /
6.3.14.[15]	punarapi 'vātasya raṃhitasya' ityudakaṃ saṅgṛhya 'śamagnaye' ityabhayaṃ dattvā 'yo va āpo'pāṃ vatso'psvantaḥ' iti vajraṃ prakṣipet /
6.3.14.[16]	'vātasya raṃhitasya' ityudakaṃ saṅgṛhya 'śamagnaye' ityabhayaṃ dattvā 'yo va āpo'pāṃ vṛṣabho'psvantaḥ' ityṛcā vajraṃ prakṣipet /
6.3.14.[17]	punaḥ 'vātasya raṃhitasya' ityudakaṃ gṛhītvā 'śamagnaye' ityabhayaṃ dattvā 'yo va āpo'pāṃ hiraṇyagarbho'psvantaḥ' ityṛcā vajraṃ prakṣipet /
6.3.14.[18]	punaḥ 'vātasya raṃhitasya' ityudakaṃ saṅgṛhya 'śamagnaye' ityabhayaṃ dattvā 'yo va āpo'pāmaśmā pṛśniḥ' ityṛcā vajraṃ prakṣipet /
6.3.14.[19]	punaḥ 'vātasya raṃhitasyāmṛtasya yoniḥ' iti mantreṇodakaṃ saṅgṛhya 'śamagnaye' ityabhayaṃ dattvā 'yo va āpo'pāmagnayo'psvantaḥ' ityṛcā vajraṃ prakṣipet /
6.3.14.[20]	'enamenānadharācaḥ parācaḥ' iti kalpajayarcā bhājanasthamudakaṃ bhūmau ninayati /
6.3.14.[21]	'yaṃ vayam' iti sūktenaivam 'apāmasmai vajram' ityekayaivameva /
6.3.14.[22]	'indrasyaujaḥ' ityādi kartavyam /
6.3.14.[23]	tatra rudrakṛtāḥ ślokāḥ /
6.3.14.[24]	prakṣālanaṃ tathā yogo apsu pātranidhāpanam /
6.3.14.[25]	apohanamanenaiva taṃ niveṣṭya pātrapūraṇam //
6.3.14.[26]	apakrāmastadāyaṃ tu sūktenedamahaṃ tataḥ /
6.3.14.[27]	nidhāpanādi tenaiva sarvatrānīya sādayet //
6.3.14.[28]	vibhāgadānasantāpā grahaṇaṃ śāntayaśca yāḥ /
6.3.14.[29]	vajrātisargāvityete sapta vajrasya kevalāḥ //
6.3.14.[30]	grahaṇaṃ prativajraṃ cābhayadānaṃ tathaiva ca //
6.3.14.[31]	ete ślokāḥ /
6.3.14.[32]	'viṣṇoḥ kramo'si' iti dvādaśabhiḥ pratyṛcaṃ viṣṇukramān kramate śatrorabhimukham //
6.3.15.[1]	savavidhānena bṛhaspatiśirasamodanaṃ dveṣyāya dadāti /
6.3.15.[2]	'mamāgne varcaḥ' iti sūktena taṃ pṛṣātakenopasicya 'tasyaudanasya' ityarthasūktenābhimantrya dadāti /
6.3.15.[3]	sūktenābhimṛśati /
6.3.15.[4]	sūktena sampātavantaṃ karoti /
6.3.15.[5]	tantram /
6.3.15.[6]	sūktaṃ vācayati /
6.3.15.[7]	'tribhiḥ sthānaiḥ' ityuktam //
6.3.16-18.[1]	'udehi vājin' ityardharcena nāvacaṭitaṃ dveṣyamanvāha //
6.3.19-21.[1]	'samiddho agniḥ samidhāno ghṛtavṛddhaḥ' iti pañcarcena śaṅkusahitān pāśānabhimantryāraṇye nidadhāti /
6.3.19-21.[2]	'samiddho agniḥ' iti sūktena pañcarcena pāśānabhimantrya dveṣyasya padaṃ vṛścati vidhānena /
6.3.19-21.[3]	'samiddho agniḥ' iti sūktena pañcarcena śaṅkusahitān pāśān pade'vacchinatti /
6.3.19-21.[4]	tān sannahya bhraṣṭe'bhyasyati /
6.3.19-21.[5]	'ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī' ityanuvākena śaṅkusahitāñchatruṣu pāśān baddhvābhimantrya vṛścati padepade /
6.3.19-21.[6]	'ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī' ityanuvākenādhipāśān bādhakāñchaṅkūṃstān saṅkṣudya sannahya bhraṣṭe'bhyasyati /
6.3.19-21.[7]	aṣṭau sūktāvṛttiḥ /
6.3.19-21.[8]	'ajaiṣma' iti sūktacatuṣṭayena 'aganma svaḥ' ityavasānadvayavarjitena śatruṣu pāśān baddhvābhimantryāraṇye nidadhāti /
6.3.19-21.[9]	'ajaiṣma' iti sūktacatuṣṭayenottamāvasānadvayavarjitena pāśān abhimantrya pade pade vṛścati /
6.3.19-21.[10]	'ajaiṣma' iti sūktacatuṣṭayena 'aganma svaḥ' iti varjitenādhipāśān bādhakāñchaṅkūṃstān saṅkṣudya sannahya bhraṣṭe'bhyasyati //
6.3.22.[1]	'samiddho agniḥ samidhānaḥ' iti pañcarcenāmapātrasyopari dveṣyāya hastaprakṣālanaṃ dadāti /
6.3.22.[2]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'samiddho agniḥ' iti pañcarcena vṛṣabhaṃ sampātyātisṛjati /
6.3.22.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
6.3.22.[4]	'ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī' ityanuvākena raktaśālikṣīraudanaṃ sampātyābhimantrya dveṣyāya dadāti /
6.3.22.[5]	'ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī' ityanuvākenāmapātrasyopari dveṣyāya hastaprakṣālanaṃ dadāti /
6.3.22.[6]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī' ityanuvākena vṛṣabhaṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvā śatrumabhimukhaṃ visṛjati /
6.3.22.[7]	uttaratantram /
6.3.22.[8]	'ajaiṣma' iti caturbhiḥ paryāyaiḥ 'aganma svaḥ' ityavasānadvayavarjyaṃ raktaśālikṣīraudanamabhimantrya dadāti /
6.3.22.[9]	tantre /
6.3.22.[10]	'ajaiṣma' iti pūrvam /
6.3.22.[11]	āmapātrasyopari dveṣyāya hastaprakṣālanaṃ dadāti /
6.3.22.[12]	'ajaiṣma' iti pūrvaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvā śatrugṛhānabhimṛśati /
6.3.22.[13]	vṛṣotsargavat //
6.3.23.[1]	prathame divase'bhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā śatrupratikṛtiṃ ca mṛnmayāṃ kṛtvā vedimadhya ūrdhvaṃ sthāṇau nibadhya 'samiddho agniḥ' iti pañcarcena mūrdhni sampātānānayati /
6.3.23.[2]	ghṛtena pācayati pradidinam /
6.3.23.[3]	ekatantraṃ yāvat /
6.3.23.[4]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
6.3.23.[5]	ābhicārikaṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī' ityanuvākena śatrupratikṛtiṃ mṛnmayāṃ paścādagneḥ sthāṇau baddhvā tasya mūrdhni sampātānānayati /
6.3.23.[6]	pratidinaṃ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
6.3.23.[7]	dvādaśame divase'bhyātānādyuttaratantram /
6.3.23.[8]	abhicāraṃ tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ajaiṣma' iti caturbhiḥ sūktairgartedhmāvantareṇāvalekhanīṃ sthāṇau nibadhya dvādaśarātraṃ sampātānānayati /
6.3.23.[9]	abhyātānāni hutvā /
6.3.23.[10]	tataḥ sviṣṭakṛdādyuttaratantram //
6.3.24.[1]	'yasmin ṣaḍurvīḥ pañca' ityudavajrān praharati /
6.3.24.[2]	uktena vidhānena //
6.3.25.[1]	'yo annādo'nnapatiḥ' ityṛcodakamabhimantrya dveṣyaṃ manasā cādhyāyan sa cācāmati /
6.3.25.[2]	svayaṃ kartā /
6.3.25.[3]	dveṣyasya maraṇaṃ bhavati //
6.3.26.[1]	'yaśca gāṃ padā sphurati' ityardharcena dveṣyaṃ dṛṣṭvānvāha japati /
6.3.26.[2]	uttaratantram /
6.3.26.[3]	ābhicārike tantre viśeṣaḥ /
6.3.26.[4]	pārvaṇau samṛddhiḥ sannatirete homā na bhavanti /
6.3.26.[5]	abhyātānāni hutvā tataḥ sviṣṭakṛdādyuttaratantraṃ bhavati /
6.3.26.[6]	'niramuṃ nuda' iti saṃsthitahomaḥ /
6.3.26.[7]	'viṣṇoḥ kramo'si' iti viṣṇukramān /
6.3.26.[8]	dvādaśa bhavanti /
6.3.26.[9]	jāṅmāyane sampātā na bhavanti /
6.3.26.[10]	śeṣaṃ samānam /
6.3.26.[11]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'idāvatsarāya' iti vratavisarjanamājyaṃ juhuyāt /
6.3.26.[12]	samidho'bhyādadhyāt /
6.3.26.[13]	vratasamāpanīraṣṭau samidha ādadhyāt /
6.3.26.[14]	abhyātānādi śāntam uttaratantram //
6.3.27.[1]	avabhṛthaṃ snātvā 'nirdurmaṇyaḥ' iti sūktena sarvauṣadhirātmānamabhimṛśati /
6.3.27.[2]	spṛśatītyarthaḥ /
6.3.27.[3]	abhicāraṃ kṛtvā kartemāṃ śāntiṃ karoti /
6.3.27.[4]	maraṇaṃ bandhanaṃ vā vyasanaṃ vā praṇipāto vonmattatābhāvo vā bhavati /
6.3.27.[5]	abhicārapaddhatiḥ samāptā //
6.3.27.[6]	bhadramatena bhāṣyakāra tathā dārilamatena ca /
6.3.27.[7]	ebhistribhirbhāṣyakāraiḥ kauśikīyo vicāritaḥ //
6.3.27.[8]	tasya tasyaite padārthā bhavanti /
6.3.27.[9]	maraṇaṃ vā bandhanaṃ vā vyasanaṃ vā praṇipāto vonmattatā vā daivopahatirvā putradhanādivināśo bhavati /
6.3.27.[10]	tatra ślokāḥ /
6.3.27.[11]	maraṇaṃ vyasanaṃ caiva bandhanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ /
6.3.27.[12]	praṇipātonmattatā vā daivopahatireva ca //
6.3.27.[13]	putrādidhananāśaśca gṛhe doṣān bahūnapi /
6.3.27.[14]	abhicarati puruṣa etāni tu vinirdiśet /
6.3.27.[15]	trayāṇāṃ bhāṣyakārāṇāṃ mataṃ jagrāha kauśikī //
6.3.27.[16]	upādhyāyakavīśvareṇa nāmato'bhicāraḥ kṛtaḥ turuṣkamahumadasyopari kāritaḥ //
6.3.27.[17]	pṛthivyāṃ duṣṭa utpannaḥ sarvadā ca vināśayet /
6.3.27.[18]	adharmasambhavo duṣṭaḥ prajāhiṃsanatatparaḥ //
6.3.27.[19]	turuṣkanāmnā pāpiṣṭhā devabrāhmaṇahiṃsakāḥ /
6.3.27.[20]	pṛthivyāṃ śrībhojadevo dharmasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca //
6.3.27.[21]	deśe mālavaka utpannaḥ śrīrājagṛheṣu ca /
6.3.27.[22]	śrībhojadevo jagadvikhyāto rājñāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca mūrdhani //
6.3.27.[23]	na ca tulyo jagatpatirna bhūto na bhaviṣyati /
6.3.27.[24]	atharvavedavihitānāmanuṣṭhātā savakarmaṇām /
6.3.27.[25]	pratiboddhāraśāstrāṇāṃ svayaṃ rājyasya cintakaḥ /
6.3.27.[26]	devabrāhmaṇabhaktaśca guruśuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ //
6.3.27.[27]	atharvavedavihitā mahāśāntiranekaśaḥ /
6.3.27.[28]	kārāpitā yathoktāstena yathāvihitadakṣiṇāḥ //
6.3.27.[29]	brahmakṣatriyarakṣaṇārthā abhicārā maharṣiṇā /
6.3.27.[30]	krameṇa sūtritāḥ ṣaṣṭhe saṃhitākramakāraṇāt //
6.3.27.[31]	iti ṣaṣṭhe tṛtīyā kaṇḍikā //
7.1.0.[1]	svastyayanakarmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
7.1.1.[1]	yadā grāme gacchati tadācamanaṃ kṛtvā 'svastidāḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā dakṣiṇena pādena prakrāmatyadhvānam /
7.1.1.[2]	'ye te panthāno'va divaḥ' ityṛcaṃ japitvādhvānaṃ dakṣiṇena pādena prakrāmati /
7.1.1.[3]	tato grāmaṃ gacchati /
7.1.1.[4]	svastyayanaṃ bhavati //
7.1.2.[1]	'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena śarkarā abhimantrya gṛhe kṣetre'nyatra vā prakṣipati /
7.1.2.[2]	svastyarthī /
7.1.2.[3]	idaṃ karma /
7.1.2.[4]	sarvārthakāmaḥ /
7.1.2.[5]	'ye te panthānaḥ' ityekarcena sūktenāsaṅkhyātāḥ śarkarā abhimantrya gṛhādiṣu prakṣipati /
7.1.2.[6]	idaṃ karma sarvārthasvastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.2.[7]	yatra kṣipati tatrāvināśo bhavati /
7.1.2.[8]	dvipadacatuṣpadādīnāṃ svastyayanaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ //
7.1.3.[1]	'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena darbhādīni tṛṇānyabhimantrya gṛhe vā kṣetre vā prakṣipati svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.3.[2]	'ye te panthāno'va divaḥ' ityṛcā tṛṇānyabhimantrya prakṣipati /
7.1.3.[3]	gṛhe pathi vā svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.3.[4]	'svastidāḥ' iti sūktena indramupatiṣṭhate svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.3.[5]	'ye te panthāno'va divaḥ' ityṛcendramupatiṣṭhate svastyayanakāmaḥ //
7.1.4.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'āre'sau' iti sūktena śastraṃ sampātyābhimantrya prayacchatyabhyātānādyuttaratantram /
7.1.4.[2]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'amūḥ pāre' iti sūktena khaïgādiśastraṃ sampātya hastena vimṛjyābhimantrya dhārayati /
7.1.4.[3]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.4.[4]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'pātaṃ naḥ' iti sūktena churikādiśastraṃ sampātya vimṛjyābhimantrya rājñe prayacchati /
7.1.4.[5]	sukhaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ /
7.1.4.[6]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'ya enaṃ pariṣīdanti' iti sūktena yasya yacchastraṃ tat sampātya vimṛjyābhimantrya yudhi vīrāya prayacchati /
7.1.4.[7]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.4.[8]	uttaratantram /
7.1.4.[9]	śastram /
7.1.4.[10]	churikā /
7.1.4.[11]	dhanuṣam /
7.1.4.[12]	kaṇḍa /
7.1.4.[13]	khaïgam /
7.1.4.[14]	kunta /
7.1.4.[15]	kaḍanala /
7.1.4.[16]	vajra /
7.1.4.[17]	gadā /
7.1.4.[18]	paraśu /
7.1.4.[19]	kuṭhāra /
7.1.4.[20]	bhiṇḍamālā /
7.1.4.[21]	trāsagaṇḍā /
7.1.4.[22]	lohadaṇḍa /
7.1.4.[23]	laṣṭi /
7.1.4.[24]	pāgānim /
7.1.4.[25]	ityādyāyudham //
7.1.5.[1]	'āre'sau' iti sūktaṃ japitvā diṣṭyā mukhaṃ mītvā svapiti rātrau svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.5.[2]	madhyamāṅgulyaṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ prādeśinyaṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ prādeśī diṣṭirityucyate /
7.1.5.[3]	'amūḥ pāre' iti sūktaṃ japitvā diṣṭyā mukhaṃ vimāya svapiti rātrau svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.5.[4]	'pātaṃ naḥ' iti sūktena diṣṭyā mukhaṃ mītvā svapiti rātrau svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.5.[5]	'ya enaṃ pariṣīdanti' iti sūktaṃ japitvā diṣṭyā mukhaṃ vimāya svapiti /
7.1.5.[6]	svastyayanakāmaḥ //
7.1.6.[1]	'āre'sau' iti sūktena yadottiṣṭhati tadā sūktaṃ japitvā trīṇi padāni prakramya tato gacchati svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.6.[2]	prabhāte nidrāṃ tyaktvā 'amūḥ pāre' iti sūktaṃ japitvā trīṇi padāni prakramya tato gacchati prātargrāme vā /
7.1.6.[3]	yadā prayojanārthaṃ gacchati tadā 'pātaṃ naḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā trīṇi padāni prakramya tato gacchati /
7.1.6.[4]	gacchatāṃ svastirbhavati /
7.1.6.[5]	yo mantraṃ paṭhati sa svayaṃ karoti /
7.1.6.[6]	anyakartṛke dakṣiṇādānaṃ sarvatra /
7.1.6.[7]	nidrāṃ tyaktvā 'ya enaṃ pariṣīdanti' iti sūktaṃ japitvā trīṇi padāni prakramya tato gacchati /
7.1.6.[8]	svastyayanakāmaḥ //
7.1.7.[1]	suptotthāya 'āre'sau' iti sūktaṃ japitvā bhūmau tisro diṣṭīrmītvā tato gacchati /
7.1.7.[2]	prayojanārtham /
7.1.7.[3]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.7.[4]	nidrāṃ tyaktvā 'amūḥ pāre' iti sūktaṃ japitvā tisraḥ prādeśīrbhūmau mītvotthāya gacchati /
7.1.7.[5]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.7.[6]	yadā prayojanārthaṃ gacchati tadā 'pātaṃ naḥ' iti sūktaṃ japitvā tisro diṣṭīḥ prādeśīrmītvā bhūmau tato gacchati /
7.1.7.[7]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.7.[8]	suptvotthāya 'ya enaṃ pariṣīdanti' iti sūktena tisraḥ prādeśīrbhūmau mītvā tata uttiṣṭhan gacchati /
7.1.7.[9]	prayojanārtham /
7.1.7.[10]	grāme vā'dhvani vā /
