7.1.4.[1]	rudradevatākaṃ pākayajñamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bhavāśarvau mṛḍatam' ityarthasūktena sārūpavatsasya caruṃ trirvibhajya tataḥ tisra āhutīrjuhoti /
7.1.4.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.1.4.[3]	rudrabhūtapretarākṣasalokapāladevagrahamahādevagaṇādyupahatābhighāte svastyayanam /
7.1.4.[4]	samāptaṃ mahādevābhighāte svastyayanam //
7.1.4.[5]	atha śīghreṇa puṇyamaṅgalakarmakaraṇe svastyayanamucyate
7.1.15-16.[1]	'śakadhūmam' iti caturṛcena suhṛdo brāhmaṇasya śakṛtpiṇḍān parvasvādhāyāgre bhūtvābhimantrya tataḥ śakadhūmaṃ 'kimadyāhaḥ' iti pṛcchati /
7.1.15-16.[2]	sa ca 'śobhanamadyāhaḥ' 'maṅgalamadyāhaḥ' iti brāhmaṇo vadati /
7.1.15-16.[3]	yadā kartā karma kuryāccaturdaśyāṃ caturthyāṃ navamyāṃ vā śanidine vyatīpāte viṣṭāvanyatrāpi nindite'hani tataścandanam /
7.1.15-16.[4]	annaprāśanacūḍākarmanāmakaraṇagṛhapraveśavastrāyalaṅkāradhāraṇam /
7.1.15-16.[5]	rājadarśanāśvahastyādiyānarathārohaṇaṃ puṇyakarme nityanaimittikakāmyādīni karmāṇi /
7.1.15-16.[6]	yadā śīghre prayojane kāryaṃ kartumicchatīdaṃ karma kṛtvā tataḥ śāntikapuṇyakarma karoti /
7.1.15-16.[7]	samāptā śīghrakarmakaraṇe śāntiḥ //
7.1.15-16.[8]	atha sarpādisvastyayanamucyate
7.1.17.[1]	sarpavṛścikadvidaṃśakamaśakabhramarabhūmikīṭakakṛmaya eteṣāṃ bhayaṃ na bhavati /
7.1.17.[2]	'ye'syām' 'prācī dik' iti sūktābhyāṃ sikatāmabhimantrya śayanaṃ parikirati /
7.1.17.[3]	'ye'syāṃ stha' iti sūktena sikatāmabhimantrya śālāṃ paritaḥ kirati /
7.1.17.[4]	'ye'syāṃ stha' iti sūktena sikatāmabhimantrya kṣetre parikirati /
7.1.17.[5]	'prācī dik' iti sūktena śālāṃ parikirati /
7.1.17.[6]	'prācī dik' iti sūktena sikatāmabhimantrya kṣetre parikirati /
7.1.17.[7]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.17.[8]	'mā no devāḥ' iti sūktena śarkarāmabhimantrya śayanaṃ śālāṃ vā kṣetre vā parikirati /
7.1.17.[9]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.17.[10]	'bhavāśarvo mṛḍatam' iti sūktena śarkarāmabhimantrya gṛhe kṣetre vā prakirati svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.17.[11]	'yaste sarpo vṛścikaḥ' ityṛcā śarkarāmabhimantrya śayane vā śālāyāṃ vorvarāyāṃ vā gṛhe vā vane vā grāme vā pattane vā tatra parikirati /
7.1.17.[12]	sarpādisvastyayanaṃ bhavati /
7.1.17.[13]	śāntiḥ /
7.1.17.[14]	nirbhayo bhavatītyarthaḥ //
7.1.18.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ye'syāṃ stha prācyām' iti sūktena tṛṇamālāṃ sampātyābhimantrya dvāre badhnāti /
7.1.18.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
7.1.18.[3]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.18.[4]	mahānavamyāṃ dīpotsave ca śiṣṭācāraḥ /
7.1.18.[5]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'prācī dik' iti sūktena tṛṇamālāṃ yugacchidreṇa sampātyābhimantrya dvāre pracṛtati /
7.1.18.[6]	tata abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
7.1.18.[7]	mahānavamyāmidaṃ jayakarma /
7.1.18.[8]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcā tṛṇamālāṃ yugacchidreṇa sampātyābhimantrya abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'namo devavadhebhyaḥ' iti tṛcena sūktena tṛṇāni yugachidreṇa sampātya dvāre badhnāti /
7.1.18.[9]	tata uttaratantram /
7.1.18.[10]	pathi vā gṛhadvāre vā pattanadvāre vā pracṛtati /
7.1.18.[11]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
7.1.18.[12]	ahibhaye vṛścikabhaye maśakabhaye bhramarasaṅghe kṛmibhaye idaṃ karma //
7.1.19.[1]	'ye'syām' 'prācī dik' iti sūktābhyāṃ gomayamabhimantrya gṛhe visṛjati /
7.1.19.[2]	'mā no devāḥ' iti sūktena gomayamabhimantrya dvāre visṛjati /
7.1.19.[3]	'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcā gomayam abhimantrya dvāre sambhinatti //
7.1.20.[1]	'ye'syām' 'prācī dik' iti sūktābhyāṃ gomayamabhimantrya dvāre nikhanati /
7.1.20.[2]	'mā no devāḥ' iti sūktena śuṣkagomayamabhimantrya gṛhe nikhanati /
7.1.20.[3]	'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcā gomayamabhimantrya gṛhe nikhanati //
7.1.21.[1]	'ye'syām' 'prācī dik' iti sūktābhyāṃ śuṣkagomayamādadhātyagnau /
7.1.21.[2]	'mā no devāḥ' iti sūktena gomayamagnau juhoti /
7.1.21.[3]	'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcā gomayamagnau juhoti /
7.1.21.[4]	gṛhe kṣetre grāme nagare vā svastyayanakāmaḥ //
7.1.22.[1]	'ye'syām' iti sūktenāpāmārgamañjarīmabhimantrya dvāre sambhinatti /
7.1.22.[2]	'ye'syāṃ stha' iti sūktenāpāmārgamañjarīmabhimantrya dvāre nikhanati /
7.1.22.[3]	'ye'syāṃ stha' iti sūktenāpāmārgamañjarīmabhimantryāgnau juhoti /
7.1.22.[4]	'prācī dik' iti sūktenāpāmārgamañjarīmabhimantrya gṛhe stṛṇāti /
7.1.22.[5]	'prācī dik' iti sūktenāpāmārgaprasūnamabhimantrya dvāre nikhanati /
7.1.22.[6]	'prācī dik' iti sūktenāpāmārgamañjarīṃ juhoti /
7.1.22.[7]	'mā no devāḥ' iti sūktenāpāmārgamabhimantrya gṛhe stṛṇāti /
7.1.22.[8]	'mā no devāḥ' iti sūktenāpāmārgamabhimantrya bhūmau nikhanati svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.22.[9]	'mā no devāḥ' iti sūktenāpāmārgamañjarīmabhimantrya agnau juhoti /
7.1.22.[10]	'yaste sarpaḥ' iti apāmārgamañjarīmabhimantrya sambhinatti /
7.1.22.[11]	'yaste sarpaḥ' iti apāmārgamañjarīṃ nikhanati grāmamadhye svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.22.[12]	'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcāpāmārgaṃ juhoti /
7.1.22.[13]	'ye'syāṃ stha' iti sūktena guḍūcīmabhimantrya nānā karoti /
7.1.22.[14]	'ye'syām' iti sūktena guḍūcīmabhimantrya nikhanati /
7.1.22.[15]	'ye'syām' iti sūktena guḍūcīpādānabhimantryāgnau juhoti /
7.1.22.[16]	'prācī dik' iti guḍūcīpādānabhimantrya gṛhe stṛṇāti /
7.1.22.[17]	'prācī dik' iti guḍūcīpādā ye adhomukhāstānabhimantrya nikhanati /
7.1.22.[18]	'prācī dik' iti guḍūcīmagnau juhoti /
7.1.22.[19]	'mā no devāḥ' iti guḍūcīmabhimantrya grāme stṛṇāti /
7.1.22.[20]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.1.22.[21]	'mā no devāḥ' iti guḍūcīmabhimantrya nikhanati /
7.1.22.[22]	'mā no devāḥ' iti guḍūcīmagnau juhoti /
7.1.22.[23]	'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcā guḍūcīmabhimantrya stṛṇāti /
7.1.22.[24]	'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcā guḍūcīmabhimantrya nikhanati /
7.1.22.[25]	'yaste sarpaḥ' ityṛcā guḍūcīmagnau juhoti /
7.1.22.[26]	maśakakīṭakasarpavṛścikādisvastyayanāni bhavanti /
7.1.22.[27]	samāptāni maśakādīnāṃ svastyayanāni //
7.1.22.[28]	saptame prathamā kaṇḍikā //
7.2.0.[1]	atha vyāghracauravṛkacarakasiṃhāraṇyakādīnāṃ bhaye svastyayanāny ucyante
7.2.1.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'uditastrayo akraman' iti sūktena khadirakīlakaṃ sampātya tata uttaratantraṃ kṛtvā kīlakaṃ nikhanannutpāṭayan gṛhādaraṇyaṃ gāṃ pṛṣṭhato gacchati /
7.2.1.[2]	vyāghrādisvastyayanakāmaḥ //
7.2.2.[1]	'uditaḥ' iti sūktenodakaghaṭamabhimantrya gopracāre ninayati /
7.2.2.[2]	tataḥ pāṃśukūṭaṃ tatra kṛtvārddhaṃ dakṣiṇena hastena vikṣipati /
7.2.2.[3]	indrāya pākayajñavidhānenājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'uditaḥ' iti sūktena saptarcena dvābhyāṃ dve āhutī tisṛbhirṛgbhistṛtīyā /
7.2.2.[4]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram //
7.2.3.[1]	sārūpavatsena dugdhe caruśrapaṇaṃ havirucchiṣṭena baliharaṇaṃ kuryāt //
7.2.4-5.[1]	'ye'syāṃ stha' iti sūktena pratyṛcamupatiṣṭhate /
7.2.4-5.[2]	madhye pañca baliharaṇam /
7.2.4-5.[3]	prācī /
7.2.4-5.[4]	dakṣiṇā /
7.2.4-5.[5]	pratīcī /
7.2.4-5.[6]	udīcī /
7.2.4-5.[7]	evaṃ madhyaṃ ca /
7.2.4-5.[8]	prācī /
7.2.4-5.[9]	dakṣiṇā /
7.2.4-5.[10]	pratīcī /
7.2.4-5.[11]	udīcī /
7.2.4-5.[12]	evaṃ copasthānāni //
7.2.6.[1]	anirdiṣṭaṃ śeṣaṃ havirbhūmau ninayatīti pañcamam //
7.2.7.[1]	parvatadevatāyā araṇye pākayajñavidhānenājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'brahma jajñānam' 'anāptā ye' iti sūktena juhoti /
7.2.7.[2]	'himavate juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi /
7.2.7.[3]	himavate tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi /
7.2.7.[4]	himavantaṃ gacchatu haviḥ svāhā' iti /
7.2.7.[5]	nikaṭaparvataṃ yajate /
7.2.7.[6]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram //
7.2.8.[1]	parvatadevatāyai pākayajñamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bhavāśarvau mṛḍatam' ityarthasūktena caruṃ juhoti /
7.2.8.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.2.8.[3]	pākayajñatantraṃ kṛtvā 'bhavāya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' ityādi /
7.2.8.[4]	bhava /
7.2.8.[5]	śarva /
7.2.8.[6]	paśupati /
7.2.8.[7]	ugra /
7.2.8.[8]	rudra /
7.2.8.[9]	mahādeva /
7.2.8.[10]	īśāna /
7.2.8.[11]	etāḥ sapta devatāḥ /
7.2.8.[12]	devatānirvāpaṃ kṛtvaikasmin bhāṇḍake śrapaṇam /
7.2.8.[13]	'brahma jajñānam' iti sūktasya saptāvṛttiḥ /
7.2.8.[14]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.2.8.[15]	bhavāśarvādibhyo devatābhyo nirvāpaṃ kṛtvā bṛhadbhāṇḍake śrapaṇam /
7.2.8.[16]	ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bharvāśarvau mṛḍatam' iti sūktasya saptāvṛttiḥ /
7.2.8.[17]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.2.8.[18]	bhavam /

7.2.8.[21]	ugram /

7.2.8.[23]	mahādevam /
7.2.8.[24]	īśānaṃ yajate /
7.2.8.[25]	ete sapta parvatadevatāḥ /
7.2.8.[26]	vyāghracauravṛścikahastyāraṇyakamahiṣāraṇyakagoityādibhaye svastyayanam //
7.2.8.[27]	goṣṭhakarmocyate
7.2.9.[1]	gośāntiḥ /
7.2.9.[2]	pākayajñatantraṃ kṛtvendradevatāyai 'brahma jajñānam' 'anāptā ye' iti sūktena caruṃ juhoti /
7.2.9.[3]	tata uttaratantram /
7.2.9.[4]	tantraṃ kṛtvā bhavāśarvādibhyo nirvāpaṃ kṛtvaikasmin bhāṇḍe śrapaṇaṃ kṛtvā tato brahmajajñānena juhoti /
7.2.9.[5]	sūktasya saptāvṛttiḥ /
7.2.9.[6]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.2.9.[7]	parvatadevatāyai pākayajñavidhānamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bhavāśarvau mṛḍatam' iti sūktena caruṃ juhoti /
7.2.9.[8]	tata uttaratantram /
7.2.9.[9]	tantraṃ kṛtvā bhavaśarvapaśupatyugrarudramahādeveśānāntaṃ nirvāpaṃ kṛtvaikasmin bhāṇḍake śrapaṇaṃ kṛtvā 'bhavāśarvau' iti sūktena juhoti /
7.2.9.[10]	pratidevataṃ sūktāvṛttiḥ /
7.2.9.[11]	tata uttaratantram /
7.2.9.[12]	rudradevasya carorhavirucchiṣṭaṃ yajamāno'śnāti /
7.2.9.[13]	yaddhi karmaṇi tatra sarvatra //
7.2.10.[1]	agnau darbhānādhāya yajamāno dhūmaṃ niyacchati /
7.2.10.[2]	'bhūtyai vaḥ puṣṭyai vaḥ' iti mantreṇa /
7.2.10.[3]	dvitīyacarorhavirucchiṣṭabhakṣaṇaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca /
7.2.10.[4]	iti goṣṭhakarmāṇi samāptāni /
7.2.10.[5]	iti gośāntiḥ /
7.2.10.[6]	indrayāgo bhavādiyāgaścaikaṃ karma dvitantram //
7.2.10.[7]	prathamaprasave gavāṃ śāntir ucyate
7.2.11.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' sahasradhāreṇa ghṛtamabhimantrya vatsavātsikāmukhamanakti /
7.2.11.[2]	evaṃ 'bhavāśarvau mṛḍatam' ityarthasūktena ghṛtamabhimantrya vatsasya vatsikāyā vā mukhaṃ mrakṣati /
7.2.11.[3]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.2.11.[4]	goṣṭhe prathamaprasava etatkarma //
7.2.12.[1]	'brahma jajñānam' iti sūktena tisro naladaśākhāḥ piṣṭvābhimantrya vatsikāṃ pāyayati /
7.2.12.[2]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.2.12.[3]	'bhāvāśarvau' ityarthasūktena tisro naladaśākhā udakena piṣṭvābhimantrya vatsikāṃ pāyayati /
7.2.12.[4]	svastyayanakāmaḥ //
7.2.13.[1]	gavāṃ prathamaprasave 'brahma jajñānam' iti mahatkāṇḍikena sūktena śākhāmudakamabhimantrya gobhyo bahirudakadhārāṃ ninayati /
7.2.13.[2]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.2.13.[3]	nalado māsikā nalo vā /
7.2.13.[4]	'bhavāśarvau' ityarthasūktena śākhāmudakamabhimantrya tata udakadhārāṃ gorbahirninayati /
7.2.13.[5]	śākhayā sahāvyavacchinnā dhārā /
7.2.13.[6]	samāptā gobhyaḥ prathamaprasave śāntiḥ //
7.2.13.[7]	atha pattanagrāmasya gṛhasya śāntirucyate
7.2.14.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'aśmavarma me' iti ṣaḍarcena sūktena saptamyṛcā sarvāsāṃ dvitīyā kartavyā /
7.2.14.[2]	'ye diśāmantardeśebhyaḥ' iti ṣaṭsu ṛkṣu dvitīyā /
7.2.14.[3]	ṣaṭ sampātāḥ /
7.2.14.[4]	ṣaḍaśmanaḥ sampātavato'bhimantrya tato gṛhakoṇeṣu nikhanati caturaḥ /
7.2.14.[5]	ekaṃ gṛhamadhya ekaṃ gṛhopari nidadhāti /
7.2.14.[6]	uttaratantram /
7.2.14.[7]	gṛhagrāmanagarapattanānāṃ sarvatra svastyayanaṃ samāptam //
7.2.14.[8]	athānnasvastyayanamucyate

7.2.15-16.[3]	atha mūṣakapataṅgaśalabhahariṇaroruśalyādīni sasyavināśakāni teṣāṃ śāntirucyate
7.2.17.[1]	'hataṃ tardam' iti sūktena sīsaṃ lohamudgharṣan sūktaṃ japitvābhiprakrāmati /
7.2.17.[2]	mūṣakādisthāne //

7.2.20.[1]	aśvinadevatāyai pākayajñamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'hataṃ tardam' iti sūktena sārūpavatsaṃ caruṃ juhoti /
7.2.20.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
7.2.20.[3]	'aśvibhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi /

7.3.0.[1]	atha deśāntaragamanasya svastyayanamucyate
7.3.1-2.[1]	'ye panthāno bahavo devayānāḥ' iti tṛcena sūktenājyaṃ juhoti /
7.3.1-2.[2]	ājyatantre /
7.3.1-2.[3]	'ye panthānaḥ' iti samidha ādadhāti /
7.3.1-2.[4]	puroḍāśādi yojyaṃ sarvatra /
7.3.1-2.[5]	'ye panthānaḥ' iti sūktena tṛcena manthamabhimantrya pathikāya prayacchati svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.3.1-2.[6]	'ye panthānaḥ' iti tṛcena bhaktamabhimantrya prayacchati bhojanārtham /
7.3.1-2.[7]	samāptā grāmadūrāgamanasya śāntiḥ /
7.3.1-2.[8]	anena karmaṇā kalahādi doṣo na bhavati //
7.3.1-2.[9]	puruṣabandhane mocanaśāntirucyate
7.3.3.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yasyāste' iti sūktena caturṛcena yena baddhaḥ tatsadṛśaṃ sampātavantaṃ kṛtvā sūktasadṛśaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca sampātavantaṃ karoti /
7.3.3.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
7.3.3.[3]	ājyatantraṃ kṛtvā 'yatte devī nirṛtiḥ' iti tṛcena sūktena bandhasadṛśaṃ nigaḍayugaladvayaṃ ca sampātavantaṃ karoti /
7.3.3.[4]	nābhimantraṇam /
7.3.3.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
7.3.3.[6]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'viṣāṇā pāśān' iti caturṛcena nigaḍayugaladvayaṃ sampātyaikaṃ muktaṃ nigaḍaṃ carmamayaṃ vā lohamayaṃ vā yena baddhastanmayaṃ kṛtvā /
7.3.3.[7]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
7.3.3.[8]	samāptaṃ bandhamocanam //
7.3.3.[9]	vācābandhasya mocanamucyate
7.3.4.[1]	tantraṃ kṛtvā 'yasyāste' iti sūktena bhūmilekhāṃ sampātya /
7.3.4.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
7.3.4.[3]	samāptaṃ vācābandhanam /
7.3.4.[4]	svastyayanakāmaḥ /
7.3.4.[5]	baddho anena karmaṇā kṛtena mucyate bandhanāt //
7.3.4.[6]	agnidāgharakṣārthamucyate
7.3.5.[1]	'āyane te parāyaṇe' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya garte prakṣipati madhye dāghe /
7.3.5.[2]	adāghe ca kṛtvā udakapūraṇaṃ karoti //
7.3.6.[1]	'āyane te' iti sūktena śālāmadhye dvayorudakamabhimantrya garte prakṣipati /
7.3.6.[2]	agnirakṣā bhavati //
7.3.7.[1]	'āyane te' iti sūktena avakāmabhimantrya śālāmupari paritanoti dāgharakṣārthī /
7.3.7.[2]	agnyupasarge etat karma //
7.3.8.[1]	'āyane te' iti sūktena divyamabhimantrya śapyamānāya prayacchati /
7.3.8.[2]	divye śudhyati /
7.3.8.[3]	taptamāṣake divye //

7.3.11.[2]	uttaratantram /

7.3.16-17.[70]	ājyatantre vā /

7.3.18-19.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'viśve devā' iti sūktena sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā tatsthālīpāke ghṛtapiṇḍatrayaṃ pratinīya sampātyābhimantrya ghṛtena saha sthālīpākamaśnāti /
7.3.18-19.[2]	tririti /

7.3.20-21.[1]	'asmin vasu' iti sūktena hiraṇyamaṇiṃ yugmakṛṣṇalaṃ sthālīpāke sthāpayitvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /

7.3.20-21.[6]	sthālīpākaṃ sampātyābhimantryāśnāti /

7.3.20-21.[18]	'manase cetase dhiyaḥ' iti sūktena mahāvrīhīṇāṃ sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā śāntyudakena prokṣya tamabhimantrya prāśnāti /
7.3.20-21.[19]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /

7.4.1-6.[1]	'āyurdā' iti sūktena uktasambhārān sambharati /

7.5.1.[1]	atha nāpitāya praiṣaṃ dadāti /
7.5.1.[2]	'akṣaṇvan vapa keśaśmaśru roma parivapa nakhāni ca kuru' iti //
7.5.2-3.[1]	ardhamuṇḍite 'punaḥ prāṇaḥ', 'punarmaitvindriyam' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ trirnimṛjya kṣuraṃ 'somadevaśarmaṇi tvayi mahimānaṃ sādayāmi' iti kṣuraṃ mārjayitvā nāpitāya prayacchati /
7.5.2-3.[2]	punarvapanārtham //
7.5.4-5.[1]	tato 'hiraṇyavarṇāḥ' iti sūktena śāntikalaśamabhimantrya tena kumāramāplāvayati /
7.5.4-5.[2]	'yaste gandhaḥ' iti tisṛbhiḥ ṛgbhiḥ puṣpaṃ kuṅkumaṃ candanādyabhimantrya kumāramalaṅkaroti hiraṇyālaṅkārān //
7.5.6.[1]	'svāktaṃ me' ityṛcā añjana abhimantryākṣiṇī aṅkte //

7.5.8.[1]	'ehyaśmānamā tiṣṭha' ityṛcā dakṣiṇena pādenāśmamaṇḍalamāsthāpya vedyupari pradakṣiṇam agnim anupariṇīya //
7.5.9.[1]	'yasya te vāsaḥ' ityṛcoparitanaṃ vastraṃ gṛhṇāti kartā //
7.5.10.[1]	'ayaṃ vaste garbhaṃ pṛthivyāḥ' iti pañcabhirṛgbhiḥ paridhānavastreṇopaparyācchādayati māṇavakam //
7.5.11-12.[1]	'yathā dyauśca' 'manase cetase dhiyaḥ' ityādi prathamato vyākhyānaṃ kṛtvā tato godānaṃ prārabdham /

7.5.11-12.[5]	prakṛtamucyate //
7.5.13.[1]	'tubhyameva jariman' iti sūktena putraṃ mātāpitarau triḥ samprayacchete /
7.5.13.[2]	pitā mantraṃ japitvā mātuḥ samarpayati /

7.5.13.[5]	pitur mantraḥ //

7.5.14.[2]	mātāpitarau //

7.5.15-18.[2]	'pārthivasya' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[3]	'mā pra gāma' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[4]	etābhirṛgbhiḥ vrīhiyavaśamīmabhimantrya kumārasya mūrdhni dadāti /
7.5.15-18.[5]	'śivau te stām' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[6]	'pārthivasya' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[7]	'mā pra gāma' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[8]	etābhiḥ ṛgbhiḥ vrīhiyavaśamīmabhimantrya mūrdhni dadāti /
7.5.15-18.[9]	'ahne ca tvā' ityekā /
7.5.15-18.[10]	'pārthivasya' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[11]	'mā pra gāma' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[12]	'ahorātrābhyāṃ paridadāmi' /
7.5.15-18.[13]	vrīhyādi mūrdhni dadāti /
7.5.15-18.[14]	'śarade tvā' ityekā /
7.5.15-18.[15]	'pārthivasya' dve /
7.5.15-18.[16]	'mā pra gāma' iti dve /
7.5.15-18.[17]	'ṛtubhyaṣṭvā paridadāmi' /
7.5.15-18.[18]	vrīhyādi mūrdhni dadāti /
7.5.15-18.[19]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
7.5.15-18.[20]	godānaṃ samāptam //
7.5.15-18.[21]	atha cūḍākaraṇamucyate
7.5.19-22.[1]	dvisaṃvatsare vā godānavat cūḍākaraṇaṃ kāryaṃ pūrvatantraṃ kṛtvā /
7.5.19-22.[2]	cūḍākaraṇaṃ ca godānena vyākhyātaṃ paridhāpanāśmamaṇḍalavarjam /
7.5.19-22.[3]	śeṣaṃ godānavat kāryam /
7.5.19-22.[4]	śāntyudake 'tubhyameva' iti sūktamanuyojayet /
7.5.19-22.[5]	śeṣaṃ samānam /
7.5.19-22.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
7.5.19-22.[7]	iti cūḍākaraṇam /
7.5.19-22.[8]	tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ 'cūḍā kāryā yathākulam' /
7.5.19-22.[9]	punarupanayane godānavidhānena vapanaṃ kartavyam /
7.5.19-22.[10]	savān dāsyato godānavat vapanam /
7.5.19-22.[11]	agnihotraṃ kariṣyamāṇasya godānavidhānena vapanam /
7.5.19-22.[12]	yathā brahmacaryaparimokṣe godānena vapanam /
7.5.19-22.[13]	somayāge godānavidhānena vapanam /
7.5.19-22.[14]	dīkṣaṇīyāprāk evaṃ bhavati /
7.5.19-22.[15]	anyatra yatra vapanaṃ paṭhyate tatra sarvatra godānavidhānena vapanaṃ kuryāt iti dārilamatam /
7.5.19-22.[16]	punarupanayanādiṣveteṣāṃ tadeva śāntyudakamuṣṇodakaṃ kṛtvodapātre viśeṣaḥ /
7.5.19-22.[17]	śeṣaṃ godānavat bhavati //
7.5.19-22.[18]	pañcamī kaṇḍikā //
7.6.0.[1]	athopanayanamucyate
7.6.1.[1]	garbhapañcame garbhāṣṭame varṣe kuryāditi paiṭhīnasiḥ /
7.6.1.[2]	vasante brāhmaṇamupanayīteti ca mīmāṃsāyām /
7.6.1.[3]	ājyatantre godānikamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ śāntyudake 'ā yātu mitraḥ' iti sūktamanuyojayet /
7.6.1.[4]	tato'bhyātānāni /
7.6.1.[5]	tataḥ 'ā yātu mitraḥ' iti /
7.6.1.[6]	'āyurdā' iti kecit /
7.6.1.[7]	sūktena mūrdhni sampātānānayati /
7.6.1.[8]	dakṣiṇe pāṇau /
7.6.1.[9]	aśmamaṇḍalavarjam /
7.6.1.[10]	śāntyudakamuṣṇodakaṃ kṛtvā tasminnudapātre sampātānānayati /
7.6.1.[11]	uttarasampātān sthālarūpa ānayati //
7.6.2.[1]	'āyamagan savitā kṣureṇa' iti pādenodapātramanumantrayate //
7.6.3.[1]	'yatkṣureṇa' ityṛcā kṣuraṃ mārjayati triḥ /
7.6.3.[2]	'uṣṇena vāya' iti pādenodapātramanumantrayate /
7.6.3.[3]	'ādityā rudrā vasavaḥ' iti pādena 'aditiḥ śmaśru' ityṛcā undanaṃ karoti //
7.6.4.[1]	'somasya rājño vapata pracetasaḥ' iti pādena 'yenāvapad' ityṛcā vapanaṃ karoti /
7.6.4.[2]	sakṛt dakṣiṇe piñjūlīvarjam /
7.6.4.[3]	evamuttare śiraḥpārśve vapanaṃ sakṛt piñjūlīvarjaṃ ca //
7.6.5-6.[1]	laukikaṃ ca samānaṃ godānena vyākhyātamā paridhānāt /
7.6.5-6.[2]	puṇyāhavācanam /
7.6.5-6.[3]	vṛddhāstrīgītaṃ ca kārayet //
7.6.7.[1]	tataḥ pradakṣiṇamagnimanupariṇīya purastādagneḥ pratyaṅmukhamavasthāpya svayaṃ prāṅmukhaḥ //
7.6.8-9.[1]	brahmacārī bravīti /
7.6.8-9.[2]	'āha brūhi brahmacaryamāgāmupa mā nayasva' iti //
7.6.10.[1]	tata ācāryo bravīti 'ko nāmāsi kiṅgotraḥ' iti /
7.6.10.[2]	punarbrahmacārī bravīti 'somadevadattaśarmanāmāham /
7.6.10.[3]	amukasagotro'ham /
7.6.10.[4]	yathāsaṅkhyapravaro'ham' //
7.6.11.[1]	punaḥ brahmacārī vadati - 'ārṣeyaṃ mā kṛtvā bandhumantamupanaya' //
7.6.12.[1]	tataḥ punarācārya āha - 'ārṣeyaṃ tvā kṛtvā bandhumantamupanayāmi' iti //
7.6.13.[1]	'OM bhūrbhuvaḥsvarjanadom' iti mantreṇodakāñjalimādityāya dadāti brahmacārī //
7.6.14.[1]	'uttaro'sāni' iti mantreṇa dakṣiṇapāṇiṃ gṛhṇātyācāryaḥ //
7.6.15.[1]	'eṣa ma ādityaputraḥ' iti mantreṇādityaṃ nirīkṣate //
7.6.16-17.[1]	'apakrāman' ityṛcā paścādagneḥ pūrvābhimukhaṃ brahmacāriṇamupaveśya tato dakṣiṇena pāṇinā nābhideśaṃ saṃspṛśya tataḥ 'asmin vasu vasavo dhārayantu' iti gaṇaṃ japatyācāryaḥ //
7.6.18.[1]	athavā 'ā yātu mitra' iti sūktaṃ japati //
7.6.19.[1]	brahmacāriṇaṃ vastreṇa pracchādya tatastrīn prāṇāyāmān kṛtvā /
7.6.19.[2]	tata avacchādya brahmacāriṇamudapātre vatsikāmukhamavekṣayet //
7.6.20.[1]	'samindra naḥ' 'saṃ varcasā' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ gāmutsṛjati //
7.6.20.[2]	saptame ṣaṣṭhī kaṇḍikā //
7.7.1.[1]	'śraddhāyā duhitā' iti dvābhyāṃ mauñjīṃ mekhalāṃ tripravarāṃ catuḥpravarāṃ vābhimantrya brahmacāriṇaḥ kaṭipradeśe badhnāti //
7.7.2-4.[1]	tato 'mitrāvaruṇayostvā hastābhyām' iti mantreṇa 'śyeno'si' iti ca sūktena pālāśadaṇḍamabhimantrya brahmacāriṇe prayacchati /
7.7.2-4.[2]	'mitrāvaruṇayostvā' iti 'śyeno'si' iti ca paṭhitvā brahmacārī daṇḍaṃ gṛhṇāti /
7.7.2-4.[3]	'punarmaitvindriyam' ityṛcā yajñopavītamabhimantrya paridhatte manvādivihitam /
7.7.2-4.[4]	'ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ' iti sūktaṃ pratyṛcaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ vācayati /
7.7.2-4.[5]	atha vratagrahaṇaṃ karoti /
7.7.2-4.[6]	'brahmacārivrataṃ dvādaśavārṣikaṃ ṣaḍvārṣikaṃ vā trivārṣikaṃ vā yathāśāstravihitaṃ yathāsmaryamāṇadharmakam' ityādyuktamāṅgirasakalpe vrataśrāvaṇam /
7.7.2-4.[7]	agnaye gurave ca brahmacārī vrataṃ nivedayet //
7.7.5-7.[1]	'agne vratapate' iti pratyṛcaṃ brahmacārī aṣṭau samidha ādadhāti /
7.7.5-7.[2]	pāṭhayitvā aṣṭau mantrān //
7.7.8-11.[1]	tataḥ sāvitrīṃ vācayati pādaṃ pādaṃ prathamam /

7.7.8-11.[3]	tataḥ sakalām //
7.7.12.[1]	atha ācārya ācāraṃ kathayati /

7.7.12.[4]	'nityaṃ bhojane apo'śāna /

7.9.7.[1]	'śuddhā na āpaḥ' ityṛcā śleṣmaṃ tyaktvātmānamanumantrayate /
7.9.7.[2]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.7.[3]	'jīvā stha' iti sūktena ācamyānumantrayate /
7.9.7.[4]	'vi devā' iti gaṇaḥ punarvikalpena /
7.9.7.[5]	āyuṣkāmaḥ //
7.9.8.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ehi jīvam' iti sūktenāñjanamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
7.9.8.[2]	uttaratantram /
7.9.8.[3]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.8.[4]	'ehi jīvam' iti sūktenāñjanatucchakamabhimantrya pāyayati /
7.9.8.[5]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.8.[6]	yuddhe rakṣārtham /
7.9.8.[7]	nainaṃ prāpnoti śapatho na kṛtyā nābhiśocanam //
7.9.9.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'vātājjāta' iti sūktena śaṅkhamaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
7.9.9.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
7.9.9.[3]	āyuṣkāmaḥ rakṣārthī /
7.9.9.[4]	upanayane nityaṃ bandhanam //
7.9.10.[1]	abhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'nava prāṇān' iti sūktena suvarṇarajatalohatrīṇi śakalānyekatra kṛtvā navaśālākaṃ maṇiṃ trivṛtaṃ kṛtvā sampātyābhimantrya badhnāti /
7.9.10.[2]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram //
7.9.11.[1]	trayodaśyādayastisro dadhimadhumadhyāduddhṛtya trivṛtamaṇiṃ 'ghṛtādulluptam' ityṛcā, 'ā tvā cṛtatu' ityṛcā, 'ṛtubhiṣṭvā' ityṛcā badhnāti /
7.9.11.[2]	anyatra sarvatra puṇyāhānte bandhanam /
7.9.11.[3]	āyuṣkāmo rakṣākāmaśca /
7.9.11.[4]	'muñcāmi tvā' iti sūktenābhimantrayate āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[5]	rājayakṣmaṇi jvare cānyasarvavyādhau ca /
7.9.11.[6]	'uta devāḥ' iti sūktenābhimṛśati dvābhyāṃ hastābhyām /
7.9.11.[7]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[8]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyaṃ rakṣākāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[9]	iti nirodhe ca /
7.9.11.[10]	'āvataste' iti śarīramabhimantrayate /
7.9.11.[11]	āyuṣkāma ārogyakāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[12]	sarvavyādhibhaiṣajyam /
7.9.11.[13]	hṛdroge ca /
7.9.11.[14]	aṅgabhaṅge ca jvare ca /
7.9.11.[15]	rakṣākāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[16]	'upa priyam' ityṛcā bālaśarīramabhimantrayate /
7.9.11.[17]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[18]	yuvānaṃ bālaṃ ca /
7.9.11.[19]	'antakāya' 'ā rabhasva' iti sūktābhyāṃ śarīramabhimantrayate /
7.9.11.[20]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[21]	mṛtyūbhaye ca /
7.9.11.[22]	'prāṇāya namaḥ' iti sūktena puruṣamabhimantrayate /
7.9.11.[23]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[24]	kṣubhitvā kāsitvā khāsitvā pītvā suptvā bhuktvā japati /
7.9.11.[25]	'viṣāsahim' ityabhimantrayate /
7.9.11.[26]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.11.[27]	sumatikāmaḥ sakāmajātirāsāratvakāmaḥ //
7.9.12.[1]	'nirdurarmaṇya' iti sūktena sarvauṣadhimabhimantrya puruṣaṃ pralimpati puruṣasyāraṇye /
7.9.12.[2]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.12.[3]	śrotraṃ vāk manaḥ cakṣurdantaḥ nāsikā anyacca sarvaṃ vikalendriyaṃ dṛḍhaṃ bhavati /
7.9.12.[4]	viṣakaṃ bhavati /
7.9.12.[5]	yo vikalendriyastasyedaṃ karma /
7.9.12.[6]	anulomaṃ pralimpati /
7.9.12.[7]	samāptamāyuṣyam /
7.9.12.[8]	punaragre bhaviṣyati //
7.9.13.[1]	ekādaśe'hani nāma dvādaśe'hani nāma śatarātrau vā puṇye nakṣatre vā yathākuladharmeṇa vā /
7.9.13.[2]	nāmakaraṇasyaite kālāḥ smṛtivihitāḥ //
7.9.14.[1]	ājyatantramabhyātānāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ā rabhasvemām' ityarthasūktena kumārasya dakṣiṇe hasta udakadhārāmavicchinnāṃ ninayati //
7.9.15-16.[1]	tata 'ā rabhasva' iti sūktena devadārumaṇiṃ sampātyābhimantrya puṇyāhānte badhnāti /
7.9.15-16.[2]	maṇiṃ ghṛṣya pāyayati badhnāti ca /
7.9.15-16.[3]	tataḥ pitā nāma karoti /
7.9.15-16.[4]	atha ācāryo vā dakṣiṇe karṇe śrāvayati kṛttikādaivataṃ someśvaradattaśarmā nāma athavā agnidaivataṃ somadevadattaśarmā nāma nakṣatrakalpoktaṃ nāma dvyakṣaraṃ caturakṣaramityādi //
7.9.17.[1]	'yatte vāsaḥ' ityṛcā'hatenottarasicā pracchādayati /
7.9.17.[2]	'śive te stām' ityādi paridānāni siṃhāvalokananyāyena godānamadhye uktāni /
7.9.17.[3]	abhyātānādyuttaratantram /
7.9.17.[4]	tataḥ śrāddham /
7.9.17.[5]	nāmakaraṇaṃ samāptam //
7.9.17.[6]	atha nirṇayanakarma ucyate
7.9.18.[1]	caturthe māsi niṣkramaṇam /
7.9.18.[2]	'śive te stām' iti dvābhyāṃ kumāraṃ puṇyāhānte niṣkrāmayati tataḥ pūrvoktāni paridānāni dadāti /
7.9.18.[3]	tataḥ śrāddham /
7.9.18.[4]	samāptaṃ nirṇayanakarma /
7.9.18.[5]	śiṣṭā avaśyaṃ kurvanti //
7.9.18.[6]	athānnaprāśanam
7.9.19.[1]	ṣaṣṭhe māsi prāśanaṃ kuryāditi paiṭhīnasiḥ /
7.9.19.[2]	sarvasyāṃ smṛtau pañcame kumāryā iti /
7.9.19.[3]	prathamaṃ 'bhūme mātaḥ' ityṛcā bhūmyāmupaveśya tataḥ 'udvayaṃ tamasaspari' ityādityaṃ darśayitvā tato'nnaprāśanaṃ kuryāt puṇyāhānte /
7.9.19.[4]	tataḥ 'śivau te stāṃ vrīhiyavau' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ vrīhiyavau piṣṭvābhimantrya kumāraṃ prāśayati /
7.9.19.[5]	ājyatantre annāni ca sarvāṇi /
7.9.19.[6]	tataḥ sruvaṃ pustakaṃ dadāti /
7.9.19.[7]	'śive te stām' iti dvābhyāṃ 'pārthivasya' iti dve 'mā pra gāma' iti dve etābhiḥ ṛgbhirvrīhyādi mūrdhni dadāti /
7.9.19.[8]	'dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ tvā paridadāmi' /
7.9.19.[9]	'śivau te stām' ityādi /
7.9.19.[10]	'vrīhiyavābhyāṃ tvā paridadāmi' //
7.9.20-21.[1]	'ahne ca tvā' iti 'ahorātrābhyāṃ paridadāmi' /
7.9.20-21.[2]	'śarade tvā' ityādi 'ṛtubhyastvā paridadāmi' /
7.9.20-21.[3]	godānavat paridānāni dadāti /
7.9.20-21.[4]	nāmakaraṇe niṣkramaṇe annaprāśane ca godānikāni paridānāni bhavati /
7.9.20-21.[5]	tata uttaratantram /
7.9.20-21.[6]	ityannaprāśanaṃ samāptam //
7.9.20-21.[7]	ūno vātirikto vā yaḥ svaśākhodito vidhiḥ /
7.9.20-21.[8]	tenaiva sarvaṃ sampūrṇaṃ syānna kuryāt pāratantrikam //
7.9.20-21.[9]	paścāt śrāddhaṃ sarveṣu saṃskāreṣu kuryāt iti dārilabhāṣyakārasyābhiprāyeṇa vyākhyāta iti /
7.9.20-21.[10]	śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā paścāt karmeti rudrabhadrau /
7.9.20-21.[11]	ete bhāṣyakārāḥ kauśikasya /
7.9.20-21.[12]	tathā ca manuḥ - 'akṛtvā mātaraḥ śrāddhaṃ na kuryāt karma vaidikam' /
7.9.20-21.[13]	vaidikeṣu karmasu nityanaimittikakāmyeṣu śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ karma kuryāt /
7.9.20-21.[14]	sarvatra śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā śāntikapauṣṭikābhicārakādbhutāni atharvavedavihitāni kartavyāni /
7.9.20-21.[15]	puṃsavanādisaṃskārāḥ svaśākhāvihitāḥ kartavyā na kuryāt pāratantrikāḥ /
7.9.20-21.[16]	punaḥ /
7.9.20-21.[17]	svaśākhāṃ tu parityajya paraśākhāmupāsate /
7.9.20-21.[18]	sa śūdravad bahiḥ kāryo havyakavyeṣu garhitaḥ //
7.9.20-21.[19]	punarāyuṣyakarma ucyate
7.9.22-23.[1]	'udasya ketanaḥ' ityanuvākenādityamupatiṣṭhate /
7.9.22-23.[2]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.22-23.[3]	'mūrdhāhaṃ', 'nābhiraham' iti sūktābhyāmādityamupatiṣṭhate /
7.9.22-23.[4]	trikālamāyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.22-23.[5]	'viṣāsahim' ityanuvākena etasmin kāle ādityamupatiṣṭhate āyuṣkāmaḥ //
7.9.24.[1]	aṃholiṅgānāmāpo bhojanahavīṃṣi kuryāt /
7.9.24.[2]	'āśānām' iti sūktenodakamabhimantrya pibati /
7.9.24.[3]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.24.[4]	'āśānām' iti sūktena bhojanamabhimantrayate /
7.9.24.[5]	āyuṣkāmo nityaṃ kuryāt /
7.9.24.[6]	'āśānām' iti sūktenājyaṃ juhoti ājyatantre /
7.9.24.[7]	'āśānām' iti sūktena samidha ādadhāti /
7.9.24.[8]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.24.[9]	puroḍāśādyapyevaṃ yojanīyam /
7.9.24.[10]	'agnermanve' iti saptabhiḥ sūktairudakamabhimantrya pibati /
7.9.24.[11]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.24.[12]	'agnermanve' iti saptabhi sūktaiḥ saktumabhimantrya bhuṅkte /
7.9.24.[13]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.24.[14]	'agnermanve' iti saptabhi sūktairhavirupadadhīta /
7.9.24.[15]	yathāsambhavaṃ tantram /
7.9.24.[16]	vikalpo vā /
7.9.24.[17]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.24.[18]	'yā oṣadhayaḥ' iti bhaktamupadhānāni yojanīyāni /
7.9.24.[19]	'vaiśvānaro na āgamat' ityṛcā udakaṃ bhaktamupadhānaṃ kuryāt /
7.9.24.[20]	'śumbhanī' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ tritayaṃ kuryāt /
7.9.24.[21]	'yadarvācīnam' ityṛcā udakamabhimantrya pibati /
7.9.24.[22]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.9.24.[23]	'yadarvācīnam' ityṛcā bhaktamabhimantrya bhakṣayati /
7.9.24.[24]	'yadarvācīnam' ityṛcā upadhānaṃ kuryāt /
7.9.24.[25]	sarvatra dakṣiṇādānam /
7.9.24.[26]	svayaṅkartṛke anyasmai dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti śubhaṃ vā bahavo'pi kurvanti /
7.9.24.[27]	eko'pi karoti /
7.9.24.[28]	paśvādīnāmāyuṣyaṃ karma bhavati /
7.9.24.[29]	puruṣastrīṇāmapi vṛddhabālataruṇānāṃ sarveṣāṃ mānuṣapaśumṛgapakṣiṇa aśvādīnāmāyuṣyaṃ karma bhavati /
7.9.24.[30]	sarvatra dakṣiṇā dhenuḥ /
7.9.24.[31]	tantre vā'tantre vā /
7.9.24.[32]	āyuṣkāmaḥ //
7.9.25.[1]	'agniṃ brūmaḥ' iti sūktasya 'yanmātalī rathakrītam' iti sarvāsāṃ dvitīyā /
7.9.25.[2]	vyatiṣaṅgeṇa yanmātalī kartavyā /
7.9.25.[3]	'agniṃ brūmaḥ' ityasya sūktasya pratyṛcaṃ mātalī kāryā /
7.9.25.[4]	ante ca /
7.9.25.[5]	abhyātānānte haviṣāmupadadhīta /
7.9.25.[6]	tata uttaratantram /
7.9.25.[7]	samāptāni āyuṣyāṇi /
7.9.25.[8]	na dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ kurvīta /
7.9.25.[9]	yadā svayaṃ karoti tadā'nyasmai dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt //
7.9.25.[10]	saptame'dhyāye navamī kaṇḍikā //
7.10.0.[1]	atha kāmyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
7.10.0.[2]	sambhāralakṣaṇe maṇḍapavidhānamuktam /
7.10.0.[3]	gṛhe vā kuryāt /
7.10.0.[4]	nityāni karmāṇi gṛhe kuryāt /
7.10.0.[5]	avabhṛthaṃ na vā kuryāt /
7.10.0.[6]	sarvatra kauśike karmaṇāṃ vikalpaḥ /
7.10.0.[7]	sarvatrāvabhṛthaṃ karmasamāptau /
7.10.0.[8]	pañcānāṃ kalpānāṃ kauśikoktaṃ tantraṃ kuryādityarthaḥ /
7.10.0.[9]	atha vidhānamucyate
7.10.1.[1]	vaiśvadevaṃ carum /
7.10.1.[2]	pākayajñatantramājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'viśve devā' iti caruṃ juhoti /
7.10.1.[3]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.10.1.[4]	āyuṣkāmaḥ /
7.10.1.[5]	'viśvebhyo devebhyo juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' /
7.10.1.[6]	'viśvebhyo devebhyastvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi' /
7.10.1.[7]	'viśvān devān gacchatu haviḥ svāhā' iti viśeṣaḥ /
7.10.1.[8]	śatavarṣaparimitamāyurbhavati /
7.10.1.[9]	nityaṃ kuryāt //
7.10.2.[1]	athavā 'viśve devā' iti sūktenopatiṣṭhate viśvān devān //
7.10.3.[1]	pākayajñatantramājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'idaṃ janāsa' itisūkte na dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ caruṃ juhoti /
7.10.3.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.10.3.[3]	'dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' /
7.10.3.[4]	'dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi' /
7.10.3.[5]	'dyāvāpṛthivī gacchatu haviḥ svāhā' iti /
7.10.3.[6]	puṣṭikāmaḥ dravyavṛddhikāmaḥ //
7.10.4.[1]	manobhilaṣitakāmaḥ ityarthaḥ /
7.10.4.[2]	nityaṃ kuryāt /
7.10.4.[3]	'idaṃ janāsa' iti sūktena upatiṣṭhate dyāvāpṛthivyau /
7.10.4.[4]	sakṛnmantraḥ /
7.10.4.[5]	puṣṭikāmaḥ /
7.10.4.[6]	sampatkāmaḥ /
7.10.4.[7]	sampacchabda udayaśabda ucyate /
7.10.4.[8]	putrakāmaḥ dhanakāmaḥ paśukāmaḥ dhānyakāmaḥ hiraṇyakāmaḥ ratnakāmaḥ hastikāmaḥ aśvakāmaḥ puṣṭikāmaḥ phalakāmaḥ āyuṣyakāmaḥ vaśīkaraṇakāmaḥ cakṣurādīnīndriyāṇi vikale sati dṛṣṭikāmaḥ patnīkāmaḥ gṛhakāmaḥ saubhāgyakāmaḥ parasya daurbhāgyakāmaḥ /
7.10.4.[9]	anyo'pyanuktakāmaḥ sampatkāmamadhye jñātavyaḥ /
7.10.4.[10]	sarvakāma ityarthaḥ /
7.10.4.[11]	kāmāvṛttau karmāvṛttiḥ /
7.10.4.[12]	karmāvṛttau sūktāvṛttiḥ //
7.10.5.[1]	pākatantre 'indra juṣasva' iti sūktena aindraṃ caruṃ juhoti /
7.10.5.[2]	pāvaṇādyuttaratantram /
7.10.5.[3]	'devasya tvā' ityādi 'indrāya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' /
7.10.5.[4]	'indrāya tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi' /
7.10.5.[5]	'saṃ barhiḥ' ityādi 'indraṃ gacchatu haviḥ svāhā' iti barhipraharaṇe /
7.10.5.[6]	cāturaṅgahastiaśvapuruṣādibalakāmo rājā nityaṃ kuryāt /
7.10.5.[7]	'indra juṣasva' iti sūktena indramupatiṣṭhate /
7.10.5.[8]	nityaṃ rājā balakāmaḥ //
7.10.6.[1]	tantramājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'indramaham' iti sūktena aindraṃ caruṃ juhoti /
7.10.6.[2]	tata uttaratantram /
7.10.6.[3]	vaṇijādiartharatnadhānyaputralābho'sti sarvaṃ vaṇijyotiparimuccairbhavati tataḥ kuryāt /
7.10.6.[4]	'indramahaṃ vaṇijam' iti sūktenendramupatiṣṭhate /
7.10.6.[5]	vāṇijyakāmaḥ /
7.10.6.[6]	aśvādipaṇyakāmaḥ //
7.10.7.[1]	'udenamuttaraṃ naya', 'yo'smān brahmaṇaspate' iti sūktābhyāṃ pākatantre aindraṃ caruṃ juhoti /
7.10.7.[2]	uttaratantram /
7.10.7.[3]	grāmakāmaḥ /
7.10.7.[4]	grāmapattanamaṇḍalapurakāmaḥ /
7.10.7.[5]	grāmaśabda upalakṣaṇārthaḥ /
7.10.7.[6]	'udenamuttaraṃ naya' 'yo'smān' iti sūktābhyāmupatiṣṭhate /
7.10.7.[7]	grāmakāmaḥ /
7.10.7.[8]	pākatantre 'indraḥ sutrāmā' ityṛcā carum aindraṃ juhoti /
7.10.7.[9]	grāmakāmaḥ /
7.10.7.[10]	'indraḥ sutrāmā' ityṛcā aindramupatiṣṭhate /
7.10.7.[11]	grāmakāmaḥ //
7.10.8.[1]	'udenamuttaraṃ naya' iti sūktābhyām udumbarasamidha ādadhāti /
7.10.8.[2]	tantravikalpaḥ /
7.10.8.[3]	grāmakāmaḥ /
7.10.8.[4]	'udenamuttaraṃ naya' iti sūktābhyāṃ pālāśasamidha ādadhāti /
7.10.8.[5]	grāmakāmaḥ /
7.10.8.[6]	'udenamuttaraṃ naya' 'yo asmān brahmaṇaspate' iti sūktābhyāṃ karkandhūsamidha ādadhāti /
7.10.8.[7]	'udenamuttaraṃ naya' 'yo asmān brahmaṇaspate' iti sūktābhyāṃ sabhānāmupastaraṇāni juhoti /
7.10.8.[8]	grāmakāmaḥ /
7.10.8.[9]	evaṃ 'indraḥ sutrāmā' iti yojyam /
7.10.8.[10]	grāmakāmaḥ /
7.10.8.[11]	nāsti nirṛtikarma /
7.10.8.[12]	adhikāre tadbhavati /
7.10.8.[13]	iha na bhavati //
7.10.9.[1]	indradaivataṃ carumājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yaśasaṃ mendraḥ' iti sūktena indrāya caruṃ juhoti /
7.10.9.[2]	athavā 'yaśasaṃ mendraḥ' iti tṛcena sūktenendramupatiṣṭhate /
7.10.9.[3]	yaśaskāmaḥ /
7.10.9.[4]	pratiprakāśatādityavat yaśasvī bhavatītyarthaḥ //

8.1.29.[2]	avyasaśca , barhirlavanam, vedyuttaravedyagnipratiṣṭhāpanam, anvādhānam, vratagrahaṇam, pavitrakaraṇam, pavitreṇedhmaprokṣaṇam, idhmopasamādhānam, barhiḥprokṣaṇam, brahmāsanam, brahmavaraṇam, brahmasthāpanam, staraṇam, stīrṇaprokṣaṇam, ātmāsanam, udapātrasaṃskāraḥ /

8.2.5.[3]	atha nirvāpakaraṇam
8.2.6.[1]	dātā muṣṭiprasṛtāñjalidvayaparimite triguṇān vrīhīṃścarmaṇi kṛtvā darbhapavitrābhyāṃ tūṣṇīṃ carmahaviḥ samprokṣati /
8.2.6.[2]	tataḥ carmaṇi trīṇi vibhāgāni karoti //
8.2.7.[1]	tato devapitṛmanuṣyatrayaṃ patnī anajānatyai prayattaiḥ prayacchati /
8.2.7.[2]	kartā praiṣaṃ dadāti //
8.2.8-11.[1]	vrīhīn vibhāgeṣu kartā 'tredhā bhāgo nihitaḥ' iti tribhiḥ pādairvibhāgān devapitṛmanuṣyasambandhānanumantrayate /
8.2.8-11.[2]	'yo devānām' iti pādena patnīmanumantrayate /
8.2.8-11.[3]	yaḥ pitṛbhāgastenāvabhṛthānte vṛddhiśrāddhaṃ karoti /
8.2.8-11.[4]	yo manuṣyāṇāṃ bhāgastaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayati /
8.2.8-11.[5]	dvābhyāṃ tantrāgnau śrapaṇam /
8.2.8-11.[6]	'yo devānām' ityetena vakṣyamāṇaṃ karma kuryāt //
8.2.12-14.[1]	evaṃ caturṇāmekaikaṃ prati nirvāpamanuyojayet /
8.2.12-14.[2]	niruptānanyasyāṃ kumbhyāṃ kṛtvā tasyāṃ śrapaṇakumbhyāvaśeṣāccaturthaṃ nirvapati /
8.2.12-14.[3]	evaṃ pratimantraṃ catvāro nirvāpā bhavanti /
8.2.12-14.[4]	athavā śrapaṇakumbhyāvaśeṣāccaturthaṃ nirvapati /
8.2.12-14.[5]	anaḍuhi kṛtvā niruptaṃ haviḥ savasūktenābhimṛśati kartā //
8.2.15.[1]	'trīn varān vṛṇīṣva' iti dātṛpraiṣaṃ dattvā evaṃ patnyai dadāti /
8.2.15.[2]	tau vṛṇantau 'trayo varāḥ' ityardharcena pratipratyanumantrayate //
8.2.16.[1]	dātā savakarmaṇāṃ samṛddhīḥ prathamaṃ vṛṇīte //
8.2.17.[1]	yāvaparau varau manyeta tau vṛṇīte /
8.2.17.[2]	evaṃ tāveva patnī //
8.2.18.[1]	kartā 'arātīyoḥ' iti takṣati /
8.2.18.[2]	'yadyat kṛṣṇaḥ' ityṛcolūkhalamusale prakṣālayati /
8.2.18.[3]	'yattvā śikvaḥ' ityṛcā śūrpamadhaḥ gomayena lepayati /
8.2.18.[4]	tāni 'etau grāvāṇau' iti pādena dātā carmaṇi nidadhāti //
8.2.19.[1]	'gṛhāṇa grāvāṇau' ityardharcenolūkhalamusalaṃ grāhayati //
8.2.20-21.[1]	'sākaṃ sajātaiḥ' ityardharcena patnī vrīhīnulūkhala āvapati /
8.2.20-21.[2]	'ūrdhvo nākasya' ityardharcena musalamucchrayantīmanumantrayate //
8.2.22.[1]	'nirbhindhyaṃśūn' iti pādadvayenāvaghnatīmanumantrayate //
8.2.23.[1]	'iyaṃ te dhītiḥ' ityardharcena śūrpaṃ gṛhṇāti //
8.2.24.[1]	'ūrdhvaṃ prajām' iti pādena ulūkhalādudūhantīm //
8.2.25.[1]	'parā punīhi' iti pādena, niṣpunantīm //
8.2.26.[1]	'asyai rayim' iti pādena avakṣiṇatīm //
8.2.27-29.[1]	'upaśvase' iti pādena udvapatīm /
8.2.27-29.[2]	'upaśvase' ityardharcenāpavivaktīmanumantrayate /
8.2.27-29.[3]	'śriyā samānān' ityardharcaṃ dātāraṃ vācayati //
8.2.30.[1]	'ayaṃ yajñaḥ' ityardharcena kumbhīṃ mṛdālimpatīmanumantrayate //
8.2.31.[1]	'agne caruḥ' ityṛcā adhiśrayantam //
8.2.32.[1]	'sahasrapṛṣṭhaḥ' ityṛcā agnau kāṣṭhāni paryādadhantaṃ vācayati //
8.2.33.[1]	'ṛṣipraśiṣṭā' iti pādena udakumbhāt patnīmudakamapakarṣatīmanumantrayate //
8.2.34-35.[1]	'śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ' iti tribhiḥ pādaiḥ kumbhyāṃ pavitre antardhāyodakamāsiñcantaṃ vācyam /
8.2.34-35.[2]	'paktaudanasya' iti pādena dātāramanumantrayate /
8.2.34-35.[3]	mitamudakamāsecayedvibhāgam /
8.2.34-35.[4]	yāvantastaṇḍulāḥ syurnāvasiñcenna pratiṣiñcet /
8.2.34-35.[5]	yadyavasiñcet 'mayi varco atho yaśaḥ' iti brahmā yajamānaṃ vācayet /
8.2.34-35.[6]	atha pratiṣiñcet 'ā pyāyasva' 'saṃ te payāṃsi' iti dvābhyāṃ pratiṣiñcet //
8.2.36.[1]	'brahmaṇā śuddhāḥ' ityṛcā āpastāsu niktvā dātā taṇḍulān kumbhyāṃ nivapati //
8.2.37.[1]	'uruḥ prathasva' ityardharcena śrapayantaṃ yajamānamanumantrayate /
8.2.37.[2]	'pitāmahāḥ pitaraḥ' ityardharcena dātāraṃ vācayati //
8.2.38.[1]	darbhāhārāya dātraṃ prayacchati //
8.2.39-40.[1]	upari parvaṇāṃ lūtvā tūṣṇīmāhṛtyottarato'gnerupasādayati /
8.2.39-40.[2]	tadādāvāstṛtasyopari paścādagneḥ tūṣṇīṃ stṛṇāti kartā //
8.2.41.[1]	'udehi vedim' ityṛcā patnyā kumbhīmudvāsyamānāmanumantrayate /
8.2.41.[2]	'prajayā vardhayainām' iti mantreṇa patnīmanumantrayate /
8.2.41.[3]	'nudasva rakṣaḥ' iti kumbhīm /
8.2.41.[4]	'prataraṃ dhehyenām' iti patnīm /
8.2.41.[5]	'śriyā samānān' ityardharcena dātāraṃ vācayati //
8.2.42-43.[1]	'ṛtena taṣṭhā' ityardharcena nave barhiṣi pātrīṃ nidadhatīmanumantrayate //
8.2.44.[1]	'aṃsadhrīṃ śuddhām' ityardharcena upadadhāti kumbhīm //
8.2.45-46.[1]	dātāra tūṣṇīṃ pātrīmājyenopastṛṇāti //
8.3.1.[1]	kartā 'aditerhastām' ityṛcā patnyā darvīṃ grāhayati //
8.3.2-4.[1]	dātā tūṣṇīṃ sruveṇa sakṛdantarād udapātrādudakamādāya pātryāmānayati /
8.3.2-4.[2]	punaḥ darvyām /
8.3.2-4.[3]	odanakumbhyāṃ ca //
8.3.5-6.[1]	suhṛdāyavanena amuṣyodanasya uttamamādāya dakṣiṇato'gnerudaṅmukha āsīno dhārayati /
8.3.5-6.[2]	tasmin darvīkṛte śeṣamantarodapātra eva pātryāṃ kṛtsnamodanamuddharati //
8.3.7-15.[1]	'babhreradhvaryo mukham' ityardharcena dātrā preṣitaḥ /
8.3.7-15.[2]	'aditerhastām' ityṛcānumantrayate /
8.3.7-15.[3]	'babhreradhvaryo mukham' ityardharcena dātrā preṣitaḥ odanasyopari gartaṃ karoti //
8.3.16-17.[1]	'ghṛtena gātrā' iti pādena preṣitaḥ /
8.3.16-17.[2]	tenodanaṃ viṣyandayati /
8.3.16-17.[3]	'kṛṇve panthām' iti pādaṃ dātāraṃ vācayati /
8.3.16-17.[4]	'babhre rakṣaḥ' ityṛcodanamanumantrayate //
8.3.18-21.[1]	'atyāsaratprathamā dhokṣyamāṇā' ityardharcena abhisarantīṃ gāmanumantrayate /
8.3.18-21.[2]	'upa vatsaṃ sṛjata' iti pādena vatsaṃ saṃsarjayati /
8.3.18-21.[3]	'vāśyate gauḥ' iti vāśyāmānāmanumantrayate /
8.3.18-21.[4]	'vyasṛṣṭa sumanā hiṅkṛṇoti' iti hiṅkurvatīmanumantrayate /
8.3.18-21.[5]	'badhāna vatsamabhi dhehi' iti vatsaṃ bandhayati /
8.3.18-21.[6]	'bhuñjatī nijya' iti niyojayati /
8.3.18-21.[7]	'godhugupa sīda' iti brāhmaṇaṃ dohāyopasādayati /
8.3.18-21.[8]	'dugdhi' ityādi padasahitenārdharcena dohayati /
8.3.18-21.[9]	'sā dhāvatu' ityardharcena vimucyamānāṃ gāmanumantrayate /
8.3.18-21.[10]	'atūrṇadattā' ityardharcena punaḥ vatsena saṃsarjayati /
8.3.18-21.[11]	evaṃ dohayitvā dugdhenodanamavasicya //
8.3.22.[1]	'idaṃ me jyotiḥ' iti pādaṃ dātāraṃ vācayati /
8.3.22.[2]	hiraṇyamabhinidadhāti //
8.3.23.[1]	dātā sūktena sarvaṃ sampātavantaṃ karoti /
8.3.23.[2]	'śrāmyataḥ' itiprabhṛtibhirvā dātṛpatnyapatyāni anvārambhaṃ karoti //
8.4.1-2.[1]	tantraṃ sūktaṃ pacchaḥ snānena sarvaṃ vācayati /
8.4.1-2.[2]	tataḥ pūrvatantramucyate - 'yau te pakṣau' ityekā, 'yadatiṣṭhau divaḥ' ityekā, 'kramadhvamagninā' ityekā, 'pṛṣṭātpṛthivyāḥ' ityekā, 'svaryanto nāpekṣante' ityekā, 'uruḥ prathasva' ityekā, 'idaṃ me jyotiḥ' ityekā etatsarvaṃ tantram /
8.4.1-2.[3]	tataḥ savasūktaṃ vācayati /
8.4.1-2.[4]	tataḥ pradhānaṃ 'agne jāyasva' sūktaṃ vācayati /
8.4.1-2.[5]	athottaratantramucyate /
8.4.1-2.[6]	'satyāya ca' iti tisraḥ 'samagnayaḥ' ityṛcā 'eṣā tvacām' ityardharcaḥ /
8.4.1-2.[7]	ityuttaratantram /
8.4.1-2.[8]	atha pāṇitantramucyate dātā 'karmaṇe vām' iti pāṇī prakṣālya jīvābhirācamya 'ahe daidhiṣavya' ityādi 'vimṛgvarīm' ityetayā codaṅmukha upaviśya antarādudapātrāt sruveṇa karturhastena juhoti //
8.4.3.[1]	atha atharvavedabrāhmaṇānām āhvānakālaḥ /
8.4.3.[2]	dātā 'soma rājan' ityṛcā catura ārṣeyān bhṛgvaṅgirovida āhūya 'śṛtaṃ tvā havyam' ityardharcena tāneva āsanenopaveśayati //
8.4.4-5.[1]	'śuddhāḥ pūtā yoṣito yajñiyā imā brahmaṇā hasteṣu' ityṛcā teṣāṃ hastaprakṣālanaṃ dattvā 'pakvaṃ kṣetrāt' pādatrayeṇa odanapātraṃ brāhmaṇasamīpe karoti //
8.4.6.[1]	'agnau tuṣān' iti pādena dātā tuṣānagnau ca juhoti //
8.4.7-8.[1]	'paraḥ kambūkān' iti tribhiḥ pādairdātā savyena pādena phalīkaraṇānudūhati tūṣṇīm //
8.4.9.[1]	dātā 'agne prehi' ityṛcā 'samācinuṣva' ityṛcā dve etābhirājyaṃ juhuyāt //
8.4.9.[2]	idāvatsarāya iti vratavisarjanamājyaṃ juhuyāt //
8.4.10-25.[1]	iti brahmaudanaprakṛtisarvasavavidhānaṃ samāptam /
8.4.10-25.[2]	yaḥ ekaṃ savayajñaṃ karoti tasyaikakratuphalaṃ bhavati /
8.4.10-25.[3]	yo bahūni savayajñāni karoti tasya bahukratuphalaṃ bhavati /
8.4.10-25.[4]	atharvavedavihitā yāgā ete /
8.4.10-25.[5]	āvasathyādhāne savayajñān kṛtvā tato'gnyādhānaṃ kuryāt /
8.4.10-25.[6]	brahmaudanaṃ vā kṛtvādhānaṃ kuryāt /
8.4.10-25.[7]	ādhāne nityaṃ savadānaṃ kuryāt /
8.4.10-25.[8]	athavā phalakāmo'pi savayajñaṃ kuryāt /
8.4.10-25.[9]	trividhāḥ savayajñā nityanaimittikakāmyā bhavanti /
8.4.10-25.[10]	mantre trividhā vijñāyante /
8.4.10-25.[11]	samāpto brahmaudanaḥ /
8.4.10-25.[12]	savayajñāḥ kāmyā bhavanti /
8.4.10-25.[13]	naimittikā bhavanti /
8.4.10-25.[14]	trividhā bhavanti /
8.4.10-25.[15]	brahmaudanatantreṇa vā kuryāt /
8.4.10-25.[16]	sarveṣāṃ sarve savāḥ /
8.4.10-25.[17]	svargaudanatantreṇa vā kuryāt /
8.4.10-25.[18]	sarveṣāṃ savānāṃ brahmaudanatantraṃ svargaudanatantraṃ vā bhavati /
8.4.10-25.[19]	athavā sarve pṛthaktantrāḥ /
8.4.10-25.[20]	ekamantro nāsti /
8.4.10-25.[21]	sa tūṣṇīṃ kartavyaḥ /
8.4.10-25.[22]	dvāviṃśatiḥ savāḥ /
8.4.10-25.[23]	pañcaudana-śataudana-ajaudaneṣu viśeṣaḥ //
8.4.29.[1]	dātā karturhaste 'etaṃ bhāgam' 'etaṃ sadhasthāḥ' iti dvābhyāṃ sūktābhyāṃ, 'ulūkhale musale' ityṛcā etābhiḥ saṃsthitahomān juhoti //
8.4.30-31.[1]	kartā 'ulūkhale' ityṛcā vrīhīn juhoti //

8.9.34.[2]	dātā 'puṇyāhaṃ dīrghamāyurastu' ityevamādi vācanam //
8.5.1-2.[1]	savatantra ājyabhāgānte paśvālambhaḥ /
8.5.1-2.[2]	'yad rājānaḥ' iti ṣaïbhiravimīkṣate //
8.5.3.[1]	aveḥ pādaprakṣālanaṃ karoti tūṣṇīm /
8.5.3.[2]	caturṣu pādeṣu pṛthagapūpān nidadhāti //
8.5.4.[1]	pañcamamapūpaṃ nābhyāṃ vasanena bandhanaṃ karoti //

8.5.6.[1]	'ā nayaitam' ityṛcā avimānīyamānamanumantrayate //

8.5.17.[5]	ājyabhāgānte paśvālambhaḥ //
8.5.18-28.[1]	śeṣaṃ sūtrapaṭhitamavagantavyam /

8.7.1.[1]	'vāṅma āsan' iti mantroktānyabhimṛśata indriyāṇi //

8.7.22-33.[3]	abhicārakāmasya /

8.8.5-17.[1]	ekādaśyāṃ varaṇaṃ kṛtvā godānikena vidhānena keśaśmaśraromanakhāni vāpayitvā //
8.8.5-17.[2]	keśavarjaṃ patnī nakhāni kartayet /
8.8.5-17.[3]	snātāvahatavāsasau surabhiṇau bhūtvā dātā /
8.8.5-17.[4]	upanayanavad daṇḍamekhalā /

8.8.5-17.[6]	trirātraṃ dīkṣāgrahaṇaṃ saha patnyā /

9.3.4.[1]	'apāvṛtya' iti ṣaïbhirṛgbhiḥ kravyādaṃ gṛhītvā ekāgniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi niṣkramya tato gṛhadvāre bhūmau nidadhāti kravyādam //

11.2.34-37.[3]	ekāgnerapi /

11.2.34-37.[5]	'aṅgiraso naḥ pitaro navagvāḥ' iti saṃhatāḥ sapta iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ /
11.2.34-37.[6]	'pareyivāṃsam' iti dve 'aṅgiraso naḥ pitaraḥ' iti sapta 'ye naḥ pituḥ pitaro ye pitāmahāḥ' iti dve etāḥ samastā ekādaśa tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ /
11.2.34-37.[7]	etaiḥ samuccitairājyaṃ juhoti /

11.6.27.[2]	ṣaṣṭhī kaṇḍikā //85 //
11.7.1.[1]	'idaṃ kasāmbu' ityṛcā tānyasthīni gartasthitāni sarve gotriṇaḥ avekṣante /

11.7.2.[1]	'ye ca jīvāḥ' ityekā, 'ye te pūrve parāgatāḥ' ityekā iti dvābhyāṃ dvau carū sarpirmadhubhyāṃ pūrayitvābhimantrya śīrṣadeśe nidadhāti asthisamīpe //
11.7.3-4.[1]	'apūpavān' iti navabhirṛgbhiḥ paścimadiśi prabhṛti aṣṭau caravaḥ /
11.7.3-4.[2]	pratidiśaṃ nidadhāti /
11.7.3-4.[3]	ekaṃ madhye nidhāya tato'bhimantrayate /

11.7.5.[1]	'sahasradhāram' ityekā, 'śatadhāram' iti dve etābhiḥ śatacchidre sahasracchidre carupātramadhye nidhāyopari tata udakamabhimantrya tenodakenāplāvayatyasthīni //
11.7.6.[1]	'parṇo rājā' ityṛcā madhyamapalāśapatraiḥ śatacchidrasahasracchidrādi caravaśca sarvam ācchādayanti /

11.7.8.[1]	'utte stabhnāmi' ityṛcā loṣṭena ca carumasthīni ca pūrayati nidhānakrameṇa //

11.7.10.[1]	'idamidvā' iti tisraḥ, 'upa sarpa' iti tisraḥ, 'asau hā iha te' iti dve etābhirṛgbhiḥ śmaśānaṃ pitṛgṛhaṃ śilābhirviṣamābhiḥ iṣṭakābhirvā prasavyaṃ cinvanti /

11.7.17.[1]	tataḥ 'varcasā mām' iti dve 'vivasvānaḥ' ityādi 'indra kratuṃ naḥ' ityantam etaiḥ paścāt sthita upatiṣṭhante kartā gotriṇaśca //
11.7.18.[1]	'samindhate amartyam' iti dvābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ grāmamadhye yanmaṇḍapaṃ kṛtaṃ tat ānīya śmaśānapaścāddeśe prajvālayati dahati /

11.7.23-29.[4]	'śāmyākīrādadhāti /

13.1.40.[1]	grāmyo'gniḥ śālāṃ dahati grāmanagaraśālādidāhye laukikenāgninā //
13.1.41.[1]	vidyute vā sūryaprajvalite vā gṛhaṃ dahati āganturvā //
13.1.42.[1]	vaṃśaḥ sphoṭayati vaṃśasphoṭanaṃ balaharaṇabhaṅgadvārabhaṅgakapāṭādibhaṅgeṣu //
13.1.43.[1]	udakumbhe svayaṃ bhagne udakadhānamaliñjare bhagne ukhādibhāṇḍe saktudhānyāṃ haṇḍikā //
13.1.43.[2]	trayodaśe'dhyāye prathamā kaṇḍikā //93 //
13.2.1.[1]	'atha yatraitāni' ityādi pratinimittaśāntiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ /
13.2.1.[2]	athādbhutaśāntiryatra na kriyate tatra doṣo bhavati /
13.2.1.[3]	'tat parābhavati' ityādi paribhāṣā ucyate /
13.2.1.[4]	athādbhutaṃ yatra bhavati tat parābhavati vinaśyati /
13.2.1.[5]	vināśārthe adbhutaṃ devāḥ sṛjanti /
13.2.1.[6]	tathā coktaṃ sṛjanti divyā devādbhutāni prāgupasargapratibodhanārtham /
13.2.1.[7]	vināśe samupasthite /
13.2.1.[8]	kulaṃ vā grāmo vā janapado vā kule grāme nagare vā rāṣṭre vā yatrādbhutaṃ dṛśyate tatsarvaṃ vinaśyati //
13.2.2-4.[1]	tatra gṛhastho vā grāmapatirvā rājā vā bhūmipatiḥ /
13.2.2-4.[2]	yad bhṛgvaṅgirasa atharvāṅgirasa ityarthaḥ //
13.2.5-6.[1]	bāhye tantraprayogaḥ //
13.2.7-12.[1]	tato dvitīye'hani prātaḥ karmaprayogaḥ /
13.2.7-12.[2]	prathamata ayutahomalakṣahomau vā īśānayāgagrahayāganakṣatrayāganirṛtiyāgamaṇḍapasaṃskāravāstusaṃskārādi /
13.2.7-12.[3]	uttarataḥ sarvakarmaprayogaḥ /
13.2.7-12.[4]	iti sarvakarmasu paribhāṣā samāptā //
13.2.7-12.[5]	atha varṣādbhute śāntirucyate
13.2.13-14.[1]	ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'ghṛtasya dhārā' iti dvābhyāmājyaṃ juhuyāt //
13.2.15.[1]	'divyo gandharvaḥ' ityādi mātṛnāmnā gaṇenājyaṃ juhuyāt /
13.2.15.[2]	sarvatra śāntyudakaṃ yojayet /
13.2.15.[3]	sarvatra cātanānyanuyojayet /
13.2.15.[4]	mātṛnāmāni cānuyojayet /
13.2.15.[5]	varāṃ dhenuṃ kartre dadyāt /
13.2.15.[6]	sarvatra kaṃsavasanaṃ gaurdakṣiṇā /
13.2.15.[7]	brāhmaṇān bhaktenopepsanti /
13.2.15.[8]	tataḥ pārvaṇādyuttaratantram //
13.2.16-18.[1]	dhenvādīni sarvatra kāṃsyādīni ca dakṣiṇā vā /
13.2.16-18.[2]	ghṛtavarṣe /
13.2.16-18.[3]	māṃsavarṣe /
13.2.16-18.[4]	madhuvarṣe /
13.2.16-18.[5]	hiraṇyavarṣe /
13.2.16-18.[6]	pāṃsuvarṣe /
13.2.16-18.[7]	sarpamatsyapakṣiṇo yadābhyavarṣanti /
13.2.16-18.[8]	asthīni rudhiraṃ vasā majjā pāṣāṇāstrairvā kīṭāni anyāścānyaṃ ca ghoraṃ varṣaṇaṃ dadhi payo tailaṃ ca pakvānnavikārāśca /
13.2.16-18.[9]	anyeṣāṃ ghorāṇāṃ varṣaṇe idaṃ karma kuryāt /
13.2.16-18.[10]	samāptā vikṛtavarṣādbhūtaśāntiḥ //
13.2.16-18.[11]	dvitīyā kaṇḍikā //94 //
13.3.0.[1]	atha yakṣādbhutaśāntirucyate
13.3.1-5.[1]	śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā kārayitācamanaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ kṛtvājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yanmarkaṭaḥ śvāpadaḥ' ityṛcājyaṃ juhuyāt /
13.3.1-5.[2]	mātṛnāmagaṇenājyaṃ juhuyāt /
13.3.1-5.[3]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /

13.3.1-5.[5]	rakṣo vā hastino vā sūkaro vā kūpe ghaṭe vāraṇye vā gṛhe vā rakṣorūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā vapustatkṣaṇādeva na dṛśyate /

13.5.0.[1]	atha kulakalahe adbhutaśāntirucyate

13.14.0.[1]	atha lāṅgalasaṃsarge śāntirucyate
13.14.1-9.[1]	araṇye gatvā tatra prācīṃ sītāṃ sthāpayitvā sītāyā madhye śāntyudakādi ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ śamyāḥ paridhīn kṛtvā tataḥ puroḍāśaṃ juhoti /

13.24.0.[1]	atha yatraitat pipīlikā anācārarūpā dṛśyante tatra śāntirucyate
13.24.1-3.[1]	śāntyudakādi ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'bhuvāya svāhā' iti sūktenājyaṃ juhuyāt /
13.24.1-3.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
13.24.1-3.[3]	raktā kṛṣṇā pītā vā bahuśaḥ pipīlikā bhavanti tatra śāntiḥ //
13.24.1-3.[4]	atha pipīlikābhicāra ucyate
13.24.4-8.[1]	śāntyudakādi ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā śaramayaṃ barhirubhayataḥ paricchinnaṃ prasavyaṃ paristaraṇaṃ viṣāvadhvastamiṅgiḍamājyam /
13.24.4-8.[2]	śākapalāśenājyasya utpavanaṃ bādhakena sruveṇa homaḥ /
13.24.4-8.[3]	'uttiṣṭhata nirdravatam' iti sūktena iṅgiḍaṃ juhoti /
13.24.4-8.[4]	yathārthamudarkān yojayet /
13.24.4-8.[5]	'uktānuktasya' iti pañcapaṭalikāyāmuktaṃ punaruktalakṣaṇam /
13.24.4-8.[6]	'anuṣaṅgo vākparisamāptiḥ' mīmāṃsāyām /
13.24.4-8.[7]	'yamo vaḥ sarvāsāṃ sākam' /
13.24.4-8.[8]	'varuṇo vaḥ sarvāsām' /
13.24.4-8.[9]	'agnirvaḥ sarvāsām' /
13.24.4-8.[10]	'vāyurvaḥ sarvāsām' /
13.24.4-8.[11]	'sūryo vaḥ sarvāsām' /
13.24.4-8.[12]	'candro vaḥ sarvāsām' /
13.24.4-8.[13]	'prajāpatirvaḥ sarvāsām' /
13.24.4-8.[14]	'īśāno vaḥ sarvāsām' /
13.24.4-8.[15]	'sākaṃ garbhānāṇḍāni bhetsyati /
13.24.4-8.[16]	phaḍḍhatāḥ pipīlikāḥ' /
13.24.4-8.[17]	pratimantram uccārayati /
13.24.4-8.[18]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
13.24.4-8.[19]	pipīlikābhicāraśāntiḥ samāptā /
13.24.4-8.[20]	anyā yadi pipīlikā dṛṣṭvā vyādhiṃ janayati raktakṛṣṇaśvetapītanīlā anekavidhāḥ pipīlikā gṛhe bhavanti /
13.24.4-8.[21]	agniśaraṇe vā kṣetre vā nagare vā grāme vā api bahuśo bhavanti /
13.24.4-8.[22]	annamadhye rasamadhye ghṛte vā ājātvatā dṛśyante tatrābhicāraḥ kriyate //
13.24.4-8.[23]	caturviṃśī kaṇḍikā //116 //
13.25.0.[1]	atha makṣikāśāntirucyate
13.25.1-5.[1]	śāntyudakādi ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yā matyaiḥ saratham' iti sūktena 'vāta ā vātu bheṣajam' iti sūktena ca dvābhyāmājyaṃ juhoti /
13.25.1-5.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
13.25.1-5.[3]	nīlamakṣikā gṛhe patati anyavarṇā vā bhavanti makṣikāśāntiḥ samāptā //
13.25.1-5.[4]	pañcaviṃśī kaṇḍikā //117 //
13.26.0.[1]	atha madhujālake gṛhe lagna śāntirucyate
13.26.1-2.[1]	śāntyudakamājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'madhu vātā ṛtāyate' ityetena sūktenājyaṃ juhuyāt /
13.26.1-2.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
13.26.1-2.[3]	madhujālake gṛhe lagne'bhyantare bahirvā dṛṣṭadeśe vā lagne tatra śāntiḥ samāptā //
13.26.1-2.[4]	ṣaḍviṃśī kaṇḍikā //118 //
13.27.0.[1]	atha sarvādbhuteṣu śāntirucyate
13.27.1-5.[1]	śāntyudakādi ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'yadājñātam' iti 'puruṣasammitaḥ' sūktābhyāmājyaṃ juhuyāt /
13.27.1-5.[2]	'yathārthamudarkān yojayet' ityatraivoktam /
13.27.1-5.[3]	'anuṣaṅgo vākyaparisamāptiḥ' iti mīmāṃsāyām /
13.27.1-5.[4]	'uktānuktasya' ityuktaṃ pañcapaṭalikāyām /
13.27.1-5.[5]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram //
13.27.1-5.[6]	anājñāte'dbhute yad granthe na paṭhyate tat sarvamanājñātamityucyate /
13.27.1-5.[7]	yadapi pariśiṣṭeṣu paṭhyate sarve gṛhe praviṣṭe sarvamevālpakaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvasammito vāyuṃ sambhrame udakaprādurbhāve gamaneṣu dhanuḥsandhyolkāḥ pariveṣāḥ vidyuddaṇḍāśaniparipraparighārddhe nirghāte rajovarṣa-upalavarṣadakṣimadhughṛtavarṣamajjārudhiravarṣatihīnagabhastī dve mārge vidyut vittakṣaye somasya kṣaye pūrṇapūraṇe kṣayasyavabhāsā sadyopararātrādi digdāhopadhūpanagrahavaiṣamyamārohaṇamākramaṇaṃ gandharvanagaramārutaprakopaḥ tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatrayogadhruvakakāni grahādīnāṃ samaviyogaḥ /
13.27.1-5.[8]	pratisrotagāminyo nadyaḥ /
13.27.1-5.[9]	prasravaṇāni ca /
13.27.1-5.[10]	prāsādatoraṇāṭṭāladhvajachatre ca vāyasāḥ samavāyād vṛkaśakaṭārohaṇam /
13.27.1-5.[11]	vṛṣadaṃśābhighātamajjanam /
13.27.1-5.[12]	sulabhamamulūkapratigarjanam /
13.27.1-5.[13]	śyenāśca tāni gṛdhrādīnāṃ dhvajāliṅghanam /
13.27.1-5.[14]	vikṛtāśca mānuṣo manujā manuṣaprabhavāḥ striyo vā bālaṃ vā vṛddhaṃ vā pralāpāḥ yuvānaḥ vā yuvataraḥ pralapati pradīptendriyayaṣṭipādabhaṅge dravye dvicchāyāpraticchāyāmṛjyatamapṛktam /
13.27.1-5.[15]	ata ūrdhvaṃ chāyām adhachāyāmadhyachāyordhvachāyā akasmāccaityavṛkṣastambhapatane virohaṇāt skandharohe maṣṭatyachinnaparṇa pramā vā śuṣko vā śuṣkaśākhino dhūmarajataudakaprādurbhāvagamaneṣu vanaspatiṣu vanataruṣu bāhuśastrabhaṅge vā indranīlagopurāṭṭālakādi dhvajachatrādīnāṃ bhaṅgeṣu vā bhaṅgaḥ ucitānyabhyucchedane'nucitānāṃ pravartane dṛḍhabhaṅge vā śuṣkavirohe gṛhe valmīke śayanadeśe garbhāstasyotpattau viparītau mitraprītau ca devatārcanayoḥ anayoḥ chedane yatra ca rājā prasṛtyādiṣu ca bhavanti /
13.27.1-5.[16]	bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ /
13.27.1-5.[17]	yadā tu prakṛtiḥ somaḥ viparītaṃ hi dṛśyati /
13.27.1-5.[18]	madhye chidramiti dṛśyet maraṇaṃ rājagocaram //
13.27.1-5.[19]	yadā tu pratipatsomaḥ prakṛtyā vikṛto bhavet /
13.27.1-5.[20]	anudbhinno vilūne vā rājño maraṇamādiśet //
13.27.1-5.[21]	āyudhākārarūpāṇi śatavarṇākṛtīni ca /
13.27.1-5.[22]	pañcavarṇāni cābhrāṇi tathā daṇḍanibhāni ca //
13.27.1-5.[23]	yadā candrārkayormadhye kṛṣṇaṃ bhavati maṇḍalam /
13.27.1-5.[24]	saṃ śaṅkuriti vijñeyo grahaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ //
13.27.1-5.[25]	tatra rājā vadhaṃ vindyāt sarvabhūtabhayāvaham /
13.27.1-5.[26]	tatra kuryānmahāśāntimamṛtāṃ viśvabheṣajīm //
13.27.1-5.[27]	atha yasminneva janapade gobrāhmaṇasūtasāṃvatsaravaidyānāṃ parivrājakacāraṇavānaprasthabrahmacāriṇāṃ strīṇāṃ vāpyaparaḥ pravartante tadbhutaṃ vidyāt /
13.27.1-5.[28]	tat karmasaṅkaraṃ yajanavyavahārayajñasaṅkaraṃ ca bhavataḥ /
13.27.1-5.[29]	yatra ca dharmo'dharmeṇa pīḍyate tatra dharmo adharmeṣu tadādbhutaṃ vidyāt /
13.27.1-5.[30]	brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrādi parasparaṃ bādhate eteṣu yadi śāntiṃ na kuryāt tadā mahādbhutāni bhavanti /
13.27.1-5.[31]	devatāprādurbhāvagamaneṣu paravante ca anṛte gavāṃ roge pravṛtte /
13.27.1-5.[32]	durbhikṣe ca janapadādivināśe ādityabhedeṣu mūṣikeṣu pravṛtteṣu kīṭapataṅge matkuṇayūkālikṣāpakṣiṇe pravṛtte rājakulavāde aśvāstraṃ śastraṃ vā gṛhasarvagajavājivastrālaṅkārapīṭhikāvyañjanāni agninā pradaheta ariṣṭadarśane śāntibhedaḥ /
13.27.1-5.[33]	pṛthivyāmantarikṣe divye ca eṣā śāntiḥ /
13.27.1-5.[34]	sevitaṃ rājamaśvānāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ ṣaṇmukhānāṃ tathā rūpāṇi vikṛtāni yatrāraṇyaṃ ca pathi ca tathā rājā darvīnāṃ kṛtatritākṣīṇāṃ grāme kule vā yadi vāpi deśe rājanyamānyeṣu tathā dvijeṣu bhāvaḥ paśūnāṃ vikṛtau rūpaḥ tathā mānuṣe ca /
13.27.1-5.[35]	atha svanakṣatraṃ ahopahatamulkābhihataṃ grastaṃ nirastamupadhūpitaṃ vā yadasyojjanmanakṣatraṃ karmanakṣatramabhiṣecanīyaṃ janapadanakṣatraṃ rājaṣṭame candramasaḥ sthāne vajre'vasṛṣṭe skambhe vāvasṛṣṭe skandhe vāvasṛṣṭe nānārūpabahurūpe śṛṅgiṇi vādityena kilavati cembudani colkābhihate kambu dhuvati ṣavati hasati hāse bhāse nāde śabde vāsate ca vaiśvānaraprajvalite antarikṣe ca bhasma asthi aṅgārā gṛhe vā śirasi vā patanti vīdhrī cendradhanuṣi rātrau vīdhra eva tu candrārkanakṣatragrahatārādi parikhe kākakapotagṛdhrayakṣarākṣasapiśācaśvāpadeṣu rātrau vadatsu gāyatsu vādyatsu vāte prādurbhāvagamane cakradhvajaveśmāvasavaprasādāgrāṃ vā kūpa udadhāne codgirati nadati vidyotati rathayantrapravahaṇavāditrāṇi sūktādayodgārā dhūmarci vā prādurbhāvaliṅgāṅgaviliṅge rājñaḥ prādurbhāve vā rājñī rājā kākolūkakṛkalāsagṛhagodhikāvāsenādhipatite rājachatre bhagne dhvaje śukrasya bhagne rājñe daṇḍasya bhagne hastinyāṃ ca mattāyāṃ grāme ca prasūtāyāṃ rājarathaśca rājādhirūḍho bhagnākṣaḥ saptarātrau rājño hanti /
13.27.1-5.[36]	purohitavināśe vā senāpatināśe hastinaṃ mahiṣīvināśe kumāravināśe paśumānuṣe vā vikāraḥ /
13.27.1-5.[37]	dviśīrṣā pratiśīrṣā vā pādahasti tathaiva ca dvināsikaḥ tathā hīnādhikāṅgulivināśe taistu jāyate /
13.27.1-5.[38]	tathā pādajaṅghayoḥ karṇanāsikāvināśe śiracchedastu jāyate //
13.27.1-5.[39]	bījaṃ yatra praroheta phalamadhye pramādataḥ /
13.27.1-5.[40]	madhvājyadadhidugdheṣu bhakṣamāṇe vilepane /
13.27.1-5.[41]	yantravāhanaharmyeṣu bhavaneṣvāyudheṣu ca /
13.27.1-5.[42]	kākolūkakapotānāmadvīrvā darśanaṃ bhavet /
13.27.1-5.[43]	anye ca praśnānāmagame mṛgapakṣiṇām /
13.27.1-5.[44]	kṛṣṇayugmānāṃ darśanaṃ gṛhe vāmitatejasaḥ /
13.27.1-5.[45]	sarpāṇāṃ darśanaṃ caiva sarīsṛpagaṇasya vā /
13.27.1-5.[46]	vikārā yatra dṛśyante kṣīraudanahaviḥṣu vā /
13.27.1-5.[47]	āyurjanānāṃ puruṣasya tathāyuṣyasya yuñjanāt /
13.27.1-5.[48]	yānti yānānyayuktāni vinā vātairnṛbhistathā /
13.27.1-5.[49]	yuktāni vā na gacchanti narendrāṇāṃ mahadbhayam /
13.27.1-5.[50]	bheryo mṛdaṅgāḥ paṭahā vādyante vāpyanāhatāḥ /
13.27.1-5.[51]	āhatāśca na vādyante acalāni calanti vā /
13.27.1-5.[52]	araṇye tūryanirghoṣo yadi śrūyeta nābhasaḥ /
13.27.1-5.[53]	goṣṭho vā nṛtyate yatra haste darvī kadācana /
13.27.1-5.[54]	patate musalaṃ yatra hanyamāne viśeṣataḥ /
13.27.1-5.[55]	ulūkhalaṃ śūrpaṃ vā dhūyate svayam /
13.27.1-5.[56]	pāṣāṇaḥ kūpaṃ parvatāprasarpaṇe /
13.27.1-5.[57]	golāṅgalānāṃ saṃsarge vikāraścandrasūryayoḥ /
13.27.1-5.[58]	nārī vā dhayate nārīṃ jāyate taṇḍulaṃ bhayam /
13.27.1-5.[59]	pratyāhāraṃ visarpanti stambapāṣāṇapādapāḥ /
13.27.1-5.[60]	śakunānāṃ payasi tathaiva mṛgapakṣiṇām /
13.27.1-5.[61]	amānuṣāṇāṃ vyāhāre sthāvarāṇāṃ vyatikrame /
13.27.1-5.[62]	yonivyatikare vaidhā māṃsaśoṇitavarṣaṇe /
13.27.1-5.[63]	anagnijvalane caiva tathā nābhravarṣaṇe /
13.27.1-5.[64]	śastraprajvalane caiva caityaśuṣkāvarohaṇe /
13.27.1-5.[65]	liṅgāyatanacitrāṇāṃ rodane garjane tathā /
13.27.1-5.[66]	udadhāne taḍāgānāṃ jvalane garjite'pi vā /
13.27.1-5.[67]	matsyasarpadvijātīnāṃ rasānāṃ ca pravarṣaṇe /
13.27.1-5.[68]	gītavāditraśabdāstu yatra syuranimittataḥ /
13.27.1-5.[69]	ye cānye kiñcidutpātā jāyante vikṛtātmakāḥ /
13.27.1-5.[70]	teṣāṃ sarveṣāmutpātānāmeṣā śāntirvidhīyate /
13.27.1-5.[71]	candraprātipadike grahayuddhe grahasaṅgrahe rāhucāre ketucāre rāhuketulakṣaṇe kūmavibhāge maṇḍaleṣu digdāheṣu ulkāpataneṣu vidyutpataneṣu vidyuddarśaneṣu nirghātapataneṣu candrasūryayoḥ pariveṣe nakṣatragrahotpātalakṣaṇe utpātalakṣaṇe sadyovṛṣṭilakṣaṇe adbhutaśāntipaṭhiteṣu svapnādhyāyapaṭhiteṣu duḥsvapneṣu sarveṣu yadājñātā śāntiḥ /
13.27.1-5.[72]	atharvahṛdayeṣu adbhuteṣu paṭhiteṣu bhārgavīyeṣu paṭhiteṣu gārgyapaṭhiteṣu adbhuteṣu bārhaspatyagrantheṣu paṭhiteṣu uśanasagrantheṣu paṭhiteṣu mahādbhuteṣu paṭhiteṣu itihāsapurāṇe jyotiḥśāstre aśvavaidyake naravaidyakeṣu paṭhiteṣu adbhuteṣu sarvādbhuteṣu eṣā śāntiḥ /
13.27.1-5.[73]	athavā mahāśāntiramṛtā ghṛtakambalaṃ koṭihomaḥ sarvādbhuteṣu kauśikāpaṭhiteṣu eṣā śāntiḥ mahāśāntirvā vikalpāt iti bhāṣyakāraḥ //
13.27.1-5.[74]	saptaviṃśī kaṇḍikā //119 //
13.28.0.[1]	agniśaraṇe vā samajyāyāṃ vāvadaraṇe śāntirucyate
13.28.1-14.[1]	catasro dhenava upaklṛptā bhavanti śvetā kṛṣṇā rohiṇī surūpā caturthī /
13.28.1-14.[2]	tāsāmetad dvādaśarātraṃ sandugdhaṃ navanītaṃ nidadhāti /
13.28.1-14.[3]	dvādaśyāḥ prātaryatraivādo'vadīrṇaṃ bhavati tata uttarataḥ śāntyudakādi ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā śvetāyā ājyena odanaṃ sannīya tataḥ 'agnirbhūmyām' iti tisṛbhiranvālabhya gṛhaṃ tataḥ pūrvato juhoti /
13.28.1-14.[4]	tathā kṛṣṇāyā dakṣiṇārdhe tathā rohiṇyā dakṣiṇārdhe tathā surūpāyā dakṣiṇārdhe tasminnevāgnau odanamājyena sannīya tato vāstoṣpatyena gaṇenājyaṃ juhvannavadīrṇadeśaṃ sampātānānayati /
13.28.1-14.[5]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
13.28.1-14.[6]	tato'vadīrṇaṃ śāntyudakena samprokṣya gāṃ dadāti /
13.28.1-14.[7]	sarvatra dhenvādīni ca /
13.28.1-14.[8]	gṛhe patite grāme vā śmaśāne vā agniśaraṇe vā kṣetrabhūmipātane bhūmicchidradarśane bhūmipāte gṛhapāte grāmādipatane eṣā śāntiḥ /
13.28.1-14.[9]	athavā caturdikṣu catvāri vā tantrāṇi yathāsaṅkhyam /
13.28.1-14.[10]	śvetākṛṣṇādi pratidiśaṃ juhoti /
13.28.1-14.[11]	pūrvārdhe juhoti /
13.28.1-14.[12]	pūrvatantre dakṣiṇā dhenuḥ sarvatra /
13.28.1-14.[13]	tantropaveśanakhim tantre vedyuttaraveditantram /
13.28.1-14.[14]	tataḥ śaṅkhādyāḥ sampātāḥ /
13.28.1-14.[15]	sarvasmin tantre bhavati dārilamatam /
13.28.1-14.[16]	pūrvaṃ samāpya tantraṃ tato dakṣiṇataḥ paścāduttarataḥ /
13.28.1-14.[17]	samāpya tantraṃ śāntyudakena samprokṣya tā gā brāhmaṇo dadyāt /
13.28.1-14.[18]	sīraṃ vaiśyo'śvaṃ prādeśiko grāmavaraṃ rājā /
13.28.1-14.[19]	varaṃ dhenvādi sarvatra dadyāt /
13.28.1-14.[20]	gṛhagrāmajanapade ca śāntiḥ samāptā /
13.28.1-14.[21]	aṣṭāviṃśī kaṇḍikā //120 //
13.29.0.[1]	atha yatraitadanudakadeśe udakātiśayo bhavati tatra śāntirucyate
13.29.1-2.[1]	śāntyudakādyājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'hiraṇyavarṇāḥ' 'yadadaḥ' ityapāṃ sūktaiḥ sarvaiḥ ājyaṃ juhoti /
13.29.1-2.[2]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
13.29.1-2.[3]	anudakadeśe yadyatiśayena udakaṃ dṛśyate /
13.29.1-2.[4]	udakonmīlanaśāntiḥ samāptā //
13.29.1-2.[5]	ūnatriṃśī kaṇḍikā //121 //
13.30.0.[1]	atha tilāḥ samatalā bhavanti tatra śāntirucyate
13.30.1-3.[1]	śāntyudakādi ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā 'anūnāya svāhā' ityetaiścaturbhirājyaṃ juhoti /
13.30.1-3.[2]	sa yaṃ dviṣyāt iti mantreṇa dakṣiṇāmukho bhūtvā śāntyudakena tilān siñcet /
13.30.1-3.[3]	pārvaṇādyuttaratantram /
13.30.1-3.[4]	yadā tailaṃ na bhavati tadā śāntiḥ /
13.30.1-3.[5]	tilāḥ samatailabhavane śāntiḥ samāptā //

13.35.0.[1]	atha dhūmaketuśāntirucyate
13.35.1-13.[1]	ekatantre vā kuryāt pṛthaktantre vā kuryāt /

13.35.1-13.[3]	evaṃ dvādaśarātrau bhūtvā trayodaśe'hani karmaprayogaḥ /
13.35.1-13.[4]	pākatantramājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā pañca paśavastāyante vāruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo'jaḥ vāyavo harito'jaḥ diśyo bahurūpo'jaḥ mārutī meṣī apāṃ naptre udraḥ jalavirālaḥ biḍālo vā āgneyaśca prājāpatyaśca kṣīraudanau /
13.35.1-13.[5]	mantramadhye śrapaṇam /

13.35.1-13.[11]	sarveṣāṃ samānatantrapakṣaḥ /

13.35.1-13.[15]	vapāhomānte paśvitikartavyatā /
13.35.1-13.[16]	tato'vadānāni dadāti /
13.35.1-13.[17]	juhotītyarthaḥ /
13.35.1-13.[18]	'uteyaṃ bhūmiḥ' ityṛcāgniprayogaḥ /
13.35.1-13.[19]	varuṇaṃ manasā dhyāyet /
13.35.1-13.[20]	'apsu te rājan' iti catasṛbhiḥ vāruṇasya paśoravadānāni juhuyāt pratyṛcaṃ sthālīpākaṃ ca /
13.35.1-13.[21]	tathā 'vāyavā rundhi naḥ' iti vāyavyasya /
13.35.1-13.[22]	'āśānām' iti sūktena pratyṛcaṃ diśyasya paśoḥ sthālīpākaṃ caiva /
13.35.1-13.[23]	'prati tyaṃ cārumadhvaram' ityṛcā mārutasya paśoravadānaṃ carośca /
13.35.1-13.[24]	'apāmagniḥ' ityṛcāgneyapaśorāgneyaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ juhoti /
13.35.1-13.[25]	'prajāpatiḥ salilādā' ityṛcā prajāpatikṣīraudanaṃ juhoti dvitīyām /
13.35.1-13.[26]	'niḥsālābhityulmukena triḥ prasavyaṃ pariharati' iti /
13.35.1-13.[27]	tantraṃ kṛtvā tato'pāṃ sūktaiḥ sarvairhiraṇyaśakalena sahodramapsu praveśayet /
13.35.1-13.[28]	pāśukaṃ tantraṃ samāpayet /
13.35.1-13.[29]	yavaiḥ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ dadāti /
13.35.1-13.[30]	vyāpakaradāpadārtho bhedena ārādupakāratantreṇa bhavati /
13.35.1-13.[31]	evaṃ mīmāṃsā yojayitavyā /
13.35.1-13.[32]	śeṣaṃ samānam /
13.35.1-13.[33]	tantrapakṣe atideśo viśeṣātideśo yojayitavyaḥ /
13.35.1-13.[34]	ūhabādhābhyudayatantraṃ maṅgalalakṣaṇāni yojayitavyāni /
13.35.1-13.[35]	samāptā dhūmaketuśāntiḥ /
13.35.1-13.[36]	dhūmaketu re vā nānyo dhūmaketurvidyate /
13.35.1-13.[37]	tathā ketucāre /

14.3.1.[1]	śrāvaṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā proṣṭhapadyāṃ vā abhijiti nakṣatre śiṣyānupanīya ācāryasamīpa āgacchanti //

14.3.7.[1]	tata uttarairgaṇairājyaṃ juhvan dadhisaktuṣu sampātānānayati /

14.3.7.[3]	'vidmā śarasya' 'mā no vidan' 'adārasṛt' 'svastidā' 'ava manyuḥ' , 'nirhastaḥ' 'parivartmāni' /
14.3.7.[4]	'abhibhūḥ' 'indro jayāti' 'abhi tvendra' ityaparājitagaṇaḥ /
14.3.7.[5]	'sahṛdayam' , 'tadū ṣu' 'sañjānīdhvam' 'eha yātu' , 'saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantām' 'saṃ vo manāṃsi' 'sañjñānaṃ naḥ' iti gaṇakarmagaṇaḥ /
14.3.7.[6]	'ye triṣaptāḥ' iti viśvakarmagaṇaḥ /
14.3.7.[7]	'asmin vasu vasavo dhārayantu' , 'viśve devā vasavaḥ' 'ā yātu mitraḥ' 'amutra bhūyāt' 'antakāya mṛtyave' 'ā rabhasva' 'prāṇāya namaḥ' 'viṣāsahim' ityāyuṣyagaṇaḥ /
14.3.7.[8]	'tyamū ṣu' 'trātāraṃ' 'ā mandraiḥ' iti svastyayanagaṇaḥ //
14.3.8.[1]	'mā no devā ahirvadhīt' 'arasasya śarkoṭasya', 'indrasya prathamo rathaḥ', 'yaste sarpo vṛścikastṛṣṭadaṃśmā', 'namaste astu vidyute', 'āre'sāvasmadastu', 'yaste pṛthu stanayitnuḥ' ityupākarmagaṇaḥ /

14.5.30-32.[2]	tathā brahmacāriṇaṃ ca rājānaṃ ca nādhīyīta /
14.5.30-32.[3]	anṛtau varṣe garjite vidyutkṛte ekarātraṃ nādhīyīta /
14.5.30-32.[4]	ṛtau upasadi nādhīyīta /
14.5.30-32.[5]	daivopahatau ekarātraṃ nādhīyīta /
14.5.30-32.[6]	ṛtau tu tāvatkālaṃ nādhīyīta //
14.5.33-41.[1]	nirghātabhūmikampolkāketudarśananakṣatrapātadigdāhavarṣakṛtlohitaindradhanuḥpratisūryagomāyūlūkakalahādīni adbhuteṣu sarveṣu trirātraṃ nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[2]	kalpanāṃ yathā vedeṣu tathā kuryāt /
14.5.33-41.[3]	athavādbhuteṣu tāvatkālaṃ nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[4]	athavā madhyāhna dārabhyānadhyāyaḥ /
14.5.33-41.[5]	rātrau vidyuddarśane anadhyāyaḥ /
14.5.33-41.[6]	rātrau garjite ca rātriśeṣe nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[7]	atha tāvatkālaṃ bhuktvā pradoṣamadhyarātre nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[8]	ubhe ca sandhye nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[9]	apsumadhye nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[10]	śmaśāne nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[11]	abhiśaste pātakinaḥ saṃsarge sannidhāne nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[12]	khile ūṣare nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[13]	gṛhe śavapatite catuṣpādadvipadeṣu patite nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[14]	adhvāyāṃ gacchannādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[15]	grāmamadhye nagaramadhye nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[16]	cāṇḍālasannidhāne śabdaśravaṇe nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[17]	durgandhapurīṣādigandhe nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[18]	yatra bahavaḥ śūdrā militvā śṛṇvanti tatra nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[19]	paiṅgaśabde yatra cāturvedyādiṣu ekarātraṃ militvā śabdaṃ kurvanti tatra nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[20]	athavā dravyādināśe vā vaidhṛtyanagaragrāmādicaurarājādinarādyupadrave brāhmaṇādyupadrave nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[21]	malinavāsasā parihito nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[22]	yena vastreṇa parihitena maithunamācarati tena vastreṇa parihito nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[23]	śayanakhaṭvāyāmārūḍho nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[24]	prauḍhapādau pādopari pādaṃ kṛtvā nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[25]	agre guroḥ prasārya pādaṃ śuktikāṃ vā baddhvā nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[26]	viramya mārute śīghre nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[27]	svādhyāyaṃ samāpya punarnādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[28]	athavā kāṇḍaṃ samāpya nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[29]	ativāte nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[30]	pratyārambhaṃ kṛtvā nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[31]	eteṣu anadhyāyeṣu apararātri viramya nādhīyīta /
14.5.33-41.[32]	prabhāte adhyayanaṃ kuryāt //
14.5.42-43.[1]	pauṣīpramāṇaṃ prabhṛti abhreṣu /
14.5.42-43.[2]	varṣaṃ vidyutstanayitnurvā nādhīyīta //
14.5.44-45.[1]	anadhyāye paṭhite idaṃ prāyaścittaṃ kuryāt /
14.5.44-45.[2]	trirātraṃ divā ūrdhvas tiṣṭhet rātrau upaviśed etad eva prāyaścittam /
14.5.44-45.[3]	brahmacārī rasabhakṣaṇe etad eva prāyaścittam /
14.5.44-45.[4]	sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ //
14.5.44-45.[5]	caturdaśe'dhyāye pañcamī kaṇḍikā //141 //
